[0001,i_0021,i]	pramaṇataḥ artha pratipattau pravṛtti sāmarthyāt arthavat pramāṇam pramāṇam antareṇa na artha pratipattiḥ na artha pratipattim antareṇa pravṛtti sāmarthyam pramāṇena khalu ayam jñāta artham abhīpsati jihāsati vā tasya īpsā ajihāsā prayuktasya samīhā pravṛttiḥ iti ucyate sāmrthyam punar asyāḥ phalena abhisambandhaḥ samīhamānaḥ tam artham abhīpsan jihāsan vā tam artham āpnoti jahāti vā arthaḥ tu sukham sukha hetuḥ ca duḥkham duḥkha hetuḥ ca 
[0022,i_0025,i]	saḥ ayam pramāṇa arthaḥ aparisaṅkhyeyaḥ prāṇabhṛt bhedasya aparisaṅkhyeya tvāt arthavati ca pramāṇe pramātā prameyam pramitiḥ iti arthavanti bhavanti kasmāt anyatama apāye arthasya anupapatteḥ tatra yasya īpsā ajihāsā prayuktasya pravṛttiḥ sa pramātā sa yena artham pramiṇoti tat pramāṇam yaḥ arthaḥ pramīyate tat prameyam yat artha vijñānam sā pramitiḥ catasṛṣu ca evaṃvidhāsu artha tattvam parisamāpyate kim punar tattvam sataḥ ca sadbhāvaḥ asataḥ ca asadbhāvaḥ sat sat iti gṛhyamāṇam yathābhūtam aviparītam tattvam bhavati asat ca asat iti gṛhyamāṇam yathābhūtam aviparītam tattvam bhavati 
[0026,i]	katham uttarasya pramāṇena upalabdhiḥ iti sati upalabhyamāne tad anupalabdheḥ pradīpa vat yathā darśakena dīpena dṛśye gṛhyamāṇe tat iva yat na gṛhyate tat na asti yadi abhaviṣyat idam iva vyajñāsyata vijñāna abhāvāt na asti iti evam pramāṇena sati gṛhyamāṇe tat iva yat na gṛhyate tat na asti yadi abhaviṣyat idam iva vyajñāsyata vijñāna abhāvāt na asti iti tat evam sataḥ prakāśakam pramāṇam asat api prakāśayati iti 
[0028,i_0029,i]	sat ca khalu ṣoḍaśadhā vyūḍham upadekṣyate tāsām khalu āsām sadvidhānām pramāṇa prameya saṃśaya prayojana dṛṣṭānta siddhānta avayava tarka nirṇaya vāda jalpa vitaṇḍā hetvābhāsa chala ja ati nigraha sthānānām tattva jñānāt niḥśreyasa adhigamaḥ nirdeśe yathāvacanam vigrahaḥ ca arthe dvandva samāsaḥ pramāṇa ādīnām tattvam iti śaiṣikī ṣaṣṭhī 
[0031,i_0034,i]	tattvasya jñānam niḥśreyasasya adhigamaḥ iti karmaṇi ṣaṣṭhau te etāvantaḥ vidyamāna arthāḥ yeṣām aviparīta jñāna artham iha upadeśaḥ saḥ ayam anavayavena tantra arthaḥ uddiṣṭaḥ veditavyaḥ ātma ādeḥ khalu prameyasya tattva jñānāt niḥśreyasa adhigamaḥ tat ca etat uttara sūtreṇa anūdyate iti heyam tasya nirvartakam hānam ātyantikam tasya upāyaḥ adhigantavyaḥ iti etāni catvāri artha padāni samyak buddhvā niḥśreyasam adhigacchati tatra saṃśaya ādīnām pṛthak vacanam anarthakam saṃśaya ādayaḥ yathāsambhavam pramāṇeṣu prameyeṣu ca antarbhavantaḥ na vyatiricyante iti satyam etat imāḥ tu catasraḥ vidyāḥ pṛthak prasthānāḥ prāṇabhṛtām anugrahāya upadiśyante yāsām caturthī iyam ānvīkṣikī nyāya vidyā 
[0035,i]	tasyāḥ pṛthak prasthānāḥ saṃśaya ādayaḥ padārthāḥ teṣām pṛthak vacanam antareṇa adhyātma vidyā mātram iyam syāt yathā upaniṣadaḥ tasmāt saṃśaya ādibhiḥ padārthaiḥ pṛthak prasthāpyate tatra na anupalabdhe na nirṇīte arthe nyāyaḥ pravartate kim tarhi saṃśayite arthe yathā uktam vimṛśya pakṣa pratipakṣābhyām artha avadhāraṇam nirṇayaḥ iti vimarśaḥ saṃśayaḥ pakṣa pratipakṣau nyāya pravṛttiḥ artha avadhāraṇam nirṇayaḥ tattva jñānam iti sa ca ayam kiṃsvid iti vastu vimarśa mātram anavadhāraṇam jñānam saṃśayaḥ prameye antarbhavan evam artham pṛthak ucyate 
[0037,i_0039,i]	atha prayojanam yena prayuktaḥ pravartate tat prayojanam yam artham abhīpsan jihāsan vā karma ārabhate tena anena sarve prāṇinaḥ sarvāṇi karmāṇi sarvāḥ ca vidyāḥ vyāptāḥ tad āśrayaḥ ca nyāyaḥ pravartate kaḥ punar ayam nyāyaḥ pramāṇaiḥ artha parīkṣaṇam nyāyaḥ pratyakṣa āgama āśritam anumānam sa anvīkṣā pratyakṣa āgamābhyām īkṣitasya anvīkṣaṇam anvīkṣā tayā pravarttate iti ānvīkṣikī nyāya vidyā nyāya śāstram yat punar anumānam pratyakṣa āgama viruddham nyāya ābhāsaḥ saḥ iti 
[0044,i]	tatra vāda jalpau sa prayojanau vitaṇḍā tu parīkṣyate vitaṇḍayā pravartamānaḥ vaitaṇḍikaḥ sa prayojanam anuyuktaḥ yadi pratipadyate saḥ asya pakṣaḥ saḥ asya siddhānte iti vaitaṇḍika tvam jahāti atha na pratipadyate na ayam laukikaḥ na parīkṣakaḥ iti āpadyate atha api para pakṣa pratiṣedha jñāpanam prayojanam bravīti etat api tādṛś eva yaḥ jñāpayati yaḥ jānāti yena jñāpyate yat ca jñāpyate etat ca pratipadyate yadi tadā vaitaṇḍika tvam jahāti atha na pratipadyate para pakṣa pratiṣedha jñāpanam prayojanam iti etat asya vākyam anarthakam bhavati vākya samūhaḥ ca sthāpanā hīnaḥ vitaṇḍā tasya yadi abhidheyam pratipadyate saḥ asya pakṣaḥ sthāpanīyaḥ bhavati atha na pratipadyate pralāpa mātram anarthakam bhavati vitaṇḍā tvam nivartate iti 
[0044,ii_0045,i]	atha dṛṣṭāntaḥ pratyakṣa viṣayaḥ arthaḥ yatra laukika parīkṣakāṇām darśanam na vyāhanyate sa ca prameyam tasya pṛthak vacanam ca tad āśrayau anumāna āgamau tasmin sati syātām anumāna āgamau asati ca na syātām tad āśrayā ca nyāya pravṛttiḥ dṛṣṭānta virodhena ca para pakṣa pratiṣedhaḥ vacanīyaḥ bhavati dṛṣṭānta samādhinā ca sva pakṣaḥ sādhanīyaḥ bhavati nāstikaḥ ca dṛṣṭāntam abhyupagacchan āstika tvam jahāti anabhyupagacchan kiṃsādhanaḥ param upālabheta iti niruktena ca dṛṣṭāntena śakyam abhidhātum sādhya sādharmyāt tad dharma bhāvī dṛṣṭāntaḥ udāharaṇam tad viparyayāt viparītam iti 
[0046,i_0048,i]	asti ayam iti anujñāyamānaḥ arthaḥ siddhāntaḥ sa ca prameyam tasya pṛthak vacanam satsu siddhānta bhedeṣu vāda jalpa vitaṇḍāḥ pravartante na atas anyathā iti sādhanīya arthasya yāvati śabda samūhe siddhiḥ parisamāpyate tasya pañca avayavāḥ pratijña ādayaḥ samūham apekṣya avayavāḥ ucyante teṣu pramāṇa samavāyaḥ āgamaḥ pratijñā hetuḥ anumānam 
[0051,i_0053,ii]	udāharaṇam pratyakṣam upanayanam upamānam sarveṣām eka artha samavāye sāmarthya pradarśanam nigamanam iti saḥ ayam paramaḥ nyāyaḥ iti etena vāda jalpa vitaṇḍāḥ pravartante na atas anyathā iti tad āśrayā ca tattva vyavasthā te ca ete avayavāḥ śabda viśeṣāḥ santaḥ prameye antarbhūtāḥ evam artham pṛthak ucyante iti tarkaḥ na pramāṇa saṃgṛhītaḥ na pramāṇa antaram pramāṇānām anugrāhakaḥ tattva jñānāya kalpate tasya udāharaṇam kim idam janma kṛtakena hetunā nirvartyate āhosvit akṛtakena atha ākasmikam iti 
[0054,i]	evam avijñāte arthe kāraṇa upapattyā ūhaḥ pravarttate yadi kṛtakena hetunā nirvartyate hetu ucchedāt upapannaḥ ayam janma ucchedaḥ atha ākṛtakena hetunā tatas hetu ucchedasya aśakya tvāt anupapannaḥ janma ucchedaḥ atha ākasmikam atas akasmāt nirvartyamānam na punar nivartsyati iti nivṛtti kāraṇam na upapadyate tena janma anucchedaḥ iti etasmin tarka viṣaye karma nimittam janma iti pramāṇāni pravarttamānāni tarkeṇa anugṛhante tattva jñāna viṣayasya vibhāgāt tattva jñānāya kalpate tarkaḥ iti saḥ ayam itthambhūtaḥ tarkaḥ pramāṇa sahitaḥ vāde sādhanāya upālambhāya ca arthasya bhavati iti evam artham pṛghak ucyate prameya antarbhūtaḥ api iti 
[0056,i_0057,i]	nirṇayaḥ tattva jñānam pramāṇānām phalam tad avasānaḥ vādaḥ tasya pālana artham jalpa viṭaṇḍe tau etau tarka nirṇayau lokayātrām vahate iti saḥ ayam nirṇayaḥ prameya antarbhūtaḥ evam artham pṛthak uddīṣṭaḥ iti vādaḥ khalu nānā pravaktṛkaḥ pratyadhikaraṇa sādhanaḥ anyatara adhikaraṇa nirṇaya avasānaḥ vākya samūhaḥ 
[0058,i_0063,i]	pṛthak uddiṣṭaḥ upalakṣaṇa artham upalakṣitena vyavahāraḥ tattva jñānāya bhavati iti tad viśeṣau jalpa vitaṇḍe tattva adhyavasāya saṃrakṣaṇa artham iti uktam nigraha sthānebhyaḥ pṛthak uddhiṣṭāḥ hetvābhāsāḥ vāde codanīyāḥ bhaviṣyanti iti jalpa vitaṇḍayoḥ tu nigraha sthānāni iti chala ja ati nigraha sthānānām pṛthak upadeśaḥ upalakṣaṇa artham iti upalakṣitānām sva vākye parivarjanam chala ja ati nigraha sthānānām para vākye paryanuyogaḥ jāteḥ ca pareṇa prayujyamānāyāḥ sulabhaḥ samādhiḥ svayam ca sukaraḥ prayogaḥ iti 
[0064,i_0065,i]	sā iyam ānvīkṣikī pramāṇa ādibhiḥ padārthaiḥ vibhajyamānā pradīpaḥ sarva vidyānām upāyaḥ sarva karmaṇām āśrayaḥ sarva dharmāṇām vidyā uddeśe prakīrtitā tat idam tattva jñānam niḥśreyasa adhigama artham yathāvidyam veditavyam iha tu adhyātma vidyāyām ātma ādi jñānam tattva jñānam niḥśreyasa adhigamaḥ apavarga prāptiḥ 
[0067,i_0071,i]	tat khalu niḥśreyasam kim tattva jñāna antaram eva bhavati na iti ucyate kim tarhi tattva jñānāt duḥkha janma pravṛtti doṣa mithyā jñānām uttarottara apāye tad anantara apāyāt apavargaḥ tatra ātma ādi apavarga paryanta prameye mithyājñānam aneka prakārakam varttate ātmani tāvat na asti iti anātmani ātmā iti duḥkhe sukham iti anitye nityam iti atrāṇe trāṇam iti sa bhaye nirbhayam iti jugupsite abhimatam iti hātavye apratihātavyam iti pravṛttau na asti karma na asti karma phalam iti doṣeṣu na ayam doṣa nimittaḥ saṃsāraḥ iti pretyabhāve na asti jantuḥ jīvaḥ vā sattvaḥ ātmā vā yaḥ preyāt pretya ca bhavet iti animittam janma animittaḥ janma uparamaḥ iti ādimān pretyabhāvaḥ anantaḥ ca iti naimittikaḥ san akarma nimittaḥ pretyabhāvaḥ iti deha indriya buddhi vedanā santāna uccheda pratisandhānābhyām nirātmakaḥ pretyabhāvaḥ iti apavarge bhīṣmaḥ khalu ayam sarva kāya uparamaḥ sarva viprayoge apavarge bahu ca bhadrakam lupyate iti katham buddhimān sarva sukha ucchedam acaitanyam amum apavargam rocayet iti 
[0071,ii]	etasmāt mithyājñānāt anukūleṣu rāgaḥ pratikūleṣu dveṣaḥ rāga dveṣa adhikārāt ca asatya īrṣya māyā lobha ādayaḥ doṣāḥ bhavanti doṣaiḥ prayuktaḥ śarīreṇa pravarttamānaḥ hiṃsā steya pratiṣiddha maithunāni ācarati vācā anṛta paruṣa sūcanā sambaddhāni manasā para droham para dravya abhīpsām nāstikyam ca iti sā iyam pāpa ātmikā pravṛttiḥ adharmāya 
[0071,iii_0078,i]	atha śubhā śarīreṇa dānam paritrāṇam paricaraṇam ca vācā satyam hitam priyam svādhyāyam ca iti manasā dayām aspṛhām śraddhām ca iti sā iyam dharmāya atra pravṛtti sādhanau dharma adharmau pravṛtti śabdena uktau yathā anna sādhanāḥ prāṇāḥ annam vai prāṇinaḥ prāṇāḥ iti sā iyam pravṛttiḥ kutsitasya abhipūjitasya ca janmanaḥ kāraṇam janma punar śarīra indriya buddhīnām nikāya viśiṣṭaḥ prādurbhāvaḥ tasmin sati duḥkham tat punar pratikūla vedanīyam bādhanā pīḍā tāpaḥ iti te ime mithyājñāna ādayaḥ duḥkhāntāḥ dharmāḥ avicchedena eva pravartamānāḥ saṃsāraḥ iti yadā tu tattva jñānāt mithyājñānam apaiti tadā mithyā jñāna apāye doṣāḥ apayanti doṣa apāye pravṛttiḥ apaiti pravṛtti apāye janma apaiti janma apāye duḥkham apaiti duḥkha apāye ca ātyantikaḥ apavargaḥ niḥśreyasam iti 
[0082,i]	tattva jñānam tu khalu mithyājñāna viparyayeṇa vyākhyātam ātmani tāvat asti iti anātmani anātmā iti evam duḥkhe anitye atrāṇe sa bhaye jugupsite hātavye ca yathā viṣayam veditavyam pravṛttau asti karma asti karma phalam iti doṣeṣu doṣa nimittaḥ ayam saṃsāraḥ iti pretyabhāve khalu asti jantuḥ jīvaḥ sattvaḥ ātmā vā yaḥ pretya bhavet iti nimitta vat janma nimittavān janma uparamaḥ iti anādiḥ pretyabhāvaḥ apavarga ante iti naimittikaḥ san pretyabhāvaḥ pravṛtti nimittaḥ iti sa ātmakaḥ san deha indriya buddhi vedanā santāna uccheda pratisandhānābhyām pravarttate iti apavarge śāntaḥ khalu ayam sarva viprayogaḥ sarva uparamaḥ apavargaḥ bahu ca kṛccham ghoram pāpakam lupyate iti katham buddhimān sarva duḥkha ucchedam sarva duḥkhā saṃvidam apavargam na rocayet iti tat yathā madhu viṣa sampṛkta annam anādeyam iti evam sukham duḥkha anuṣaktam anādeyam iti 
[0082,ii_0084,i]	trividhā ca asya śāstrasya pravṛttiḥ uddeśaḥ lakṣaṇam parīkṣā ca iti tatra nāmadheyena padārtha mātrasya abhidhānam uddeśaḥ tatra uddiṣṭasya tattva vyavacchedakaḥ dharmaḥ lakṣaṇam lakṣitasya yathālakṣaṇam upapadyate na vā iti pramāṇaiḥ avadhāraṇam parīkṣā tatra uddiṣṭasya pravibhaktasya lakṣaṇam ucyate yathā pramāṇānām prameyasya ca uddhiṣṭasya lakṣitasya ca vibhāga vacanam yathā chalasya vacana vighātaḥ artha vikalpa upapattyā cchalam tat trividham iti atha uddiṣṭasya vibhāga vacanam pratyakṣa anumāna upamāna śabdāḥ pramāṇāni 
[0086,i_0091,ii]	akṣasya akṣasya prativiṣayam vṛttiḥ pratyakṣam vṛttiḥ tu sannikarṣaḥ jñānam vā yadā sannikarṣaḥ tadā jñānam pramitiḥ yadā jñānam tadā hāna upādāna upekṣā buddhayaḥ phalam anumānam mitena liṅgena liṅginaḥ arthasya paścāt mānam anumānam upamānam sāmīpya jñānam yathā gauḥ evam gavayaḥ iti sāmīpyam tu sāmānya yogaḥ śabdaḥ śabdyate anena arthaḥ iti abhidhīyate jñāpyate upalabdhi sādhanāni pramāṇāni samākhyā nirvacana sāmarthyāt boddhavyam pramīyate anena iti karaṇa artha abhidhānaḥ hi pramāṇa śabdaḥ tad viśeṣa samākhyāyāḥ api tathā eva vyākhyānam kim punar pramāṇāni prameyam abhisaṃplavante atha pratiprameyam vyavatiṣṭhante iti 
[0092,i]	ubhayathā darśanam asti ātmā iti āpta upadeśāt pratīyate tatra anumānam icchā dveṣa prayatna sukha duḥkha jñānāni ātmanaḥ liṅgam iti pratyakṣam yuñjānasya yoga samādhi jam ātma manasoḥ saṃyoga viśeṣāt ātmā pratyakṣaḥ iti agniḥ āpta upadeśāt pratīyate atra agniḥ iti pratyāsīdatā dhūma darśanena anumīyate pratyāsannena ca pratyakṣataḥ upalabhyate vyavasthā punar agnihotra juhuyāt svarga kāmaḥ iti laukikasya svarge na liṅga darśanam na pratyakṣam stanayitnu śabde śrūyamāṇe śabda hetoḥ anumānam tatra na pratyakṣam na āgamaḥ pāṇau pratyakṣataḥ upalabhyamāne na anumānam na āgamaḥ iti 
[0092,ii_0092,iii]	sā ca iyam pramitiḥ pratyakṣa parā jijñāsitam artham āpta upadeśāt pratipadyamānaḥ liṅga darśanena api bubhutsate liṅga darśana anumitam ca pratyakṣataḥ didṛkṣate upalabdhe arthe jijñāsā nivarttate pūrva uktam udāharaṇam agniḥ iti pramātuḥ pramāṇānām sambhavaḥ abhisaṃplavaḥ asambhavaḥ vyavasthā iti iti tri sūtrī bhāṣyam 
[0092,iv_0094,i]	atha vibhaktānām lakṣaṇa vacanam iti indriya artha sannikarṣa uttpannam jñānam avyapadeśyam avyabhicāri vyavasāya ātmakam pratyakṣam indriyasya arthena sannikarṣāt utpadyate yat jñānam tat pratyakṣam na tarhi idānīm idam bhavati ātmā manasā saṃyujyate manaḥ indriyeṇa indriyam arthena iti 
[0098,i_0100,i]	na idam kāraṇa avadhāraṇam etāvat pratyakṣe kāraṇam iti kim tu viśiṣṭa kāraṇa vacanam iti yat pratyakṣa jñānasya viśiṣṭa kāraṇam tat ucyate yat tu samānam anumāna ādi jñānasya na tat nivarttate iti manasaḥ tarhi indriyeṇa saṃyogaḥ vaktavyaḥ bhidyamānasya pratyakṣa jñānasya na ayam bhidyate iti samāna tvāt na uktaḥ iti 
[0109,i]	yāvat artham vai nāmadheya śabdāḥ taiḥ artha sampratyayaḥ artha sampratyayāt ca vyavahāraḥ tatra idam indriya artha sannikarṣāt utpannam artha jñānam rūpam iti vā rasaḥ iti evam vā bhavati rūpa rasa śabdāḥ ca viṣaya nāmadheyam tena vyapadiśyate jñānam rūpam iti jānīte rasaḥ iti jānīte nāmadheya śabdena vyapadiśyamānam sat śābdam prasajyate atas āha avyapadeśyam iti 
[0110,i]	yat idam anupayukte śabda artha sambandhe artha jñānam na tat nāmadheya śabdena vyapadiśyate gṛhīte api ca śabda artha sambandhe asya arthasya ayam śabdaḥ nāmadheyam iti yadā tu saḥ arthaḥ gṛhyate tadā tat pūrvasmāt artha jñānāt na viśiṣyate tat artha vijñānam tādṛś eva bhavati tasya tu artha jñānasya anyaḥ samākhyā śabdaḥ na asti iti yena pratīyamānam vyavahārāya lakpeta na ca apratīyamānena vyavahāraḥ tasmāt jñeyasya arthasya saṃjñā śabdena iti karaṇa yuktena nirdiśyate rūpam iti jñānam rasaḥ iti jñānam iti tat evam artha jñāna kāle sa na samākhyā śabdaḥ vyāpriyate vyavahāra kāle tu vyāpriyate tasmāt aśa abdam artha jñānam indriya artha sannikarṣa utpannam iti 
[0112,i_0121,i]	grīṣme marīcayaḥ bhaumena ūṣmaṇā saṃsṛṣṭāḥ spandamānāḥ dūra sthasya cakṣuṣā sannikṛṣyante tatra indriya artha sannikarṣāt udakam iti jñānam utpadyate tat ca pratyakṣam prasajyate iti atas āha avyabhicāri iti yat atasmin tat iti tat vyabhicāri pratyakṣam iti dūrāt cakṣuṣā hi ayam artham paśyan na avadhārayati dhūmaḥ iti vā reṇuḥ iti vā tat etat indriya artha sannikarṣa utpannam anavadhāraṇa jñānam pratyakṣam prasajyate iti atas āha vyavasāya ātmakam iti na ca etat mantavyam ātma manaḥ sannikarṣa jam eva anavadhāraṇa jñānam iti cakṣuṣā hi ayam artham paśyan na avadhārayati yathā ca indriyeṇa upalabdham artham manasā upalabhate evam indriyeṇa anavadhārayat manasā na avadhārayati yat ca tad indriya anavadhāraṇa pūrvakam manasā anavadhāraṇam tat viśeṣa apekṣam vimarśa mātram saṃśayaḥ na pūrvam iti sarvatra pratyakṣa viṣaye jñātuḥ indriyeṇa vyavasāyaḥ paścāt manasā anuvyavasāyaḥ upahata indriyāṇām anuvyavasāya abhāvāt iti 
[0121,ii_0129,i]	ātma ādiṣu sukha ādiṣu ca pratyakṣa lakṣaṇam vaktavyam anindriya artha sannikarṣa jam hi tat iti indriyasya vai sataḥ manasaḥ indriyebhyaḥ pṛthak upadeśaḥ dharma bhedāt bhautikāni indriyāṇi niyata viṣayāṇi sa guṇānām ca eṣām indriya bhāvaḥ iti manaḥ tu abhautikam sarva viṣayam ca na asya sa guṇasya indriya bhāvaḥ iti sati ca indriya artha sannikarṣe sannidhim asannidhim ca asya yugapad jñāna anutpatti kāraṇam vakṣyāmaḥ iti manasaḥ ca indriya bhāvāt na vācyam lakṣaṇa antaram iti tantra antara samācārāt ca etat pratyetavyam iti para matam apratiṣiddham anumatam iti hi tantra yuktiḥ vyākhyātam pratyakṣam 
[0132,i_0146,i]	atha tad pūrvakam trividham anumānam pūrvavat śeṣavat sāmānyatas dṛṣṭam ca tad pūrvakam iti anena liṅga liṅginoḥ sambandha darśanam liṅga darśanam ca abhisambadhyate liṅga liṅginoḥ sambaddhayoḥ darśanena liṅga smṛtiḥ abhisambadhyate smṛtyā liṅga darśanena ca apratyakṣaḥ arthaḥ anumīyate 
[0146,ii_0148,i]	pūrvavat iti yatra kāraṇena kāryam anumīyate yathā megha unnatyā bhaviṣyati vṛṣṭiḥ iti śeṣavat tat yatra kāryeṇa kāraṇam anumīyate pūrva udaka viparītam udakam nadyāḥ pūrṇa tvam śīghra tvan ca dṛṣṭvā srotasaḥ anumīyate bhūtāḥ vṛṣṭiḥ iti sāmānyatodṛṣṭam vrajyā pūrvakam anyatra dṛṣṭasya ṇi atra darśanam iti tathā ca ādityasya tasmāt asti apratyakṣā api ādityasya vrajyā iti 
[0152,i]	atha vā pūrvavat iti yatra yathāpūrvam pratyakṣa bhūtayoḥ anyatara darśanena anyatarasya anumānam apratyakṣasya anumānam yathā dhūmena agniḥ iti śeṣa vat nāma pariśeṣaḥ sa ca prasakta pratiṣedhe ṇi atra aprasaṅgāt śiṣyamāṇe sampratyayaḥ yathā sat anityam evamādinā dravya guṇa karmaṇām aviśeṣeṇa sāmānya viśeṣa samavāyebhyaḥ vibhaktasya śabdasya tasmin dravya karma guṇa saṃśaye na dravyam eka dravya tvāt na karma śabda antara hetutvāt yaḥ tu śiṣyate saḥ ayam iti śabdasya guṇa tva pratipattiḥ 
[0156,i_0158,i]	sāmānyatodṛṣṭam nāma yatra apratyakṣe liṅga liṅginoḥ sambandhe kenacid arthena liṅgasya sāmānyāt apratyakṣaḥ liṅgī gamyate yathā icchā ādibhiḥ ātmā icchā ādayaḥ guṇāḥ guṇāḥ ca dravya saṃsthānāḥ tat tat eṣām sthānam saḥ ātmā iti vibhāga vacanāt eva trividham iti siddhe trividha vacanam mahataḥ mahā viṣayasya nyāyasya laghīyasā sūtreṇa upadeśāt param vākya lāghavam manyamānasya anyasmin vākya lāghave anādaraḥ tathā ca ayam itthaṃbhūtena vākya vikalpena pravṛttaḥ siddhānte chale śabda ādiṣu ca bahulam samācāraḥ śāstre iti sat viṣayam ca pratyakṣam sat asat viṣayam ca anumānam kasmāt traikālya grahaṇāt tri kāla yuktāḥ arthāḥ anumānena gṛhyante bhaviṣyati iti anumīyate bhavati iti ca abhūt iti ca asat ca khalu attam anāgatam ca iti 
[0168,i_0172,i]	atha upamānam prasiddha sādharmyāt sādhya sādhanam upamānam prajñātena sāmānyāt prajñāpanīyasya prajñāpanam upamānam iti yathā gauḥ evam gavayaḥ iti kim punar atra upamānena kriyate yadā khalu ayam gavā samāna dharmam pratipadyate tadā pratyakṣataḥ tam artham pratipadyate iti samākhyā sambandha pratipattiḥ upamāna arthaḥ iti āha yathā gauḥ evam gavayaḥ iti upamāne prayukte gavā samāna dharmam artham indriya artha sannikarṣāt upalabhamānaḥ asya gavaya śabdaḥ saṃjñā iti saṃjñā saṃjñi sambandham pratipadyate iti yathā mudgaḥ tathā mudgaparṇī yathā māṣaḥ tathā māṣaparṇī iti upamāne prayukte upamānāt saṃjñā saṃjñi sanandham pratipadyamānaḥ tām oṣadhīm bhaiṣajyāya āharati evam anyaḥ api upamānasya loke viṣayaḥ bubhutsitavyaḥ iti 
[0173,i_0176,i]	atha śabdaḥ āpta upadeśaḥ śabdaḥ āptaḥ khalu sākṣātkṛta dharmā yathādṛṣṭasya arthasya cikhyā apayiṣayā prayuktaḥ upadeṣṭā sākṣātkaraṇam arthasya āptiḥ tayā pravartate iti āptaḥ ṛṣi āri amlecchānām samānam lakṣaṇam tathā ca sarveṣām vyavahārāḥ pravarttante iti evam ebhiḥ pramāṇaiḥ deva manuṣya tiraścām vyavahārāḥ prakalpante na atas anyathā iti 
[0179,i_0179,ii]	sa dvividhaḥ dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa artha tvāt yasya iha dṛśyate arthaḥ sa dṛṣṭa arthaḥ yasya amutra pratīyate saḥ adṛṣṭa arthaḥ evam ṛṣi laukika vākyānām vibhāgaḥ iti kimartham punar idam ucyate sa na manyeta dṛṣṭa arthaḥ eva āpta upadeśaḥ pramāṇam arthasya avadhāraṇāt iti adṛṣṭa arthaḥ api pramāṇam arthasya anumānāt iti 
[0180,i_0182,i]	kim punar anena pramāṇena artha jātam pramātavyam iti ātma śarīra indriya artha buddhi manaḥ pravṛtti doṣa pretya bhāva phala duḥkha apavargāḥ tu prameyam tatra ātmā sarvasya draṣṭā sarvasya bhoktā sarvajñaḥ sarva anubhāvī tasya bhoga āyatanam śarīram bhoga sādhanāni indriyāṇi bhoktavyāḥ indriya arthāḥ bhogaḥ buddhiḥ sarva artha upalabdhau na indriyāṇi prabhavanti iti sarva viṣayam antaḥkaraṇam manaḥ śarīra indriya artha buddhi sukha vedanānām nivṛtti kāraṇam pravṛttiḥ doṣāḥ ca na asya idam śarīram apūrvam anuttaram ca pūrva śarīrāṇām ādiḥ na asti uttareṣām apavargaḥ antaḥ iti pretyabhāvaḥ sa sādhana sukha duḥkha upabhogaḥ phalam duḥkham iti na idam anukūla vedanīyasya sukhasya pratīteḥ pratyākhyānam kim tarhi janmanaḥ eva idam sa sukha sādhanasya duḥkha anuṣaṅgāt duḥkhena aviprayogāt vividha bādhana ayogāt duḥkham iti samādhi bhāvanam upadiśyate 
[0183,i]	samāhitaḥ bhāvayati bhāvayan nirvidyate nirviṇṇasya vairāgyam viraktasya apavargaḥ iti janma maraṇa prabandha ucchedaḥ sarva duḥkha prahāṇam apavargaḥ iti asti anyat api dravya guṇa karma sāmānya viśeṣa samavāyāḥ prameyam tad bhedena ca aparisaṅkhyā iyam asya tu tattva jñānāt apavargaḥ mithyājñānāt saṃsāraḥ iti atas etat upadiṣṭam viśeṣeṇa iti 
[0184,i_0185,i^1]	tatra ātmā tāvat pratyakṣataḥ na gṛhyate sa kim āpta upadeśa mātrāt eva pratipadyate iti na iti ucyate anumānāt ca pratipattavyaḥ iti katham icchā dveṣa prayatna sukha duḥkha jñānāni ātmanaḥ liṅgam iti yat jātīyasya arthasya sannikarṣāt sukham ātma upalabdhavān tad jātīyam eva artham paśyan upādātum icchati sā iyam ādātum icchā ekasya aneka artha darśinaḥ darśana pratisandhānāt bhavati liṅgam ātmanaḥ niyata viṣaye hi buddhi bheda mātre na sambhavati deha antara vat iti evam ekasya aneka artha darśinaḥ darśana pratisandhānāt duḥkha hetau dveṣaḥ yat jātīyaḥ asya arthaḥ sukha hetuḥ prasiddhaḥ tad jātīyam artham paśyan ādātum prayatate ekam aneka artha darśinam darśana pratisandhātāram antareṇa na syāt niyata viṣaye buddhi mātre na sambhavati deha antara vat iti 
[0185,i^2_0188,i]	etena duḥkha hetau prayatnaḥ vyākhyātaḥ sukha duḥkha smṛtyā ca ayam tad sādhanam ādadānaḥ sukham upalabhate duḥkham upalabhate sukha duḥkhe vedayate pūrva uktaḥ eva hetuḥ bubhutsamānaḥ khalu ayam vimṛśati kiṃsvid iti vimṛśan ca jānīte idam iti tat idam jñānam bubhutsā vimarśābhyām abhinna kartṛkam gṛhyamāṇam ātma liṅgam pūrva uktaḥ eva hetuḥ iti tatra deha antara vat iti vibhajyate yathā anātma vādinaḥ deha antareṣu niyata viṣayā buddhi bhedā na pratisandhīyante tathā eka deha viṣayāḥ api na pratisandhīyeran aviśeṣāt saḥ ayam eka sattvasya samācāraḥ svayaṃdṛṣṭasya smaraṇam na anyat dṛṣṭasya na adṛṣṭasya iti evam khalu nānā sattvānām samācāraḥ anya dṛṣṭam anyaḥ na smarati iti tat etat ubyayam aśakyam anātma vādinā vyavasthāpayitum iti evam upapannam asti ātmā iti 
[0193,i_0195,i]	tasya bhoga adhiṣṭhānam ceṣṭa indriya artha āśrayaḥ śarīram katham ceṣṭā āśrayaḥ īpsitam jihāsitam vā artham adhikṛtya īpsā ājihāsa aprayuktasya tad upāya anuṣṭhāna lakṣaṇā samīhā ceṣṭā sā yatra varttate tat śarīram katham indriya āśrayaḥ yasya anugraheṇa anugṛhītāni upaghāte ca upahatāni sva viṣayeṣu sādhu asādhuṣu vartante saḥ eṣām āśrayaḥ tat śarīram katham artha āśrayaḥ yasmin āyatane indriya artha sannikarṣāt utpannayoḥ sukha duḥkhayoḥ pratisaṃvedanam pravartate saḥ eṣām āśrayaḥ tat śarīram iti 
[0197,i_0199,i]	bhoga sādhanāni punar ghrāṇa rasana cakṣuḥ tvac śrotrāṇi indriyāṇi bhūtebhyaḥ jighrati anena iti ghrāṇam gandham gṛhṇāti iti rasayati anena iti rasanam rasam gṛhṇāti iti caṣṭe anena iti cakṣuḥ rūpam paśyati iti tvac sthānam indriyam tvac tad upacāraḥ sthānāt iti śṛṇoti anena iti śrotram śabdam gṛhṇāti iti evam samākhyā nirvacana sāmarthyāt bodhyam sva viṣaya grahaṇa lakṣaṇāni indriyāṇi iti bhūtebhyaḥ iti nānā prakṛtīnām eṣām satām viṣaya niyamaḥ na eka prakṛtīnām sati ca viṣaya niyame sva viṣaya grahaṇa lakṣaṇa tvam bhavati iti 
[0201,i_0201,iii]	kāni punar indriya kāraṇāni pṛthivī āpaḥ tejaḥ vāyuḥ ākāśam iti bhūtāni saṃjñā śabdaiḥ pṛthak upadeśaḥ bhūtānām vibhaktānām su vacam kāryam bhaviṣyati iti 
[0202,i_0202,iii]	ime tu khalu gandha rasa rūpa sparśa śabdāḥ pṛthivī ādi guṇāḥ tad arthāḥ pṛthivī ādīnām yathā viniyogam guṇāḥ indriyāṇām yathākramam arthāḥ viṣayāḥ iti 
[0213,i_0214,i]	acetanasya karaṇasya buddheḥ jñānam vṛttiḥ cetanasyākartuḥ upalabdhiḥ iti yukti viruddham artham pratyācakṣāṇakaḥ iva idam āha buddhiḥ upalabdhiḥ jñānam iti anartha antaram na acetanasya karaṇasya buddheḥ jñānam bhavitum arhati tat dhi cetanam syāt ekaḥ ca ayam cetanaḥ deha indriya saṃghāta vyatiriktaḥ iti prameya lakṣaṇa arthasya vākyasya anya artha prakāśanam upapatti sāmarthyāt iti 
[0215,i_0217,i]	smṛti anumāna āgama saṃśaya pratibhāsvapna jñāna ūhāḥ sukha ādi pratyakṣam icchā ādayaḥ ca manasaḥ liṅgāni teṣu satsu ayam api yupagat jñāna anutpattiḥ manasaḥ liṅgam anindriya nimittāḥ smṛti ādayaḥ karaṇa antara nimittāḥ bhavitum arhanti iti yugapad ca khalu ghrāṇa ādīnām gandha ādīnām ca sannikarṣeṣu satsu yugapad jñānāni na utpadyante tena anumīyate asti tat tat indriya saṃyogi sahakāri nimitta antaram avyāpi yasya asannidheḥ na utpadyate jñānam sannidheḥ ca utpadyate iti manaḥ saṃyoga anapekṣasya hi indriyārtha sannikarṣasya jñāna hetu tve yugapad uptadyeran jñānāni iti 
[0218,i_0218,iii]	krama prāptā tu pravṛttiḥ vāc buddhi śarīra ārambhaḥ manaḥ atra buddhiḥ iti abhipretam budhyate anena iti buddhiḥ saḥ ayam ārambhaḥ śarīreṇa vācā manasā ca puṇyaḥ pāpaḥ ca daśavidhaḥ tat etat kṛta bhāṣyam dvitīya sūtraḥ iti 
[0220,i_0220,ii]	pravartanā lakṣaṇāḥ doṣāḥ pravartanā pravṛtti hetu tvam jñātāram hi rāga ādayaḥ pravartayanti puṇye pāpe vā yatra mithyājñānam tatra rāga dveṣau iti pratyātma vedanīyāḥ hi ime doṣāḥ kasmāt lakṣaṇataḥ nirdiśyante iti karma lakṣaṇāḥ khalu rakta dviṣṭa mūḍhāḥ raktaḥ hi tat karma kurute yena karmaṇā sukham duḥkham vā labhate tathā dviṣṭaḥ tathā mūḍhaḥ iti rāga dveṣa mohāḥ iti ucyamāne bahu na uktam bhavati iti 
[0221,i_0222,i]	punar utpattiḥ pretyabhāvaḥ utpannasya kvacid sattva nikāye mṛtvā yā punar utpattiḥ sa pretyabhāvaḥ utpannasya sambaddhasya sambandhaḥ tu deha indriya manaḥ buddhi vedanābhiḥ punar utpattiḥ punar deha ādibhiḥ sambandhaḥ punar iti abhyāsa abhidhānam yatra kvacid prāṇa bhṛt nikāye vartamānaḥ pūrva upāttān deha ādīn jahāti tat praiti yat tatra anyatra vā deha ādīn anyān upādatte tat bhavati pretyabhāvaḥ mṛtvā punarjanma saḥ ayam janma maraṇa prabandha abhyāsaḥ anādiḥ apavarga antaḥ pretyabhāvaḥ veditavyaḥ iti 
[0222,ii_0223,i]	pravṛtti doṣa janitaḥ arthaḥ phalam sukha duḥkha saṃvedanam phalam sukha vipākam karma duḥkha vipākam ca tat punar deha indriya viṣaya buddhiṣu satīṣu bhavati iti saha deha ādibhiḥ phalam abhipretam tathā hi pravṛtti doṣa janitaḥ arthaḥ phalam etat sarvam bhavati tat etat phalam upātam upātam heyam tyaktam tyaktam upādeyam iti na asya hāna upādānayoḥ niṣṭhā paryavasānam vā asti sa khalu ayam phalasya hāna upādāna srota sohyate lokaḥ iti 
[0224,i_0224,iii]	atha etat eva bādhanā lakṣaṇam duḥkham bādhanā pīḍā tāpaḥ iti tayā anuviddham anuṣaktam avinirbhāgena vartamānam duḥkha yogāt duḥkham iti saḥ ayam sarvam duḥkhena anuviddham iti paśyan duḥkham jihāsuḥ janmani duḥkha darśī nirvidyate nirviṇṇaḥ virajyate viraktaḥ vimucyate 
[0225,i_0225,iii]	yatra tu niṣṭhā yatra tu paryavasānam saḥ ayam tad atyanta vimokṣaḥ apavargaḥ tena duḥkhena janmanā atyantam vimuktiḥ apavargaḥ katham upāttasya janmanaḥ hānam anyasya ca anupādānam etām avasthām aparyantam apavargam vedayante apavarga vidaḥ tat abhayam ajaram amṛtyu padam brahma kṣema prāptiḥ iti 
[0226,i_0226,ii]	nityam sukham ātmanaḥ mahat tva vat mokṣe vyajyate yena abhivyaktena atyantam vimuktaḥ sukhī bhāti iti kecid manyante teṣām pramāṇa abhāvāt anupapattiḥ na pratyakṣam na anumānam na āgamaḥ vā vidyate nityam sukham ātmanaḥ mahat tva vat mokṣe abhivyajyate iti nityasya abhivyaktiḥ saṃvedanam tasya hetu vacanam nityasya abhivyaktiḥ saṃvedanam jñānam iti tasya hetuḥ vācyaḥ yatas tat utpadyate iti 
[0227,i_0228,i]	sukha vat nityam iti ced saṃsāra sthasya muktena aviśeṣaḥ yathā muktaḥ sukhena tad saṃvedanena ca sannityena upapannaḥ tathā saṃsāra sthaḥ api prasajyate iti ubhayasya nitya tvāt abhyanujñāne ca dharma adharma phalena sāhacaryam yaugapadyam gṛhyeta yat idam utpatti sthāneṣu dharma adharma phalam sukham duḥkham vā saṃvedyate paryāyeṇa tasya ca nitya saṃvedanasya ca sahabhāvaḥ yaugapadyam gṛhyeta na sukha abhāvaḥ na anabhivyaktiḥ asti ubhayasya nitya tvāt 
[0228,ii_0228,iv]	anitya tve hetu vacanam atha mokṣe nityasya sukhasya saṃvedanam anityam yatas utpadyate sa hetuḥ vācyaḥ ātma manaḥ saṃyogasya nimitta antara sahitasya hetu tvam ātma manaḥ saṃyogaḥ hetuḥ iti ced evam api tasya sahakāri nimitta antaram vacanīyam iti dharmasya kāraṇa vacanam yadi dharmaḥ nimitta antaram tasya hetuḥ vācyaḥ yatas utpadyate iti yoga samādhi jasya kārya avasāya virodhāt prakṣaye saṃvedana nivṛttiḥ yadi yoga samādhi jaḥ dharmaḥ hetuḥ 
[0229,i_0229,iii]	tasya kārya avasāya virodhāt prakṣaye saṃvedanam atyantam nivartate asaṃvedane ca avidyamānena aviśeṣaḥ yadi dharma kṣayāt saṃvedana uparamaḥ nityam sukham na saṃvedyate iti kim vidyamānam na saṃvedyate atha avidyamānam iti na anumānam viśiṣṭe asti iti aprakṣayaḥ ca dharmasya niranumānam utpatti dharmaka tvāt yoga samādhi jaḥ dharmaḥ na kṣīyate iti na asti anumānam utpatti dharmakam anityam iti viparyayasya tu anumānam yasya tu saṃvedana uparamaḥ na asti tena saṃvedana hetuḥ nityaḥ iti anumeyam 
[0229,iv_0230,i]	nitye ca mukta saṃsāra sthayoḥ aviśeṣaḥ iti uktam yathā muktasya nityam sukham tad saṃvedana hetuḥ ca saṃvedanasya tu uparamaḥ na asti kāraṇasya nitya tvāt tathā saṃsāra sthasya api iti evam ca sati dharma adharma phalena sukha duḥkha saṃvedanena sāhacaryam gṛhyeta iti śarīra ādi sambandhaḥ pratibandha hetuḥ iti ced na śarīra ādīnām upabhoga artha tvāt viparyayasya ca ananumānāt syāt matam saṃsāra avasthasya śarīra ādi sambandhaḥ nitya sukha saṃvedana hetoḥ pratibandhakaḥ tena aviśeṣaḥ na asti iti etat ca ayuktam śarīra ādayaḥ upabhoga arthāḥ te bhoga pratibandham kariṣyanti iti anupapannam na ca asti anumānam aśarīrasya ātmanaḥ bhogaḥ kaścid asti iti 
[0231,i]	iṣṭa adhigama arthā pravṛttiḥ iti ced na aniṣṭa uparama artha tvāt idam anumānam iṣṭa adhigama arthaḥ mokṣa upadeśaḥ pravṛttiḥ ca mumukṣūṇām na ubhayam anarthakam iti etat ca ayuktam aniṣṭa uparama arthaḥ mokṣa upadeśaḥ pravṛttiḥ ca mumukṣūṇām iti na iṣṭam aniṣṭena ananuviddham sambhavati iti iṣṭam api aniṣṭam sampadyate aniṣṭa hānāya ghaṭamānaḥ iṣṭam api jahāti viveka hānasya aśakya tvāt iti 
[0231,ii_0231,iii]	dṛṣṭa atikramaḥ ca deha ādiṣu tulyaḥ yathā dṛṣṭam anityam sukham parityajya nityam sukham kāmayate evam deha indriya buddhīḥ anityāḥ dṛṣṭāḥ atikramya muktasya nityāḥ deha indriya buddhayaḥ kalpayitavyāḥ sādhīyaḥ ca evam muktasya ca aikātmyam kalpitam bhavati iti upapatti viruddham iti ced samānam deha ādīnām nitya tvam pramāṇa viruddham kalpayitum aśakyam iti samānam sukhasya api nitya tvam pramāṇa viruddham kalpayitum aśakyam iti 
[0231,iv_0232,iii]	ātyantike ca saṃsāra duḥkha abhāve sukha vacanāt āgame api sati avirodhaḥ yadi api kaścid āgamaḥ syāt muktasya ātyantikam sukham iti sukha śabdaḥ ātyantike duḥkha abhāve prayuktaḥ iti evam upapadyate dṛṣṭaḥ hi duḥkha abhāve sukha śabda prayogaḥ bahulam lokaḥ iti nitya sukha rāgasya aprahāṇe mokṣa adhigama abhāvaḥ rāgasya bandhana samājñānāt yadi ayam mokṣaḥ nityam sukham abhivyajyate iti nitya sukha rāgeṇa mokṣāya ghaṭamānaḥ na mokṣam adhigacchet na adhigantum arhati iti bandhana samājñātaḥ hi rāgaḥ na ca bandhane sati api kaścid muktaḥ iti upapadyate iti prahīṇa nitya sukha rāgasya apratikūla tvam atha asya nitya sukha rāgaḥ prahīyate tasmin prahīṇe na asya nitya sukha rāgaḥ pratikūlaḥ bhavati yadi evam muktasya nityam sukham bhavati atha api na bhavati na asya ubhayoḥ pakṣayoḥ mokṣa adhigamaḥ vikalpyate iti 
[0233,i_0234,ii]	sthānavataḥ eva tarhi saṃśayasya lakṣaṇam vācyam iti tat ucyate samāna aneka dharma upapatteḥ vipratipatteḥ upalabdhi anupalabdhi avyavasthātaḥ ca viśeṣa apekṣaḥ vimarśaḥ saṃśayaḥ samāna dharma upapatteḥ viśeṣa apekṣaḥ vimarśaḥ saṃśayaḥ iti sthāṇu puruṣayoḥ samānam dharmam āroha pariṇāhau paśyan pūrva dṛṣṭam ca tayoḥ viśeṣam bubhutsamānaḥ kiṃsvid iti anyataram na avadhārayati tad anavadhāraṇam jñānam saṃśayaḥ samānam anayoḥ dharmam upalabhe viśeṣam anyatarasya na upalabhaḥ iti eṣā buddhiḥ apekṣā saṃśayasya pravṛttikā vartate tena viśeṣa apekṣaḥ vimarśaḥ saṃśayaḥ 
[0240,ii]	aneka dharma upapatteḥ iti samāna jātīyam asamāna jātīyam ca anekam tasya anekasya dharma upapatteḥ viśeṣasya ubayathāḥ dṛṣṭa tvāt samāna jātīyebhyaḥ asamāna jātīyebyaḥ ca arthāḥ viśiṣyante gandhavat tvāt pṛthivī ap ādhibyaḥ viśiṣyate guṇa karmabhyaḥ ca asti ca śabde vibhāga janya tvam viśeṣaḥ tasmin dravyam guṇaḥ karma vā iti sandehaḥ viśeṣasya ubayathāḥ dṛṣṭa tvāt 
[0249,i_0249,ii]	kim dravyasya sataḥ guṇa karmabhyaḥ viśeṣaḥ āhosvit guṇasya sataḥ iti atha karmaṇaḥ sataḥ iti viśeṣa apekṣā anyatamasya vyavasthāpakam dharma na upalabaḥ iti buddhiḥ iti vipratipatteḥ iti vyāhatam eka artha darśanam vipratipattiḥ vyāghātaḥ virodhaḥ asahabhāvaḥ iti asti ātmā iti ekam darśanam na asti ātmā iti aparam na ca sadbhāva asadbhāvau saha ekatra sambhavataḥ na ca anyatara sādhakaḥ hetuḥ upalabhyate tatra tattva anavadhāraṇam saṃśayaḥ iti 
[0249,iii_0255,i]	upalabdhi avayava sthātaḥ khalu api sat ca udakam upalabhyate taḍāga ādiṣu marīciṣu ca avidyamānam udakam iti atas kvacid upalabhyamāne tattva vyavasthāpakasya pramāṇasya anupalabdheḥ kim sat upalabhyate atha asat iti saṃśayaḥ bhavati anupalabdhi avyavasthātaḥ sat ca na upalabyate mūlakīlaka udaka ādi asat ca anutpannam niruddham vā tatas kvacid anupalabhyamāne saṃśayaḥ kim san na upalabyate uta asat iti saṃśayaḥ bhavati viśeṣa apekṣā pūrvavat pūrvaḥ samānaḥ anekaḥ ca dharmaḥ jñeya sthaḥ upalabdhi anupalabdhī punar jñātṛ sthe etāvatā viśeṣeṇa punarvacanam samāna dharma adhigamāt samāna dharma upapatteḥ viśeṣa smṛti apekṣaḥ vimarśaḥ iti 
[0256,i_0256,iii]	sthānavatām lakṣaṇam iti samānam yam artham adhikṛtya pravartate tat prayojanam yam artham āptavyam hātavyam vā vyavasāya tad āpti hāna upāyam anutiṣṭhati prayojanam tat veditavyam pravṛtti hetu tvāt imam artham āpsyāmi hāsyāmi vā iti vyavasāyaḥ arthasya adhikāraḥ evam vyavasīyamānaḥ arthaḥ adhikriyate iti 
[0258,i_0258,ii]	laukika parīkṣakāṇām yasmin arthe buddhi sāmyam sa dṛṣṭa ānataḥ loka sāmānyam anatītāḥ laukikāḥ naisargikam vainayikam buddhi atiśayam aprāptāḥ tad viparītāḥ parīkṣakāḥ tarkeṇa pramāṇaiḥ artham parīkṣitum arhanti iti yathā yam artham laukikāḥ budhyante tathā parīkṣakāḥ api saḥ arthaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ dṛṣṭānta virodhena hi pratipakṣāḥ pratiṣeddhavyāḥ bhavanti iti dṛṣṭānta samādhinā ca sva pakṣāḥ sthāpanīyāḥ bhavanti iti avayaveṣu ca udāharaṇāya kalpate iti 
[0260,i_0261,i]	atha siddhāntaḥ idam itthambhūtan ca iti abhyanujñāyamānam artha jātam siddham siddhasya saṃsthitiḥ siddhāntaḥ saṃsthitiḥ ittham bhāva vyavasthā dharma niyamaḥ sa khalu ayam tantra adhikaraṇa abhyupagama saṃsthitiḥ siddhāntaḥ tantra artha saṃsthitiḥ tantra saṃsthitiḥ tantram itaretara abhisambaddhasya artha samūhasya upadeśaḥ śāstram adhikaraṇa anuṣakta artha saṃsthitiḥ adhikaraṇa saṃsthitiḥ abhyupagama saṃsthitiḥ anavadhārita artha parigrahaḥ tad viśeṣa parīkṣaṇāya abhyupagama siddhāntaḥ 
[0261,ii_0262,i]	tantra bhedāt tu khalu sa caturvidhaḥ sarva tantra pratitantra adhikaraṇa abhyupagama saṃsthiti artha antara bhāvāt tatra etāḥ catasraḥ saṃsthitayaḥ artha antara bhūtāḥ 
[0263,i_0263,iii]	tāsām sarva tantra aviruddhaḥ tantre adhikṛtaḥ arthaḥ sarva tantra siddhāntaḥ yathā ghrāṇa ādīnīnindriyāṇi gandha ādayaḥ indriya arhāḥ pṛthivī ādīni bhūtāni pramāṇaiḥ arthasya grahaṇam iti 
[0264,i_0264,ii]	samāna tantra siddhaḥ pratantra asiddhaḥ prati tantra siddhāntaḥ yathā na asataḥ ātma lābhaḥ na sataḥ ātma hānam niratiśayāḥ cetanāḥ deha indriya manaḥsu viṣayeṣu tad tad kāraṇeṣu ca viśeṣaḥ iti sāṅkhyānām puruṣa karma ādi nimittaḥ bhūta sargaḥ karma hetavaḥ doṣāḥ pravṛttiḥ ca sva guṇa viśiṣṭāḥ cetanāḥ asat utpadyate utpannam nirudhyate iti yogānām 
[0264,iii_0264,iv]	yat siddhau anya prakaraṇa siddhiḥ saḥ adhikaraṇa siddhāntaḥ yasya arthasya siddhau anye arthāḥ anuṣajyante na taiḥ vinā saḥ arthaḥ sidhyati te arthāḥ yat adhiṣṭhānāḥ saḥ adhikaraṇa siddhāntaḥ yathā deha indriya vyatiriktaḥ jñātā darśana sparśanābhyām eka artha grahaṇāt iti atra anuṣaṅgiṇaḥ arthāḥ indriya nānā tvam niyata viṣayāṇi indriyāṇi sva viṣaya grahaṇa liṅgāni jñātuḥ jñāna sādhanāni gandha ādi guṇa vyatiriktam dravyam guṇa adhikaraṇam aniyata viṣayāḥ cetanāḥ iti pūrva artha siddhau ete arhāḥ sidhyanti na taiḥ vinā saḥ arthaḥ sambhavati iti 
[0266,i_0266,ii]	aparīkṣita abhyupagamāt tad viśeṣa parīkṣaṇam abhyupagama siddhāntaḥ yatra kiñcid artha jātam aparīkṣitam abhyupagamyate astu dravyam śabdaḥ sa tu nityaḥ atha anityaḥ iti dravyasya sataḥ nitya tā anitya tā vā tad viśeṣaḥ parīkṣyate saḥ abhyupagama siddhāntaḥ sva buddhi atiśaya cikhyā apayiṣayā para buddhi avajñānāt ca pravartate iti 
[0269,i_0271,i]	atha avayavāḥ pratijñā hetu udāharaṇa upanaya nigamanāni avayavāḥ daśa avayavān eke naiyāyikāḥ vākye sañcakṣate jijñāsā saṃśayaḥ śakya prāptiḥ prayojanam saṃśaya vyudāsaḥ iti te kasmāt na ucyantaḥ iti tatra apratīyamāne arthe pratyaya arthasya pravartikā jijñāsā apratīyamānam artham kasmāt jijñāsate tam tattvataḥ jñātam hāsyāmi vā upāda āsyaḥ upekṣiṣye vā iti tāḥ etāḥ hāna upādāna upekṣā buddhayaḥ tattva jñānasya arthaḥ tad arthaḥ ayam jijñāsate sā khalu ayam asādhanam arthasya iti jijñāsā adhiṣṭhānam saṃśayaḥ ca vyāhata dharma upasaṅghātāt tattva jñāne pratyāsannaḥ vyāhatayoḥ hi dharmayoḥ anyatara tattvam bhavitum arhati iti sa pṛthak upadiṣṭaḥ api asādhanam arthasya iti pramātuḥ pramāṇāni prameya adhigama arthāni sā śakya prāptiḥ na sādhakasya vākyasya bhāgena yujyate pratijña ādi vat iti prayojanam tattva avadhāraṇam artha sādhakasya vākyasya phalam na eka deśaḥ iti saṃśaya vyudāsaḥ pratipakṣa upavarṇanam tat pratiṣedhena tattva jñāna abhyanujñāna artham na tu ayam sādhaka vākya eka deśaḥ iti prakaraṇe tu jijñāsā ādayaḥ samarthāḥ avadhāraṇīya artha upakārāt tattva artha sādhaka bhāvāt tu pratijña ādayaḥ sādhaka vākyasya bhāgāḥ eka deśāḥ avayavāḥ iti 
[0272,i_0272,iii]	teṣām tu yathā vibhaktānām sādhya nirdeśaḥ pratijñā prajñāpanīyena dharmeṇa dharmiṇaḥ viśiṣṭasya parigraha vacanam pratijñā sādhya nirdeśaḥ anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti 
[0283,i_0288,i]	udāharaṇa sādharmyāt sādhya sādhanam hetuḥ udāharaṇena sāmānyāt sādhyasya dharmasya sādhanam prajñāpanam hetuḥ sādhye pratisandhāya dharmam udāharaṇe ca pratisandhāya tasya sādhana tā vacanam hetuḥ utpatti dharmaka tvāt iti utpatti dharmakam anityam dṛṣṭam iti 
[0290,i_0290,iii]	kim etāvat dhetu lakṣaṇam iti na iti ucyate kim tarhi tathā vaidharmyāt udāharaṇa vaidharmyāt ca sādhya sādhanam hetuḥ katham anityaḥ śabdaḥ utpatti dharmaka tvāt anutpatti dharmakam nityam yathā ātmā ādi dravyam iti 
[0306,i_0309,i]	sādhya sādharmyāt tad dharma bhāvī dṛṣṭāntaḥ udāharaṇam sādhyena sādharmyam samāna dharma tā sādhya sādharmyāt kāraṇāt tad dharma bhāvī dṛṣṭāntaḥ iti tasya dharmaḥ tad dharmaḥ tasya sādhyasya sādhyam ca dvividham dharmi viśiṣṭaḥ vā dharmaḥ śabdasya anitya tvam dharma viśiṣṭaḥ vā dharmī anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti iha uttaram tad grahaṇena gṛhyate iti kasmāt pṛthak dharma vacanāt tasya dharmaḥ tad dharmaḥ tasya bhāvaḥ tad dharma bhāvaḥ sa yasmin dṛṣṭānte vartate sa dṛṣṭāntaḥ sādhya sādharmyāt utpatti dharmaka tvat tad dharma bhāvī bhavati sa ca udāharaṇam iṣyate tatra yat utpadyate tat utpatti dharmakam tat ca bhūtvā na bhavati ātmānam jahāti nirudhyate iti anityam evam utpatti dharmaka tvam sādhanam anitya tvam sādhyam saḥ ayam ekasmin dvayoḥ dharmayoḥ sādhya sādhana bhāvaḥ sādharmyāt vyavasthitaḥ upalabhyate tam dṛṣṭāntaḥ upalabhamānaḥ śabde api anuminoti śabdaḥ api utpatti dharmaka tvāt anityaḥ sthālī ādi vat iti udāhriyate anena dharmayoḥ sādhya sādhana bhāvaḥ iti udāharaṇam 
[0309,ii_0309,iii]	tad viparyayāt vā viparītam dṛṣṭāntaḥ udāharaṇam iti prakṛtam sādhya vaidharmyāt atad dharma bhāvī dṛṣṭāntaḥ udāharaṇam iti anityaḥ śabdaḥ utpatti dharmaka tvāt anutpatti dharmakam nityam ātma ādi saḥ ayam ātma ādiḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ sādhya vaidharmyāt anutpatti dharmaka tvāt atad dharma bhāvī yaḥ asau sādhyasya dharmaḥ anitya tvam sa tasmin na bhavati iti 
[0310,i]	atra ātma ādau dṛṣṭāntaḥ utpatti dharmaka tvasya abhāvāt anitya tvam na bhavati iti upalabhamānaḥ śabde viparyayam anuminoti utpatti dharmaka tvasya bhāvāt anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti sādharmya uktasya hetoḥ sādhya sādharmyāt tad dharma bhāvī dṛṣṭāntaḥ udāharaṇam vaidharmya uktasya hetoḥ sādhya vaidharmyāt atad dharma bhāvī dṛṣṭāntaḥ udāharaṇam 
[0311,i_0312,i]	pūrvasmin dṛṣṭānte yau tau dharmau sādhya sādhana bhūtau paśyati sādhye api tayoḥ sādhya sādhana bhāvam anuminoti uttarasmin dṛṣṭānte tayoḥ dharmayoḥ ekasya abhāvāt itarasya abhāvam paśyati tayoḥ ekasya bhāvāt itarasya bhāvam sādhye anuminoti iti tat etat dhetuvā ābhāseṣu na sambhavati iti ahetavaḥ hetvābhāsāḥ tat idam hetu udāharaṇayoḥ sāmarthyam parama sūkṣmam duḥkha bodham paṇḍita rūpa vedanīyam iti 
[0313,i_0313,ii]	udāharaṇa apekṣaḥ tathā iti upasaṃhāraḥ na tathā iti vā sādhyasya upanayaḥ udāharaṇa apekṣaḥ udāharaṇa tantraḥ udāharaṇa vaśaḥ vaśaḥ sāmarthyam sādhya sādharmya yukte udāharaṇe sthālī ādi dravyam utpatti dharmakam anityam dṛṣṭam tathā śabdaḥ utpatti dharmakaḥ iti sādhyasya śabdasya utpatti dharmaka tvam upasaṃhriyate 
[0314,i]	sādhya vaidharmya yukte punar udāharaṇaḥ ātma ādi dravyam anutpatti dharmakam nityam dṛṣṭam na ca tathā śabdaḥ iti anutpatti dharmaka tvasya upasaṃhāra ra pratiṣedhena utpatti dharmaka tvam upasaṃhriyate tat idam upasaṃhāra dvaitam udāharaṇa dvaitāt bhavati upasaṃhriyate anena iti ca upasaṃhāraḥ veditavyaḥ iti 
[0315,i_0315,iii]	dvividhasya punar hetoḥ dvividhasya ca udāharaṇasya upasaṃhāra dvaite ca samānam hetu apadeśāt pratijñāyāḥ punarvacanam nigamanam sādharmya ukte vā vaidharmya ukte vā yathā udāharaṇam upasaṃhriyate tasmāt utpatti dharmaka tvāt anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti nigamanam nigamyante anena iti pratijñā hetu udāharaṇa upanayā ekatra iti nigamanam nigamyante samarthyante sambadhyante tatra sādharma ukte tāvat dhetau vākyam anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti pratijñā utpatti dharmaka tvāt iti hetuḥ utpatti dharmakam sthālī ādi dravyam anityam iti udāharaṇam tathā ca utpatti dharmakaḥ śabdaḥ iti upanayaḥ tasmāt utpatti dharmaka tvāt anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti nigamanam vaidharmya ukte api anityaḥ śabdaḥ utpatti dharmaka tvāt anutpatti dharmakam ātma ādi dravyam nityam dṛṣṭam na ca tathā anutpatti dharmakaḥ śabdaḥ tasmāt utpatti dharmaka tvāt anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti 
[0315,iv]	avayava samudāye ca vākye sambhūya itara itara abhisambandhāt pramāṇāni arthān sādhayanti iti sambhavaḥ tāvat śabda viṣayā pratijñā āpta upadeśasya pratyakṣa anumānābhyām pratisandhānāt anṛṣeḥ ca svātantrya anupapatteḥ anumānam hetuḥ udāharaṇe sādṛśya pratipatteḥ tat ca udāharaṇa bhāṣye vyākhyātam pratyakṣa viṣayam udāharaṇam dṛṣṭena adṛṣṭa siddheḥ upamānam upanayaḥ tathā iti upasaṃhārāt na ca tathā iti vā upamāna dharma pratiṣedehe viparīta dharma upasaṃhāra siddheḥ sarveṣām eka artha pratipattau sāmarthya pradarśanam nigamanam iti 
[0315,v_0317,i]	itaretara abhisambandhaḥ api asatyām pratijñāyām anāśrayāḥ hetu ādayaḥ na pravarteran asati hetau kasya sādhana bhāvaḥ pradarśyeta udāharaṇe sādhye ca kasya upasaṃhāraḥ syāt kasya ca apadeśāt pratijñāyāḥ punarvacanam nigamanam syāt iti asati udāharaṇe kena sādharmyam vaidharmyam vā sādhya sādhanam upādīyeta kasya vā sādharmya vaśāt upasaṃhāraḥ pravarteta upanayam ca antareṇa sādhye anupasaṃhṛtaḥ sādhakaḥ dharmaḥ na artham sādhayet nigamana abhāve ca anabhiyukta sambandhānām pratijña ādīnām eka arthena pravartanam tathā iti pratipādanam kasya iti 
[0317,ii]	atha avayava arthaḥ sādhyasya dharmasya dharmiṇā sambandha upādānam pratijñā arthaḥ udāharaṇena samānasya viparītasya vā sādhyasya dharmasya sādhaka bhāva vacanam hetu arthaḥ dharmayoḥ sādhya sādhana bhāva pradarśanam ekatra udāharaṇa arthaḥ sādhana bhūtasya dharmasya sādhyena dharmeṇa sāmānādhikaraṇya upapādanam upanaya arthaḥ udāharaṇa sthayoḥ dharmayoḥ sādhya sādhana bhāva upapattau sādhye viparīta prasaṅga pratiṣedha artham nigamanam na ca etasyām hetu udāharaṇa pariśuddhau satyām sādharmya vaidharmyābhyām pratyavasthānasya vikalyāt jāti nigraha sthāna bahu tvam prakramate avyavasthāpya khalu dharmayoḥ sādhya sādhana bhāvam udāharaṇe jāti vādī pratyavatiṣṭhate vyavasthite tu khalu dharmayoḥ sādhya sādhana bhāve dṛṣṭānta sthe gṛhyamāṇe sādhana bhūtasya dharmasya hetu tvena upādānam na sādharmya mātrasya na vaidharmya mātrasya vā iti 
[0320,i_0320,iii]	atas ūrdhvam tarkaḥ lakṣaṇīyaḥ iti atha idam ucyate avijñāta tattve arthe kāraṇa upapattitaḥ tattva jñāna artham ūhaḥ tarkaḥ avijñāyamāna tattve arthe jijñāsā tāvat jāyate jānīya imam artham iti atha jijñāsitasya vastunaḥ vyāhatau dharmau vibhāgena vimṛśati kiṃsvid ittham āhosvit na ittham iti vimṛśyamānayoḥ dharmayoḥ ekam kāraṇa upapattyā anujānāti sambhavati asmin kāraṇam pramāṇam hetuḥ iti kāraṇa upapattyā syāt evam etat na itarat iti 
[0321,ii]	tatra nidarśanam yaḥ ayam jñātā jñātavyam artham jānīte tam tattvataḥ jānīya iti jijñāsā sa kim utpatti dharmakaḥ atha anutpatti dharmakaḥ iti vimarśaḥ vimṛśyamāne avijñāta tat te arthe yasya dharmasya abhyanujñā kāraṇam upapadyate tam anujānāti yadi ayam anutpatti dharmakaḥ tatas sva kṛtasya karmaṇaḥ phalam anubhavati jñātā duḥkha janma pravṛtti doṣa mithyā jñānānām uttaram uttaram pūrvasya pūrvasya kāraṇam uttarottara apāye tad anantara apāyāt apavargaḥ iti syātām saṃsāra apavargau 
[0322,i]	utpatti dharmake jñātari punar na syātām utpannaḥ khalu jñātā deha indriya buddhi vedanābhiḥ sambadhyate iti na asya idam sva kṛtasya karmaṇaḥ phalam utpannaḥ ca bhūtvā na bhavati iti tasya avidyamānasya niruddhasya vā sva kṛta karmaṇaḥ phala upabhogaḥ na asti tat evam ekasya aneka śarīra yogaḥ śarīra viyogaḥ ca atyantam na syāt iti yatra kāraṇam anupapadyamānam paśyati tat na anujānāti saḥ ayam evaṃlakṣaṇaḥ ūhaḥ tarkaḥ iti ucyate 
[0322,ii_0323,i]	katham punar ayam tattva jñāna arthaḥ na tattva jñānam eva iti anavadhāraṇāt anujānāti ayam ekataram dharmam kāraṇa upapattyā na tu avadhārayati na vyavasyati na niścinoti evam eva idam iti katham tattva jñāna arthaḥ iti tattva jñāna viṣaya abhyanujñā lakṣaṇa anugraha bhāvitāt prasannāt anatara pramāṇa sāmarthyāt tattva jñānam utpadyate iti evam tattva jñāna arthaḥ iti saḥ ayam tarkaḥ pramāṇāni pratisanda dhānaḥ pramāṇa abhyanujñānāt pramāṇa sahitaḥ vāde apadiṣṭaḥ iti avijñāta tattvam anujānāti yathā saḥ arhaḥ bhavati tasya tathā abhāvaḥ tattvam aviparyayaḥ yāthātathyam 
[0329,i_0330,i]	etasmin ca tarka viṣaye vimṛśya pakṣa pratipakṣābhyām artha avadhāraṇam nirṇayaḥ sthāpanā sādhanam pratiṣedhaḥ upālambhaḥ tau sādhana upālambhau pakṣa pratipakṣa āśrayau vyatiṣaktau anubandhena pravartamānau pakṣa pratipakṣau iti ucyete tayoḥ anyatarasya nivṛttiḥ ekatarasya avasthānam avaśyambhāvi yasya avasthānam tasya artha avadhāraṇam nirṇayaḥ na idam pakṣa pratipakṣābhyām artha avadhāraṇam sambhavati iti ekaḥ hi pratijñātam artham hetutaḥ sthāpayati pratiṣiddham ca uddharati dvitīyasya dvitīyena sthāpanā hetuḥ pratiṣidhyate tasya eva pratiṣedha hetuḥ ca uddhriyate sa nivartate tasya nivṛttau yaḥ avatiṣṭhate tena artha avadhāraṇam nirṇayaḥ 
[0330,ii_0330,iii]	ubhābhyām eva artha avadhāraṇam iti āha kayā yuktyā ekasya sambhavaḥ dvitīyasya asambhavaḥ tau etau sambhava asambhavau vimarśam saha nivarttayataḥ ubhaya sambhave ubhayā sambhave vā anivṛttaḥ vimarśaḥ iti vimṛśya iti vimarśam kṛtvā saḥ ayam vimarśaḥ pakṣa pratipakṣau avadyotya nyāyam pravartayati iti upādīyate iti etat ca viruddhayoḥ eka dharmi sthayoḥ boddhavyam yatra tu dharmi sāmānya gatau viruddhau dharmau hetutaḥ sambhavataḥ tatra samuccayaḥ hetutaḥ arthasya tathā abhāva upapatteḥ yathā kriyāvat dravyam iti lakṣaṇa vacane yasya dravyasya kriyā yogaḥ hetutaḥ sambhavati tat kriyāvat yasya na sambhavati tat akriyam iti eka dharmi sthayoḥ ca viruddhayoḥ dharmayoḥ ayugapad bhāvinoḥ kāla vikalpaḥ yathā tat eva dravyam kriyā yuktam kriyāvat anutpanna uparata kriyam punar akriyam iti na ca ayam nirṇaye niyamaḥ vimṛśya eva pakṣa pratipakṣābhyām artha avadhāraṇam nirṇayaḥ iti kim tu indriya artha sannikarṣa utpanna pratyakṣe artha avadhāraṇam nirṇayaḥ iti parīkṣā viṣaye tu vimṛśya pakṣa pratipakṣābhyām artha avadhāraṇam nirṇayaḥ vāde śāstre ca vimarśa varjam 
[0335,i_0336,i]	tisraḥ kathāḥ bhavanti vādaḥ jalpaḥ vitaṇḍā ca iti tāsām pramāṇa tarka sādhana upālambhaḥ siddhānta aviruddhaḥ pañca avayava upapannaḥ pakṣa pratipakṣa parigrahaḥ vādaḥ eka adhikaraṇa sthau viruddhau dharmau pakṣa pratipakṣau pratyanīka bhāvāt asti ātmā na asti ātmā iti nānā adhikaraṇa sthau viruddhau na pakṣa pratipakṣau yathā nityaḥ ātmā anityā buddhiḥ iti parigrahaḥ abhyupagama vyavasthā saḥ ayam pakṣa pratipakṣa parigrahaḥ vādaḥ tasya viśeṣanam pramāṇa tarka sādhana upālambhaḥ pramāṇaiḥ tarkeṇa ca sādhanam upālambhaḥ ca asmin kriyate iti sādhanam sthāpanā upālambhaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ tau sādhana upālambhau ubhayoḥ api pakṣayoḥ vyatiṣaktau anubaddhau ca yāvat ekaḥ nivṛttaḥ ekataraḥ vyavasthitaḥ iti nivṛttasya upālambhaḥ vyavasthitasya sādhanam iti 
[0339,i]	jalpe nigraha sthāna viniyogāt vāde tad pratiṣedhaḥ pratiṣedhe kasyacid abhyanujñāna artham siddhānta aviruddhaḥ iti vacanam siddhāntam abhyupetya tad virodhī viruddhaḥ iti hetvābhāsasya nigraha sthānasya abhyanujñā vāde pañca avayava upapanne iti hīnam anyatamena api avayavena nyūnam hetu udāharaṇa adhikam adhikam iti ca etayoḥ abhyanujñāna artham iti avayaveṣu pramāna tarka antarbhāve pṛthak pramāṇa tarka grahaṇam sādhana upālambha vyatiṣaṅga jñāpana artham anyathā ubhau api pakṣau sthāpanā pravṛttau vādaḥ iti syāt 
[0342,i]	antareṇa api ca avayava sambandham pramāṇāni artham sādhayanti iti dṛṣṭam tena api kalpena sādhana upālambhau vāde bhavataḥ iti jñāpayati chala ja ati nigraha sthāna sādhana upālambhaḥ jalpaḥ iti vacanāt vinigrahaḥ jalpaḥ iti mā vijñāyi chala ja ati nigraha sthāna sādhana upālambhaḥ eva jalpaḥ pramāṇa tarka sādhana upālambhaḥ vād eva iti mā vijñāyi iti evam artham pṛthak pramāna tarka grahaṇam iti 
[0356,i_0356,ii]	yathā ukta upapannaḥ chala ja ati nigraha sthāna sādhana upālambhaḥ jalpaḥ yathā ukta upapannaḥ iti pramāṇa tarka sādhana upālambhaḥ siddhānta aviruddhaḥ pañca avayava upapannaḥ pakṣa pratipakṣa parigrahaḥ chala ja ati nigraha sthāna sādhana upālambhaḥ iti chala ja ati nigraha sthānaiḥ sādhanam upālambhaḥ ca asmin kriyate iti evaṃviśeṣaṇaḥ jalpaḥ 
[0358,i_0359,i]	na khalu vai chala ja ati nigraha sthānaiḥ sādhanam kasyacid arthasya sambhavati pratiṣedha artha tā eva eṣām sāmānya lakṣaṇe viśeṣa lakṣaṇe ca śrūyate vacana vighātaḥ artha vikalpa upapattyā chalam iti sādharmya vaidharmyābhyām pratyavasthānam jātiḥ vipratipattiḥ apratipattiḥ ca nigraha sthānam iti viśeṣa lakṣaṇeṣu api yathāsvam iti na ca etat vijānīyāt pratiṣedha artha tayā eva artham sādhayanti iti chala ja ati nigraha sthāna upālambhaḥ jalpaḥ iti evam api ucyamāne vijñāyate etat iti 
[0359,ii_0360,i]	pramāṇaiḥ sādhana upālambhayoḥ chala jāti nigraha sthānānām aṅga bhāvaḥ sva pakṣa rakṣaṇa artha tvāt na svatantrāṇām sādhana bhāvaḥ yat tat pramāṇaiḥ arthasya sādhanam tatra chala jāti nigraha sthānānām aṅga bhāvaḥ rakṣaṇa artha tvāt tāni hi prayujyamānāni para pakṣa vighātena sva pakṣam rakṣanti tathā ca uktam tattva adhyavasāya saṃrakṣaṇātham jalpa vitaṇḍe bīja praroha saṃrakṣaṇa artham kaṇṭaka śākhā āvaraṇa vat iti yaḥ ca asau pramāṇaiḥ pratipakṣasya upālambhaḥ tasya ca etāni prayujyamānāni pratiṣedha vighātāt saha kārīṇi bhavanti tat evam aṅgī bhūtanām chala ādīnām upādānam jalpe na svatantrāṇām sādhana bhāvaḥ upālambhe tu svātantryam api asti iti 
[0361,i_0362,i]	sa pratipakṣa sthāpanā hīnaḥ vitaṇḍā sa jalpaḥ vitaṇḍā bhavati kiṃviśeṣaṇaḥ pratipakṣa sthāpanayā hīnaḥ yau tau samāna adhikaraṇau viruddhau dharmau pakṣau iti uktam tayoḥ ekataram vaitaṇḍikaḥ na sthāpayati iti prapakṣa pratiṣedhena eva pravartate iti astu tarhi sa pratipakṣa hīnaḥ vitaṇḍā yat vai khalu tat para pratiṣedha lakṣaṇam vākyam sa vaitaṇḍikasya pakṣaḥ na tu asau sādhyam kañcid artham pratijñāya sthāpayati iti tasmāt yathānyāsam eva astu iti 
[0363,i_0372,i]	hetu lakṣaṇa abhāvāt ahetavaḥ hetu sāmānyāt dhetu vat ābhāsamānāḥ te ime savyabhicāra viruddha prakaraṇa sama sādhya sama kāla atītāḥ hetvābhāsāḥ teṣām 
[0373,i_0375,ii]	anaikāntikaḥ savyabhicāraḥ vyabhicāraḥ ekatra avyavasthitiḥ saha vyabhicāreṇa vartate iti svayabhicāraḥ nidarśanam nityaḥ śabdaḥ asparśa tvāt sparśavān kumbhaḥ anityaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ na ca tathā sparśavān śabdaḥ tasmāt asparśa tvāt nityaḥ śabdaḥ iti dṛṣṭānte sparśavat tvam anitya tvam ca dharmau na sādhya sādhana bhūtau gṛhyete sparśavān ca aṇuḥ nityaḥ ca iti ātma ādau ca dṛṣṭānte udāharaṇa sādharmyāt sādhya sādhanam hetuḥ iti asparśa tvāt iti hetuḥ nitya tvam vyabhicarati asparśā buddhiḥ anityā ca iti evam dvividhe api dṛṣṭānte vyabhicārāt sādhya sādhana bhāvaḥ na asti iti lakṣaṇa abhāvāt ahetuḥ iti nitya tvam api ekaḥ antaḥ anitya tvam api ekaḥ ntaḥ ekasmin ante vidyate iti aikāntikaḥ viparyayāt anaikāntikaḥ ubhaya anta vyāpaka tvāt iti 
[0377,i_0379,i]	siddhāntam abhyupetya tad virodhī viruddhaḥ tam viruṇaddhi iti tad virodhi abhyupetam siddhāntam vyāhanti iti yathā saḥ ayam vikāraḥ vyakteḥ apaiti nitya tva pratiṣedhāt na nityaḥ vikāraḥ upapadyata apetaḥ api vikāraḥ asti vināśa pratiṣedhāt saḥ ayam nitya tva pratiṣedhāt iti hetuḥ vyakteḥ apetaḥ api vikāraḥ asti iti anena sva siddhāntena virudhyate katham vyaktiḥ ātma lābhaḥ apāyaḥ pracyutiḥ yadi ātma lābhāt pracyutaḥ vikāraḥ asti nitya tva pratiṣedhaḥ na upapadyate yat vyakteḥ apetasya api vikārasya astitvam tat khalu nitya tvam iti nityatvapratiṣedhaḥ nāma vikārasya ātma lābhāt pracyuteḥ upapattiḥ yat ātma lābhāt pracyavate tat anityam dṛṣṭam yat asti na tat ātma lābhāt pracyavate astitvam ca ātma lābhāt pracyutiḥ iti ca viruddhau etau dharmau na saha sambhavataḥ iti saḥ ayam hetuḥ yam siddhāntam āśritya pravartate tam eva vyāhanti iti 
[0380,i_0380,ii]	yasmāt prakaraṇa cintā sa nirṇaya artham apadiṣṭaḥ prakaraṇa samaḥ vimarśa adhiṣṭhānau pakṣa pratipakṣau ubhau anavasitau prakaraṇam tasya cintā vimarśāt prabhṛti prāk nirṇayāt yat samīkṣaṇam sā jijñāsā yad kṛtā sa nirṇaya artham prayuktaḥ ubhaya pakṣa sāmyāt prakaraṇam anativartamānaḥ prakaraṇa samaḥ nirṇayāya na prakalpate 
[0380,iii_0380,iv]	prajñāpanam tu anityaḥ śabdaḥ nitya dharma anupalabdheḥ iti anupalabhyamānan iti adharmakam nityam dṛṣṭam sthālī ādi nityaḥ śabdaḥ vā anitya dharma anupalabdheḥ anupalabhyamāna anitya dharmakam nityam dṛṣṭam ākāśa ādi yatra samānaḥ dharmaḥ saṃśaya kāraṇam hetu tvena upādīyate sa saṃśaya samaḥ savyabhicāraḥ eva 
[0382,i_0383,i]	yā tu vimarśasya viśeṣa apekṣitāḥ ubhaya pakṣa viśeṣa anupalabdhiḥ ca sā prakaraṇam pravartayati yathā śabde nitya dharmaḥ na upalabhyate evam anitya dharmaḥ api sā iyam ubhaya pakṣa viśeṣa anupalabdhiḥ prakaraṇa cintām pravartayati katham viparyaye hi prakaraṇa nivṛtteḥ yadi nitya dharmaḥ śabde gṛhyeta na syāt prakaraṇam yadi na syāt prakaraṇam yadi vā anitya dharmaḥ gṛhyeta evam api nivarteta prakaraṇam saḥ ayam hetuḥ ubhau pakṣau pravartayan anyatarasya nirṇayāya na prakalpate 
[0384,i_0386,i]	sādhya aviśiṣṭaḥ sādhya tvāt sādhya samaḥ dravyam chāyā iti sādhyam gatimat tvāt iti hetuḥ sādhyena aviśiṣṭaḥ sādhanīya tvāt sādhya samaḥ ayam api asiddha tvāt sādhya vat prajñāpayitavyaḥ sādhyam tāvat etat kim puruṣa vat śāyā api gacchati āhosvit āvaraka dravye saṃsarpati āvaraṇa santānāt asannidhi santānaḥ ayam tejasaḥ gṛhyate iti sarpatā khalu dravyeṇa yaḥ yaḥ tejaḥ bhāgaḥ āvriyate tasya tasya asannidhiḥ eva avicchinnaḥ gṛhyate iti āvaraṇam tu prāpti pratiṣedhaḥ 
[0388,i_0389,i]	kāla atyaya apadiṣṭaḥ kāla atītaḥ kāla atyayena yuktaḥ yasya artha eka deśaḥ apadiśyamānasya sa kāla atyaya apadiṣṭaḥ kāla atītaḥ iti ucyate nidarśanam nityaḥ śabdaḥ saṃyoga vyaṅgya tvāt rūpavat prāk ūrdhvam ca vyakteḥ avasthitam rūpam pradīpa ghaṭa saṃyogena vyajyate tathā ca śabdaḥ api avasthitaḥ bherī daṇḍa saṃyogena vyajyate dāruparaśu saṃyogena vā tasmāt samyoga vyaṅgya tvāt nityaḥ śabdaḥ iti ayam ahetuḥ kāla atyaya apadeśāt vyañjakasya saṃyogasya kālam na vyaṅgyasya rūpasya vyaktiḥ atyeti sati pradīpa saṃyoge rūpasya grahaṇam bhavati na nivṛtte saṃyoge rūpam gṛhyate nivṛtte dāruparaśu saṃyoge dūra sthena śabdaḥ śrūyate vibhāga kāle sā iyam śabdasya vyaktiḥ saṃyoga kālam atyeti iti na saṃyoga nirmitā bhavati kasmāt kāraṇa abhāvāt dhi kārya abhāvaḥ iti evam udāharaṇa sādharmi asya abhāvāt asādhanam ayam hetuḥ hetvābhāse iti 
[0390,i_0390,ii]	avayava viparyāsa vacanam tu na sūtra arthaḥ kasmāt yasya yena artha sambandhaḥ dūra sthasya api tasya saḥ arthataḥ hi asamarthānām ānantaryam akāraṇam iti etad vacanāt viparyāsena uktaḥ hetuḥ udāharaṇa sādharmyāt tathā vaidharmyāt sādhya sādhanam hetu lakṣaṇam na jahāti ajahat hetu lakṣaṇam na hetvābhāsaḥ bhavati iti avayava viparyāsa vacanam aprāpta kālam iti nigraha sthānam uktam tat eva idam punar ucyate iti atas tat na sūtra arthaḥ 
[0391,i_0391,ii]	atha chalam vacana vighātaḥ artha vikalpa upapattyā chalam na sāmānya lakṣaṇe chalam śakyam udāhartum vibhāge tu udāharaṇāni 
[0392,i_0392,v]	vibhāgaḥ ca tat trividham vākchalam sāmānyacchalam upacāracchalam ca iti teṣām aviśeṣa abhihite arthe vaktuḥ abhiprāyāt artha antara kalpanā vākchalam nava kambalaḥ ayam māṇavakaḥ iti prayogaḥ atra navaḥ kambalaḥ asya iti vaktuḥ abhiprāyaḥ vigrahe tu viśeṣaḥ na samāse tatra ayam chala vādī vaktuḥ abhiprāyāt avivakṣitam anyam artham nava kambalā asya iti tāvat abhihitam bhavatā iti kalpayati kalpayitvā ca asambhavena pratiṣedhati ekaḥ asya kambalaḥ kutas nava kambalāḥ iti 
[0392,vi_0392,viii]	tat idam sāmānya śabde vāci chalam vākchalam iti asya pratyavasthānam sāmānya śabdasya aneka artha tve anyatara abhidhāna kalpanāyām viśeṣa vacanam nava kambalaḥ iti aneka artha abhidhānam navaḥ kambalaḥ asya iti nava kambalā asya iti etasmin prayukte yā iyam kalpanā nava kambalā asya iti etat bhavatā abhihitam tat ca na sambhavati iti etasyām anyatara abhidhāna kalpanāyām viśeṣaḥ vaktavyaḥ yasmāt viśeṣaḥ artha viśeṣeṣu vijñāyate ayam arthaḥ anena abhihitaḥ iti sa ca viśeṣaḥ na asti tasmāt mithyā abhiyoga mātram etat iti prasiddhaḥ ca loke śabda artha sambandhaḥ abhidhāna abhidheya niyama niyogaḥ asya abhidhānasya ayam arthaḥ abhidheyaḥ iti samānaḥ sāmānya śabdasya viśeṣaḥ viśiṣṭa śabdasya prayukta pūrvāḥ ca ime śabdāḥ arthe prayujyante na aprayukta pūrvāḥ prayogaḥ ca artha sampratyaya arthaḥ artha pratyayāt ca vyavahāraḥ iti 
[0394,i]	tatra evam artha gati arthe śabda prayoge sāmarthyāt sāmānya śabdasya prayoga niyamaḥ ajām grāmam naya sarpiḥ āhāra brāhmaṇam bhojaya iti sāmānya śabdāḥ santaḥ artha avayaveṣu prayujyante sāma arthyat yatra artha kriyā codanā sambhavati tatra pravartante na artha sāmānye kriyā deśanā sambhavāt evam ayam sāmānya śabdaḥ nava kambalaḥ iti yaḥ arthaḥ sambhavati navaḥ kambalaḥ asya iti tatra pravartate yaḥ tu na sambhavait nava kambalāḥ asya iti tatra na pravartate saḥ ayam anupapadyamāna artha kalpanayā para vākya upālambhaḥ na kalpate iti 
[0395,i_0396,i]	sambhavataḥ arthasya ati sāmānya yogāt asambhūta artha kalpanā sāmānyacchalam aho khalu asau brāhmaṇaḥ vidyā caraṇa sampannaḥ iti ukte kaścid āha sambhavati brāhmaṇe vidyā caraṇa sampad iti asya vacanasya vighātaḥ artha vikalpa upapattyā sambhūta artha kalpanayā kriyate yadi brāhmaṇe vidyā caraṇa sampad sambhavati vrātye api sambhavet vrātyaḥ api brāhmaṇaḥ saḥ api astu vidyā caraṇa sampannaḥ iti yat vivakṣitam artham āpnoti ca atyeti ca tat atisāmānyam yathā brāhmaṇa tvam vidyā caraṇa sampadam kvacid āpnoti kvacid atyeti sāmānya nimittam chalam sāmānyacchalam iti 
[0396,ii]	asya ca pratyavasthānam avivakṣita hetukasya viṣaya anuvādaḥ praśaṃsā artha tvāt vākyasya tat atra asambhūta artha kalpanā anupapattiḥ yathā sambhavanti asmin kṣetre śālayaḥ iti anirākṛtam avivakṣitam ca bīja janma pravṛtti viṣayaḥ tu kṣetram praśasyate saḥ ayam kṣetra anuvādaḥ na asmin śālayaḥ vidhīyante iti bījāt tu śāli nirvṛttiḥ satī na vivakṣitā evam sambhavati brāhmaṇe vidyā caraṇa sampad iti sampad viṣayaḥ brāhmaṇa tvam na sampad hetuḥ na ca atra hetuḥ vivakṣitaḥ viṣaya anuvādaḥ tu ayam praśaṃsā artha tvāt vākyasya sati brāhmaṇa tve sampad hetuḥ samarthaḥ iti viśayam ca praśaṃsatā vākyena yathā hetutaḥ phala nirvṛttiḥ na pratyākhyāyate tat evam sati vacana vighātaḥ asambhūta artha kalpanayā na upapadyate iti 
[0397,i_0397,iii]	dharma vikalpa nirdeśe artha sadbhāva pratiṣedhaḥ upacāracchalam abhidhānasya dharmaḥ yathā artha prayogaḥ dharma vikalpaḥ anyatra dṛṣṭasya anyatra prayogaḥ tasya nirdeśe dharma vikalpa nirdeśe yathā mañcāḥ krośanti iti artha sadbhāvena pratiṣedhaḥ mañca sthāḥ puruṣāḥ krośanti na tu mañcāḥ krośanti kā punar atra artha vikalpa upapattiḥ anyathā prayuktasya anyathā artha kalpanam bhaktyā prayoge prādhānyena kalpanam upacāra viṣayam chalam upacāracchalam upacāraḥ nīta arthaḥ sahacaraṇa ādi nimittena atadbhāve tadvat abhidhānam upacāraḥ iti 
[0397,iv]	atra samādhiḥ prasiddhe prayoge vaktuḥ yathā abhiprāyam śabda arthayoḥ abhyanujñā pratiṣedhāḥ vā na cchandataḥ pradhāna bhūtasya śabdasya bhāktasya ca guṇa bhūtasya prayogaḥ ubhayoḥ loka siddhaḥ siddhe prayoge yathā vaktuḥ abhiprāyaḥ tathā śabda arthau anujñeyau pratiṣedhyau vā na cchandataḥ yadi vaktā pradhāna śabdam prayuṅkte yathābhūtasya abhyanujñā pratiṣedhaḥ vā na cchandataḥ atha guṇa bhūtam tadā guṇa bhūtasya yatra tu vaktā guṇa bhūtam śabdam prayuṅkte pradhāna bhūtam abhipretya paraḥ pratiṣedhati sva manīṣayā pratiṣedhaḥ asau bhavati na para upālambhaḥ iti 
[0399,i_0399,ii]	vākchalam eva upacāra chalam tat aviśeṣāt na vākchalāt upacāracchalam bhidyate tasya api artha antara kalpanāyāḥ aviśeṣāt iha api sthāni arthaḥ guṇa śabdaḥ pradhāna śabdaḥ sthāna arthaḥ iti kalpayitvā pratiṣidhyate iti 
[0400,i_0400,ii]	na tad artha antara bhāvāt na vākchalam eva upacāra chalam tasya artha sadbhāva pratiṣedhasya artha antara bhāvāt kutas artha antara kalpanātaḥ anyā hi artha antara kalpanā anyaḥ artha sadbhāva pratiṣedhaḥ iti 
[0401,i_0401,ii]	aviṣeṣe vā kiñcid sādharmyāt eka chala prasaṅaḥ chalasya dvi tvam abhyanujñāya tritvam pratiṣidhyate kiñcid sādharmyāt yathā ca ayam hetuḥ tritvam pratiṣedhati tathā dvi tvam api abhyanujñātam pratiṣedhati vidyate hi kiñcid sādharmyam dvayoḥ api iti atha dvi tvam kiñcid sādharmyāt na nivartate tritvam api na nivartsyati 
[0401,iii_0401,v]	chala lakṣaṇāt ūrdhvam sādharmya vaidharmyābhyām pratyavasthānam jātiḥ prayukte hi hetau yaḥ prasaṅgaḥ jāyate sa jātiḥ sa ca prasaṅgaḥ sādharmya vaidharmyābhyām pratyavasthānam upālambhaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ iti udāharaṇa sādharmyāt sādhya sādhanam hetuḥ iti asya udāharaṇa vaidharmyeṇa pratyavasthānam udāharaṇa vaidharmyāt sādhya sādhanam hetuḥ iti asya udāharaṇa sādharmyeṇa pratyavasthānam pratyanīka bhāvāt jāyamānaḥ arthaḥ jātiḥ iti 
[0403,i_0403,ii]	vipratipattiḥ apratipattiḥ ca nigraha sthānam viparītā vā kutsitā vā pratipattiḥ vipratipattiḥ vipratipadyamānaḥ parājayam prāpnoti nigraha sthānam khalu parājaya prāptiḥ apratipattiḥ tu ārambha viṣaye anārambhaḥ pareṇa sthāpitam vā na pratiṣedhati pratiṣedham vā na uddharati asamāsāt ca na ete eva nigraha sthāne iti 
[0404,i_0405,i]	kim punar dṛṣṭānta vat jāti nigraha sthānayoḥ abhedaḥ atha siddhānta vat bhedaḥ iti atas āha tad vikalpāt jāti nigraha sthāna bahu tvam tasya sādharmya vaidharmyābhyām pratyavasthānasya vikalpāt jāti bahu tvam tayoḥ ca vipratipatti apratipattyoḥ vikalpāt nigraha sthāna bahu tvam nānā kalpaḥ vikalpaḥ vividhaḥ vā kalpaḥ vikalpaḥ tatra ananubhāṣaṇam ajñānam apratibhā vikṣepaḥ mata anujñā paryanuyojya upekṣaṇam iti apratipattiḥ nigrasthānam śeṣaḥ tu vipratipattiḥ iti ime pramāṇa ādayaḥ padārthāḥ uddiṣṭāḥ yathoddeśam lakṣitāḥ yathālakṣaṇam parīkṣiṣyante iti trividhā ca asya śāstrasya pravṛttiḥ veditavyā iti 
[0408,i_0408,iii]	atas ūrdhvam pramāṇa ādi parīkṣā sā ca vimṛśya pakṣa pratipakṣābhyām artha avadhāraṇam nirṇayaḥ iti agre vimarṣaḥ eva parīkṣyate samāna aneka dharma adhyavasāyāt anyatara dharma adhyavasāyāt vā na saṃśayaḥ samānasya dharmasya adhyavasāyāt saṃśayaḥ na dharma mātrāt atha vā samānam anayoḥ dharmam upalabhaḥ iti dharma dharmi grahaṇe saṃśaya abhāvaḥ iti 
[0409,i]	atha vā samāna dharma adhyavasāyāt artha antara bhūte dharmiṇi saṃśayaḥ anupapannaḥ na jātu rūpasya artha antara bhūtasya adhyavasāyāt artha antara bhūte sparśe saṃśayaḥ iti atha vā na adhyavasāyāt artha avadhāraṇāt anavadhāraṇa jñānam saṃśayaḥ upapadyate kārya kāraṇayoḥ sārūpya abhāvāt iti etena aneka dharma adhyavasāyāt iti vyākhyātam anyatara dharma adhyvasāyāt ca saṃśayaḥ na bhavati tatas hi anyatara avadhāraṇam eva iti 
[0411,i_0411,ii]	vipratipatti avyavasthā adhyavasāyāt ca na vipratipatti mātrāt avyavasthā mātrāt vā saṃśayaḥ kim tarhi vipratipattim upalabhamānasya saṃśayaḥ evam avyavasthāyām api iti atha vā asti ātmā iti eke na asti ātmā iti apare manyante iti upalabdheḥ katham saṃśayaḥ syāt iti tathā upalabdhiḥ avyavasthitāḥ anupalabdhiḥ ca avyavasthitā iti vibhāgena adhyavasite saṃśayaḥ na upapadyate iti 
[0411,iii_0411,iv]	vipratipattau ca sampratipatteḥ yām ca vipratipattim bhavān saṃśaya hetuḥ manyate sā sampratipattiḥ sā hi dvayoḥ pratyanīka dharma viṣayā tatra yadi vipratipatteḥ saṃśayaḥ sampratipatteḥ eva saṃśayaḥ iti 
[0412,i_0412,iii]	avyavasthā ātmani vyavasthita tvāt ca avyavasthāyāḥ na saṃśayaḥ yadi tāvat iyam avyavasthā ātmani eva vyavasthitā vyavasthānāt avyavasthā na bhavati iti anupapannaḥ saṃśayaḥ atha avyavastha ātmani na vyavasthitā evam atādātmyāt avyavasthā na bhavati iti saṃśaya abhāvaḥ iti 
[0412,iv_0412,v]	tathā atyanta saṃśayaḥ tad dharma sātatya upapatteḥ yena kalpena bhavān samāna dharma upapatteḥ saṃśayaḥ iti manyate tena khalu atyanta saṃśayaḥ prasajyate samāna dharma upapatteḥ anucchedāt saṃśaya anucchedaḥ na hi ayam ataddharmā dharmī vimṛśyamāṇaḥ gṛhyate satatam tu tat dharmā bhavati iti 
[0413,i_0413,iii]	asya pratiṣedha prapañcasya saṅkṣepeṇa uddhāraḥ yathā ukta adhyavasāyāt eva tad aviśeṣa apekṣāt saṃśaye na asaṃśayaḥ na atyanta saṃśayaḥ vā na saṃśaya anutpattiḥ saṃśayānucchedaḥ ca prasajyate katham yat tāvat samāna dharma adhyavasāyaḥ saṃśaya hetuḥ na samāna dharma mātram iti evam etat kasmāt evam na ucyate iti viśeṣa apekṣaḥ iti vacanāt tad siddheḥ viśeṣasya apekṣā ākaṅkṣā sā ca anupalabhyamāne viśeṣe samarthā na ca uktam samāna dharma apekṣaḥ iti samāne ca dharme katham ākaṅkṣāḥ na bhavet yadi ayam pratyakṣaḥ syāt etena sāmarthyena vijñāyate samāna dharma adhyavasāyāt iti 
[0413,iv_0413,v]	upapatti vacanāt vā samāna dharma upapatteḥ iti ucyate na ca anyā sadbhāva saṃvedanāt ṛte samāna dharma upapattiḥ asti anupalabhyamāna sadbhāvaḥ hi samānaḥ dharmaḥ avidyamāna vat bhavati iti viṣaya śabdena vā viṣayiṇaḥ pratyayasya abhidhānam yathā loke dhūmena agniḥ anumīyate iti ukte dhūma darśanena agniḥ anumīyate iti jñāyate katham dṛṣṭvā hi dhūmam atha agnim anuminoti na adṛṣṭvā iti na ca vākye darśana śabdaḥ śrūyate anujānāti ca vākyasya artha pratyāyaka tvam tena manyāmahe viṣaya śabdena viṣayiṇaḥ pratyayasya abhidhānam boddha anujānāti evam iha api samāna dharma śabdena samāna dharma adhyvasāyam āha iti 
[0414,i]	yathohitvā samānam anayoḥ dharmam upalabhaḥ iti dharma dharmi grahaṇe saṃśaya abhāvaḥ iti pūrva dṛṣṭa viṣayam etat yau aham arthau pūrvam adrākṣam tayoḥ samānam dharmam upalabhe viśeṣam na upalabhaḥ iti katham nu viśeṣam paśyeyam yena anyataram avadhārayeyam iti na ca etat samāna dharma upalabdhau dharma dharmi grahaṇa mātreṇa nivartate iti 
[0414,ii_0415,i]	yat ca uktam na artha antara adhyavasāyāt anyatra saṃśayaḥ iti yaḥ hi artha antara adhyavasāya mātram saṃśaya hetum upādadīta saḥ evam vācyaḥ iti yat punar etat kārya kāraṇayoḥ sārūpya abhāvāt iti kāraṇasya bhāva abhāvayoḥ kāryasya bhāva abhāvau kārya kāraṇayoḥ sārūpyam yasya utpādāt yat utpadyate yasya ca anutpādāt yat na utpadyate tat kāraṇam kāryam itarat iti etat sārūpyam asti ca saṃśaya kāraṇe saṃśaye ca etat iti etena aneka dharma adhyavasāyāt iti pratiṣedhaḥ parihṛtaḥ iti 
[0415,ii]	yat punar etat uktam vipratipatti avyavasthā adhyavasāyāt ca na saṃśayaḥ iti pṛthak pravādayoḥ vyāhatam artham upalabhe viśeṣam ca na jānāmi na upalabhe yena anyataram avadhārayeyam tat kaḥ atra viśeṣaḥ syāt yena ekataram avadhārayeyam iti saṃśayaḥ vipratipatti janitaḥ ayam na śakyaḥ vipratipatti sampratipatti mātreṇa nivartayitum iti evam upalabdhi anupalabdhi avyavasthā kṛte saṃśaye veditavyam iti 
[0415,iii]	yat punar etat vipratipattau ca sampratipatteḥ iti vipratipatti śabdasya yaḥ arthaḥ tad adhyavasāyaḥ viśeṣa apekṣaḥ saṃśaya hetuḥ tasya ca samākhyā antareṇa na nivṛttiḥ samāne adhikaraṇe vyāhata arthau pravādau vipratipatti śabdasya arthaḥ tad adhyavasāyaḥ ca viśeṣa apekṣaḥ saṃśaya hetuḥ na ca asya sampratipatti śabde samākhyā antare yojyamāne saṃśaya hetutuvam nivartate tat idam akṛtabuddhi sammohanam iti 
[0415,iv_0417,i]	yat punar avyavasthā ātmani vyavasthita tvāt ca avyavasthāyāḥ iti saṃśaya hetoḥ arthasya apratiṣedhāt avyavasthā abhyanujñānāt ca nimitta antareṇa śabda antara kalpanā vyarthā śabda antara kalpanā vyavasthā khalu avyavasthā na bhavati avyavasthā ātmani vyavasthita tvāt iti na anayoḥ upalabdhi anupalabdhyoḥ sat asat viṣaya tvam viśeṣa apekṣam saṃśaya hetuḥ na bhvati iti pratiṣidhyate yāvatā ca avyavasthā ātmani vyavasthitā na tāvatā ātmānam jahāti tāvatā hi anujñāta avyavasthā evam iyam kriyamāṇā api śabda antara kalpanā na artha antaram sādhayati iti 
[0417,ii_0417,iii]	yat punar etat tathā atyanta saṃśayaḥ tad dharma sātatya upapatteḥ iti na ayam samāna dharma ādibhyaḥ eva saṃśayaḥ kim tarhi tad viṣaya adhyavasāyāt viśeṣa smṛti sahitāt iti atas na atyanta saṃśayaḥ iti anyatara dharma adhyavasāyāt vā na saṃśayaḥ iti tat na yuktam viśeṣa apekṣaḥ vimarṣaḥ saṃśayaḥ iti vacanāt viśeṣaḥ ca anyatara dharmaḥ na tasmin adhyvasīyamāne viśeṣa apekṣā sambhavati iti 
[0418,i_0418,ii]	yathra saṃśayaḥ tatra evam uttarottara prasaṅgaḥ yatra yatra saṃśaya pūrvikā parīkṣā śāstre kathāyām vā tatra tatra evam saṃśaye pareṇa pratiṣiddhe samādhiḥ vācyaḥ iti atas sarva parīkṣā vyāpi tvāt prathamam saṃśayaḥ parīkṣitaḥ iti 
[0419,i_0419,iii]	atha pramāṇa parīkṣā pratyakṣa ādīnām aprāmāṇyam traikālya asiddheḥ pratyakṣa ādīnām pramāṇa tvam na asti traikālya asiddheḥ pūrva apara sahabhāva anupapatteḥ iti arthaḥ 
[0420,i_0420,iii]	asya sāmānya vacanasya artha vibhāgaḥ pūrvam hi pramāṇa siddhau na indriya artha sannikarṣāt pratyakṣa utpattiḥ gandha ādi viṣayam jñānam pratyakṣam tat yadi pūrvam paścāt gandha ādīnām siddhiḥ na idam gandha ādi sannikarṣāt utpadyate iti 
[0420,iv_0420,v]	paścāt siddhau na pramāṇebhyaḥ prameya siddhiḥ asati pramāṇe kena pramīyamāṇaḥ arthaḥ prameyaḥ syāt pramāṇena khalu pramīyamāṇaḥ arthaḥ prameyam iti etat sidhyati 
[0421,i_0421,ii]	yugapad siddhau pratyartha niyata tvāt krama vṛtti tva abhāvaḥ buddhīnām yadi pramāṇam prameyam ca yugapad bhavataḥ evam api gandha ādiṣu indriya artheṣu jñānāni pratyartha niyatāni yugapad sambhavanti iti jñānānām pratyakṣa niyata tvāt krama vṛtti tva abhāvaḥ yāḥ imāḥ buddhayaḥ krameṇa artheṣu varttante tāsām krama vṛtti tvam na sambhavati iti vyāghātaḥ ca yugapad jñāna anutpattiḥ manasaḥ liṅgam iti etāvān ca pramāṇa prameyayoḥ sadbhāva viṣayaḥ sa ca anupapannaḥ iti tasmāt pratyakṣa ādīnām pramāṇa tvam na sambhavati iti 
[0421,iii_0423,i]	asya samādhiḥ upalabdhi hetoḥ upalabdhi viṣayasya ca arthasya pūrva apara sahabhāva aniyamāt yathādarśanam vibhāga vacanam kavacid upalabdhi hetuḥ paścāt upalabdhi viṣayaḥ yathā ādityasya prakāśaḥ utpadyamānānām kvacid pūrvam upalabdhi viṣayaḥ paścāt upalabdhi hetuḥ yathā avasthitānām pradīpaḥ kvacid upalabdhi hetuḥ upalabdhi viṣayaḥ ca saha bhvataḥ yathā dhūmena agneḥ grahaṇam iti upalabdhi hetuḥ ca pramāṇam prameyam tu upalabdhi viṣayaḥ evam pramāṇa prameyayoḥ pūrva apara sahabhāve aniyate yathārthaḥ dṛśyate tathā vibhajya vacanīyaḥ iti tatra ekāntena pratiṣedha anupapattiḥ sāmānyena khalu vibhajya pratiṣedhaḥ uktaḥ iti 
[0423,ii]	samākhyā hetoḥ traikālya yogāt tathābhūtā samākhyā yat punar idam paścāt siddhau asati pramāṇe prameyam na sidhyati pramāṇena pramīyamāṇaḥ arthaḥ prameyam iti vijñāyate iti pramāṇam iti etasyāḥ samākhyāyāḥ upalabdhi hetu tvam nimittam tasya traikālya yogaḥ upalabdhim akārṣīt upalabdhim karoti upalabdhim kariṣyati iti samākhyā hetoḥ traikālya yogāt samākhyā tathābhūtā pramitaḥ anena arthaḥ pramīyate pramāsyate iti pramāṇam pramitam pramīyate pramāsyate iti ca prameyam evam sati bhaviṣyati asmin hetutaḥ upalabdhiḥ pramāsyate ayam arthaḥ prameyam idam iti etat sarvam bhvati iti traikālyān abhyanujñāne ca vyavahāra anupapattiḥ yaḥ ca evam na abhyanujānīyāt tasya pācakam ānaya pakṣyati lāvakam ānaya laviṣyati iti vyavahāraḥ na upapadyate iti 
[0423,iii_0425,i]	pratyakṣa ādīnām aprāmāṇyam traikālya asiddheḥ iti evamādi vākyam pramāṇa pratiṣedhaḥ tatra ayam praṣṭavyaḥ atha anena pratiṣedhena bhavatā kim kriyate iti kim sambhavaḥ nivartyate atha asambhavaḥ jñāpyate iti tat yadi sambhavaḥ nivartyate sati sambhave pratyakṣa ādīnām pratiṣedha anupapattiḥ atha asambhavaḥ jñāpyate pramāṇa lakṣaṇam prāptaḥ tarhi pratiṣedhaḥ pramāṇa asambhavasya upalabdhi hetu tvāt iti 
[0425,ii_0426,i]	kim ca atas traikālya asiddheḥ pratiṣedha anupapattiḥ asya tu vibhāgaḥ pūrvam hi pratiṣedha siddhau asati pratiṣedhye kim anena pratiṣidhyate paścāt siddhau pratiṣedhya asiddhiḥ pratiṣedha abhāvāt iti yugapad siddhau pratiṣedhya siddhi abhyanujñānāt anarthakaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ iti pratiṣedha lakṣaṇe ca vākye anupapadyamāne siddham pratyakṣa ādīnām pramāṇa tvam iti 
[0427,i_0427,iii]	katham sarva pramāṇa pratiṣedhāt ca pratiṣedha anupapattiḥ traikālya asiddheḥ iti asya hetoḥ yadi udāharaṇam upādīyate hetu arthasya sādhaka tvam dṛṣṭānte darśayitavyam iti na ca tarhi pratyakṣa ādīnām aprāmāṇyam atha pratyakṣa ādīnām aprāmāṇyam upādīyamānam api udāharaṇam na artham sādhayiṣyati iti saḥ ayam sarva pramāṇa vyāhataḥ hetuḥ ahetuḥ siddhāntam abhyupetya tad virodhī viruddhaḥ iti vākya arthaḥ hi asya siddhāntaḥ sa ca vākya arthaḥ pratyakṣa ādīni na artham sādhayanti iti idam ca avayavānām upādānam arthasya sādhanāya iti atha na upādīyate apradarśitam hetu arthasya dṛṣṭāntena sādhaka tvam iti niṣedhaḥ na upapadyate hetu tva asiddheḥ iti 
[0429,i_0429,ii]	tad prāmāṇye vā na sarva pramāṇa vipratiṣedhaḥ pratiṣedha lakṣaṇe sva vākye teṣām avayava āśritānām pratyakṣa ādīnām prāmāṇye abhyanujñāyamāne para vākye api avayava āśritānām prāmāṇyam prasajyate aviśeṣāt iti evam ca na sarvāṇi pramāṇāni pratiṣidhyante iti vipratiṣedhaḥ iti vi iti ayam upasargaḥ sampratipatti arthe na vyāghāte artha abhāvāt iti 
[0430,i_0430,ii]	traikālya apratiṣedhaḥ ca śabdāt ātodya siddhi vat tad siddheḥ kim artham punar idam ucyate pūrva ukta nibandhana artham yat tāvat pūrva uktam upalabdhi hetoḥ upalabdhi viṣayasya ca arthasya pūrva apara sahabhāva aniyamāt yathādarśanam vibhāga vacanam iti tat itas samutthānam yathā vijñāyeta anityam adarśī khalu ayam ṛṣiḥ niyamena pratiṣedham pratyācaṣṭe traikālyasya ca ayuktaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ iti tatra ekām vidhām udāharati śabdāt ātodya siddhi vat iti 
[0431,i_0431,ii]	yathā paścāt siddhena śabdena pūrva siddham ātodyam anumīyate sādhyam ca ātodyam sādhanam ca śabdaḥ antarhite hi ātodye svanataḥ anumānam bhavati iti vīṇā vādyate veṇuḥ pūryate iti svana viśeṣeṇa ātodya viśeṣam pratipadyate tathā pūrva siddham upalabdhi viṣayam paścāt siddhena upalabdhi hetunā pratipadyate iti nidarśana artha tvāt ca asya śeṣayoḥ vidhayoḥ yathoktam udāharaṇam veditavyam iti kasmāt punar iha tat na ucyate pūrva uktam upapādyate iti sarvathā tāvat ayam arthaḥ prakāśayitavyaḥ saḥ iha vā prakāśyeta tatra vā na kaścid viśeṣaḥ iti 
[0432,i]	pramāṇam prameyam iti ca samākhyā samāveśena varttate samākhyā nimitta vaśāt samākhyā nimittam tu upalabdhi sādhanam pramāṇam upalabdhi viṣayaḥ ca prameyam iti yadā ca upalabdhi viṣayaḥ kvacid upalabdhi sādhanam bhavati tadā pramāṇam prameyam iti ca ekaḥ arthaḥ abhidhīyate asya arthasya avadyotana artham idam ucyate prameyā ca tulā prāmāṇya vat 
[0433,ii_0437,i]	guru tva parimāṇa jñāna sādhanam tulā pramāṇam jñāna viṣayaḥ guru dravyam suvarṇa ādi prameyam yathā suvarṇa ādinā tulā antaram vyavasthāpyate tadā tulā antara pratipattau suvarṇa ādi pramāṇam tulā antaram prameyam iti evam anavayavena tantra arthaḥ uddiṣṭaḥ veditavyaḥ ātmā tāvat upalabdhi viṣaya tvāt prameye paripaṭhitaḥ upalabdhau svātantryāt pramātā buddhiḥ upalabdhi sādhana tvāt pramāṇam upalabdhi viṣaya tvāt prameyam ubhaya abhāvāt tu pramitiḥ evam artha viśeṣe samākhyā samāveśaḥ yojyaḥ tathā ca kāraka śabdāḥ nimitta vaśāt samāveśena varttante iti vṛkṣaḥ tiṣṭhati iti sva sthitau svātantryāt kartā vṛkṣam paśyati iti darśanena āptum iṣyamāṇatama tvāt karma vṛkṣeṇa candramasam jñāpayati iti jñāpakasya sādhakatama tvāt karaṇam 
[0438,i]	vṛkṣāya udakam āsiñcati iti āsicyamānena udakena vṛkṣam abhipraiti iti sampradānam vṛkṣāt parṇam patati iti dhruvam apāye apādānam iti apādānam vṛkṣe vayāṃsi santi iti ādhāraḥ adhikaraṇam iti adhikaraṇam evam ca sati na dravya mātram kārakam na kriyā mātram kim tarhi kriyā sādhanam kriyā viśeṣa yuktam kārakam yat kriyā sādhanam svatantram sa kartā na dravya mātram na kriyā mātram kriyayā vyāptum iṣyamāṇatamam karma na dravya mātram na kryā mātram evam sādhakatama ādiṣu api evam ca kāraka an vā ākhyānam yathā eva upapattitaḥ evam lakṣaṇataḥ kāraka an vā ākhyānam api na dravya mātre na kriyāyām vā kim tarhi kriyā sādhane kriyā viśeṣa yuktaḥ iti kāraka śabdaḥ ca ayam pramāṇam prameyam iti sa ca kāraka dharmam na hātum arhati 
[0440,i]	asti bhoḥ kāraka śabdānām nimitta vaśāt samāveṣaḥ pratyakṣa ādīni ca pramāṇāni upalabdhi hetu tvāt prameyam ca upalabdhi viṣaya tvāt saṃvedyāni ca pratyakṣa ādīni pramāṇāni pratyakṣeṇa upalabhe anumānena upalabhe upamānena upalabhe āgamena upalabhe pratyakṣam me jñānam ānumānikam me jñānam aupamānikam me jñānam āgamikam me jñānam iti viśeṣāḥ gṛhyante lakṣaṇataḥ ca jñāpyamānāni jñāyante viśeṣeṇa indriya artha sannikarṣa utpannam jñānam iti evamādinā 
[0441,i_0442,i]	sā iyam upalabdhiḥ pratyakṣa ādi viṣayā kim pramāṇa antarataḥ atha antareṇa pramāṇa antaram asādhana iti kaḥ ca atra viśeṣaḥ pramāṇataḥ siddheḥ pramāṇānām pramāṇa antara siddhi prasaṅgaḥ yadi pratyakṣa ādīni pramāṇena upalabhyante yena pramāṇena upalabhyante tat pramāṇa antaram asti iti pramāṇa antara sadbhāvaḥ prasajyate iti anavasthām āha tasya api anyena tasya api anyena iti na ca anavasthā śakya anujñātum anupapatteḥ iti 
[0442,ii_0442,iv]	astu tarhi pramāṇa antaram antareṇa niḥsādhana iti tad vinivṛtteḥ vā pramāṇa siddhi vat prameya siddhiḥ yadi pratyakṣa ādi upalabdhau pramāṇa antaram nivarttane ātma ādi upalabdhau api pramāṇa antaram nivartsyati aviśeṣāt 
[0443,i_0443,iii]	evam ca sarva pramāṇa vilopaḥ iti atas āha na pradīpa prakāśa siddhi vat tad siddheḥ yathā pradīpa prakāśaḥ pratyakṣa aṅga tvāt dṛśya darśane pramāṇam sa ca pratyakṣa antareṇa cakṣuṣaḥ sannikarṣeṇa gṛhyate pradīpa bhāva abhāvayoḥ darśanasya tathā abhāvāt darśana hetuḥ anumīyate tamasi pradīpam upādadīthāḥ iti āpta upadeśena api pratipadyate evam pratyakṣa ādīnām yathādarśanam pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ eva upalabdhiḥ indriyāṇi tāvat sva viṣaya grahaṇena eva anumīyante arthāḥ pratyakṣataḥ gṛhyante indriya artha sannikarṣāḥ tu āvaraṇena liṅgena anumīyante 
[0444,i]	indriya artha sannikarṣa utpannam jñānam ātma manasoḥ saṃyoga viśeṣāt ātma samavayāt ca sukha ādi vat gṛhyate evam pramāṇa viśeṣaḥ vibhajya vacanīyaḥ yathā ca dṛśyaḥ san pradīpa prakāśaḥ dṛśya antarāṇām darśana hetuḥ iti dṛśya darśana vyavasthām labhate evam prameyam sat kiñcid artha jātam upalabdhi hetu tvāt pramāṇa prameya vyvasthām labhate sā iyam pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ eva pratyakṣa ādīnām yathādarśanam upalabdhiḥ na pramāṇa antarataḥ na ca pramāṇam antareṇa niḥsādhana iti 
[0444,ii]	tena eva tasya agrahaṇam iti ced na artha bhedasya lakṣaṇa sāmānyāt pratyakṣa ādīnām pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ eva grahaṇam iti ayuktam anyena hi anyasya grahaṇam dṛṣṭam iti na artha bhedasya lakṣaṇa sāmānyāt pratyakṣa lakṣaṇena anekaḥ arthaḥ saṃgṛhītaḥ tatra kenacid kasyacid grahaṇam iti adoṣaḥ evam anumāna ādiṣu api iti yata uddhṛtena udakena āśaya sthasya grahaṇam iti 
[0445,i_0445,iii]	jñātṛ manasoḥ ca darśanāt aham sukhī aham duḥkhī ca iti tena eva jñātrā tasya eva grahaṇam dṛśyate yugapad jñāna anutpattiḥ manasaḥ liṅgam iti ca tena eva manasā tasya eva anumānam dṛśyate jñātuḥ jñeyasya ca abhedaḥ grahaṇasya grāhyasya ca abhedaḥ iti nimitta bhedaḥ atra iti ced samānam na nimitta antareṇa vinā jñātā ātmānam jānīte na ca nimitta antareṇa vinā manasā manaḥ gṛhyate iti samānam etat pratyakṣa adbhiḥ pratyakṣa ādīnām grahaṇam iti atra api artha bhedaḥ na gṛhyate iti pratyakṣa ādīnām ca aviṣayasya anupapatteḥ yadi syāt kiṃcid artha jātam pratyakṣa ādīnām aviṣayaḥ yat pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ na śakyam grahītum tasya grahaṇāya pramāṇa antaram upādīyeta tat tu na śakyam kenacid upapādayitum iti pratyakṣa ādīnām yathādarśanam eva idam sat ca asat ca sarvam viṣayaḥ iti
