[0446,i_0446,ii]	kvacid nivṛtti darśanāt anivṛtti darśanāt ca kvacid anekāntaḥ kecid tu dṛṣṭāntam aparigṛhītam hetunā viśeṣa hetum antareṇa sādhya sādhanāya upādadate yathā pradīpa prakāśaḥ pradīpa antara prakāśam antareṇa gṛhyate tathā pramāṇāni pramāṇa antaram antareṇa gṛhyate iti sa ca ayam yathā ca ayam prasaṅgaḥ nivṛtti darśanāt pramāṇa sādhāya upādīyate evam prameya sādhanāya api upādeyaḥ aviśeṣa hetu tvāt yathā ca sthālī ādi rūpa grahaṇe pradīpa prakāśaḥ prameya sādhanāya upādīyate evam pramāṇa sādhāya api upādeyaḥ viśeṣa hetu abhāvāt saḥ ayam viśeṣa hetu parigraham antareṇa dṛṣṭānte ekasmin pakṣe upādeyaḥ na pratipakṣaḥ iti anekāntaḥ ekasmin ca pakṣe dṛṣṭāntaḥ iti anekāntaḥ viśeṣa hetu abhāvāt iti 
[0448,i_0449,i]	viśeṣa hetu parigrahe sati upasaṃhāra abhyanujñānāt apratiṣedhaḥ viśeṣa hetu parigṛhītaḥ tu dṛṣṭānte ekasmin pakṣe upasaṃhriyamāṇaḥ na śakyaḥ anujñātum evam ca sati anekāntaḥ iti ayam pratiṣedhaḥ na bhavati pratyakṣa ādīnām pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ upalabdhau anavasthā iti ced na saṃvid viṣaya nimittānām upalabdhyā vyavahāra upapatteḥ pratyakṣeṇa artham upalabhe anumānena artham upalabhe upamānena artham upalabhe āgamena artham upalabhe iti pratyakṣam me jñānam ānumānikam me jñānam aupamānikam me jñānam āgamikam me jñānam iti saṃvid viṣayam saṃvid nimittam ca upalabhamānasya dharma artha sukha apavarga prayojanaḥ tad pratyanīka parivarjana prayojanaḥ ca vyavahāraḥ upapadyate saḥ ayam tāvatī eva nivartate na ca asti vyavahāra antaram anavasthā sādhanīyam yena pratyukta anavasthām upādadīta iti 
[0449,ii_0449,iv]	sāmānyena pramāṇāni parīkṣya viśeṣeṇa parīkṣyante tatra pratyakṣa lakṣaṇa anupapattiḥ asamagra vacanāt ātma manaḥ sannikarṣaḥ hi kāraṇa antaram na uktam iti 
[0450,i_0451,iii]	na ca asaṃyukte dravye saṃyoga janyasya guṇasya utpattiḥ iti jñāna utpatti darśanāt ātma manaḥ sannikarṣaḥ kāraṇam manaḥ sannikarṣa anapekṣasya ca indriya artha sannikarṣasya jñāna kāraṇa tve yugapad utpadyeran buddhayaḥ iti manaḥ sannikarṣaḥ api kāraṇam tat idam sūtram purastāt kṛta bhāṣyam na ātma manasoḥ sannikarṣa abhāve pratyakṣa utpattiḥ ātma manasoḥ sannikarṣa abhāve na utpadyate pratyakṣam indriya artha sannikarṣa abhāva vat iti 
[0452,i_0452,iii]	sati ca indriya artha sannikarṣe jñāna utpatti darśanāt kāraṇa bhāvam bruvataḥ diś deśa kāla ākāśeṣu api evam prasaṅgaḥ diś ādiṣu satsu jñāna bhāvāt tāni api kāraṇāni iti akāraṇa bhāve api jñāna utpattiḥ diś ādi sannidheḥ avarjanīya tvāt yadā api akāraṇam diś ādīni jñāna utpattau tadā api satsu diś ādiṣu jñānena bhavitavyam na hi diś ādīnām sannidhiḥ śakyaḥ parivarjayitum iti tatra kāraṇa bhāve hetu vacanam etasmāt dhetoḥ diś ādīni jñāna kāraṇāni iti 
[0452,iv_0454,i]	ātma manaḥ sannikarṣaḥ tarhi upasaṅkhyeyaḥ iti tatra idam ucyate jñāna liṅga tvāt ātmanaḥ na anavarodhaḥ jñānam ātma liṅgam tad guṇa tvāt na ca asaṃyukte dravye saṃyoga jasya guṇasya utpattiḥ asti iti 
[0455,i_0455,ii]	tad ayaugapadya liṅga tvāt ca na manasaḥ anavarodhaḥ iti varttate yugapad jñāna anutpattiḥ manasaḥ liṅgam iti ucyamāne sidhyati eva manaḥ sannikarṣa apekṣaḥ indriya artha sannikarṣaḥ jñāna kāraṇam iti 
[0456,i_0456,ii]	pratyakṣa nimitta tvāt ca indriya arthayoḥ sannikarṣasya sva śabdena vacanam pratyakṣa anumāna upamāna śabdānām nimittam ātma manaḥ sannikarṣaḥ pratyakṣasya eva indriya artha sannikarṣaḥ iti asamānaḥ asamāna tvāt tasya grahaṇam 
[0457,i_0457,ii]	supta vyāsakta manasām ca indriya arthayoḥ sannikarṣa nimitta tvāt indriya artha sannikarṣasya grahaṇam na ātma manasoḥ sannikarṣasya iti ekadā khalu ayam prabodha kālam praṇidhāya suptaḥ praṇidhāna vaśāt prabudhyate yadā tu tīvrau dhvani sparśau prabodha kāraṇam bhavataḥ tadā prasuptasya indriya sannikarṣa nimittam prabodha jñānam utpadyate tatra na jñātuḥ manasaḥ ca sannikarṣasya prādhānyam bhavati kim tarhi indriya arthayoḥ sannikarṣasya na hi ātmā jijñāsamānaḥ prayatnena manaḥ tadā prerayati iti 
[0457,iii_0458,i]	ekadā khalu ayam viṣaya antara āsakta manāḥ saṅkalpa vaśāt viṣaya antaram jijñāsamānaḥ prayatna preritena manasā indriyam saṃyojya tat viṣaya antaram jānīte yadā tu khalu asya niḥsaṅkalpasya nirjijñāsasya ca vyāsakta manasaḥ bāhya viṣaya upanipātanāt jñānam utpadyate tadā indriya artha sannikarṣasya prādhānyam na hi atra asau jijñāsamānaḥ prayatnena manaḥ prerayati iti prādhānyāt ca indriya artha sannikarṣasya grahaṇam kāryam guṇa tvāt na ātma manasoḥ sannikarṣasya iti 
[0458,ii_0458,iv]	prādhānye ca hetu antaram taiḥ ca apadeśaḥ jñāna viśeṣāṇām taiḥ indriyaiḥ arthaiḥ ca vyapadiśyante jñāna viśeṣāḥ katham ghrāṇena jighrati cakṣuṣā paśyati rasanayā rasayati iti ghrāṇa vijñānam cakṣuḥ vijñānam rasanā vijñānam gandha vijñānam rūpa vijñānam rasa vijñānam iti ca indriya viṣaya viśeṣāt ca pañcadhā buddhiḥ bhavati atas prādhānyam indriya artha sannikarṣasya iti 
[0451,i_0460,i]	yat uktam indriya artha sannikarṣa grahaṇam kāryam na ātma manasoḥ sannikarṣasya iti kasmāt supta vyāsakta manasām indriya arthayoḥ sannikarṣasya jñāna nimitta tvāt iti saḥ ayam vyāhata tvāt ahetuḥ yadi tāvat kvacid ātma manasoḥ sannikarṣasya jñāna kāraṇa tvam na iṣyate tadā yugapad jñāna anutpattiḥ manasaḥ liṅgam iti vyāhanyeta na idānīm manasaḥ sannikarṣam indriya artha sannikarṣaḥ apekṣate manaḥ saṃyoga anapekṣāyām ca yugapad jñāna utpatti prasaṅgaḥ atha mā bhūt vyāghātaḥ iti sarva vijñānānām ātma manasoḥ sannikarṣaḥ kāraṇam iṣyate tad avastham eva idam bhavati jñāna kāraṇa tvāt ātma manasoḥ sannikarṣasya grahaṇam kāryam iti 
[0460,ii_0461,i]	na artha viśeṣa prābalyāt na asti vyāghātaḥ na hi ātma manaḥ sannikarṣasya jñāna kāraṇa tvam vyabhicarati indriya artha sannikarṣasya prādhānyam upādīyate artha viśeṣa prābalyāt dhi supta vyāsakta manasām jñāna utpattiḥ ekadā bhavati artha viśeṣaḥ kaścid eva indriya arthaḥ tasya prābalyam tīvra tā paṭute tat ca artha viśeṣa prābalyam indriya artha sannikarṣa viṣayam na ātma manasoḥ sannikarṣa viṣayam tasmāt indriya artha sannikarṣaḥ pradhānam iti asati praṇidhāne saṅkalpe ca asati supta vyāsakta manasām yat indriya artha sannikarṣāt utpadyate jñānam tatra manaḥ saṃyogaḥ api kāraṇam iti manasi kriyā kāraṇam vācyam iti 
[0461,ii]	yathā eva jñātuḥ khalu ayam icchā janitaḥ prayatnaḥ manasaḥ prerakaḥ ātma guṇaḥ evam ātmani guṇa antaram sarvasya sādhakam pravṛtti doṣa janitam asti yena preritam manaḥ indriyeṇa sambadhyate tena hi apreryamāṇe manasi saṃyoga abhāvāt jñāna anutpattau sarva artha tā asya nivarttate eṣitavyam ca asya guṇa antarasya dravya guṇa karma kāraṇa tvam anyathā hi caturvidhānām aṇūnām bhūta sūkṣmāṇām manasām ca tatas anyasya kriyā hetoḥ asambhavāt śarīra indriya viṣayāṇām anutpatti prasaṅgaḥ 
[0462,i_0462,ii]	pratyakṣam anumānam eka deśa grahaṇāt upalabdheḥ yat idam indriya artha sannikarṣāt utpadyate jñānam vṛkṣaḥ iti etat kila pratyakṣam tat khalu anumānam eva kasmāt eka deśa grahaṇāt vṛkṣasya upalabdheḥ arvāc bhāgam ayam gṛhītvā vṛkṣam upalabhate na ca eka deśaḥ vṛkṣaḥ tatra yathā dhūmam gṛhītvā vahnim anuminoti tādṛś eva tat bhavati 
[0463,i_0467,i]	kim punar gṛhyamāṇāt eka deśāt artha antaram anumeyam manyase avayava samūha pakṣe avayava antarāṇi dravya antara utpatti pakṣe tāni ca avavavī ca iti avayava samūha pakṣe tāvat eka deśa grahaṇāt vṛkṣa buddheḥ abhāvaḥ na agṛhyamāṇam eka deśa antaram vṛkṣaḥ gṛhyamāṇa eka deśa vat iti atha eka deśa grahaṇāt eka deśa antara anumāne samudāya pratisandhānāt tatra vṛkṣa buddhiḥ na tarhi vṛkṣa buddhiḥ anumānam evam sati bhavitum arhati iti dravya antara utpatti pakṣe na avaya vi anumeyaḥ asya eka deśa sambaddhasya agrahaṇāt grahaṇe ca aviśeṣāt anumeya tva abhāvaḥ tasmāt vṛkṣa buddhiḥ anumānam na bhavati 
[0468,i_0468,iv]	eka deśa grahaṇam āśritya pratyakṣasya anumāna tvam upapādyate tat ca na pratyakṣeṇa yāvat tāvat api upalambhāt na pratyakṣam anumānam kasmāt pratyakṣeṇa eva upalambhāt yat tad eka deśa grahaṇam āśrīyate pratyakṣeṇa asau upalambhaḥ na ca upalambhaḥ nirviṣayaḥ asti yāvat ca artha jātam tasya viṣayaḥ tāvat abhyupajñāyamānam pratyakṣa vyavasthāpakam bhavati kim punar tatas anyat artha jātam avayavī samudāyaḥ vā na ca eka deśa grahaṇam anumānam bhāvayitum śakyam hetu abhāvāt iti 
[0469,i]	anyathā api ca pratyakṣasya na anumāna tva prasaṅgaḥ tad pūrvaka tvāt pratyakṣa pūrvakam anumānam sambaddhau agni dhūmau pratyakṣataḥ dṛṣṭavataḥ dhūma pratyakṣa darśanāt agnau anumānam bhavati yat ca sambaddhayoḥ liṅga liṅginoḥ pratyakṣam yat ca liṅga mātra pratyakṣa grahaṇam na etat antareṇa anumānasya pravṛttiḥ asti na tu etat anumānam indriya artha sannikarṣa ja tvāt na ca anumeyasya indriyeṇa sannikarṣāt anumānam bhavati saḥ ayam pratyakṣa anumānayoḥ lakṣaṇa bhedaḥ mahān āśrayitavyaḥ iti 
[0470,i_0470,ii]	na ca eka deśa upalabdhiḥ avayavi sadbhāvāt na ca eka deśa upalabdhi mātram kim tarhi eka deśa upalabdhiḥ tad sahacarita avayavī upalabdhiḥ ca kasmāt avayavi sadbhāvāt asti hi ayam eka deśa vyatiriktaḥ avayavī tasya avayava sthānasya upalabdhi kāraṇa prāptasya eka deśa upalabdhau anupalabdhiḥ anupapanna iti akṛtsna grahaṇāt iti ced na kāraṇataḥ anyasya eka deśasya abhāvāt na ca avayavāḥ kṛtsnāḥ gṛhyante avayavaiḥ eva avayava antara vyavadhānāt na avayavī kṛtsnaḥ gṛhyate iti na ayam gṛhyamnāṇeṣu avayaveṣu parisamāptaḥ iti sā iyam ekaddeśa upalabdhiḥ anivṛttā eva iti 
[0470,iii_0473,i]	kṛtsnam iti vai khalu aśeṣa tāyām satyām bhavati akṛtsnam iti śeṣe sati tat ca etat avayaveṣu bahuṣu asti avyavadhāne grahaṇāt vyavadhāne ca agrahaṇāt iti aṅga tu bhavān pṛṣṭaḥ vyācaṣṭām gṛhyamāṇasya avayavinaḥ kim agṛhītam manyate yena eka deśa upalabdhiḥ syāt iti na hi asya kāraṇebhyaḥ anye eka deśāḥ bhavanti iti tatra avayava vṛttam na upapadyate iti idam tasya vṛttam yeṣām indriya sannikarṣāt grahaṇam avayavānām taiḥ saha gṛhyate yeṣām avayavānām vyavadhānāt agrahaṇam taiḥ saha na gṛhyate na ca etad kṛtaḥ asti bhedaḥ iti 
[0477,i]	samudāya śeṣa tā vā samudāyaḥ vṛkṣaḥ syāt tad prāptiḥ vā ubhayathā grahaṇa abhāvaḥ mūla skandha śākhā palāśa ādīnām aśeṣa tā vā samudāyaḥ vṛkṣaḥ iti syāt prāptiḥ vā samudāyinām iti ubhayathā samudāya bhūtasya vṛkṣasya grahaṇam na upapadyate iti avayavaiḥ tāvat avayava antarasya vyavadhānāt aśeṣa grahaṇam na upapadyate prāpti grahaṇam api na upapadyate prāptimatām agrahaṇāt sā iyam eka deśa grahaṇa sahacaritā vṛkṣa vuddhiḥ dravya antara utpattau kalpate na samudaya mātre iti 
[0478,i_0478,ii]	sādhya tvāt avayavini sandehaḥ yat uktam avayavi sadbhāvāt iti ayam ahetuḥ sādhya tvāt sādhyam tāvat etat kāraṇebhyaḥ dravya antaram utpadyate iti anupapāditam etat evam ca sati vipratipatti mātram bhavati vipratipatteḥ ca avayavini saṃśayaḥ iti 
[0497,i_0497,ii]	sarva agrahaṇam avayavi asiddheḥ yadi avayavī na asti sarvasya grahaṇam na upapadyate kim tat sarvam dravya guṇa karma sāmānya viśeṣa samavāyāḥ katham kṛtvā paramāṇu samavasthānam tāvat darśana viṣayaḥ na bhavati atīndriya tvāt aṇūnām dravya antaran ca avaya vi bhūtam darśana viṣayaḥ na asti darśana viṣaya sthāḥ ca ime dravya ādayaḥ gṛhante te niradhiṣṭhānāḥ na gṛhyeran gṛhyante tu kumbhaḥ ayam śyāmaḥ ekaḥ mahān saṃyuktaḥ spandate asti mṛd mayaḥ ca iti santi ca ime guṇa ādayaḥ dharmāḥ iti tena sarvasya grahaṇāt paśyāmaḥ asti dravya antara bhūtaḥ avayavi iti 
[0498,i_0498,iii]	dhāraṇa ākarṣaṇa upapatteḥ ca avayavi artha antara bhūtaḥ iti saṅgraha kārite vai dhāraṇa ākarṣaṇe saṃgrahaḥ nāma saṃyoga sahacaritam guṇa antaram sneha drava tva kāritam apām saṃyogāt āme kumbhe agni saṃyogāt pakve yadi tu avayavi kārite abhaviṣyatām pāṃśu rāśi prabhṛti śu api ajñāsyetām dravya antara anutpattau ca tṛṇa upala kāṣṭha ādiṣu jatu saṃgṛhīteṣu api na abhāviṣyatām iti 
[0499,i]	atha avayavinam pratyācakṣāṇakaḥ mā bhūt pratyakṣa lopaḥ iti aṇu sañcayam darśana viṣayam pratijānānaḥ kim anuyoktavyaḥ iti ekam idam dravyam iti eka vuddheḥ viṣayam paryanuyojyaḥ kim eka buddhiḥ abhinna artha viṣaya iti āhosvit bhinna artha viṣaya iti abhinna artha viṣaya iti ced artha antara anujñānāt avayava visiddhiḥ nānā artha viṣaya iti ced bhinneṣu eka darśana anupapattiḥ anekasmin ekaḥ iti vyāhatā buddhiḥ na dṛśyate iti 
[0500,ii_0500,iii]	senā vana vat grahaṇam iti ced na atīndriya tvāt aṇūnām yathā senā aṅgeṣu vana aṅgeṣu ca dūrāt agṛhyamāṇa pṛthaktveṣu ekam idam iti upapadyate buddhiḥ evam aṇuṣu sañciteṣu agṛhyamāṇa pṛthaktveṣu ekam idam iti upapadyate buddhiḥ iti yathā gṛhyamāṇa pṛthaktvānām senā vana aṅgānām ārāt kāraṇa antarataḥ pṛthaktu asya agrahaṇam yathā gṛhyamāṇa jātīnām palāśaḥ iti vā khadiraḥ iti vā nārāt jāti grahaṇam bhavati yathā gṛhyamāṇa praspandānām nārāt spanda grahaṇam gṛhyamāṇe ca artha jāte pṛthaktvasya agrahaṇāt ekam iti bhāktaḥ pratyayaḥ bhavati na tu aṇūnām gṛhyamāṇa pṛthaktvānām kāraṇataḥ pṛthaktu asya agrahaṇāt bhāktaḥ eka pratyayaḥ atīndriya tvāt aṇūnām iti 
[0503,i_0503,ii]	idam eva ca parīkṣyate kim eka pratyayaḥ ṇu sañcaya viṣayaḥ āhosvit na iti aṇu sañcaye eva senā avanāṅāni na ca parīkṣyamāṇam udāharaṇam iti yuktam sādhya tvāt iti dṛṣṭam iti ced na tad viṣayasya parīkṣā upapatteḥ yat api manyeta dṛṣṭam idam senā vana aṅgānām pṛthaktvasya agrahaṇāt abhedena ekam iti grahaṇam na ca dṛṣṭam śakyam pratyākhyātum iti tat ca na evam tad viṣayasya parīkṣā upapatteḥ darśana viṣayaḥ eva ayam parīkṣyate yaḥ ayam ekam iti pratyayaḥ dṛśyate sa parīkṣyate kim dravya antara viṣayaḥ vai atha aṇu sañcaya viṣayaḥ iti atra darśanam anyatarasya sādhakam na bhavati nānā bhāve ca aṇūnām pṛthaktvasya agrahaṇāt abhedena ekam iti grahaṇam atasmin tat iti pratyayaḥ yathā sthāṇau puruṣaḥ iti tatas kim 
[0504,i]	atasmin tat iti pratyayasya pradhāna apekṣi tvāt pradhāna siddhiḥ sthāṇau puruṣaḥ iti pratyayasya kim pradhānam saḥ asau puruṣe puruṣa pratyayaḥ tasmin sati puruṣa sāmānya grahaṇāt sthāṇau puruṣaḥ ayam iti evam nānā bhūteṣu ekam iti sāmānya grahaṇāt pradhāne sati bhavitum arhati pradhānam ca sarvasya agrahaṇāt iti na upapadyate tasmāt abhinnaḥ eva ayam abheda pratyayaḥ ekam iti 
[0505,i]	indriya antara viṣayeṣu abheda pratyayaḥ pradhānam iti ced na viśeṣa hetu abhāvāt dṛṣṭānta avyavasthā śrotra ādi viṣayeṣu śabda ādiṣu abhinneṣu eka pratyayaḥ pradhānam anekasmin eka pratyayasya iti evam ca sati dṛṣṭānta upādānam na vyavatiṣṭhate viśeṣa hetu abhāvāt aṇuṣu saṃśiteṣu eka pratyayaḥ kim atasmin tat iti pratyayaḥ sthāṇau puruṣa pratyaya vat atha arthasya tathā abhāvāt tasmin tat iti pratyayaḥ yathā śabdasya eka tvāt ekaḥ śabdaḥ iti viśeṣa hetu parigrahaṇam antareṇa dṛṣṭāntau saṃśayam āpādayate iti kumbha vat sañcaya mātram gandha ādayaḥ api iti anudāharaṇam gandha ādayaḥ iti 
[0507,i_0507,ii]	evam parimāṇa saṃyoga spanda jāti viśeṣa pratyayān api anuyoktavyaḥ teṣu ca evam prasaṅgaḥ iti ekatva buddhiḥ tasmin tat iti pratyayaḥ iti viśeṣa hetuḥ mahat iti pratyayena sāmānādhikaraṇyāt ekam idam mahat ca iti eka viṣayau pratyayau samāna adhikaraṇau bhavataḥ tena vijñāyate yat mahat tat ekam iti aṇu samūha atiśaya grahaṇam mahat pratyayaḥ iti ced saḥ ayam amahatsu aṇuṣu mahat pratyayaḥ atasmin tat iti pratyayaḥ bhavati iti kim ca atas atasmin tat iti pratyayasya pradhāna apekṣi tvāt pradhāna siddhiḥ iti bhavitavyam mahati eva mahat pratyayena iti 
[0508,i]	aṇuḥ śabdaḥ mahān iti ca vyavasāyāt pradhāna siddhiḥ iti ced na mandatīvra tā grahaṇam iyattā an avadhāraṇāt yathā dravye aṇuḥ śabdaḥ alpaḥ mandaḥ iti etasya grahaṇam mahan śabdaḥ paṭuḥ tīvraḥ iti etasya grahaṇam kasmāt iyattā an avadhāraṇāt na hi ayam mahān śabdaḥ iti vyavasyan iyān ayam iti avadhārayati yathā badara āmalaka bilva ādīni 
[0509,i_0509,ii]	saṃyukte ime iti ca dvi tva samāna āśraya prāpti grahaṇam dvau samudāyau āśrayaḥ saṃyogasya iti ced kaḥ ayam samudāyaḥ prāptiḥ anekasya anekā vā prāptiḥ ekasya samudāyaḥ iti ced prāpteḥ agrahaṇam prāpti āśritāyāḥ saṃyukte ime vastunī iti na atra dve prāptī saṃyukte gṛhyete aneka samūhaḥ samudāyaḥ iti ced na dvi tvena samāna adhikaraṇasya grahaṇāt dvau imau saṃyuktau arthau iti grahaṇe sati na aneka samūha āśrayaḥ saṃyogaḥ gṛhyate na ca dvayoḥ aṇvoḥ grahaṇam asti tasmāt mahatī dvi tva āśraya bhūte dravye saṃyogasya sthānam iti 
[0510,i]	pratyāsattiḥ pratīghāta avasānā saṃyogaḥ na artha antaram iti ced na artha antara hetu tvāt saṃyogasya śabda rūpa ādi spandānām hetuḥ saṃyogaḥ na ca dravyayoḥ guṇa antara upajananam antareṇa śabde rūpa ādiṣu spande ca kāraṇa tvam gṛhyate tasmāt guṇa antaram pratyaya viṣayaḥ ca artha antaram tat pratiṣedhaḥ vā kuṇḍalī guruḥ akuṇḍalaḥ chātre iti saṃyoga buddheḥ ca yadi artha antaram na viṣayaḥ artha antara pratiṣedhaḥ tarhi viṣayaḥ tatra pratiṣidhyamāna vacanam saṃyukte dravye iti yat artha antaram anyatra dṛṣṭam iha pratiṣidhyate tat vaktavyam iti dvayoḥ mahatoḥ āśritasya grahaṇāt na aṇvāśrayaḥ iti 
[0511,i]	jāti viśeṣasya pratyaya anuvṛtti liṅgasya apratyākhyānam pratyākhyāne vā pratyaya vyavasthā anupapattiḥ vyadhikaraṇasya anabhivyakteḥ adhikaraṇa vacanam aṇu samavasthānam viṣayaḥ iti ced prāpta aprāpta sāmarthya vacanam kim aprāpte aṇu samavasthāne tad āśrayaḥ jāti viśeṣaḥ gṛhyate atha prāpte iti aprāpte grahaṇam iti ced vyavahitasya aṇu samavasthānasya api upalabdhi prasaṅgaḥ vyavahite aṇu samavasthāne tad āśrayaḥ jāti viśeṣaḥ gṛhyeta prāpte grahaṇam iti ced madhya para bhāgayoḥ aprāptau anabhivyaktiḥ yāvat prāptam bhavati tāvatī abhivyaktiḥ iti ced tāvataḥ adhikaraṇa tvam aṇu samavasthānasya yāvati prāpte jāti viśeṣe gṛhyate tāvat asya adhikaraṇam iti prāptam bhavati tatra eka samudāye pratīyamāne artha bhedaḥ evam ca sati yaḥ ayam aṇu samudāyaḥ vṛkṣaḥ iti pratīyate tatra vṛkṣa bahu tvam pratīyeta yatra yatra hi aṇu samudāyasya bhāge vṛkṣa tvam gṛhyate sa sa vṛkṣaḥ iti tasmāt samudita aṇu samavasthānasya artha antarasya jāti viśeṣa abhivyakti viṣaya tvāt avayavi artha antara bhūtaḥ iti 
[0514,i_0514,iii]	parīkṣitam pratyakṣam anumānam idānīm parīkṣyate rodha upaghāta sādṛśyebhyaḥ vyabhicārāt anumānam apramāṇam apramāṇam iti ekadā api arthasya na pratipādakam iti rodhāt api nadī pūrṇā gṛhyate tadā ca upariṣṭāt vṛṣṭaḥ devaḥ iti mithyā anumānam nīḍa upaghātāt api pipīlikā aṇḍa sañcāraḥ bhavati tadā ca bhaviṣyati vṛṣṭiḥ iti mithyā anumānam iti puruṣaḥ api mayūra vāśitam anukaroti tadā api śabda sādṛśyāt mithyā anumānam bhavati 
[0516,i_0516,ii]	na eka deśa trāsa sādṛśyebhyaḥ artha antara bhāvāt na ayam anumāna vyabhicāraḥ ananumāne tu khalu ayam anumāna abhimānaḥ katham na aviśiṣṭaḥ liṅgam bhavitum arhati pūrva udaka viśiṣṭam khalu varṣa udakam śīgratara tvam srātasaḥ bahutara phena phala parṇa kāṣṭha ādi vahanam ca upalabhamānaḥ pūrṇa tvena nadyā upari vṛṣṭaḥ devaḥ iti anuminoti na udaka vṛddhi mātreṇa pipīlikā prāyasya aṇḍa sañcāre bhaviṣyati vṛṣṭiḥ iti anumīyate na kāsāñcid iti na idam mayūra vāśitam tad sadṛśaḥ ayam śabdaḥ iti viśeṣa aparijñānāt mithyā anumānam iti yaḥ tu sadṛśāt viśiṣṭāt śabdāt viśiṣṭa mayūra vāśitam gṛhṇāti tasya viśiṣṭaḥ arthaḥ gṛhyamāṇaḥ liṅgam yathā sarpa ādīnām iti saḥ ayam anumātuḥ aparādhaḥ na anumānasya yaḥ artha viśeṣeṇa anumeyam artham aviśiṣṭa artha darśanena bubhutsate iti 
[0517,i_0517,iii]	tri kāla viṣayam anumānam traikālya grahaṇāt iti uktam atas ca vartamāna abhāvaḥ patataḥ patita patitavya kāla upapatteḥ vṛntāt pracyutasya phalasya bhūmau pratyāsīdataḥ yat ūrdhvam sa patitaḥ adhvā tad saṃyuktaḥ kālaḥ patita kālaḥ yaḥ adhastāt sa patitavyaḥ adhvā tad saṃyuktaḥ kālaḥ patitavya kālaḥ na idānīm tṛtīyaḥ adhvā vidyate yatra patati iti vartamānaḥ kālaḥ gṛhyeta tasmāt vartamānaḥ kālaḥ na vidyate iti 
[0520,i_0521,i]	tayoḥ api abhāvaḥ vartamāna abhāve tad apekṣa tvāt na adhva vyaṅgyaḥ kālaḥ kim tarhi kriyā vyaṅgyaḥ patati iti yadā patana kriyā vyuparatā bhavati sa kālaḥ patita kālaḥ yadā utpatsyate sa patitavya kālaḥ yadā dravye vartamānā kriyā gṛhyate sa vartamānaḥ kālaḥ yadi ca ayam dravye vartamānam patanam na gṛhṇāti kasya uparamam utpatsyamāna tām vā pratipadyate patitaḥ kālaḥ iti bhūtā kriyā patitavyaḥ kālaḥ iti ca utpatsyamānā kriyā ubhayoḥ kālayoḥ kriyā hīnam dravyam adhas patati iti kriyā sambaddham saḥ ayam kriyā dravyayoḥ sambandham gṛhṇāti iti vartamānaḥ kālaḥ tad āśrayau ca itarau kālau tat ahāve na syātām iti 
[0522,i_0523,i]	atha api na atīta anāgatayoḥ itaretara apekṣā siddhiḥ yadi atīta anāgatau itaretara apekṣau sidhyetām pratipadyemahi vartamāna vilopam na atīta apekṣā anāgata siddhiḥ na api anāgata apekṣā atīta siddhiḥ kayā yuktyā kena kalpena atītaḥ katham atīta apekṣā anāgata siddhiḥ kena ca kalpena anāgataḥ iti na etat śakyam nirvaktum avyākaraṇīyam etat vartamāna lopaḥ iti yat ca manyeta hrasva dīrghayoḥ sthala nimnayoḥ chāyā ātapayoḥ ca yathā itara itara apekṣayā siddhiḥ evam atīta anāgatayoḥ iti tat na upapadyate viśeṣa hetu abhāvāt dṛṣṭānta vat pratidṛṣṭāntaḥ api prasajyate yathā rūpa sparśau gandharasau na itaretara apekṣau siddhi atas evam atīta anāgatau iti na itara itara apekṣā kasyacid siddhiḥ iti yasmāt eka abhāve ṇyatara abhāvāt ubhaya abhāvaḥ yadi ekasya anyatara apekṣā siddhiḥ anyatarasya idānīm kim apekṣā yadi anyatarasya eka apekṣā siddhiḥ ekasya idānīm kim apekṣā evam ekasya abhāve anyatarat na sidhyati iti ubhaya abhāvaḥ prasajyate 
[0523,ii_0523,iv]	artha sadbhāva vyaṅgyaḥ ca ayam vartamānaḥ kālaḥ vidyate dravyam vidyate guṇaḥ vidyate karma iti yasya ca ayam na asti tasya vartamāna abhāve sarva agrahaṇam pratyakṣa anupapatteḥ pratyakṣam indriya artha sannikarṣa jam na ca avidyamānam asat indriyeṇa sat nikṛṣyate naca ayam vidyamānam sat kiñcid anujānāti pratyakṣa nimittam pratyakṣa viṣayaḥ pratyakṣa jñānam sarvam na upapadyate pratyakṣa anupapattau tad pūrvaka tvāt anumāna āgamayoḥ anupapattiḥ sarva pramāṇa vilope sarva grahaṇam na bhavati iti 
[0524,i]	ubhayathā ca vartamānaḥ kālaḥ gṛhyate kvacid artha sadbhāva vyaṅgyaḥ yathā asti dravyam iti kvacid kriyā santāna vyaṅgyaḥ yathā pacati chinatti iti nānāvidhā ca eka arthā kriyā kriyā santānaḥ kriyā abhyāsaḥ ca nānāvidhā ca eka arthā kriyā pacati iti sthālī adhiśrayaṇam udaka āsecanam taṇḍulā vapanam edhaḥ apasarpaṇam agni abhijvālanam darvī ghaṭṭanam maṇḍa srāvaṇam adhas avatāraṇam iti 
[0524,ii_0525,iii]	chinatti iti kriyā abhyāsaḥ udyamya udyamya paraśum dāruṇi nipātayan chinatti iti ucyate yat ca idam pacyamānam chidyamānam ca tat kriyamāṇam tasmin kriyamāṇe kṛta tā kartavya tā upapatteḥ tu ubhayathā grahaṇam kriyā santānaḥ anārabdhaḥ cikīrṣitaḥ anāgataḥ kālaḥ pakṣyati iti prayojana avasānaḥ kriyā santāna uparamaḥ atītaḥ kālaḥ apākṣīt iti 
[0526,i]	ārabdha kriyā santānaḥ vartamānaḥ kālaḥ pacati iti tatra yā uparatā sā kṛta tā yā cikīrṣitā sā kartavyatā yā vidyamānā sā kriyamāṇa tā tat evam kriyā santāna sthaḥ traikālya samāhāraḥ pacati pacyate iti vartamāna grahaṇena gṛhyate kriyā santānasya hi atra avicchedaḥ abhidhīyate na ārambhaḥ na uparamaḥ iti saḥ ayam ubhayathā vartamānaḥ gṛhyate apavṛktaḥ vyapavṛktaḥ ca atīta anāgatābhyām sthiti vyaṅgyaḥ vidyate dravyam iti kriyā santānā viccheda abhidhāyī ca traikālya anvitaḥ pacati chinatti iti anyaḥ ca pratyāsatti prabhṛteḥ arthasya vivakṣāyām tad abhidhāyī bahu prakāraḥ lokeṣu utprekṣitavyaḥ tasmāt asti vartamānaḥ kālaḥ iti 
[0527,i_0528,i]	atyanta prāya eka deśa sādharmyāt upamāna siddhiḥ atyanta sādharmyāt upamānam na sidhyati na ca evam bhavati yathā gauḥ evam gauḥ iti prāyas sādharmyāt upamānam na sidhyati na hi bhavati yathā anaḍvān evam mahiṣaḥ iti eka deśa sādharmyāt upamānam na sidhyati na hi sarveṇa sarvam upamīyate iti 
[0528,ii_0529,i]	prasiddha sādharmyāt upamāna siddheḥ yathā ukta doṣa anupapattiḥ na sādharmyasya kṛtsna prāya alpa bhāvam āśritya upamānam pravartate kim tarhi prasiddha sādharmyāt sādhya sādhana bhāvam āśritya pravartate yatra ca etat asti na tatra upamānam pratiṣeddhum śakyam tasmāt yathā ukta doṣaḥ na upapadyate iti 
[0529,ii_0529,iv]	astu tarhi upamānam anumānam pratyakṣeṇa apratyakṣa siddheḥ yathā dhūmena pratyakṣeṇa apratyakṣasya vahneḥ grahaṇam anumānam evam gavā pratyakṣeṇa apratyakṣasya gavayasya grahaṇam iti na idam anumānāt viśiṣyate 
[0530,i_0530,iii]	viśiṣyate iti āha kayā yuktyā na apratyakṣe gavaye pramāṇa artham upamānasya paśyāmaḥ yadā hi ayam upayukta upamānaḥ godarśī gavaya samānam artham paśyati tadā ayam gavayaḥ iti asya saṃjñā śabdasya vyavasthām pratipadyate na ca evam anumānam iti para artham ca upamānam yasya hi upamānam aprasiddham tad artham prasiddha ubhayena kriyate iti para artham upamānam iti ced na svayam adhyavasāyāt bhavati ca bhoḥ svayam adhyavasāyaḥ yathā gauḥ evam gavayaḥ iti na adhyavasāyaḥ pratiṣidhyate upamānam tu tat na bhavati prasiddha sādharmyāt sādhya sādhanam upamānam na ca yasya ubhayam prasiddham tam prati sādhya sādhana bhāvaḥ vidyate iti 
[0530,iv_0530,vi]	atha api tathā iti upasaṃhārāt upamāna siddheḥ na aviśeṣaḥ tathā iti samāna dharma upasaṃhārāt upamānam sidhyati na anumānam ayam ca anayoḥ viśeṣaḥ iti 
[0534,i_0534,ii]	śabdaḥ anumānam arthasya anupalabdheḥ anumeya tvāt śabdaḥ anumānam na pramāṇa antaram kasmāt śabda arthasya anumeya tvāt katham anumeya tvam pratyakṣataḥ anupalabdheḥ yathā anupalabhyamānaḥ liṅgī mitena liṅgena paścāt mīyate iti anumānam evam mitena śabdena paścāt mīyate arthaḥ anupalabhyamānaḥ iti anumānam śabdaḥ 
[0534,iii_0534,v]	itas ca anumānam śabdaḥ upalabdheḥ at vipravṛtti tvāt pramāṇa antara bhāve dvi pravṛttiḥ upalabdhiḥ anyathā hi upalabdhiḥ anumāne anyathā upamāne tat vyākhyātam śabda anumānayoḥ tu upalabdhiḥ at vipravṛttiḥ yathā anumāne tathā śabde api viśeṣa abhāvāt anumānam śabdaḥ iti 
[0535,i_0535,ii]	sambandhāt ca śabdaḥ anumānam iti vartate sambaddhayoḥ ca śabda arthayoḥ sambandha prasiddhau śabda upalabdheḥ artha grahaṇam yathā sambaddhayoḥ liṅga liṅinoḥ sambandha pratītau liṅga upalabdhau liṅgi grahaṇam iti 
[0536,i_0538,i]	yat tāvat arthasya anumeya tvāt iti tat na āpta upadeśa sāmarthyāt śabdāt artha sampratyayaḥ svargaḥ apsarasaḥ uttarāḥ kuravaḥ sapta dvīpāḥ samudraḥ loka sanniveśaḥ iti evamādeḥ apratyakṣasya arthasya ca śabda mātrāt pratyayaḥ kim tarhi āptaiḥ ayam uktāḥ śabdaḥ iti atas sampratyayaḥ viparyayeṇa sampratyaya abhāvāt na tu evam anumānam iti yat punar upalabdheḥ at vipravṛtti tvāt iti ayam eva śabda anumānayoḥ upalabdheḥ pravṛtti bhedaḥ tatra viśeṣe sati ahetuḥ viśeṣa abhāvāt iti 
[0539,i]	yat punar idam sambandhāt ca iti asti ca śabda arthayoḥ sambandhaḥ anujñātaḥ asti ca pratiṣiddhaḥ asya idam iti ṣaṣṭhī viśiṣṭasya vākyasya artha viśeṣaḥ anujñātaḥ prāpti lakṣaṇaḥ tu śabda arthayoḥ sambandhaḥ pratiṣiddhaḥ kasmāt pramāṇataḥ anupalabdheḥ pratyakṣataḥ tāvat śabda artha prāpteḥ na upalabdhiḥ atīndriya tvāt yena indriyeṇa gṛhyate śabdaḥ tasya viṣaya bhāvam ativṛttaḥ arthaḥ na gṛhyate asti ca ati indriya viṣaya bhūtaḥ api arthaḥ samānena ca indriyeṇa gṛhyamāṇayoḥ prāptiḥ gṛhyate iti 
[0540,i_0541,i]	pūraṇa pradāha pāṭana anupalabdheḥ ca sambandha abhāvaḥ prāpti lakṣaṇe ca gṛhyamāṇe sambandhe śabda arthayoḥ śabda antike vā arthaḥ syāt artha antike vā śabdaḥ syāt ubhayam vā ubhayatra atha khalu ubhayam sthāna karaṇa abhāvāt iti ca arthaḥ na ca ayam anumānataḥ api upalabhyate śabda antike arthaḥ iti etasmin pakṣe api āsya sthāna karaṇa uccāraṇīyaḥ śabdaḥ tad antike arthaḥ iti anna agni asi śabda uccāraṇe pūraṇa pāha pāṭanāni gṛhyeran na ca gṛhyante agrahaṇāt na anumeyaḥ prāpti lakṣaṇaḥ sambandhaḥ artha antike śabdaḥ iti sthāna karaṇa asambhavāt anuccāraṇam sthānam kaṇṭha ādayaḥ karaṇam prayatna viśeṣaḥ tasya artha antike anupapattiḥ iti ubhaya pratiṣedhāt ca na ubhayam tasmāt na śabdena arthaḥ prāptaḥ iti 
[0542,i_0542,ii]	śabda artha vyavasthānāt apratiṣedhaḥ śabdāt artha pratyayasya vyavasthā darśanāt anumīyata asti śabda artha sambandhaḥ vyavasthā kāraṇam asambandhe hi śabda mātrāt artha mātre pratyaya prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt apratiṣedhaḥ sambandhasya iti 
[0543,i_0544,i]	atra samādhiḥ na sāmāyika tvāt śabda artha sampratyayasya na sambandha kāritam śabda artha vyavasthānam kim tarhi samaya kāritam yat tat avocāma asya idam iti ṣaṣṭhī viśiṣṭasya vākyasya artha viśeṣaḥ anujñātaḥ śabda arthayoḥ sambandhaḥ iti samayam tam avocāmaḥ iti kaḥ punar ayam samayaḥ asya śabdasya idam artha jātam abhidheyam iti abhidhāna abhidheya niyama niyogaḥ tasmin upayukte śabdāt artha sampratyayaḥ bhavati viparyaye hi śabda śravaṇa api pratyaya abhāvaḥ sambandha vādinaḥ api ca ayam avarjanīya iti prayujyamāna grahaṇāt ca samaya upayogaḥ laukikānām samaya paripālana artham ca idam pada lakṣaṇāyāḥ vācā anvākhyānam vyākaraṇam vākya lakṣaṇāyāḥ vācaḥ artha lakṣaṇam pada samūhaḥ vākyam artha parisamā prau iti tat evam prāpti lakṣaṇasya śabda artha sambandhasya artha tuṣaḥ api anumāna hetuḥ na bhavati iti 
[0546,i_0546,ii]	jāti viśeṣe ca aniyamāt sāmāyikaḥ śabdāt artha sampratyayaḥ na svābhāvikaḥ ṛṣi āri amlecchānām yathākāmam śabda viniyogaḥ artha pratyāyanāya pravartate svābhāvike hi śabdasya artha pratyāyaka tve yathākāmam na syāt yathā taijasasya prakāśasya rūpa pratyaya hetu tvam na jāti viśeṣe vyabhicarati iti 
[0547,i_0547,iii]	putra kāma iṣṭi havana abhyāseṣu tad aprāmāṇyam anṛta vyāghāta punarukta doṣebhyaḥ tasya iti śabda viśeṣam eva adhikurute bhagavān ṛṣiḥ śabdasya pramāṇa tvam na sambhavati kasmāt anṛta doṣāt putra kameṣṭau putra kāmaḥ putra iṣṭyā yajeta iti na iṣṭau saṃsthitāyām putra janma dṛśyate dṛṣṭa arthasya vākyasya anṛta tvāt adṛṣṭa artham api vākyam agnihotram juhuyāt svarga kāmaḥ ityādi anṛtam iti jñāyate 
[0548,i_0549,i]	vihita vyāghāta doṣāt ca havane udite hotavyam anudite hotavyam samaya adhyuṣite hotavyam iti vidhāya vihitam vyāhanti śyāvaḥ asya āhutim abhyavaharati yaḥ udite juhoti śabalaḥ asya āhutim abhyavaharati yaḥ anudite juhoti śyāva śabalau vā asya āhutim abhyavaharataḥ yaḥ samaya adhyuṣite juhoti vyāghātāt ca anyatarat mithyā iti punarukta doṣāt ca abhyāse deśyamāne tris prathamām anvāha tris uttamām iti punarukta doṣaḥ bhavati punaruktam ca pramatta vākyam iti tasmāt apramāṇam śabdaḥ anṛta vyāghāta punarukta doṣebhyaḥ iti 
[0550,i_0550,ii]	na karma kartṛ sādhana vaiguṇyāt na anṛta doṣaḥ putra kāma iṣṭau kasmāt karma kartṛ sādhana vaiguṇyāt iṣṭyā pitarau saṃyujyamānau putram janayate iti iṣṭeḥ karaṇam sādhanam pitarau kartārau saṃyogaḥ karma trayāṇām guṇa yogāt putra janma vaiguṇyāt viparyayaḥ iṣṭi āśrayam tāvat karma vaiguṇyam samīha abhreṣaḥ kartṛ vaiguṇyam avidvān prayoktā kapūya ācaraṇaḥ ca 
[0551,i]	sādhana vaiguṇyam haviḥ asaṃkṛtam upahatam iti mantrāḥ nyūna adhikāḥ svara varṇa hīnāḥ iti dakṣiṇā durāgatā hīnā ninditā ca iti atha upajana āśrayam karma vaiguṇyam mithyā samprayogaḥ kartṛ vaiguṇyam yoni vyāpadaḥ bīja upaghātaḥ ca iti sādhana vaiguṇyam iṣṭau abhihitam loke ca agni kāmaḥ dāruṇī mathnīyāt iti vidhi vākyam tatra karma vaiguṇyam mithyā abhimanthanam kartṛ vaiguṇyam prajñā prayatnataḥ pramādaḥ sādhana vaiguṇyam ārdram suṣiram dā iti tatra phalam na niṣpadyate iti na anṛta doṣaḥ guṇa yogena phala niṣpatti darśanāt na ca idam laukikāt bhidyate putra kāmaḥ putra iṣṭyā yajeta iti 
[0553,i_0553,ii]	abhyupetya kāla bhede doṣa vacanāt na vyāghātaḥ havanaḥ iti anuvartate yaḥ abhyupagatam havana kālam bhinatti tatas anyatra juhoti tatra ayam abhyupagata kāla bhede doṣaḥ ucyate śyāvaḥ asya āhutim abhyavaharati yaḥ udite juhoti tat idam vidhi bhreṣe nindā vacanam iti 
[0554,i_0555,i]	anuvāda upapatteḥ ca punarukta doṣaḥ abhyāse na iti prakṛtam anarthakaḥ abhyāsaḥ punar uktam arthavān abhyāsaḥ anuvādaḥ yaḥ ayam abhyāsaḥ tris prathamām anvāha tris uttamām iti anuvādaḥ upapadyate arthavat tvāt tris vacanena hi prathama uttamayoḥ pañcadaśa tvam sāmidhenīnām bhavati tathā ca mantra abhivādaḥ idam aham bhrātṛvyam pañcadaśa avareṇa vāc vajreṇa avabodhe yaḥ asmān dveṣṭi yam ca vayam dviṣmaḥ iti pañcadaśa sāmidhenīḥ vajramantraḥ abhivadati tat abhyāsam antareṇa na syāt iti 
[0556,i_0556,ii]	vākya vibhāgasya ca artha grahaṇāt pramāṇam śabdaḥ yathā loke 
[0556,iii_0556,v]	vibhāgaḥ ca brāhmaṇa vākyānām trividhaḥ vidhi artha vāda anuvāda vacana viniyogāt tridhā khalu brāhmaṇa vākyāni viniyuktāni vidhivacanāni arthavāda vacanāni anuvāda vacanāni iti 
[0557,i_0557,iii]	tatra vidhiḥ vidhāyakaḥ yat vākyam vidhāyakam ca udakam sa vidhiḥ vidhiḥ tu niyogaḥ anujñā vā yathā agnihotram juhuyāt svarga kāmaḥ ityādi 
[0559,i_0559,ii]	stutiḥ nindā para kṛtiḥ purākalpaḥ iti artha vādaḥ vidheḥ phala vāda lakṣaṇā yā praśaṃsā sā stutiḥ sampratyaya arthā stūyamānam śraddadhīta iti pravartikā ca phala śravaṇāt pravartate sarva jitāḥ vai devāḥ sarvam ajayan sarvasya āptyai sarvasya jityai sarvam eva etena āptena āpnoti sarvam jayati iti evamādi aniṣṭa phala vādaḥ nindā varjana arthāḥ ninditam na samācaret iti 
[0560,i_0560,iv]	saḥ eṣa vāva prathamaḥ yajñaḥ yajñānām yat jotiṣṭomaḥ yaḥ etena ādiṣṭvā anyana yajate garttapatyam eva tat jīyate vā pramīyate vā iti evamādiḥ anya kartṛkasya vyāhatasya vidheḥ vādaḥ para kṛtiḥ hutvā vapām eva agre abhighārayanti atha pṛṣat ājyam tat uha caraka adhvaryavaḥ pṛṣadājyam eva agre abhidhārayanti agneḥ prāṇāḥ pṛṣadājya stomam iti evam abhidadhati iti evamādi aitihya samācaritaḥ vidhiḥ purākalpaḥ iti tasmāt vai etena brāhmaṇāḥ bahis pavamānam sāmastomama stoṣan yone yajñam pratanavāmahe iti evamādi katham purā ākṛti purā kalpau artha vādau iti stuti nindā vākyena abhisambandhāt vidhi āśrayasya kasyacid arthasya dyotanāt artha vādaḥ iti 
[0561,i_0562,i]	vidhi vihitasya anuvacanam anuvādaḥ vidhi anuvacanam ca anuvādaḥ vihita anuvacanam ca pūrvaḥ śabda anuvādaḥ aparaḥ artha anuvādaḥ yathā punar uktam dvividham evam anuvādaḥ api kimartham punar vihitam anūdyate adhikāra artham vihitam adhikṛtya stutiḥ bodhyate nindā vā vidhi śeṣaḥ vā abhidhīyate vihita anantara arthaḥ api ca anuvādā bhavati evam anyat api utprekṣaṇīyam 
[0562,ii_0562,iii]	loke api ca vidhiḥ artha vādaḥ anuvādaḥ iti ca trividham vākyam odanam pacet iti vidhi vākyam arthavāda vākyam āyuḥ varcaḥ balam sukham pratibhānam ca anne pratiṣṭhitam anuvādaḥ pacatu pacatu bhavān iti abhyāsaḥ kṣipram pacyatām iti vā aṅga pacyatām iti adhyeṣaṇa artham pacyatām eva iti ca avadhāraṇa artham yathā laukike vākye vibhāgena artha grahaṇāt pramāṇa tvam evam veda vākyānām api vibhāgena artha grahaṇāt pramāṇa tvam bhavitum arhati iti 
[0563,i_0563,ii]	na anuvāda punaruktayoḥ viśeṣaḥ śabda abhyāsa upapatteḥ punaruktam asādhu sādhuḥ anuvādaḥ iti ayam viśeṣaḥ na upapadyate kasmāt ubhayatra hi pratīta arthaḥ śabdaḥ abhyasyate caritārthasya śabdasya abhyāsāt ubhayam asādhu iti 
[0563,iii_0564,i]	śīghratara gamana upadeśa vat abhyāsāt na aviśeṣaḥ na anuvāda punaruktayoḥ aviśeṣaḥ kasmāt arthavataḥ abhyāsasya anuvāda bhāvāt arthavān abhyāsaḥ anuvādaḥ śīghratara gamana upadeśa vat śīghram śīghram gamyatām iti kriyā atiśayaḥ abhyāsena eva ucyate udāharaṇa artham ca idam evam anyaḥ api abhyāsaḥ pacati pacati iti kriyā anuparamaḥ grāmaḥ grāmaḥ ramanīyaḥ iti vyāptiḥ pari pari trigartebhyaḥ vṛṣṭaḥ devaḥ iti parivarjanam adhi adhi kuḍyam niṣaṇṇam iti sāmīpyam tiktam tiktam iti prakāraḥ evam anuvādasya stuti nindā śeṣa vidhiṣu adhikāra artha tā vihita anantara artha tā ca iti 
[0564,ii_0565,ii]	kim punar pratiṣedha hetu uddhārāt eva śabdasya pramāṇa tvam sidhyati na atas ca mantra āyurveda prāmāṇya vat ca tad prāmāṇyam āpta prāmāṇyāt kim punar āyurvedasya prāmāṇyam yat tat āyurvedena upadiśyate idam kṛtvā iṣṭam adhigacchati idam varjayitvā aniṣṭam jahāti tasya anuṣṭhīyamānasya tathā abhāvaḥ satya artha tā viparyayaḥ mantra padānām ca viṣaya bhūta aśani pratiṣedha arthānām prayoge arthasya tathā abhāvaḥ etat prāmāṇyam kiṃkṛtam etat āpta prāmāṇya kṛtam kim punar āptānām prāmāṇyam sākṣātkṛta dharmatā bhūta dayā yathābhūta artha cikhyā payiṣā iti 
[0566,i]	āptāḥ khalu sākṣātkṛta dharmāṇaḥ idam hātavyam idam asya hāni hetuḥ idam asya adhigantavyam idam asya adhigama hetuḥ iti bhūtāni anukampante teṣām khalu vai prāṇabhṛtām svayam anavabudhyamānānām na anyat upadeśāt avabodha kāraṇam asti na ca anavabodhe samīhā varjanam vā na vā akṛtvā svastibhāvaḥ na api asya anyaḥ upakārakaḥ api asti hanta vayam ebhyaḥ yathādarśanam yathābhūtam upadiśyāmaḥ te ime śrutvā pratipadyamānāḥ heyam hāsyanti adhigantavyam eva adhigamiṣyanti iti evam āpta upadeśaḥ etena trividhena āpta prāmāṇyena parigṛhītaḥ anuṣṭhīyamānaḥ arthasya sādhakaḥ bhavati evam āpta upadeśaḥ pramāṇam evam āptāḥ pramāṇam 
[0566,ii_0566,iii]	dṛṣṭa arthena āpta upadeśena āyurvedena adṛṣṭa arthaḥ veda bhāgaḥ anumātavyaḥ pramāṇam iti āpta prāmāṇyasya hetoḥ samāna tvāt iti asya api ca eka deśaḥ grāma kāmaḥ yajeta iti evamādiḥ dṛṣṭa arthaḥ tena anumātavyam iti loke ca bhūyān upadeśa āśrayaḥ vyavahāraḥ laukikasya api upadeṣṭuḥ upadeṣṭavya artha jñānena para anujighṛkṣayā yathābhūta artha cikhyā apayiṣayā ca prāmāṇyam tad parigrahāt āpta upadeśaḥ pramāṇam iti 
[0566,iv_0566,v]	draṣṭṛ pravaktṛ sāmānyāt ca anumānam yaḥ eva āptāḥ veda arthānām draṣṭāraḥ pravaktāraḥ ca te eva āyurveda prabhṛtīnām iti āyurveda prāmāṇya vat veda prāmāṇyam anumātavyam iti nitya tvāt veda vākyānām pramāṇa tve tad prāmāṇyam āpta prāmāṇyāt iti ayuktam śabdasya vācaka tvāt artha pratipattau pramāṇa tvam na nitya tvāt nitya tve hi sarvasya sarveṇa vacanāt śabda artha vyavasthā anupapattiḥ na anitya tve vācaka tvam iti ced na laukikeṣu adarśanāt te api nityāḥ iti ced na anāpta upadeśāt artha visaṃvādaḥ anupapannaḥ nitya tvāt dhi śabdaḥ pramāṇam iti 
[0569,i]	anityaḥ saḥ iti ced aviśeṣa vacanam anāpta upadeśaḥ laukikaḥ na nityaḥ iti kāraṇam vācyam iti yathāyogam ca arthasya pratyāyanāt nāmadheya śabdānām loke prāmāṇyam nitya tvāt prāmāṇya anupapattiḥ yatra arthe nāmadheya śabdaḥ niyujyate loke tasya niyoga sāmarthyāt pratyāyakaḥ bhavati na nitya tvāt manvantara yugāntantareṣu ca atīta anāgateṣu sampradāya abhyāsa prayoga avicchedaḥ vedānām nitya tvam āpta prāmāṇyāt ca prāmāṇyam laukikeṣu śabdeṣu ca etat samānam iti 
[0572,i_0572,iii]	ayathārthaḥ pramāṇa uddeśaḥ iti matvā āha na catuṣṭvam aitihya arthāpatti sambhava abhāva prāmāṇyāt na catvāri eva pramāṇāni kim tarhi aitihyam arthāpattiḥ sambhavaḥ abhāvaḥ iti etāni api pramāṇāni tāni kasmāt na uktāni itiha ūcuḥ iti anirdiṣṭa pravaktṛkam pravāda pāramparyam aitihyam arthāt āpattiḥ arthāpattiḥ āpattiḥ prāptiḥ prasaṅgaḥ yatra abhidhīyamāne arthe yaḥ anyaḥ arthaḥ prasajyate saḥ arthāpattiḥ yathā megheṣu asatsu vṛṣṭiḥ na bhavati iti 
[0574,i]	kim atra prasajyate satsu bhavati iti sambhavaḥ nāma avinābhāvinaḥ arthasya sattā grahaṇāt anyasya sattā grahaṇam yathā droṇasya sattā grahaṇāt āḍhakasya sattā grahaṇam āḍakasya sattā grahaṇāt prasthasya iti abhāvaḥ virodhi abhūtam bhūtasya avidyamānam varṣa karma vidyamānasya vāyu abhra saṃyogasya pratipādakam vidhārake hi vāyu abhra saṃyoge guru tvāt apām patana karma na bhavati iti 
[0575,i_0575,iii]	satyam etāni pramāṇāni na tu pramāṇa antarāṇi pramāṇa antaram ca manyamānena pratiṣedhaḥ ucyate saḥ ayam śabdaḥ aitihya anartha antara bhāvāt anumāne arthāpatti sambhava abhāva anartha antara bhāvāt ca apratiṣedhaḥ anupapannaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ katham āpta upadeśaḥ śabdaḥ iti na ca śabda lakṣaṇam aitihyāt vyāvartate saḥ ayam bhedaḥ sāmānyāt saṃgṛhyate iti pratyakṣeṇa apratyakṣasya sambaddhasya pratipattiḥ anumānam 
[0576,i]	tathā ca arthāpatti sambhava abhāvaḥ vākya artha sampratyayena anabhihitasya arthasya pratyanīka bhāvāt grahaṇam arthāpattiḥ anumānam eva avinā abhāva vṛttyā ca sambaddhayoḥ samudāya samudāyinoḥ samudāyena itarasya grahaṇam sambhavaḥ tat api anumānam eva asmin sati idam na upapadyate iti virodhi tve prasiddhe kārya anupapattyā kāraṇasya pratibandhakam anumīyate saḥ ayam yathārthaḥ eva pramāṇa uddeśaḥ iti 
[0578,i_0578,iii]	satyam etāni pramāṇāni na tu pramāṇa antarāṇi iti uktam atra arthāpatteḥ pramāṇa bhāva abhyanujñā na upapadyate tathā hi iyam arthāpattiḥ apramāṇam anaikāntika tvāt asatsu megheṣu vṛṣṭiḥ na bhavati iti satsu bhavati iti etat arthāt āpadyate satsu api ca ekadā na bhavati sā iyam arthāpattiḥ apramāṇam iti 
[0579,i_0579,iii]	na anaikāntika tvam arthāpatteḥ anartha āpattau arthāpatti abhimānāt asati kāraṇe kāryam na utpadyate iti vākyāt pratyanīka bhūtaḥ arthaḥ sati kāraṇe kāryam utpadyate iti arthāt āpadyate abhāvasya hi bhāvaḥ pratyanīkaḥ iti saḥ ayam kārya utpādaḥ sati kāraṇe arthāt āpadyamānaḥ na kāraṇasya sattām vyabhicarati na khalu asati kāraṇe kāryam utpadyate tasmāt na anā ekāntikī 
[0579,iv]	yat tu sati kāraṇe nimitta pratibandāt kāryam na utpadyate iti kāraṇa dharmaḥ asau na tu arthāpatteḥ prameyam kim tarhi asyāḥ prameyam sati kāraṇe kāryam utpadyate iti yaḥ asau kārya utpādaḥ kāraṇasya sattām na vyabhicatati tat asyāḥ prameyam evam tu sati anartha āpattau arthāpatti abhimānam kṛtvā pratiṣedhaḥ ucyate iti 
[0580,i_0580,ii]	pratiṣedha aprāmāṇyam ca anaikāntika tvāt arthāpattiḥ na pramāṇam anaikāntika tvāt iti vākyam pratiṣedhaḥ tena anena arthāpatteḥ pramāṇa tvam pratiṣidhyate na sadbhāvaḥ evam anaikāntikaḥ bhavati anaikāntika tvāt apramāṇena anena na kaścid arthaḥ pratiṣidhyate iti 
[0581,i_0581,iii]	atha manyase niyata viṣayeṣu artheṣu sva viṣaye vyabhicāraḥ bhavati na ca pratiṣedhasya sadbhāvaḥ viṣayaḥ evam tarhi tad prāmāṇye vā na arthāpatti aprāmāṇyam arthāpatteḥ api kārya utpādena kāraṇa sattāyāḥ avyabhicāraḥ viṣayaḥ na ca kāraṇa dharmaḥ nimitta pratibandhāt kārya anutpādaka tvam iti 
[0582,i_0582,iii]	abhāvasya tarhi pramāṇa bhāva abhyanujñā na upapadyate katham iti na abhāva prāmāṇyam prameya asiddheḥ abhāvasya bhūyasi prameye loka siddhe vaiyātyāt ucyate na abhāva prāmāṇyam prameya asiddheḥ iti 
[0583,i_0584,i]	atha ayam artha bahu tvāt artha eka deśaḥ udāhriyate lakṣiteṣu alakṣaṇa lakṣita tvāt alakṣitānām tat prameya siddheḥ tasya abhāvasya sidhyati prameyam katham lakṣiteṣu vāsaḥsu anupādeyeṣu upādeyānām alakṣitānām alakṣaṇa lakṣita tvāt lakṣaṇa abhāvena lakṣita tvāt iti ubhaya sannidhau alakṣitāni vāsāṃsi ānaya iti prayuktaḥ yeṣu vāsaḥsu lakṣaṇāni na bhavanti tāni lakṣaṇa abhāvena pratipadyate pratipadya ca ānayati pratipatti hetuḥ ca pramāṇam iti 
[0584,ii_0585,i]	asati arthe na abhāvaḥ iti ced na anya lakṣaṇa upapatteḥ yatra bhūtvā kiñcid na bhavati tatra tasya abhāvaḥ upapadyate na ca ālakṣiteṣu vāsaḥsu lakṣitāni bhūtvā na bhavanti tasmāt teṣu lakṣaṇa abhāvaḥ anupapannaḥ iti na anya lakṣaṇa upapatteḥ yathā ayam anyeṣu vāsaḥsu lakṣaṇānām upapattim paśyati na evam alakṣiteṣu saḥ ayam lakṣaṇa abhāvam paśyan abhāvena artham pratipadyate iti 
[0586,i_0586,ii]	tad siddheḥ alakṣiteṣu ahetuḥ teṣu vāsaḥsu lakṣiteṣu siddhiḥ vidhyamāna tā yeṣām bhavati na teṣām abhāvaḥ lakṣaṇānām yāni ca lakṣiteṣu vidyante lakṣaṇāni teṣām alakṣiteṣu abhāvaḥ iti ahetuḥ yāni khalu bhavanti teṣām abhāvaḥ vyāhate iti 
[0586,iii_0586,iv]	na lakṣaṇa avasthita apekṣa siddheḥ na brūmaḥ yāni lakṣaṇāni bhavanti teṣām abhāvaḥ iti kin tu keṣucid lakṣaṇāni avasthitāni anavasthitāni keṣucid apekṣamāṇaḥ yeṣu lakṣaṇānām bhāvam na paśyati tāni lakṣaṇa abhāvena pratipadyate iti 
[0587,i_0587,ii]	prāk utpatteḥ abhāva upapatteḥ ca abhāva dvaitam khalu bhavati prāk ca utpatteḥ avidyamāna tā utpannasya ca ātmanaḥ hānāt avidyamāna tā tatra ālakṣiteṣu vāsaḥsu prāk utpatteḥ avidyamāna tā lakṣaṇaḥ lakṣaṇānām abhāvaḥ na itaraḥ iti 
[0588,i_0589,i]	āpta upadeśaḥ śabdaḥ iti pramāṇa bhāve viśeṣaṇam bruvatā nānā prakāraḥ śabdaḥ iti jñāpyate tasmin sāmanyena vicāraḥ kim nityaḥ atha anityaḥ iti vimarśa hetu anuyoge ca vipratipatteḥ saṃśayaḥ ākāśa guṇaḥ śabdaḥ vibhuḥ nityaḥ abhivyakti dharmakaḥ iti eke gandha ādi saha vṛttiḥ dravyeṣu sanniviṣṭaḥ gandha ādi vat avasthitaḥ abhivyakti dharmakaḥ iti apare 
[0589,ii_0594,iii]	ākāśa guṇaḥ śabdaḥ utpatti nirodha dharmakaḥ buddhi vat iti apare mahābhūta saṃkṣobha jaḥ śabdaḥ anāśritaḥ utpatti dharmakaḥ nirodha dharmakaḥ iti anye atas saṃśayaḥ kim atra tattvam iti anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti uttaram katham ādhimat tvāt aindriyaka tvāt kṛtaka vat upacārāt ca ādiḥ yoniḥ kāraṇam ādīyate asmāt iti kāraṇa vat anityam dṛṣṭam saṃyoga vibhāga jaḥ ca śabdaḥ kāraṇavat tvāt anityaḥ iti kā punar iyam artha deśanā kāraṇavat tvāt iti utpatti dharmaka tvāt anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti bhūtvā na bhavati vināśa dharmakaḥ iti 
[0594,iv_0594,v]	sāṃśayikam etat kim utpatti kāraṇam saṃyoga vibhāgau śabdasya āhosvit abhivyakti kāraṇam iti atas āha aindriyaka tvāt indriya pratyāsattigrāhya aindriyakaḥ kim ayam vyañjakena samāna deśaḥ abhivyajyate rūpa ādi vat atha saṃyoga jāt śabdāt śabda santāne sati śrotra pratyāsannaḥ gṛhyate iti saṃyoga nivṛttau śabda grahaṇāt na vyañjakena samāna deśasya grahaṇam dāru vraścane dāruparaśu saṃyoga nivṛttau dūra sthena śabdaḥ gṛhyate na ca vyañjaka abhāve vyaṅgya grahaṇam bhavati tasmāt na vyañjakaḥ saṃyogaḥ utpādake tu saṃyoge saṃyoga jāt śabdāt śabda santāne sati śrotra pratyāsannasya grahaṇam iti yuktam saṃyoga nivṛttau śabdasya grahaṇam iti 
[0600,i_0603,i]	itas ca śabdaḥ utpadyate na abhivyajyate kṛtaka vat upacārāt tīvram mandam iti kṛtakam upacaryate tīvram sukham mandam sukham tīvram duḥkham mandam duḥkham iti upacaryate ca tīvraḥ śabdaḥ mandaḥ śabdaḥ iti vyañjakasya tathā abhāvāt grahaṇasya tīvra manda tā rūpavat iti ced na abhibhava upapatteḥ saṃyogasya vyañjakasya tīvra manda tayā śabda grahaṇasya tīvra manda tā bhavati na tu śabdaḥ bhidyate yathā prakāśasya tīvra manda tayā rūpa grahaṇasya iti tat ca na evam abhibhava upapatteḥ tīvraḥ bherī śabdaḥ mandam tantrī śabdam abhibhavati na mandaḥ na ca śabda grahaṇam abhibhāvakam śabdaḥ ca na bhidyate śabde tu bhidyamāne yuktaḥ abhibhavaḥ tasmāt utpadyate śabdaḥ na abhivyajyate iti 
[0604,i_0606,i]	abhibhava anupapattiḥ ca vyañjaka samāna deśasya abhivyaktau prāpti abhāvāt vyañjakena samāna deśe abhivyajyate śabdaḥ iti etasmin pakṣe na upapadyate abhibhavaḥ na hi bherī śabdena tantrī svanaḥ prāptaḥ iti aprāpte abhibhavaḥ iti ced śabda mātra abhibhava prasaṅgaḥ atha manyeta asatyām prāptau abhibhavaḥ bhavati iti evam sati yathā bherī śabdaḥ kañcid tantrī svanam abhibhavati evam antika stha upādānam iva davīyaḥ sthaḥ pādānān api tantrī svanān abhibhavet aprāpteḥ aviśeṣāt tatra kvacid eva bheryām praṇāditāyām sarva lokeṣu samāna kālāḥ tantrī svanāḥ na śrūyeran iti nānā bhūteṣu śabda santāneṣu satsu śrotra pratyāsatti bhāvena kasyacid śabdasya tīvreṇa mandasya abhibhavaḥ yuktaḥ iti kaḥ punar ayam abhibhavaḥ nāma grāhya samāna jātīya grahaṇa kṛtam agrahaṇam abhibhavaḥ yathā ulkā prakāśasya grahaṇa arhasya āditya prakāśena iti 
[0607,i_0607,ii]	na ghaṭa abhāva sāmānya nitya tvāt nityeṣu api anitya vat upacārāt ca na khalu ādimattvāt anityaḥ śabdaḥ kasmāt vyabhicārāt ādimataḥ khalu ghaṭa abhāvasya dṛṣṭam nitya tvam katham ādimān kāraṇa vibhāgebhyaḥ hi ghaṭaḥ na bhavati katham asya nitya tvam yaḥ asau kāraṇa vibhāgebhyaḥ na bhavati na tasya abhāvaḥ bhāvena kadācid nivartyate iti yat api aindriyaka tvāt tat api vyabhicarati aindriyakam ca sāmānyam nityam ca iti yat api kṛtaka vat upacārāt iti etat api vyabhicarati nityeṣu anitya vat upacāraḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tathā hi bhavati vṛkṣasya pradeśaḥ kambalasya pradeśaḥ evam ākāśasya pradeśaḥ ātmanaḥ pradeśaḥ iti bhavati iti 
[0608,i_0608,ii]	tattva bhāktayoḥ nānātvasya vibhāgāt avyabhicāraḥ nityam iti atra kim tāvat tattvam artha antarasya anutpatti dharmakasya ātma hāna anupapattiḥ nitya tvam tat ca abhāve na upapadyate bhāktam tu bhavati yat tatra ātmānam ahāsīt yat bhūtvā na bhavati na jātu tat punar bhavati tatra nityaḥ iva nityaḥ ghaṭa abhāvaḥ iti ayam padārthaḥ iti tatra yathājātīyakaḥ śabdaḥ na tathājātīyakam kāryam kiṃcid nityam dṛśyate iti avyabhicāraḥ 
[0609,i_0609,iii]	yat api sāmānya nitya tvāt iti indriya pratyāsatti grāhyam aindriyakam iti santāna anumāna viśeṣaṇāt nityeṣu avyabhicāraḥ iti prakṛtam na indriya grahaṇa sāmarthyāt śabdasya anitya tvam kim tarhi indriya pratyāsatti grāhya tvāt santāna anumānam tena anitya tvam iti 
[0609,iv_0613,i]	yat api nityeṣu api anitya vat upacārāt iti na kāraṇa dravyasya pradeśa śabdena abhidhānāt nityeṣu api avyabhicāraḥ iti evam ākāśa pradeśaḥ ātma pradeśaḥ iti na atra ākāśa ātmanoḥ kāraṇa dravyam abhidhīyate yathā kṛtakasya katham hi avidyamānam abhidhīyate avidyamāna tā ca pramāṇataḥ anupalabdheḥ kim tarhi tatra abhidhīyate saṃyogasya avyāpya vṛtti tvam paricchinnena dravyena ākāśasya saṃyogaḥ na ākāśam vyāpnoti avyāpya vartate iti tat asi kṛtakena dravyeṇa sāmānyam na hi āmalakayoḥ saṃyogaḥ āśrayam vyāpnoti sāmānya kṛtā ca bhaktiḥ ākāśasya pradeśaḥ iti anena ātma pradeśaḥ vyākhyātaḥ saṃyoga vat ca śabda buddhi ādīnām avyāpya vṛtti tvam iti parīkṣitā ca tīvra manda tā śabda tattvam na bhakti kṛta iti kasmāt punar sūtrakārasya asmin arthe sūtram na śrūyate iti śīlam idam bhagavataḥ sūtrakārasya bahuṣu adhikaraṇeṣu dvau pakṣau na vyavasthāpayati tatra śāstra siddhāntāt tattva avadhāraṇam pratipattum arhati iti manyate śāstra siddhāntaḥ tu nyāya samākhyātam anumatam bahu śākham anumānam iti 
[0614,i_0614,iii]	atha api khalu idam asti idam na asti iti kutas etat pratipattavyam iti pramāṇataḥ upalabdheḥ anupalabdheḥ ca iti avidyamānaḥ tarhi śabdaḥ prāk uccāraṇāt anupalabdheḥ āvaraṇa ādi anupalabdheḥ ca prāk uccāraṇāt na asti śabdaḥ kasmāt anupalabdheḥ sataḥ nupalabdhiḥ āvaraṇa ādibhyaḥ etat na upapadyate kasmāt āvaraṇa ādīnām anupalabdhi kāraṇānām agrahaṇāt anena āvṛtaḥ śabdaḥ na upalabhyata asannikṛṣṭaḥ ca indriya vyavadhānāt iti evamādi anupalabdhi kāraṇam na gṛhyate iti saḥ ayam anuccāritaḥ na asti iti uccāraṇam asya vyañjakam tad abhāvāt prāk uccāraṇāt anupalabdhiḥ iti kim idam uccāraṇam nāma iti vivakṣā janitena prayatnena koṣṭhyasya vāyoḥ preritasya kaṇṭha tālu ādi pratighātaḥ yathāsthānam pratighātāt varṇa abhivyaktiḥ iti saṃyoga viśeṣaḥ vai pratighātaḥ pratiṣiddham ca saṃyogasya vyañjaka tvam tasmāt na vyañjaka abhāvāt agrahaṇam api tu abhāvāt eva iti saḥ ayam uccāryamāṇaḥ śrūyate śrūyamāṇaḥ ca abhūtvā bhavati iti anumīyate ūrdhvam ca uccāraṇāt na śrūyate sa bhūtvā na bhavati abhāvāt na śrūyate iti katham āvaraṇa ādi anupalabdheḥ iti uktam tasmāt utpatti tiraḥ bhāva dharmakaḥ śabdaḥ iti 
[0614,iv_0614,vi]	evam ca sati tattvam pāṃśubhiḥ iva avakiran idam āha tad anupalabdheḥ anupalambhāt āvaraṇa upapattiḥ yadi anupalambhāt āvaraṇam na asti āvaraṇa anupalabdhiḥ api tarhi anupalambhāt na asti iti tasyāḥ abhāvāt apratiṣiddham āvaraṇam iti katham punar jānīte bhavān na āvaraṇa anupalabdhiḥ upalabhyate iti 
[0616,i]	kim atra jñeyam pratyātma vedanīya tvāt samānam ayam khalu āvaraṇam anupalambhamānaḥ pratyātmam eva saṃvedayate na āvaraṇam upalabhaḥ iti yathā kuḍyena āvṛtasya āvaraṇam upalabhamānaḥ pratyātmam eva saṃvedayate sā iyam āvaraṇa upalabdhi vat āvaraṇa anupalabdhiḥ api saṃvedya eva iti evam ca sati apahṛta viṣayam uttara vākyam asti iti 
[0617,i_0617,iii]	abhyanujñā vādena tu ucyate jāti vādinā anupalambhāt api anupalabdhi sadbhāvāt na āvaraṇa anupapattiḥ anupalambhāt yathā anupalambhamānā api āvaraṇa anupalabdhiḥ asti evam anupalabhyamānam api āvaraṇam asti iti yadi abhyanujānāti bhavān anupalabhyamāna āvaraṇa anupalabdhiḥ asti iti abhyanujñāya ca vadati na asti āvaraṇam anupalambhāt iti etasmin api abhyanujñā vāde pratipatti niyamaḥ na upapadyate iti 
[0618,i_0619,i]	anupalambha ātmaka tvāt anupalabdheḥ ahetuḥ yat upalabhyate tat asti yat na upalabhyate tat na asti iti anupalambha ātmakam asat iti vyavasthitam upalabdhi abhāvaḥ ca anupalabdhiḥ iti sā iyam abhāva tvāt na upalabhyate sat ca khalu āvaraṇam tasya upalabdhyā bhavitavyam na ca upalabhyate tasmāt na asti iti tatra yat uktam na āvaraṇa anupapattiḥ anupalambhāt iti ayuktam iti 
[0619,ii_0620,ii]	atha śabdasya nitya tvam pratijānānaḥ kasmāt dhetoḥ pratijānīte asparśa tvāt asparśam ākāśam nityam dṛṣṭam iti tathā ca śabdaḥ iti 
[0620,iii_0620,vi]	saḥ ayam ubhayatas savyabhicāraḥ sparśavān ca aṇuḥ nityaḥ asparśam ca karma anityam dṛṣṭam asparśa tvāt iti etasya sādhya sādharmyeṇa udāharaṇam na karma anitya tvāt sādhya vaidharmyeṇa udāharaṇam 
[0620,vii_0620,viii]	na aṇu nitya tvāt ubhayasmin udāharaṇe vyabhicārāj na hetuḥ 
[0621,i_0621,iii]	ayam tarhi hetuḥ sampradānāt sampradīyamānam avasthitam dṛṣṭam sampradīyate ca śabdaḥ ācaryeṇa antevāsane tasmāt avasthitaḥ iti 
[0621,iv_0621,v]	tad antarāla anupalabdheḥ ahetuḥ yena sampradīyate yasmai ca tayoḥ antarāle avasthānam asya kena liṅgena upalabhyate sampradīyamānaḥ ahi avasthitaḥ sampradātuḥ apaiti sampradānam ca prāpnoti iti avarjanīyam etat 
[0622,i_0622,ii]	adhyāpanāt apratiṣedhaḥ adhyayanam liṅgam asati sampradāne adhyāpanam na syāt iti 
[0622,iii_0622,iv]	ubhayoḥ pakṣayoḥ anyatarasya adhyāpanāt apratiṣedhaḥ samānam adhyāpanam ubhayoḥ pakṣayoḥ saṃśaya anivṛtteḥ kim ācārya sthaḥ śabdaḥ antevāsinam āpadyate tat adhyāpanam āhosvit nṛtya upadeśa vat gṛhītasya anukaraṇam adhyāpanam iti evam adhyāpanam aliṅgam sampradānasya iti 
[0622,v_0622,vii]	ayam tarhi hetuḥ abhyāsāt abhyasyamānam avasthitam dṛṣṭam pañca kṛtvas paśyati iti rūpam avasthitam punar punar dṛśyate bhavati ca śabde abhyāsaḥ daśa kṛtvas adhītaḥ anuvākaḥ viṃśati kṛtvas adhītaḥ iti tasmāt avasthitasya punar punar uccāraṇam abhyāse iti 
[0624,i_0624,ii]	na anya tve api abhyāsasya upacārāt anavasthāne api abhyāsasya abhidhānam bhavati dvis nṛtyatu bhavān tris nṛtyatu bhavān iti dvis anṛtyat tris anṛtyat dvis agnihotram juhoti dvis bhuṅkte 
[0624,iii_0624,v]	evam vyabhicārāt pratiṣiddha hetau anya śabdasya prayogaḥ pratiṣidhyate anyat anyasmāt ananya tvāt ananyat iti anya tā bhāvaḥ yat idam anyat iti manyase tat sva arthena ananya tvāt anyat na bhavati evam anyatāyāḥ abhāvaḥ tatra yat uktam anya tve api abhyāsa upacārāt iti etat ayuktam iti 
[0625,i_0625,iii]	śabda prayogam pratiṣedhataḥ śabda antara prayogaḥ pratiṣidhyate tad abhāve na asti ananya tā tayoḥ itaretara apekṣa siddheḥ anyasmāt ananyatām upapādayati bhavān upapādya ca anyat pratyācaṣṭe ananyat iti ca śabdam anujānāti prayuṅkte ca ananyat iti etat samāsapadam anya śat baḥ ayam pratiṣedhena saha samasyate yadi ca atra uttaram padam na asti kasya ayam pratiṣedhena saha samāsaḥ tasmāt tayoḥ anya ananya śabdayoḥ itaraḥ ananya śabdaḥ itaram anya śabdam apekṣamāṇaḥ sidhyati iti tatra yat uktam anyatāyāḥ abhāvaḥ iti etat ayuktam iti 
[0627,i_0627,iii]	astu tarhi idānīm śabdasya nitya tvam vināśa kāraṇa anupalabdheḥ yat anityam tasya vināśaḥ kāraṇāt bhavati yathā loṣṭasya kāraṇa dravya vibhāgāt śabdaḥ ced anityaḥ tasya vināśaḥ yasmāt kāraṇāt bhavati tat upalabhyeta na ca upalabhyate tasmāt nityaḥ iti 
[0628,i_0628,ii]	aśravaṇa kāraṇa anupalabdheḥ satata śravaṇa prasaṅgaḥ yathā vināśa kāraṇa anupalabdheḥ avināśa prasaṅgaḥ evam aśravaṇa kāraṇa anupalabdheḥ satatam śravaṇa prasaṅgaḥ vyañjaka abhāvāt aśravaṇam iti ced pratiṣiddham vyañjakam atha vidyamānasya nirnimittam aśra vanam iti vidyamānasya nirnimittaḥ vināśaḥ iti samānaḥ ca dṛṣṭa virodhaḥ nimittam antareṇa vināśe ca aśravaṇe ca iti 
[0628,iii_0629,i]	upalabhyamāne ca anupalabdheḥ asattvāt anapadeśaḥ anumānāt ca upalabhyamāne śabdasya vināśa kāraṇe vināśa kāraṇa anupalabdheḥ asattvāt iti anapadeśaḥ yathā yasmāt viṣāṇī tasmāt aśvaḥ iti kim anumānam iti ced santāna upapattiḥ upapāditaḥ śabda santānaḥ saṃyoga vibhāga jāt śabdāt śabda antaram tatas antat tatas api anyat iti tatra kāryaḥ śabdaḥ kāraṇa śabdam niruṇaddhi pratighāti dravya saṃyogaḥ tu antyasya śabdasya nirodhakaḥ dṛṣṭam hi tiras pratikuḍyam antika sthena api aśravaṇam śabdasya śravaṇam dūra sthena api asati vyavadhāne iti 
[0630,i]	ghaṇṭāyām abhihanyamānāyām tāraḥ tārataraḥ mandaḥ mandataraḥ iti śruti bhedāt nānā śabda santānaḥ avicchedena śrūyate tatra nitye śabde ghaṇṭā stham anya gatam vā avasthitam santāna vṛtti vā abhivyakti kāraṇam vācyam yena śruti santānaḥ bhavati iti śabda bhede vā asati śruti bhedaḥ upapādayitavyaḥ iti anitye tu śabde ghaṇṭā stham santāna vṛtti saṃyoga sahakāri nimitta antaram saṃskāra bhūtam paṭu mandam anuvartate tasta anuvṛttyā śabda santāna anuvṛttiḥ paṭu manda bhāvāt ca tīvra manda tā śabdasya tad kṛtaḥ ca śruti bhedaḥ iti 
[0633,i_0634,i]	na vai nimitta antaram saṃskāraḥ upalabhyate anupalabdheḥ na asti iti pāṇi nimitta praśleṣāt śabda abhāve na anupalabdhiḥ pāṇi karmaṇā pāṇi ghaṇṭā praśleṣaḥ bhavati tasmin ca sati śabda santānaḥ na utpadyate atas śravaṇa anupapattiḥ tatra pratighāti dravya saṃyogaḥ śabdasya nimitta antaram saṃskāra bhūtam niruṇaddhi iti anumīyate tasya ca nirodhāt śabda santānaḥ na utpadyate anutpattau śruti vicchedaḥ yathā pratighāti dravya saṃyogāt iṣoḥ kriyā hetau saṃskāre niruddhe gamana abhāvaḥ iti kampa santānasya sparśana indriya grāhyasya ca uparamaḥ kāṃsya pātra ādiṣu pāṇi saṃśleṣaḥ liṅgam saṃskāra santānasya iti tasmāt nimitta antarasya saṃskāra bhūtasya na anupalabdhiḥ iti 
[0635,i_0635,ii]	vināśa kāraṇa anupalabdheḥ ca avasthāne tad nitya tva prasaṅgaḥ yadi yasya vināśa kāraṇam na upalabhyate tat avatiṣṭhate avasthānāt ca tasya nitya tvam prasajyate evam yāni khalu imāni śabda śravaṇāni śabda abhivyaktayaḥ iti matam na teṣām vināśa kāraṇam bhavatā upapādyate anupapādanāt avasthānam avasthānāt teṣām nitya tvam prasajyate iti atha na evam na tarhi vināśa kāraṇa anupalabdheḥ śabdasya avasthānāt nitya tvam iti 
[0635,iii_0636,ii]	kampa samāna āśrayasya anunādasya pāṇi praśleṣāt kampa vat kāraṇa uparamāt abhāvaḥ vaiyadhikaraṇye hi pratighāti dravya praśleṣāt samāna adhikaraṇasya eva uparamaḥ syāt iti asparśa tvāt apratiṣedhaḥ yat idam na ākāśa guṇaḥ śabdaḥ iti pratiṣidhyate ayam anupapannaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ asparśa tvāt śabda āśrayasya rūpa ādi samāna deśasya agrahaṇe śabda santāna upapatteḥ asparśa vyāpi dravya āśrayaḥ śabdaḥ iti jñāyate na kampa samāna āśrayaḥ iti 
[0637,i_0638,i]	pratidravyam rūpa ādibhiḥ saha sanniviṣṭaḥ śabdaḥ samāna deśaḥ vyajyate iti na upapadyate katham vibhakti antara upapatteḥ ca samāse santāna upapatteḥ ca iti ca arthaḥ tat vyākhyātam yadi rūpa ādayaḥ śabdāḥ ca pratidravyam samastāḥ samuditāḥ samuditāḥ tasmin samāse samudāye yaḥ yathājātīyakaḥ sanniviṣṭaḥ tasya tathā jātīyasya eva grahaṇena bhavitavyam śabde rūpa ādi vat tatra yaḥ ayam vibhāgaḥ eka dravye nānā rūpāḥ bhinna śrutayaḥ vidharmāṇaḥ śabdāḥ abhivyajyamānāḥ śrūyante yat ca vibhāga antaram sarūpāḥ samāna śrutayaḥ sa dharmāṇaḥ śabdāḥ tīvra manda dharma tayā bhinnāḥ śrūyante tat ubhayam na upapadyate nānā bhūtānām utpadyamānānām ayam dharmaḥ na ekasya vyajyamānasya iti asti ca ayam vibhāgaḥ vibhāga antaram ca tena vibhāga upapatteḥ manyāmahe na pratidravyam rūpa ādibhiḥ saha śabdaḥ sanniviṣṭaḥ vyajyate iti 
[0638,ii_0638,iv]	dvividhaḥ ca ayam śabdaḥ varṇa ātmakaḥ dhvani mātraḥ ca tatra varṇa ātmani tāvat vikāra ādeśa upadeśāt saṃśayaḥ dadhi atra iti kecid ikāraḥ itvam hitvā yatvam āpadyate iti vikāram manyante kecid ikārasya prayoge viṣaya kṛte yat ikāraḥ sthānam jahāti tatra yakārasya prayogam bruvate saṃhitāyām viṣaye ikāraḥ na prayujyate tasya sthāne yakāraḥ prayujyate saḥ ādeśaḥ iti ubhayam idam upadiśyate tatra na jñāyate kim tattvam iti 
[0639,i_0639,ii]	ādeśa upadeśaḥ tattvam vikāra upadeśe hi anvayasya agrahaṇāt vikārān anumānam sati anvaye kiñcid nivartate kiñcid upajāyate iti śakyeta vikāraḥ anumātum na ca anvayaḥ gṛhyate tasmāt vikāraḥ na asti iti bhinna karaṇayoḥ ca varṇayoḥ aprayoge prayoga upapattiḥ vivṛta karaṇaḥ ikāraḥ īṣat spṛṣṭa karaṇaḥ yakāraḥ tau imau pṛthakkaraṇa ākhyena prayatnena uccāraṇīyau tayoḥ ekasya aprayoge anyasya prayogaḥ upapannaḥ iti 
[0639,iii_0640,i]	avikāre ca aviśeṣaḥ yatra imau ikārayakārau na vikāra bhūtau yatate yacchati prāyaṃsta iti ikāraḥ idam iti ca yatra ca vikāra bhūtau iṣṭyā dadhi āhara iti ubhayatra prayoktuḥ aviśeṣaḥ yatnaḥ śrotuḥ ca śrutiḥ iti ādeśa upapattiḥ prayujyamāna agrahaṇāt ca na khalu ikāraḥ prayujyamānaḥ yakāra tām āpadyamānaḥ gṛhyate kim tarhi ikārasya prayoge yakāraḥ prayujyate tasmāt avikāraḥ iti 
[0640,ii_0640,iv]	avikāre ca na śabdānvākhyāna lopaḥ na vikriyante varṇāḥ iti na ca etasmin pakṣe śabda anvākhyānasya asambhave yena varṇa vikāram pratipadyemahi iti na khalu varṇasya varṇa antaram kāryam na hi ikārāt yakāraḥ utpadyate yakārāt vā ikāraḥ pṛthak sthāna prayatna utpādyāḥ hi ime varṇāḥ teṣām anyonyasya sthāne prayujyate iti yuktam etāvat ca etat pariṇāmaḥ vā vikāraḥ syāt kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ vā ubhayam ca na asti tasmāt na santi varṇa vikārāḥ varṇa samudāya vikāra anupapatti vat ca varṇa vikāra anupapattiḥ asteḥ bhūḥ bruvaḥ vaciḥ iti yathā varṇa samudāyasya dhātu lakṣaṇasya kvacid viṣaye varṇa antara samudāyaḥ na pariṇāmaḥ na kāryam śabda antarasya sthāne śabda antaram prayujyate tathā varṇasya varṇa ānataram iti 
[0641,i_0641,iii]	itas ca na santi varṇa vikārāḥ prakṛti vivṛddhau vikāra vivṛddhiḥ prakṛti anuvidhānam vikāreṣu dṛṣṭam yakāre hrasva dīrgha anuvidhānam na asti yena vikāra tvam anumīyate iti 
[0642,i_0642,ii]	nyūna sama adhika upalabdheḥ vikārāṇām ahetuḥ dravya vikārāḥ nyūnāḥ samāḥ adhikāḥ ca gṛhyante tadvat ayam vikāraḥ nyūnaḥ syāt iti 
[0642,iii_0642,v]	dvividhasya api hetoḥ abhāvāt asādhanam dṛṣṭāntaḥ atra na udāharaṇa sādharmyāt dhetuḥ asti na vaidharmyāt anupasaṃhṛtaḥ ca hetunā dṛṣṭāntaḥ na sādhakaḥ iti pratidṛṣṭānte ca aniyamaḥ prasajyeta yathā nuḍuhaḥ sthāne aśvaḥ voḍhum niyuktaḥ na tad vikāraḥ bhavati evam iva ṛṇasya sthāne yakāraḥ prayuktaḥ na vikāraḥ iti na ca atra niyama hetuḥ asti dṛṣṭāntaḥ sādhakaḥ na pratidṛṣṭāntaḥ iti 
[0643,i_0643,iii]	dravya vikāra udāharaṇam ca na atulya prakṛtīnām vikāra vikalpāt atulyānām dravyāṇām prakṛti bhāvaḥ vikalpate vikārāḥ ca prakṛtīḥ anuvidhīyante na tu iva ṛṇam anuvidhīyate yakāraḥ tasmāt anudāharaṇam dravya vikāraḥ iti 
[0644,i_0644,ii]	dravya vikāra vaiṣamya vat varṇa vikāra vikalpaḥ yathā dravya bhāvena tulyāyāḥ prakṛteḥ vikāra vaiṣamyam evam varṇa abhāvena tulyāyāḥ prakṛteḥ vikāra vikalpaḥ iti 
[0644,iii_0644,iv]	na vikāra dharma anupapatteḥ ayam vikāra dharmāḥ dravya sāmānye yad ātmakam dravyam mṛd vā suvarṇam vā tasya ātmanaḥ anvaye pūrvaḥ vyūhaḥ nivartate vyūha antaram ca upajāyate tam vikāram ācaṣṭe na varṇa sāmānye kaścid śabda ātmā anvayī yaḥ ittham jahāti yatvam ca āpadyate tatra yathā sati dravya bhāve vikāra vaiṣamye na anaḍuhaḥ aśvaḥ vikāraḥ vikāra dharma anupapatteḥ evam iva ṛṇasya na yakāraḥ vikāraḥ vikāra dharma anupapatteḥ iti 
[0645,i_0645,iii]	itas ca na santi varṇa vikārāḥ vikāra prāptānām apunar āpatteḥ anupapannā punar āpattiḥ katham punar āpatteḥ ananumānāt iti ikāraḥ yakāra tvam āpannaḥ punar ikāraḥ bhavati na punar ikārasya sthāne yakārasya prayogaḥ aprayogaḥ ca iti atra anumānam na asti 
[0645,iv_0645,vi]	ananumānāt iti na idam hi anumānam suvarṇa ādīnām punar āpatteḥ ahetuḥ suvarṇam kuṇḍala tvam hitvā rucaka tvam āpadyate rucaka tvam hitvā punar kuṇḍala tvam āpadyate evam ikāraḥ api yakāra tvam āpannaḥ punar ikāraḥ bhavati iti 
[0646,i_0646,iii]	vyabhicārāt ananumānam yathā payaḥ dadhi bhāvam āpannam punar na payaḥ bhavati kim evam varṇānām na punar āpattiḥ atha suvarṇa vat punar āpattiḥ iti suvarṇa udāharaṇa upapattiḥ ca na tad vikārāṇām suvarṇa bhāva avyatirekāt avasthitam suvarṇam hīyamānena dharmeṇa upajāyamānena ca dharmi bhavati na evam kaścid śabda ātmā hīyamānena itvena upajāyamānena yatvena dharmī gṛhyate tasmāt suvarṇa udāharaṇam na upapadyate iti 
[0647,i_0647,ii]	varṇa tva avyatirekāt varṇa vikārāṇām apratiṣedhaḥ varṇa vikārāḥ api varṇa tvam na vyabhicaranti yathā suvarṇa vikāraḥ suvarṇa tvam iti sāmānyavataḥ dharma yogaḥ na sāmānyasya kuṇḍala rucakau suvarṇasya dharmau na suvarṇa tvasya evam ikārayakārau kasya varṇa ātmanaḥ dharmau varṇa tvam sāmānyam na tasya imau dharmau bhavitum arhati na ca nivartamānaḥ dharmaḥ upajāyamānasya prakṛtiḥ tatra nivartamānaḥ ikāraḥ na yakārasya upajāyamānasya prakṛtiḥ iti 
[0647,iii_0647,v]	itas ca varṇa vikāra anupapattiḥ nitya tve avikārāt anitya tve ca anavasthānāt nityāḥ varṇāḥ iti etasmin pakṣe ikārayakārau varṇau iti ubhayoḥ nitya tvāt vikāra anupapattiḥ nitya tve avināśi tvāt kaḥ kasya vikāraḥ iti atha anityāḥ varṇāḥ iti pakṣaḥ evam api anavasthānam varṇānām kim idam anavasthānam varṇānām utpadya nirodhaḥ utpadya niruddhe ikāre yakāraḥ utpadyate yakāre ca utpadya niruddhe ikāraḥ utpadyate iti kaḥ kasya vikāraḥ tat etat avagṛhya sandhāne sandhāya ca avagrahe veditavyam iti 
[0647,vi_0647,viii]	nitya pakṣe tu tāvat samādhiḥ nityānām atīndriya tvāt tad dharma vikalpāt ca varṇa vikārāṇām apratiṣedhaḥ nityāḥ varṇāḥ na vikalpante iti vipratiṣedhaḥ yathā nitya tve sati kiñcid atīndriyam kiñcid indriya grāhyam indriya grāhyāḥ ca varṇāḥ evam nitya tve sati kiñcid na vikriyate varṇāḥ tu vikriyante iti 
[0649,i]	virodhāt ahetuḥ tad dharma vikalpaḥ nityam na upajāyate na apaiti anupajana apāya dharmakam nityam anityam punar upajana apāya yuktam na ca antareṇa upajana apāyau vikāraḥ sambhavati tat yadi varṇāḥ vikriyante nitya tvam eṣām nivartate atha nityāḥ vikāra dharma tvam eṣām nivartate saḥ ayam viruddhaḥ hetvābhāsaḥ dharma vikalpaḥ iti 
[0649,ii_0650,i]	anitya pakṣe samādhiḥ anavasthāyi tve ca varṇa upalabdhi vat tad vikāra utpattiḥ yathā anavasthāyinām varṇānām śravaṇam bhavati evam eṣām vikāraḥ bhavati asambandhāt asamarthāḥ artha pratipādikā varṇa upalabdhiḥ na vikāreṇa sambandhāt asamarthāḥ yā gṛhyamāṇā varṇa vikāram anumāpayet iti tatra yādṛś idam yathā gandha guṇā pṛthivī evam śabda sukha ādi guṇā api iti tādṛś etat bhavati iti na ca varṇa upalabdhiḥ varṇa nivṛttau varṇa antara prayogasya nivartikā yaḥ ayam iva ṛṇa nivṛttau yakārasya prayogaḥ yadi ayam varṇa upalabdhyā nivartate tadā tatra upalabhyamānāḥ ivaṛṇaḥ yatvam āpadyate iti gṛhyeta tasmāt varṇa upalabdhiḥ ahetuḥ varṇa vikārasya iti 
[0650,ii_0651,i]	vikāra dharmi tve nitya tva abhāvāt kāla antare vikāra upapatteḥ ca apratiṣedhaḥ tad dharma vikalpāt iti na yuktaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ na khalu vikāra dharmakam kiñcid nityam upalabhyate iti varṇa upalabdhi vat iti na yuktaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ avagrahe hi dadhi atra iti prayujya ciram sthitvā tatas saṃhitāyām prayuṅkte dadhi atra iti cira nivṛtte ca ayam iva ṛṇe yakāraḥ prayujyamānaḥ kasya vikāraḥ iti pratīyate kāraṇa abhāvāt kārya abhāvaḥ iti anuyogaḥ prasajyate iti 
[0651,ii_0651,iv]	itas ca varṇa vikāra anupapattiḥ prakṛti aniyamāt ikāra sthāne yakāraḥ śrūyate yakāra sthāne khalu ikāraḥ vidhīyate vidhyati iti tat yadi syāt prakṛti vikāra bhāvāḥ varṇānām tasya prakṛti niyamaḥ syāt dṛṣṭaḥ vikāra dharmi tve prakṛti niyamaḥ iti 
[0652,i_0652,ii]	aniyame niyamān na aniyamaḥ yaḥ ayam prakṛteḥ aniyamaḥ uktaḥ sa niyataḥ yathā viṣayam vyavasthitaḥ niyata tvāt niyamaḥ iti bhavati evam sati aniyamaḥ na asti tatra yat uktam prakṛti aniyamāt iti etat ayuktam iti 
[0652,iii_0652,iv]	niyama aniyama virodhāt aniyame niyamāt ca apratiṣedhaḥ niyamaḥ iti atra artha abhyanujñā aniyamaḥ iti tasya pratiṣedhaḥ anujñāta niṣiddhayoḥ ca vyāghātāt anartha antara tvam na bhavati aniyamaḥ ca niyata tvāt niyamaḥ na bhavati iti na atra arthasya tathā abhāvaḥ pratiṣidhyate kim tarhi tathābhūtasya arthasya niyama śabdena abhidhīyamānasya niyata tvāt niyama śabdaḥ eva upapadyate saḥ ayam niyamāt aniyame pratiṣedhaḥ na bhavati iti 
[0653,i_0653,iii]	na ca iyam varṇa vikāra upapattiḥ pariṇāmāt kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt vā kim tarhi guṇa antara āpatti upamarda hrāsa vṛddhi leśa śleśebhyaḥ tu vikāra upapatteḥ varṇa vikārāḥ sthānyādeśa bhāvāt aprayogaḥ vikāra śabda arthaḥ sa bhidyate guṇa antara āpattiḥ udāttasya anudātte iti evamādiḥ upamardaḥ nāma eka rūpa nivṛttau rūpa antara upajanaḥ hrāsaḥ dīrghasya hrasvaḥ vṛddhiḥ hrasvasya dīrghaḥ tayoḥ vā plutaḥ leśaḥ lāghavam staḥ iti asteḥ vikāraḥ śleṣaḥ āgamaḥ prakṛteḥ pratyayasya vā ete eva viśeṣāḥ vikārāḥ iti ete eva ādeśāḥ ete ced vikārāḥ upapadyante tarhi varṇa vikārāḥ iti 
[0654,i_0657,i]	te vibhakti antāḥ padam yathādarśanam vikṛtāḥ varṇāḥ vibhakti antāḥ pada saṃjñāḥ bhavanti vibhaktiḥ dvayī nāmikī ākhyātikī ca brāhmaṇaḥ pacati iti udāharaṇam upasarga nipātāḥ tarhi na pada saṃjñāḥ lakṣaṇa antaram vācyam iti śiṣyate ca khalu nāmikyāḥ vibhakteḥ avyayāt lopaḥ tayoḥ pada saṃjñā artham iti 
[0658,i_0659,ii]	padena artha sampratyayaḥ iti prayojanam nāma padam ca adhikṛtya parīkṣā gauḥ iti padam khalu idam udāharaṇam tad arthe vyakti ākṛti jāti sannidhau upacārāt saṃśayaḥ avinā abhāva vṛttiḥ sannidhiḥ avinā abhāvena vartamānāsu vyakti ākṛti jātiṣu gauḥ iti prayujyate tatra na jñāyate kim anyatamaḥ padārthaḥ uta etat sarvam iti 
[0660,i_0660,iii]	śabdasya prayoga sāmarthyāt padārtha avadhāraṇam tasmāt yā śabda samūha tyāga parigraha saṅkhyā vṛddhi apacaya varṇa samāsa anubandhānām vyaktau upacārāt vyaktiḥ vyaktiḥ padārthaḥ kasmāt yā śabda prabhṛtīnām vyaktau upacārāt upacāraḥ prayogaḥ yā gauḥ tiṣṭhati yā gauḥ niṣaṇṇa iti na idam vākyam jāteḥ abhidhāyakam abhedāt bhedāt tu dravya abhidhāyakam 
[0661,i]	gavām samūhaḥ iti bhedāt dravya abhidhānam na jāteḥ abhedāt vaidyāya gām dadati iti dravyasya tyāgaḥ na jāteḥ amūrta tvāt pratikrama anukrama anupapatteḥ ca parigrahaḥ sva tvena abhisambandhaḥ kauṇḍinyasya gauḥ brāhmaṇasya gauḥ iti dravya abhidhāne dravya bhedāt sambandha bhedaḥ iti upapannam abhinnā tu jātiḥ iti saṅkhyā daśa gāvaḥ viṃśatiḥ gāvaḥ iti bhinnam dravyam saṅkhyāyate na jātiḥ abhedāt iti vṛddhiḥ kāraṇavataḥ dravyasya avayava upacayaḥ avardhata gauḥ iti niravayavā tu jātiḥ iti etena apacayaḥ vyākhyātaḥ varṇaḥ śuklā gauḥ kapilā gauḥ iti dravyasya guṇa yogaḥ na sāmānyasya samāsaḥ go hitam go sukham iti dravyasya sukha ādi yogaḥ na jāteḥ iti anubandhaḥ sarūpa prajanana santānaḥ gauḥ gām janayati iti tad utpatti dharma tvāt dravye yuktam na jātau viparyayāt iti dravyam vyaktiḥ iti hi na artha antaram 
[0662,i_0662,iii]	asya pratiṣedhaḥ na tad anavasthānāt na vyaktiḥ padārthaḥ kasmāt anavasthānāt yā śabda prabhṛtibhiḥ yaḥ viśeṣyate sa go śabda arthaḥ yā gauḥ tiṣṭhati yā gauḥ niṣaṇṇa iti na dravya mātram aviśiṣṭam jātyā vinā abhidhīyate kim tarhi jāti viśiṣṭam tasmāt na vyaktiḥ padārthaḥ evam samūha ādiṣu draṣṭavyam 
[0662,iv_0663,ii]	yadi na vyaktiḥ padārthaḥ katham tarhi vyaktau upacāraḥ iti nimittāt atadbhāve api tad upacāraḥ dṛśyate khalu sahacaraṇa sthāna tādarthya vṛtta māna dhāraṇa sāmīpya yoga sādhana ādhipatyebhyaḥ brāhmaṇa mañca kaṭa rāja saktu candana gaṅgā śāṭaka anna puruṣeṣu atadbhāve api tad upacāraḥ atadbhāve api tad upacāraḥ iti atad śabdasya tena śabdena abhidhānam iti sahacaraṇāt yaṣṭikām bhojaya iti yaṣṭikā sahacaritaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ abhidhīyate iti 
[0664,i]	sthānāt mañcāḥ krośanti iti mañca sthāḥ puruṣāḥ abhidhīyante tādarthyāt kaṭārtheṣu vīraṇeṣu vyuhyamāneṣu kaṭam karoti iti bhavati vṛtāt yamaḥ rājā kuberaḥ rājā iti tadvat vartate iti mānāt āḍhakena mitāḥ saktavaḥ āḍhaka saktavaḥ iti dhāraṇāt tulāyām dhṛtam candanam tulā candanam iti sāmīpyāt gaṅgāyām gāvaḥ caranti iti deśaḥ abhidhīyate sannikṛṣṭaḥ yogāt kṛṣṇena rāgeṇa yuktaḥ śāṭakaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ iti abhidhīyate sādhanāt annam prāṇāḥ iti ādhipatyāt ayam puruṣaḥ kulam ayam gotram iti tatra ayam sahacaraṇāt yogāt vā jāti śabdaḥ vyaktau prayujyate iti 
[0665,i_0665,iii]	yadi gauḥ iti asya padasya na vyaktiḥ arthaḥ astu tarhi ākṛtiḥ tad apekṣa tvāt sattva vyavasthāna siddheḥ ākṛtiḥ padārthaḥ kasmāt tad apekṣa tvāt sattva vyavasthāni siddheḥ sattva avayavānām tad avayavānām ca niyataḥ vyūhaḥ ākṛtiḥ tasyām gṛhyamāṇāyām sattva vyavasthānam sidhyati ayam gauḥ ayam aśvaḥ iti na agṛhyamāṇāyām yasya grahaṇāt sattva vyavasthānam sidhyati tam śabdaḥ abhidhātum arhati saḥ asya arthaḥ iti 
[0665,iv_0667,i]	tat upapadyate yasya jātyā yogaḥ tat atra jāti viśiṣṭam abhidhīyate gauḥ iti na ca avayava vyūhasya jātyā yogaḥ kasya tarhi niyata avayava vyūhasya dravyasya tasmāt na ākṛtiḥ padārthaḥ astu tarhi jātiḥ padārthaḥ vyakti ākṛti yukte api aprasaṅgāt prokṣa ādīnām mṛda gavake jātiḥ jātiḥ padārthaḥ kasmāt vyakti ākṛti yukte api mṛd gavake prokṣaṇa ādīnām aprasaṅgāt iti gām prokṣaya gām ānaya gām dehi iti na etāni mṛdgavake prayujyante kasmāt jāteḥ abhāvāt asti hi tatra vyaktiḥ asti ākṛtiḥ yat abhāvāt tatra asampratyayaḥ sa padārthaḥ iti 
[0670,i_0670,ii]	na ākṛti vyakti apekṣa tvāt jāti abhivyakteḥ jāteḥ abhivyaktiḥ ākṛti vyaktī apekṣate na agṛhyamāṇāyām ākṛtau vyaktau ca jāti mātram śuddham gṛhyate tasmāt na jātiḥ padārthaḥ iti 
[0670,iii_0671,i]	na vai padārthena na bhavitum śakyam kaḥ khalu idānīm padārthaḥ iti vyakti ākṛti jātayaḥ tu padārthaḥ tuśabdaḥ viśeṣaṇa arthaḥ kim viśiṣyate pradhāna aṅga bhāvasya aniyamena padārtha tvam iti yadā hi bheda vivakṣā viśeṣa gatiḥ ca tadā vyaktiḥ pradhānam aṅgam tu jāti ākṛtī yadā tu bhedaḥ avivakṣitaḥ sāmānya gatiḥ ca tadā jātiḥ pradhānam aṅgam tu vyakti ākṛtī tat etat bahulam prayogeṣu ākṛteḥ tu pradhāna bhāvaḥ utprekṣitavyaḥ 
[0689,i_0690,i]	katham punar jñāyate nānā vyakti ākṛti jātayaḥ iti lakṣaṇa bhedāt tatra tāvat vyaktiḥ guṇa viśeṣa āśrayaḥ mūrtiḥ vyajyate iti vyaktiḥ indriya grāhyā iti na sarvam dravyam vyaktiḥ yaḥ guṇa viśeṣāṇām sparśa antānām guru tva ghana tva drava tva saṃskārāṇām avyāpinaḥ parimāṇasya āśrayaḥ yathāsambhavam tat dravyam mūrtiḥ mūrcchita avayava tvāt iti 
[0691,i_0692,i]	ākṛtiḥ jāti liṅga ākhyā yayā jātiḥ jāti liṅgāni ca prakhyāyante tām ākṛtim vidyāt sā ca na anyā sattva avayavānām tad avayavānām ca niyatāt vyūhāt iti niyata avayava vyūhāḥ khalu sattva avayavāḥ jāti liṅgam śirasā pādena gām anuminvanti niyate ca sattva avayavānām vyūhe sati go tvam prakhyāyate iti anākṛti vyaṅgyāyām jātau mṛd suvarṇam rajatam iti evamādiṣu ākṛtiḥ nivartate jahāti padārtha tvam iti 
[0693,i_0693,ii]	samāna prasava ātmikā jātiḥ yā samānam buddhim prasūte bhinneṣu adhikaraṇeṣu yayā bahūni iteḥ a itarataḥ na vyāvartante yaḥ arthaḥ anekatra pratyaya anuvṛtti nimittam tat sāmānyam yat ca keṣāñcid abhedam kutaścid bhedam karoti tat sāmānya viśeṣaḥ jātiḥ iti 
[0697,i_0709,i]	parīkṣitāni pramāṇāni prameyam idānīm parīkṣyate tat ca ātmā ādi iti ātmā vivicyate kim deha indriya manaḥ buddhi vedanā saṅghāta mātram ātmā āhosvit tat vayatiriktaḥ iti kutas saṃśayaḥ vyapadeśya ubhayathā siddheḥ kriyā karaṇayoḥ kartrā sambandhasya abhidhānam vyapadeśaḥ sa dvividhaḥ avayavena samudāyasya mūlaiḥ vṛkṣaḥ tiṣṭhati stambhaiḥ prāsādaḥ dhriyate iti anyena anyasya vyapadeśaḥ paraśunā vṛścati pradīpena paśyati asti ca ayam vyapadeśaḥ cakṣuṣā paśyati manasā vijānāti buddhyā vicārayati śarīreṇa sukha duḥkham anubhavati iti tatra na avadhāryate kim avayavena samudāyasya deha ādi saṅghātasya atha anyena anyasya tad vyatiriktasya vā iti 
[0710,i_0710,iii]	anyena ayam anayasya vyapadeśaḥ kasmāt darśana sparśanābhyām eka artha grahaṇāt darśanena kaścid arthaḥ gṛhītaḥ sparśanena api saḥ arthaḥ gṛhyate yam aham adrākṣam cakṣuṣā tam sparśanena api spṛśāmi iti yam ca āspārkṣam sparśanena tam cakṣuṣā paśyāmi iti eka viṣayau ca imau pratyayau eka kartṛkau pratisandhīyete na ca saṅghāta kartṛkau na indriyeṇa eka kartṛkau tat yaḥ asau cakṣuṣā tvac indriyeṇa ca eka arthasya grahītā bhinna nimittau anya kartṛkau pratyayau samāna viṣayau pratisandadhāti saḥ artha antara bhūtaḥ ātmā 
[0712,i]	katham punar na indriyeṇa eka kartṛkau indriyam khalu sva sva viṣaya grahaṇam ananya kartṛkam pratisandhātum arhati na indriya antarasya viṣaya antara grahaṇam iti katham na saṅghāta kartṛkau ekaḥ khalu ayam bhinna nimittau sva ātma kartṛkau paryayau pratisaṃhitau vedayate na saṅghātaḥ kasmāt anivṛttam hi saṅghāte pratyekam viṣaya antara grahaṇasya apratisandhānam indriya antareṇa iva iti 
[0712,ii_0713,ii]	na viṣaya vyavasthānāt na deha ādi saṅghātāt anyaḥ cetanaḥ kasmāt viṣaya vyavasthānāt vyavasthita viṣayāṇi indriyāṇi cakṣuṣi asati rūpam na gṛhyate sati ca gṛhyate yat ca yasmin asati na bhavati sati bhavati tasya tat iti vijñāyate tasmāt rūpa grahaṇam cakṣuṣaḥ cakṣuḥ rūpam paśyati evam ghrāṇa ādiṣu api iti tāni indriyāṇi imāni sva sva viṣaya grahaṇāt cetanāni indriyāṇām bhāva abhāvayoḥ viṣaya grahaṇasya tathā abhāvāt evam sati kim anyena cetanena sandhigdha tvāt ahetuḥ yaḥ ayam indriyāṇām bhāva abhāvayoḥ viṣaya grahaṇasya tathā abhāvaḥ sa kim cetana tvāt āhosvit cetanā upakaraṇānām grahaṇa nimitta tvāt iti sandihyate cetanā upakaraṇa tve api indriyāṇām grahaṇa nimitta tvāt bhavitum arhati 
[0713,iii_0714,ii^1]	yat ca uktam viṣaya vyavasthānat iti tad vyavasthānāt eva ātma sadbhāvāt apratiṣedhaḥ yadi khalu ekam indriyam avyavasthita viṣayam sarvajñam sarva viṣaya grāhi cetanam syāt kaḥ tatas anyam cetanam anumātum śaknuyāt yasmāt tu vyavasthita viṣayāṇi indriyāṇi tasmāt tebhyaḥ anyaḥ cetanaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarva viṣaya grāhī viṣaya vyavasthitam atītaḥ anumīyate tatra idam abhijñānam apratyākhyeyam cetana vṛttam udāhriyate rūpa darśī khalu ayam rasam gandham vā pūrva gṛhītam anuminoti gandha pratisaṃvedī ca rūpa rasau anuminoti evam viṣaya śeṣe api vācyam rūpam dṛṣṭvā gandham jighrati ghrātvā ca gandham rūpam paśyati 
[0714,ii^2]	tat evam aniyata paryāyam sarva viṣaya grahaṇam eka cetanā adhikaraṇam ananya kartṛkam pratisandhatte pratyakṣa anumāna āgama saṃśayān pratyayān ca nānā viṣayān sva ātma kartṛkān pratisandhāya vedayate sarva viṣayam ca śāstram pratipadyate artham aviṣaya bhūtam śrotrasya krama bhāvinaḥ varṇān śrutvā pada vākya bhāvena pratisandhāya śabda artha vyavasthām ca budhyamānaḥ aneka viṣayam artha jātam agrahaṇīyam ekaikena indriyeṇa gṛhṇāti sā iyam sarvajñasya jñeya avyavasthā anupadam na śakyā parikramitum ākṛti mātram tu udāhṛtam tatra yat uktam indriya caitanye sati kim aneya cetanena tat ayuktam bhavati 
[0716,i_0716,ii]	itas ca deha ādi vyatiriktaḥ ātmā na deha ādi saṅghāta mātram śarīra dāhe pātaka abhāvāt śarīra grahaṇena śarīra indriya buddhi vedanā saṅghātaḥ prāṇi bhūtaḥ gṛhyate prāṇi bhūtam śarīram dahataḥ prāṇi hiṃsā kṛta pāpam pātakam iti ucyate tasya abhāvaḥ tad phalena kartuḥ asambandhāt akartuḥ ca sambandhāt śarīra indriya buddhi vedanā prabandhe khalu anyaḥ saṅghātaḥ utpadyate anyaḥ nirudhyate utpāda nirodha santati bhūtaḥ prabandhaḥ na anya tvam bādhate deha ādi saṅghātasya anyatva adhiṣṭhāna tvāt anya tva adhiṣṭhānaḥ hi asau prakhyāyate iti evam ca sati yaḥ deha ādi saṅghātaḥ prāṇi bhūtaḥ hiṃsām karoti na asau hiṃsā phalena sambadhyate yaḥ ca sambadhyate na tena hiṃsā kṛtā tat evam sattva bhede kṛta hānam akṛta abhyāgamaḥ prasajyate sati ca sattva utpāde sattva nirodhe ca akarma nimittaḥ sattva saṃsargaḥ prāpnoti tatra mukti arthaḥ brahmacarya vāsaḥ na syāt tat yadi deha ādi saṅghāta mātram sattvam syāt śarīra dāhe pātakam na bhavet aniṣṭam ca etat tasmāt deha ādi saṅghāta vyatiriktaḥ ātmā nityaḥ iti 
[0720,i_0721,i]	tad abhāvaḥ sa ātmaka pradāhe api tad nitya tvāt yasya api nityena ātmanā sa ātmakam śarīram dahyate tasya api śarīra dāhe pātakam na bhavet dagdhuḥ kasmāt nitya tvāt ātmanaḥ na jātu kaścid nityam hiṃsitum arhati atha hiṃsyate nitya tvam asya na bhavati sā iyam ekasmin pakṣe hiṃsā niṣphalāḥ anyasmin tu anupapanna iti 
[0724,i_0724,ii]	na kārya āśraya kartṛ vadhāt na brūmaḥ nityasya sattvasya badhaḥ hiṃsā api tu anucchitti dharmakasya sattvasya kārya āśrayasya śarīrasya sva viṣaya upalabdheḥ ca kartṛṇām indriyāṇām upaghātaḥ pīḍā vaikalya lakṣaṇaḥ prabandha ucchedaḥ vā pramāpaṇa lakṣaṇaḥ vā vadhaḥ hiṃsā iti kāryam tu sukha duḥkha saṃvedanam tasya āyatanam adhiṣṭhānam āśrayaḥ śarīram kārya āśrayasya śarīrasya sva viṣaya upalabdheḥ ca kartṛṇām indriyāṇām badhaḥ hiṃsā na nityasya ātmanaḥ tatra yat uktam tad abhāvaḥ sa ātmaka pradāhe api tad nitya tvāt iti etat ayuktam yasya sattva ucchedaḥ hiṃsā tasya kṛta hānam akṛta abhyāgamaḥ ca iti doṣaḥ etāvat ca etat syāt sattva ucchedaḥ vā hiṃsā anucchitti dharmakasya sattvasya kārya āśraya kartṛ vadhaḥ vā na kalpa antaram asti sattva ucchedaḥ ca pratiṣiddhaḥ tatra kim anyat śeṣam yathābhūtam iti 
[0724,iii]	atha vā kārya āśraya kartṛ vadhāt iti kārya āśrayaḥ deha indriya buddhi saṅghātaḥ nityasya ātmanaḥ tatra sukha duḥkha pratisaṃvedanam tasya adhiṣṭhānam āśrayaḥ tad āyatanam tat bhavati na tatas anyat iti saḥ eva kartā tad nimittā hi sukha duḥkha saṃvedanasya nivṛttiḥ na tam antareṇa iti tasya vadhaḥ upaghātaḥ pīḍā pramāpaṇam vā hiṃsā na nitya tvena ātma ucchedaḥ tatra yat uktam tad abhāvaḥ sa ātmaka pradāhe api tat nitya tvāt etat na iti 
[0726,i_0727,i]	itas ca deha ādi vyatiriktaḥ ātmā savya dṛṣṭasya itareṇa pratyabhijñānāt pūrva parayoḥ vijñānayoḥ eka viṣaye pratisandhi jñānam pratyabhijñānam tam eva etarhi paśyāmi yam ajñāsiṣam saḥ eva ayam arthaḥ iti savyena cakṣuṣā dṛṣṭasya itareṇa api cakṣuṣā pratyabhijñānāt yam adrākṣam tam eva etarhi paśyāmi iti indriya caitanye tu na anya dṛṣṭam anyaḥ pratyabhijānāti iti pratyabhijñā anupapattiḥ asti tu idam pratyabhijñanam tasmāt indriya vyatiriktaḥ cetanaḥ 
[0728,i_0728,ii]	na ekasmin nāsā asthi vyavahite dvi tva abhimānāt ekam idam cakṣuḥ madhye nāsā asthi vyavahitam tasya antau gṛhyamāṇau dvi tva abhimānam prayojayataḥ madhya vyavahitasya dīrghasya iva 
[0729,i_0729,ii]	eka vināśe dvitīya avināśāt na ekatvam ekasmin upahate ca uddhṛte vā cakṣuṣi dvitīyam avatiṣṭhate cakṣuḥ viṣaya grahaṇa liṅgam tasmāt ekasya vyavadhāna anupapattiḥ 
[0729,iii_0729,iv]	avayava nāśe api avayavi upalabdheḥ ahetuḥ eka vināśe dvitīya avināśāt iti ahetuḥ kasmāt vṛkṣasya hi kāsucid śākhāsu chinnā asu upalabhyate eva vṛkṣaḥ 
[0730,i_0730,iii]	dṛṣṭānta virodhāt apratiṣedhaḥ na kāraṇa dravyasya vibhāge kārya dravyam avatiṣṭate nitya tva prasaṅgāt bahuṣu avayaviṣu yasya kāraṇāni vibhaktāni tasya vināśaḥ yeṣām kāraṇāni avibhaktāni tāni avatiṣṭhante atha vā dṛśyamāna artha virodhaḥ dṛṣṭānta virodhaḥ mṛtasya hi śiraḥ kapāle dvau avaṭau nāsā asthi vyavahitau cakṣuṣaḥ sthāne bhedena gṛhyete na ca etat ekasmin nāsā asthi vyavahite sambhavati 
[0730,iv_0731,i]	atha vai eka vināśasya aniyamāt dvau imau arthau tau ca pṛthak āvaraṇa upaghātau anumīyete vibhinnau iti avapīḍanāt ca ekasya cakṣuṣaḥ raśmi viṣaya sannikarṣasya bhedāt dṛśya bhedaḥ iva gṛhyate tat ca eka tve virudhyate avapīḍana nivṛttau ca abhinna pratisandhānam iti tasmāt ekasya vyavadhāna anupapattiḥ
