[0731,ii_0732,ii]	anumīyate ca ayam deha ādi saṅghāta vyatiriktaḥ cetanaḥ iti indriya antara vikārāt kasyacid amla phalasya gṛhīta tad rasa sāhacarye rūpe gandhe vā kenacid indriyeṇa gṛhyamāṇe rasanasya indriya antarasya vikāraḥ rasa anusmṛtau rasa gardhi vartitaḥ danta udaka saṃplava bhūtaḥ gṛhyate tasya indriya caitanye anupapattiḥ na anya dṛṣṭam anyaḥ smarati 
[0733,i_0733,ii]	na smṛteḥ smartavya viṣaya tvāt smṛtiḥ nāma dharmaḥ nimittāt utpadyate tasyāḥ smartavyaḥ viṣayaḥ tad kṛtaḥ indriya antara vikāraḥ na ātma kṛtaḥ iti 
[0733,iii_0734,i]	tad ātma guṇa sadbhāvāt apratiṣedhaḥ tasyāḥ ātma guṇa tve sati sadbhāvāt apratiṣedhaḥ ātmanaḥ yadi smṛtiḥ ātma guṇaḥ evam sati smṛtiḥ upapadyate na anyat dṛṣṭam anyaḥ samarati iti indriya caitanye tu nānā kartṛkāṇām viṣaya grahaṇānām apratisandhānam pratisandhāne vā viṣaya vyavasthā anupapattiḥ ekaḥ tu cetanaḥ aneka artha darśī bhinna nimittaḥ pūrva dṛṣṭam artham smarati iti ekasya aneka artha darśinaḥ darśana pratisandhānāt smṛteḥ ātma guṇa tve sati sadbhāvaḥ viparyaye ca anupapattiḥ smṛti āśrayāḥ prāṇabhṛtām sarve vyavahārāḥ ātma liṅgam udāharaṇa mātram indriya antara vikāraḥ iti 
[0734,ii]	aparisaṅkhyānāḥ ca smṛti viṣayasya aparisaṅghyāya ca smṛti viṣayam idam ucyate na smṛteḥ smartavya viṣaya tvāt iti yā iyam smṛtiḥ agṛhyamāṇe arthe ajñāsiṣam aham amum artham iti etasyāḥ jñātṛ jñāna viśiṣṭaḥ pūrva jñātaḥ arthaḥ viṣayaḥ na artha mātram jñātavān aham amum artham asa arthaḥ mayā jñataḥ asmin arthe mama jñānam abhūt iti caturvidham etat vākyam smṛti viṣa ya jñāpakam samāna artham sarvatra khalu jñātā jñānam jñeyam ca gṛhyate atha pratyakṣe arthe yā smṛtiḥ tayā trīṇi jñānāni ekasmin arthe pratisandhīyante samāna kartṛkāṇi na nānā kartṛkāṇi na akartṛkāṇi kim tarhi eka kartṛkāṇi adrākṣam amum artham yam eva etarhi paśyāmi adrākṣam iti darśanam darśana saṃvid ca na khalu asaṃvidite sve darśane syāt etat adrakṣam iti te khalu ete dve jñāne yam eva etarhi paśyāmi iti tṛtīyam jñānam evam ekaḥ arthaḥ tribhiḥ jñānaiḥ yujyamānaḥ na akartṛkaḥ na nānā kartṛkaḥ kim tarhi 
[0736,i]	eka kartṛkaḥ iti saḥ ayam smṛti viṣayaḥ aparisaṅkhyāyamānaḥ vidyamānaḥ prajñātaḥ arthaḥ pratiṣidhyate na asti ātmā smṛteḥ smartavya viṣaya tvāt iti na ca idam smṛti mātram smartavya mātra viṣayam vai idam khalu jñāna pratisandhāna vat smṛti pratisandhānam ekasya sarva viṣaya tvāt ekaḥ ayam jñātā sarva viṣayaḥ svāni jñānāni pratisandhatte amum artham jñāsyāmi amum artham vijānāmi amum artham ajñāsiṣam amum artham jijñāsamānaḥ ciram ajñātvā adhyavasyati ajñāsiṣam iti evam smṛtim api tri kāla viśiṣṭām suṣmūrṣā viśiṣṭām ca pratisandhatte saṃskāra santati mātre tu sattve utpadya utpadya saṃskārāḥ tirobhavanti sa na asti ekaḥ api saṃskāraḥ yaḥ tri kāla viśiṣṭam jñānam smṛtim ca anubhavet na ca anubhavam antareṇa jñānasya smṛteḥ ca pratisandhānam aham mama iti ca utpadyate deha antara vat atas anumīyate asti ekaḥ sarva viṣayaḥ pratideham sva jñāna prabandham smṛti prabandham ca pratisandhattaḥ iti yasya deha antareṣu vṛtteḥ abhāvāt na pratisandhānam bhavati iti 
[0737,i_0737,ii]	na ātma pratipatti hetūnām manasi sambhavāt na deha ādi saṅghāta vyatiriktaḥ ātmā kasmāt ātma pratipatti hetūnām manasi sambhavāt darśana sparśanābhyām eka artha grahaṇāt iti evamādīnām ātma pratipādakānām hetūnām manasi sambhavaḥ yatas manaḥ hi sarva viṣayam iti tasmāt na śarīra indriya manaḥ buddhi saṅghāta vyatiriktaḥ ātmā iti 
[0737,iii_0738,i]	jñātuḥ jñāna sādhana upapatteḥ saṃjñā bheda mātram jñātuḥ khalu jñāna sādhanāni upapadyante cakṣuṣā paśyati ghrāṇena jighrati sparśanena spṛśati evam mantuḥ sarva viṣayasya mati sādhanam antaḥkaraṇa bhūtam sarva viṣayam vidyate yena ayam manyate iti evam sati jñātari ātma saṃjñā na mṛṣyate manaḥ saṃjñā abhyanujñāyate manasi ca manaḥ saṃjñā na mṛṣyate mati sādhanam tu abhyanujñāyate tat idam saṃjñā bheda mātram na arthe vivādaḥ iti pratyākhyāne vā sarva indriya vilopa prasaṅaḥ atha mantuḥ sarva viṣayasya mati sādhanam sarva viṣayam pratyākhyāyate na asti iti evam rūpa ādi viṣaya grahaṇa sādhanāni api na santi iti sarva indriya vilopaḥ prasajyate iti 
[0738,ii_0739,i]	niyamaḥ ca niranumānaḥ yaḥ ayam niyamaḥ iṣyate rūpa ādi grahaṇa sādhanāni asya santi mati sādhanam sarva viṣayam na asti iti ayam niyamaḥ niranumānaḥ na atra anumānam asti yena niyamam pratipadyāmahe iti rūpa ādibhyaḥ ca viṣaya antaram sukha ādayaḥ tad upalabdhau karaṇa antara sadbhāvaḥ yathā cakṣuṣā gandhaḥ na gṛhyate iti karaṇa antaram ghrāṇam evam cakṣuḥ ghrāṇābhyām rasaḥ na gṛhyate iti karaṇa antaram rasanam evam śeṣeṣu api tathā cakṣuḥ ādibhiḥ sukha ādayaḥ na gṛhyante iti karaṇa antareṇa bhavitavyam tat ca jñāna ayaugapadya liṅgam yat ca sukha ādi upalabdhau karaṇam tat ca jñāna ayaugapadya liṅgam tasya indriyam indriyam prati sannidheḥ asannidheḥ ca na yugapad jñānāni utpadyante iti tatra yat uktam ātma pratipatti hetūnām manasi sambhavāt iti tat ayuktam 
[0740,i_0741,ii]	kim punar ayam deha ādi saṅghātāt anyaḥ nityaḥ uta anityaḥ iti kutas saṃśayaḥ ubhayathā dṛṣṭa tvāt saṃśayaḥ vidyamānam ubhayathā bhavati nityam anityam ca pratipādite ca ātma sadbhāve saṃśaya anivṛttiḥ iti ātma sadbhāva hetubhiḥ eva asya prāk deha bhedāt avasthānam siddham ūrddhvam api deha bhedāt avatiṣṭhate kutas pūrva abhyasta smṛti anubandhāt jātasya harṣa bhaya śoka sampratipatteḥ 
[0741,iii]	jātaḥ khalu ayam kumārakaḥ asmin janmani agṛhīteṣu harṣa bhaya śoka hetuṣu harṣa bhaya śokān pratipadyate liṅga anumeyān te ca smṛti anubandhāt utpadyante na anyathā smṛti anubandhaḥ ca pūrva abhyāsam antareṇa na bhavati pūrva abhyāsaḥ ca pūrva janmani sati na anyathā iti sidhyati etat avatiṣṭhate ayam ūrdhvam śarīra bhedāt iti 
[0743,i_0743,iii]	padma ādiṣu prabodha sammīlana vikāra vat tatvikāraḥ yathā padma ādiṣu anityeṣu prabodhaḥ sammīlanam vikāraḥ bhavati evam anityasya ātmanaḥ harṣa bhaya śoka sampratipattiḥ vikāraḥ syāt hetu abhāvāt ayuktam anena hetunā padma ādiṣu prabodha sammīlana vikāra vat anityasya ātmanaḥ harṣa ādi sampratipattiḥ iti na atra udāharaṇa sādharmyāt sādhya sādhanam hetuḥ na vaidharmyāt asti hetu abhāvāt asambaddha arthakam apārthakam ucyate iti 
[0744,i]	dṛṣṭāntāt ca harṣa ādi nimittasya anivṛttiḥ yā ca iyam āseviteṣu viṣayeṣu harṣa ādi sampratipattiḥ smṛti anubandha kṛtā pratyātmanam gṛhyate sā iyam padma ādi sammīlana dṛṣṭāntena na nivartate yathā ca iyam na nivarttate tathā jātasya api iti kriyā jātau ca parṇa vibhāga saṃyogau prabodha sammīlane kriyā hetuḥ ca kriyā anumeyaḥ evam ca sati kim dṛṣṭāntena pratiṣidhyate 
[0744,ii_0745,i]	atha nirnimittaḥ padma ādiṣu prabodha sammīlana vikāraḥ iti matam evam ātmanaḥ api harṣa ādi sampratipattiḥ iti tat ca na uṣṇa śīta varṣā kāla nimitta tvāt pañca ātmaka vikārāṇām uṣṇa ādiṣu satsu bhāvāt asatsu abhāvāt tad nimittāḥ pañcabhūta anugraheṇa nivṛttānām padma ādīnām prabodha sammīlana vikārāḥ iti na nirnimittāḥ evam harṣa ādayaḥ api vikārāḥ nimittat bhavitum arhanti na nimittam antareṇa na ca anyat pūrva abhyasta smṛti anubandhāt nimittam asti iti na ca utpattitirodha kāraṇa anumānam ātmanaḥ dṛṣṭāntāt na harṣa ādīnām nimittam antareṇa utpattiḥ na uṣṇa ādi vat nimitta antara upādānam harṣa ādīnām tasmāt ayuktam etat 
[0745,ii_0746,i]	itas ca nityaḥ ātmā pretya āhāra abhyāsa kṛtāt stanya abhilāṣāt jāta mātrasya vatsasya pravṛtti liṅgaḥ stanya abhilāṣaḥ gṛhyate sa ca na antareṇa āhāra abhyāsam kayā yuktyā dṛśyate hi śarīriṇām kṣudhā pīḍyamānānām āhāra abhyāsa kṛtāt smaraṇa anubandhāt āhāra abhilāṣaḥ na ca pūrva śarīra abhyāsam antareṇa asau jāta mātrasya upapadyate tena anumīyate bhūta pūrvam śarīram yatra anena āhāraḥ abhyastaḥ iti sa khalu ayam ātmā pūrva śarīrāt pretya śarīra antaram āpannaḥ kṣudh pīḍitaḥ pūrva abhyastam āhāram anusmaran stanyam abhilaṣati tasmāt na deha bhedāt ātmā bhidyate bhavati eva ūrddhvam deha bhedāt iti 
[0746,ii_0746,iii]	ayasaḥ ayaskānta abhigamana vat tad upasarpaṇam yathā khalu ayaḥ abhyāsam antareṇa ayaska antam upasarpati evam āhāra abhyāsam antareṇa bālaḥ stanyam abhilaṣati 
[0747,i_0747,iii]	kim idam ayasaḥ ayaskānta abhisarpaṇam nirnimittam atha nimittāt iti nirnimittam tāvat na anyatra pravṛtti abhāvāt yadi nirnimittam loṣṭa ādayaḥ api ayaskāntam upasarpeyuḥ na jātu niyame kāraṇam asti iti atha nimittāt tat kena upalabhyate iti kriyā liṅgaḥ kriyā hetuḥ kriyā niyama liṅgaḥ ca kriyā hetu niyamaḥ tena anyatra pravṛtti abhāvaḥ bālasya api niyatam upasarpaṇa kriyā upalabhyate na ca stanya abhilāṣa liṅgam anyat āhāra abhyāsa kṛtāt smaraṇa anubandhāt nimittam dṛṣṭāntena upapādyate na ca asati nimitte kasyacid utpattiḥ na ca dṛṣṭāntaḥ dṛṣṭam abhilāṣa hetum bādhate tasmāt ayasaḥ ayaskānta abhigamanam adṛṣṭāntaḥ iti 
[0747,iv]	ayasaḥ khalu api na anyatra pravṛttiḥ bhavati na jātu ayaḥ loṣṭam upasarpati kiṃkṛtaḥ asya niyamaḥ iti yadi kāraṇa niyamāt sa ca kriyā niyama liṅgaḥ evam bālasya api niyata viṣayaḥ abhilāṣaḥ kāraṇa niyamāt bhavitum arhati tat ca kāraṇam abhyasta smaraṇam anyat vā iti dṛṣṭena viśiṣyate dṛṣṭaḥ hi śarīriṇām abhasta smaraṇāt āhāra abhilāṣaḥ iti 
[0747,v_0749,i]	itas ca nityaḥ ātmā kasmāt vīta rāga janma adarśanāt sa rāgaḥ jāyate iti arthāt āpadyate ayam jāyamānaḥ rāga anubhaddhaḥ jāyate rāgasya pūrva anubhūta viṣaya anucintanam yoniḥ pūrva anubhavaḥ ca viṣayāṇām anyasmin janmani śarīram antareṇa na upapadyate saḥ ayam ātmā pūrva śarīra anubhūtān viṣayān anusmaran teṣu teṣu rajyate tathā ca ayam dvayoḥ janmanoḥ pratisandhiḥ evam pūrva śarīrasya pūrvatareṇa pūrvatarasya pūrvatamena ityādinānādiḥ cetanasya śarīra yogaḥ anādiḥ ca rāga anubandhaḥ iti siddham nitya tvam iti 
[0750,i_0750,iii]	katham punar jñāyate pūrva anubhūta viṣaya anucintana janitaḥ jātasya rāgaḥ na punar sa guṇa dravya utpatti vat tad utpattiḥ atha utpatti dharmakasya dravyasya guṇāḥ kāraṇataḥ utpadyante tathā utpatti dharmakasya ātmanaḥ rāgaḥ kutaścid utpadyate atra ayam udita anuvādaḥ nidarśana arthaḥ 
[0750,iv_0750,v]	na saṅkalpa nimitta tvāt rāga ādīnām na khalu sa guṇa dravya utpatti vat utpattiḥ ātmanaḥ rāgasya ca kasmāt saṅkalpa nimitta tvāt rāga ādīnām ayam khalu prāṇinām viṣayān āsevamānānām saṅkalpa janitaḥ rāgaḥ gṛhyate saṅkalpaḥ ca pūrva anubhūta viṣaya anucintana yoniḥ tena anumīyate jātasya api pūrva anubhūta artha cintana kṛtaḥ rāgaḥ iti ātma utpāda adhikaraṇāt tu rāga utpattiḥ bhavantī saṅkalpāt anyasmin rāga kāraṇe sati vācyā kārya dravya guṇavat na ca ātma utpādaḥ siddhaḥ na api saṅkalpāt anyat rāga kāraṇam asti 
[0751,i_0751,iii]	tasmāt ayuktam sa guṇa dravya utpatti vat tayoḥ utpattiḥ iti atha api saṅkalpāt anyat rāga kāraṇam dharma adharma lakṣaṇam adṛṣṭam upādīyate tathā api pūrva śarīra yogaḥ apratyākhyeyaḥ tatra hi tasya nirvṛttiḥ na asmin janmani tad maya tvāt rāgaḥ iti viṣaya abhyāsaḥ khalu ayam bhāvanā hetuḥ tad maya tvam ucyate iti jāti viśeṣāt ca rāga viśeṣaḥ iti karma khalu idam jāti viśeṣa nirvartakam tādarthyāt tāt śabdyam vijñāyate tasmāt anupapannam saṅkalpāt anyat rāga kāraṇam iti 
[0752,i_0753,i]	anādiḥ cetanasya śarīra yogaḥ iti uktam sva kṛta karma nimittam ca asya śarīram sukha duḥkha adhiṣṭhānam tat parīkṣyate kim ghrāṇa ādi vat eka prakṛtikam uta nānā prakṛti iti kutas saṃśayaḥ vipratipatteḥ saṃśayaḥ pṛthivī ādīni bhūtāni saṅkhyā vikalpena śarīra prakṛtiḥ iti pratijānataḥ iti kim tatra tattvam pārthivam guṇa antara upalabdheḥ 
[0753,ii]	tatra mānuṣam pārthivam kasmāt guṇa antara upalabdheḥ gandhavatī pṛthivī gandha vat ca śarīram ap ādīnām agandha tvāt tad prakṛti agandham syāt na tu idam abādibhiḥ asampṛktayā pṛthivī ārabdham ceṣṭa indriya artha āśraya bhāvena kalpate iti atas pañcānām bhūtānām saṃyoge sati śarīram bhavati bhūta saṃyogaḥ hi mithas pañcānām na niṣiddhaḥ iti āpya taijasa vāyavyāni loka antare śarīrāṇi teṣu api bhūta saṃyogaḥ puruṣa artha tantraḥ iti sthālī ādi dravya niṣpattau api niḥsaṃśayaḥ nāba ādi saṃyogam antarena niṣpattiḥ iti 
[0754,i_0754,iv]	pārthiva apya taijasam tad aguṇa upalabdheḥ niḥśvāsa ucchvāsa upalabdheḥ cāturbhautikam gandha kleda pāka vyūha avakāśa dānebhyaḥ pāñcabhautikam te ime sandigdhāḥ hetavaḥ iti upekṣitavān sūtrakāraḥ katham sandigdhāḥ sati ca prakṛti bhāve bhūtānām dharma upalabdhiḥ asati ca saṃyoga apratiṣedhāt sannihitānām iti yathā sthālyām udaka tejaḥ vāyu ākāśānām iti tat idam aneka bhūta prakṛti śarīram agandham arasam arūpam asparśam ca prakṛti anuvidhānāt syāt na tu idam ittham bhūtam tasmāt pārthivam guṇa antara upalabdheḥ 
[0756,i_0756,ii]	śruti prāmāṇyāt ca sūryam te cakṣuḥ gacchatāt iti atra mantre pṛthivīm te śarīram iti śrūyate tat idam prakrtau vikārasya pralaya abhidhānam iti sūryam te cakṣuḥ spṛṇomi iti atra mantra antare pṛthivīm te śarīram spṛṇomi iti śrūyate sā iyam kāraṇāt vikārasya spṛtiḥ abhidhīyate iti sthālī ādiṣu ca tulya jātīyānām eka kārya ārambha darśanāt bhinna jātīyānām eka kārya ārambha anupapattiḥ 
[0756,iii_0758,iii]	atha idānīm indriyāṇi prameya krameṇa vicāryante kim āvyaktikāni āhosvit bhautikāni iti kutas saṃśayaḥ kṛṣṇasāre sati upalambhāt vyatiricya ca upalambhāt saṃśayaḥ kṛṣṇasāram bhautikam tasmin anupahate rūpa upalabdhiḥ upahate ca anupalabdhiḥ iti vyatiricya kṛṣṇasāram avasthitasya viṣayasya upalambhaḥ na kṛṣṇasāra prāptasya na ca aprāpya kāri tvam indriyāṇām tat idam abhautika tve vibhu tvāt sambhavati evam ubhaya dharma upalabdheḥ saṃśayaḥ 
[0760,i_0760,iii]	abhautikāni iti āha kasmāt mahat aṇu grahaṇāt mahat iti mahattaram mahattamam ca upalabhyate yathā nyagrodha parvata ādi aṇu iti aṇutaram aṇutamam ca gṛhyate yathā nyagrodha dhāna ādi tat ubhayam upalabhyamānam cakṣuṣaḥ bhautika tvam bādhate bhautikam hi yāvat tāvat eva vyāpnoti abhautikam tu vibhu tvāt sarva vyāpakam iti 
[0762,i_0763,i]	na mahat aṇu grahaṇa mātrāt abhautika tvam vibhu tvam ca indriyāṇām śakyam pratipattum idam khalu raśmi artha sannikarṣa viśeṣāt tad grahaṇam tayoḥ mahat aṇvoḥ grahaṇam cakṣūraśmeḥ arthasya ca sannikarṣa viśeṣāt bhavati yathā pradīpa raśmeḥ arthasya ca iti raśmi artha sannikarṣaḥ ca āvaraṇa liṅgaḥ cākṣuṣaḥ hi raśmiḥ kuḍya ādibhiḥ āvṛtam artham na prakāśayati yathā pradīpa raśmiḥ iti 
[0764,i_0764,iii]	āvaraṇa anumeya tve sati idam āha tad anupalabdheḥ ahetuḥ rūpa sparśa vat dhi tejaḥ mahat tvāt aneka dravyavat tvāt rūpavat tvāt ca upalabdhiḥ iti pradīpa vat pratyakṣataḥ upalabhyeta cākṣuṣaḥ raśmiḥ yadi syāt iti 
[0764,iv_0764,v]	na anumīyamānasya pratyakṣataḥ anupalabdhiḥ abhāva hetuḥ sannikarṣa pratiṣedha arthena āvaraṇena liṅgena anumīyamānasya raśmeḥ yā pratyakṣataḥ anupalabdhiḥ na asau abhāvam pratipādayati yathā candramasaḥ para bhāgasya prthivyāḥ ca adhobhāgasya 
[0765,i_0765,ii]	dravya guṇa dharma bhedāt ca upalabdhi niyamaḥ bhinnaḥ khalu ayam dravya dharmaḥ guṇa dharmaḥ ca mahat aneka dravya vat ca viṣakta avayavam āpyam dravyam pratyakṣataḥ na upalabhyate sparśaḥ tu śītaḥ gṛhyate tasya dravyasya anubandhāt hemanta śiśirau kalpyete tathāvidham eva ca taijasam dravyam anudbhūta rūpam saha rūpeṇa na upalabhyate sparśaḥ tu asya uṣṇaḥ upalabhyate tasya dravyasya anubandhāt grīṣma vasantau kalpyete 
[0765,iii_0767,i]	yatra tu eṣā bhavati aneka dravya samavāyāt rūpa viśeṣāt ca rūpa upalabdhiḥ tatra rūpam ca dravyam ca tad āśrayaḥ pratyakṣataḥ upalabhyate rūpa viśeṣaḥ tu yat bhāvāt kvacid rūpa upalabdhiḥ yad abhāvāt ca dravyasya kvacid anupalabdhiḥ sa rūpa dharmaḥ ayam udbhava samākhyātaḥ iti anudbhūta rūpaḥ ca ayam nāyanaḥ raśmiḥ tasmāt pratyakṣatas na upalabhyate iti dṛṣṭaḥ ca tejasaḥ dharma bhedaḥ udbhūta rūpa sparśam pratyakṣam tejaḥ yathā āditya raśmayaḥ udbhūta rūpam anudbhūta sparśam ca pratyakṣam yathā pradīpa raśmayaḥ udbhūta sparśam anudbhūta rūpam apratyakṣam yathā bādi saṃyuktam tejaḥ anudbhūta rūpa sparśaḥ apratyakṣaḥ cākṣuṣaḥ raśmiḥ iti 
[0767,ii_0767,iii]	karma kāritaḥ ca indriyāṇām vyūhaḥ puruṣa artha tantraḥ yathā cetanasya arthaḥ viṣaya upalabdhi bhūtaḥ sukha duḥkha upalabdhi bhūtaḥ ca kalpyate tathā indriyāṇi vyūḍhāni viṣaya prāpti arthaḥ ca raśmeḥ cākṣuṣasya vyūhaḥ rūpa sparśānabhivyaktiḥ ca vyavahāra prakḷpti arthā dravya viśeṣe ca pratīghātāt āvaraṇa upapattiḥ vyavahāra arthā sarva dravyāṇām viśvarūpaḥ vyūhaḥ indriya vat karma kāritaḥ puruṣa artha tantraḥ karma tu dharma adharma bhūtam cetanasya upabhoga artham iti 
[0768,i_0768,ii]	avyabhicārāt ca pratīghātaḥ bhautika dharmaḥ yaḥ ca ātvaraṇa upalambhāt indriyasya dravya viśeṣe pratighātaḥ sa bhautika dharmaḥ na bhūtāni vyabhicarati na abautikam pratighāta dharmakam dṛṣṭam iti apratighātaḥ tu vyabhicārī bhautikā bhautikayoḥ samāna tvāt iti yat api manyeta pratighātāt bhautikāni indriyāṇi apratighātāt abhautikāni iti prāptam dṛṣṭaḥ ca apratighātaḥ kāca abhra paṭala sphaṭika antarita upalabdheḥ tat na yuktam kasmāt yasmāt bhautikam api na pratihanyate kāca abhra paṭala sphaṭika antarita prakāśāt pradīpa raśmīnām sthālī ādiṣu pācakasya tejasaḥ apratighātaḥ 
[0769,i_0769,iii]	upapadyate ca anupalabdhiḥ kāraṇa bhedāt madhyandina ulkā prakāśa anupalabdhi vat tad anupalabdhiḥ yathā aneka dravyeṇa samavāyāt rūpa viśeṣāt ca upalabdhiḥ iti sati upalabdhi kāraṇe madhyandina ulkā prakāśaḥ na upakabhyate āditya prakāśena abhibhūtaḥ evam mahat aneka dravyavat tvāt rūpa viśeṣāt ca upalabhiḥ iti sati upalabdhi kāraṇe cākṣuṣaḥ raśmiḥ na upalabhyate nimitta antarataḥ tat ca vyākhyātam anudbhūta rūpa sparśasya dravyasya pratyakṣataḥ anupalabdhiḥ iti 
[0769,iv_0770,ii]	atyanta anupalabdhiḥ ca abhāva kāraṇam yaḥ hi bravīti loṣṭa prakāśaḥ madhyandine āditya prakāśa abhibhavāt na upalabhyate iti tasya etat syāt na rātrau api anupalabdheḥ api anumānataḥ anupalabdheḥ iti evam atyanta anupalabdheḥ loṣṭa prakāśaḥ na asti na tu evam cakṣuṣaḥ raśmiḥ iti 
[0770,iii_0770,v]	upapanna rūpā ca iyam bāhya prakāśa anugrahāt viṣaya upalabdheḥ anabhivyaktitaḥ anupalabdhiḥ bāhyena prakāśena anugṛhītam cakṣuḥ viṣaya grāhakam tad abhāve anupalabdhiḥ sati ca prakāśa anugrahe śīta sparśa upalabdhau ca satyām tad āśrayasya dravyasya cakṣuṣā agrahaṇam rūpasya anudbhūta tvāt sā iyam rūpa anabhivyaktitaḥ rūpa āśrayasya dravyasya anupalabdhiḥ dṛṣṭā tatra yat uktam tad anupalabdheḥ ahetuḥ iti etat ayuktam 
[0770,vi_0772,i]	kasmāt punar abhibhavaḥ anupalabdhi kāraṇam cākṣuṣasya raśmeḥ na ucyate iti abhivyaktau ca abhibhavāt bāhya prakāśa anugraha nirapekṣatāyām ca iti ca arthaḥ yat rūpam abhivyaktam udbhūtam bāhya prakāśa anugraham ca na apekṣate tat viṣayaḥ abhibhavaḥ viparyaye abhibhava abhāvāt anudbhūta rūpa tvāt ca anupalabhyamānam bāhya prakāśa anugrahāt ca upalabhyamānam na abhibhūyate iti evam upapannam asti cākṣuṣaḥ raśmiḥ iti 
[0773,i_0773,ii]	naktañcara nayana raśmi darśanāt ca dṛśyante hi naktam nayana raśmayaḥ naktañcarāṇām vṛṣadaṃśa prabhṛtīnām tena śeṣasya anumānam iti jāti bheda vat indriya bhedaḥ iti ced dharma bheda mātram ca anupapannam āvaraṇasya prātipratiṣedha arthasya darśanāt iti 
[0774,i_0774,iii]	indriya artha sannikarṣasya jñāna kāraṇa tva anupapattiḥ kasmāt aprāpya grahaṇam kāca abhra paṭala sphaṭika antarita upalabdheḥ tṛṇa ādi sarpat dravyam kāce abhra paṭale vā pratihatam dṛṣṭam avyavahitena sat nikṛṣyate vyāhanyate vai prāptiḥ vyavadhānena iti yadi ca raśmi artha sannikarṣaḥ grahaṇa hetuḥ syāt na vyavahitasya sannikarṣaḥ iti agrahaṇam syāt asti ca iyam kāca abhra paṭala sphaṭika antarita upalabdhiḥ sā jñāpayati aprāpya kārīṇi indriyāṇi atas eva abhautikāni prāpya kāri tvam hi bhautika dharmaḥ iti 
[0775,i_0775,ii]	kuḍya antarita anupalabdheḥ apratiṣedhaḥ aprāpyakaritve sati indriyāṇām kuḍya antaritasya anupalabdhiḥ na syāt 
[0775,iii_0775,v]	prāpya kāri tve api tu kāca abhra paṭala sphaṭika antarita upalabdhiḥ na syāt apratīghātāt sannikarṣa upapattiḥ na ca kācaḥ abhra paṭalam vā nayana raśmim viṣṭabhnāti saḥ apratihanyamānaḥ sat nikṛṣyate iti 
[0776,i_0776,iii]	yaḥ ca manyate na bhautikasya apratighātaḥ iti tat na āditya raśmeḥ sphaṭika antarite api dāhye avighātāt ādityaraśmeḥ avighātāt sphaṭika antarite api avighātāt dāhye avighātāt avighātāt iti ca pada abhisambandhāt vākya bhedaḥ iti prativākyam ca artha bhedaḥ iti āditya raśmiḥ kumbha ādiṣu na pratihanyate avighātāt kumbha stham udakam tapati prāptau hi dravya antara guṇasya uṣṇasya sparśasya grahaṇam tena ca śīta sparśa abhibhavaḥ iti sphaṭika antarite api prakāśanīye pradīpa raśmīnām apratighātaḥ apratighātāt prāptasya grahaṇam iti bharjana kapāla ādi stham ca dravyam āgneyena tejasā dahyate tatra avighātāt prāptiḥ prāptau tu dāhaḥ na aprāpya kāri tejaḥ iti 
[0777,i]	avighātāt iti ca kevalam padam upādīyate kaḥ ayam avighātaḥ nāma avyuhyamāna avayavena vyavadhāyena dravyeṇa sarvatas dravyasya aviṣṭhmbhaḥ kriyā hetoḥ apratibandhaḥ prāpteḥ apratiṣedhaḥ iti dṛṣṭam hi kalaśa niṣaktānām apām bahis śīta sparśasya grahaṇam na ca indriyeṇa āsat nikṛṣṭasya dravyasya sparśa upalabdhiḥ dṛṣṭau ca praspanda parisravau tatra kāca abhra paṭala ādibhiḥ nayana raśmeḥ apratighātāt vibhidya arthena saha sannikarṣāt upapannam grahaṇam iti 
[0778,i_0778,ii]	na itara itara dharma prasaṅgāt kāca abhra paṭala ādi vat vā kuḍya ādibhiḥ apratighātaḥ kuḍya ādi vat vā kāca abhra paṭala ādibhiḥ pratighātaḥ iti prasajyate niyame kāraṇam vācyam iti 
[0778,iii_0778,iv]	ādarśa udakayoḥ prasāda svābhāvyāt rūpa upalabdhi vat tad upalabdhiḥ ādarśa udakayoḥ prasādaḥ rūpa viśeṣaḥ svaḥ dharmaḥ niyama darśanāt prasādasya vā svaḥ dharmaḥ rūpa upalambhanam yathā ādarśa pratihatasya parāvṛttasya nayana raśmeḥ svena mukhena sannikarṣe sati sva mukha upalambhanam pratibimba grahaṇa ākhyam ādarśa rūpa anugrahāt tad nimittam bhavati ādarśa rūpa upaghāte tad abhāvāt kuḍya ādiṣu ca pratibimba grahaṇam na bhavati evam kāca abhra paṭala ādibhiḥ avighātaḥ cakṣūraśmeḥ kuḍya ādibhiḥ ca pratighātaḥ dravya svabhāva niyamāt iti 
[0778,v_0778,vi]	dṛṣṭa anumitānām hi niyoga pratiṣedha anupapattiḥ pramāṇasya tattva viṣaya tvāt na khalu bhoḥ parīkṣamāṇena dṛṣṭa anumitāḥ arthāḥ śakyā niyoktum evam bhavatā iti na api pratiṣeddhum evam na bhavatā iti na hi idam upapadyate rūpavat gandhaḥ api cākṣuṣaḥ bhavatu iti gandha vat vā rūpam cākṣuṣam mā bhūt iti agni pratipatti vat dhūmena udaka pratipattiḥ api bhavatu iti udaka apratipatti vat vā dhūmena agni pratipattiḥ api mā bhūt iti kim kāraṇam yathā khalu arthāḥ bhavanti yaḥ eṣām svaḥ bhāvaḥ svaḥ dharmaḥ iti tathābhūtāḥ pramāṇena pratipadyante iti tathābhūta viṣayakam hi pramāṇam iti imau khalu niyoga pratiṣedhau bhavatā deśitau kāca abhra paṭala ādi vat vā kuḍya ādibhiḥ apratighātaḥ bhavatu kuḍya ādi vat vā kāca abhra paṭala ādibhiḥ apratighātaḥ mā bhūt iti na dṛṣṭa anumitāḥ khalu ime dravya dharmāḥ pratighāta apratighātayoḥ hi upalabdhī vyavasthāpike vyavahita anupalabdhyā anumīyate kuḍya ādibhiḥ pratighātaḥ vyavahita upalabdhyā anumīyate kāca abhra paṭala ādibhiḥ apratighātaḥ iti 
[0781,i_0781,iii]	atha api khalu ekam idam indriyam bahūni indriyāṇi vā kutas saṃśayaḥ sthāna anya tve nānātvāt avayavi nānā sthāna tvāt ca saṃśayaḥ bahūni dravyāṇi nānā sthānāni dṛśyante nānā sthānaḥ ca san ekaḥ avayavī ca iti tena indriyeṣu bhinna sthāneṣu saṃśayaḥ iti 
[0783,i_0783,iv]	ekam indriyam tvac avyatirekāt tvac ekam indriyam iti āha kasmāt avyatirekāt na tvacā kiñcid indriya adhiṣṭhānam na prāptam na ca asatyām tvaci kiñcid viṣaya grahaṇam bhavati yayā satva indriya sthānāni vyāptāni yasyām ca satyām viṣaya grahaṇam bhavati sā tvac ekam indriyam iti na indriya antara artha anupalabdheḥ sparśa upalabdhi lakṣaṇāyām satyām tvaci gṛhyamāṇe tvac indriyeṇa sparśe indriya antara arthāḥ rūpa ādayaḥ na gṛhyante andhādibhiḥ na sparśa grāhakāt indriyāt indriya antaram asti iti sparśa vat andhādibhiḥ gṛhyeran rūpa ādayaḥ na ca gṛhyante tasmāt na ekam indriyam tvac iti 
[0784,i_0784,ii]	tvac avayava viśeṣeṇa dhūma upalabdhi vat tad upalabdhiḥ yathā tvacaḥ avayava viśeṣaḥ kaścid cakṣuṣi sannikṛṣṭaḥ dhūma sparśam gṛhṇāti na anyaḥ evam tvacaḥ avayava viśeṣāḥ rūpa ādi grāhakāḥ teṣām upaghātāt andhādibhiḥ na gṛhyante rūpa ādayaḥ iti vyāhata tvāt ahetuḥ tvac avyatirekāt ekam indriyam iti uktvā tvac avayava viśeṣeṇa dhūma upalabdhi vat rūpa ādi upalabdhiḥ iti ucyate evam ca sati nānā bhūtāni viṣaya grāhakāṇi viṣaya vyavasthānāt tad bhāve viṣaya grahaṇasya bhāvāt tad upaghāte ca abhāvāt tathā ca pūrvaḥ vādaḥ uttareṇa vādeṇa vyāhanyate iti sandigdhaḥ ca avyatirekaḥ pṛthivī ādibhiḥ api bhūtaiḥ indriya adhiṣṭhānāni vyāptāni na ca teṣu asatsu viṣaya grahaṇam bhavati iti tasmāt na tvac anyat vā sarva viṣayam ekam indriyam iti 
[0785,i_0785,ii]	na yugapad artha anupalabdheḥ ātmā manasā sambadhyate manaḥ indriyeṇa indriyam sarva arthaiḥ sannikṛṣṭam iti ātma indriya manortha sannikarṣebhyaḥ yugapad grahaṇāni syuḥ na ca yugapad rūpa ādayaḥ gṛhyante tasmāt na ekam indriyam sarva viṣayam asti iti asāha caryāt ca viṣaya grahaṇānām na ekam indriyam sarva viṣayakam sāhacarye hi viṣaya grahaṇānām andha ādi anupapattiḥ iti 
[0786,i_0787,i]	vipratiṣedhāt ca na tvac ekā na khalu tvac ekam indriyam vyāghātāt tvacā rūpāṇi aprāptāni gṛhyante iti aprāpya kāri tve sparśa ādiṣu api evam prasaṅgaḥ sparśa ādīnām ca prāptānām grahaṇāt rūpa ādīnām prāptānām grahaṇam iti prāptam prāpya aprāpya kāritvam iti ced āvaraṇa anupapatteḥ viṣaya mātrasya grahaṇam atha api manyeta prāptāḥ sparśa ādayaḥ tvacā gṛhyante rūpāṇi tu aprāptāni iti evam sati na asti āvaraṇam āvaraṇa anupapatteḥ ca rūpa mātrasya grahaṇam vyavahitasya ca avyavahitasya ca iti dūra antika anuvidhānam ca rūpa upalabdhi anupalabdhyoḥ na syāt aprāptam tvacā gṛhyate rūpam iti dūre rūpasya agrahaṇam antike ca grahaṇam iti etat na syāt iti 
[0787,ii_0788,i]	pratiṣedhāt ca nānātva siddhau sthāpanā hetuḥ api upādīyate indriya artha pañcatvāt arthaḥ prayojanam tat pañcavidham indriyāṇām sparśanena indriyeṇa sparśa grahaṇe sati na tena eva rūpam gṛhyate iti rūpa grahaṇa prayojanam cakṣuḥ anumīyate sparśa rūpa grahaṇe ca tābhyām eva na gandhaḥ gṛhyate iti gandha grahaṇa prayojanam ghrāṇam anumīyate trayāṇām grahaṇe na taiḥ eva rasaḥ gṛhyate iti rasa grahaṇa prayojanam rasanam anumīyate na ca caturṇām grahaṇe taiḥ eva śabdaḥ śrūyate iti śabda grahaṇa prayojanam śrotram anumīyate evam indriya prayojanasya anitaretara sādhana sādhya tvāt pañca eva indriyāṇi 
[0789,i_0789,ii]	na tad artha bahu tvāt na khalu indriya artha pañcatvāt pañca indriyāṇi iti sidhyati kasmāt teṣām arthānām bahu tvāt bahavaḥ khalu ime indriya arthāḥ sparśāḥ tāvat śīta uṣṇa an uṣṇa aśītāḥ iti rūpāṇi śukla harita ādīni gandhāḥ iṣṭa aniṣṭa upekṣaṇīyāḥ rasāḥ kaṭuka ādayaḥ śabdāḥ varṇa ātmānaḥ dhvani mātrāḥ ca bhinnāḥ tat yasya indriya artha pañcatvāt pañca indriyāṇi tasya indriya artha bahu tvāt bahūni indriyāṇi prasajyante iti 
[0789,iii_0790,i]	gandha tva ādi avyatirekāt gandha ādīnām apratiṣedhaḥ gandha tva ādibhiḥ sva sāmānyaiḥ kṛta vyavasthānām gandha ādīnām yāni gandha ādi grahaṇāni tāni asamāna sādhana sādhya tvāt grāhaka antarāṇi na prayojayanti artha samūhaḥ anumāna muktaḥ na artha eka deśaḥ artha eka deśam ca āśritya viṣaya pañcatva mātram bhavān pratiṣedhati tasmāt ayuktaḥ ayam pratiṣedhaḥ iti 
[0790,ii]	katham punar gandha tva ādibhiḥ sva sāmānyaiḥ kṛta vyavasthā gandha ādayaḥ iti sparśaḥ khalu ayam trividhaḥ śītaḥ uṣṇaḥ anuṣṇa aśītaḥ ca sparśa tvena sva sāmānyena saṃgṛhītaḥ gṛhyamāṇe ca śīta sparśe na uṣṇasya anuṣṇa aśītasya vā sparśasya grahaṇam grāhaka antaram prayojayati sparśa bhedānām eka sādhana sādhya tvāt yena eva śīta sparśaḥ gṛhyate tena eva itarau api iti evam gandha tvena gandhānām rūpa tvena rūpāṇām rasa tvena rasānām śabda tvena śabdānām iti gandha ādi grahaṇāni punar asamāna sādhana sādhya tvāt grāhaka antarāṇām prayojakāni tasmāt upapannam indriya artha pañcatvāt pañca indriyāṇi iti 
[0790,iii_0790,v]	yadi sāmānyam saṅgrāhakam prāptam indriyāṇām viṣaya tva avyatirekāt eka tvam viṣaya tvena hi sāmānyena gandha ādayaḥ saṅgṛhītāḥ iti 
[0791,i_0791,ii]	na buddhi lakṣaṇa adhiṣṭhāna gati ākṛti jñāti pañcatvebhyaḥ na khalu viṣaya tvena sāmānyena kṛta vyavasthāḥ viṣayāḥ grāhaka antara nirapekṣāḥ eka sādhana grāhyāḥ anumīyante anumīyante ca pañca gandha ādayaḥ gandha tva ādibhiḥ sva sāmānyaiḥ kṛta vyavasthāḥ indriya antara grāhyāḥ tasmāt asambaddham etat ayam eva ca arthaḥ anūdyate buddhi lakṣaṇa pañcatvāt iti 
[0791,iii_0792,i]	buddhayaḥ eva lakṣaṇāni viṣaya grahaṇa liṅga tvāt indriyāṇām tat etat indriya artha pañcatvāt iti etasmin sūtre kṛta bhāṣyam iti tasmāt buddhi lakṣaṇa pañcatvāt pañca indriyāṇi adhiṣṭhānāni api khalu pañca indriyāṇām sarva śarīra adhiṣṭhānam sparśanam sparśa grahaṇa liṅgam kṛṣṇasāra adhiṣṭhānam cakṣuḥ bahis niḥsṛtam rūpa grahaṇa liṅgam nāsādhiṣṭhānam ghrāṇam jihvā adhiṣṭhānam rasanam karṇa chidra adhiṣṭhānam śrotram gandha rasa rūpa sparśa śabda grahaṇa liṅga tvāt iti 
[0792,ii_0793,i]	gati bhedāt api indriya bhedaḥ kṛṣṇasāra upanibaddham cakṣuḥ bahis niḥsṛtya rūpa adhikaraṇāni dravyāṇi prāpnoti sparśana ādīni tu indriyāṇi viṣayāḥ eva āśraya upasarpaṇāt pratyāsīdanti santāna vṛttyā śabdasya śrotra pratyāsattiḥ iti ākṛtiḥ khalu parimāṇam iyattā sā pañcadhā sva sthāna mātrāṇi ghrāṇa rasana sparśanāni viṣaya grahaṇena anumeyāni cakṣuḥ kṛṣṇasāra āśrayam bahis niḥsṛtam viṣaya vyāpi śrotram na anyat ākāśāt tat ca vibhu śabda mātra anubhava anumā iyam puruṣa saṃskāra upagrahaṇāt ca adhiṣṭhāna niyamena śabdasya vyañjakam iti jātiḥ iti yonim pracakṣate pañca khalu indriya yonayaḥ pṛthivī ādīni bhūtāni tasmāt prakṛti pañcatvāt api pañca indriyāṇi iti siddham 
[0793,ii_0793,iv]	katham punar jñāyate bhūta prakṛtīni indriyāṇi na avyakta prakṛtīni iti bhūta guṇa viśeṣa upalabdheḥ tādātmyam dṛṣṭaḥ hi vāyu ādīnām bhūtānām guṇa viśeṣa abhivyakti niyamaḥ vāyuḥ sparśa vyañjakaḥ āpaḥ rasa vyañjikāḥ tejaḥ rūpa vyañjakam pārthivam kiñcid dravyam kasyacid dravyasya gandha vyañjakam asti ca ayam indriyāṇām bhūta guṇa viśeṣa upalabdhi niyamaḥ tena bhūta guṇa viśeṣa upalabdheḥ manyāmahe bhūta prakṛtīni indriyāṇi na avyakta prakṛtīni iti 
[0795,i]	gandha ādayaḥ pṛthivī ādi guṇāḥ iti uddiṣṭam uddeśaḥ ca pṛthivī ādīnām eka guṇa tve ca aneka guṇa tve ca samānaḥ iti atas āha gandha rasa rūpa sparśa śabdānām sparśa paryantāḥ pṛthivyāḥ 
[0795,iii_0796,i]	ap tejaḥ vāyūnām pūrvam pūrvam apohya ākāśasya uttaraḥ sparśa paryantānām iti vibhakti vipariṇāmaḥ ākāśasya uttaraḥ śabdaḥ sparśa paryantebhyaḥ iti katham tarhi tarabnirdeśaḥ svatantra viniyoga sāmarthyāt tena uttara śabdasya para artha abhidhānam vijñāyate uddeśa sūtre hi sparśa paryantebhyaḥ paraḥ śabdaḥ iti tantram vā sparśasya vivakṣita tvāt sparśa paryanteṣu niyukteṣu yaḥ anyaḥ tad uttaraḥ śabdaḥ iti 
[0797,i_0797,ii]	na sarva guṇa anupalabdheḥ na ayam guṇa niyogaḥ sādhuḥ kasmāt yasya bhūtasya ye guṇāḥ na te tad ātmakena indriyeṇa sarve upalabhyante pārthivena hi ghrāṇena sparśa paryantāḥ na gṛhyante gandhaḥ eva ekaḥ gṛhyate evam śeṣeṣu api iti 
[0797,iii_0798,iii]	katham tarhi ime guṇāḥ viniyoktavyāḥ iti ekaika śyena uttara uttara guṇa sadbhāvāt uttara uttarāṇām tad anupalabdhiḥ gandha ādīnām ekaikaḥ yathākramam pṛthivī ādīnām ekaikasya guṇaḥ atas tad anupalabdhiḥ teṣām tayoḥ tasya ca anupalabdhiḥ ghrāṇena rasa rūpa sparśānām rasanena rūpa sparśayoḥ cakṣuṣā sparśasya iti katham tarhi aneka guṇāni bhūtāni gṛhyante iti saṃsargāt ca aneka guṇa grahaṇam ap ādi saṃsargāt ca pṛthivyām rasa ādayaḥ gṛhyante evam śeṣeṣu api iti 
[0799,i_0799,iii]	niyamaḥ tarhi na prāpnoti saṃsargasya aniyamāt caturguṇā pṛthivī triguṇāḥ āpaḥ dviguṇam tejaḥ ekaguṇaḥ vāyuḥ iti niyamaḥ ca upapadyate katham viṣṭam hi aparam pareṇa pṛthivī ādīnām pūrva pūrvam uttareṇa uttareṇa viṣṭam atas saṃsarga niyamaḥ iti tat ca etat bhūta sṛṣṭau veditavyam na etarhi iti 
[0800,i_0800,ii]	na pārthiva āpyayoḥ pratyakṣa tvāt na iti tri sūtrīm pratyācaṣṭe kasmāt pārthivasya dravyasya api asya ca pratyakṣaṭvāt mahatvā aneka dravya tvāt rūpāt ca upalabdhiḥ iti taijasam eva dravyam pratyakṣam syāt na pārthivam āpyam vā rūpa abhāvāt taijasa vat tu pārthiva āpyayoḥ pratyakṣa tvāt na saṃsargāt aneka guṇa grahaṇam bhūtānām iti bhūta antara rūpa kṛtam ca pārthiva āpyayoḥ pratyakṣa tvam bruvataḥ pratyakṣaḥ vāyuḥ prasajyate niyame vā kāraṇam ucyatām iti 
[0801,i]	rasayoḥ vā pārthiva āpyayoḥ pratyakṣa tvāt pārthivaḥ rasaḥ ṣaḍvidhaḥ āpyaḥ madhuraḥ eva na ca etat saṃsargāt bhavitum arhati rūpayoḥ vā pārthiva āpyayoḥ pratyakṣa tvāt taijasa rūpa anugṛhītayoḥ saṃsarge hi vyañjakam eva rūpam na vyaṅgyam asti iti eka anekavidha tve ca pārthiva āpyayoḥ pratyakṣa tvāt rūpayoḥ pārthivam harita lohita pīta ādi anekavidham rūpam āpyam tu śuklam aprakāśakam na ca etat eka guṇānām saṃsarge sati upapadyate iti udāharaṇa mātram ca etat atas param prapañcaḥ 
[0801,ii_0801,iii]	sparśayoḥ vā pārthiva taijasayoḥ pratyakṣa tvāt pārthivaḥ anuṣṇa aśītaḥ sparśaḥ uṣṇaḥ taijasaḥ pratyakṣaḥ na ca etat eka guṇānām anuṣṇa aśīta sparśena vāyunā saṃsargeṇa upapadyate iti atha vā pārthiva āpyayoḥ dravyayoḥ vyvasthita guṇayoḥ pratyakṣa tvāt caturguṇam pārthivam dravyam triguṇam āpyam pratyakṣam tena tad kāraṇam anumīyate tathābhūtam iti tasya kāryam liṅgam kāraṇa bhāvāt dhi kārya bhāvaḥ iti evam taijasa vāyavyayoḥ dravyayoḥ pratyakṣa tvāt guṇa vyavasthāyāḥ tad kāraṇe dravye vyavasthā anumānam iti 
[0801,iv]	dṛṣṭaḥ ca vivekaḥ pārthiva āpyayoḥ pratyakṣa tvāt pārthivam dravyam ap ādibhiḥ viyuktam pratyakṣataḥ gṛhyate āpyam ca parābhyām taijasam ca vāyunā na ca ekaika guṇam gṛhyate iti niranumānam tu viṣṭam hi aparam pareṇa iti etat iti na atra liṅgam anumāpakam gṛhyate iti yena etat evam pratipadyemahi 
[0801,v]	yat ca uktam viṣṭam hi aparam pareṇa iti bhūta sṛṣṭau veditavyam na sāmpratam iti niyama kāraṇa abhāvāt ayuktam dṛṣṭam ca sāmpratam aparam pareṇa viṣṭam iti vāyunā ca viṣṭam tejaḥ iti viṣṭa tvam saṃyogaḥ sa ca dvayoḥ samānaḥ vāyunā ca viṣṭa tvāt sparśa vat tejaḥ na tu tejasā viṣṭa tvāt rūpavān vāyuḥ iti niyama kāraṇam na asti iti dṛṣṭam ca taijasena sparśena vāyavyasya sparśasya abhibhavāt agrahaṇam iti na ca tena eva tasya abhibhavaḥ iti 
[0801,vi_0801,ix]	tat evam nyāya viruddham pravādam pratiṣidhya na sarva guṇa anupalabdheḥ iti coditam samādhīyate pūrva pūrva guṇa utkarṣāt tat tat pradhānam tasmāt na sarva guṇa upalabdhiḥ ghrāṇa ādīnām pūrvam pūrvam gandha ādeḥ guṇasya utkarṣāt tat tat pradhānam kā pradhāna tā viṣaya grāhaka tvam kaḥ guṇa utkarṣaḥ abhivyaktau samartha tvam yathā bāhyānām pārthiva āpya taijasānām dravyāṇām caturguṇa triguṇa dviguṇānām na sarva guṇa vyañjaka tvam gandha rasa rūpa utkarṣāt tu yathākramam gandha rasa rūpa vyañjaka tvam evam ghrāṇa rasana cakṣuṣām caturguṇa triguṇa dviguṇānām na sarva guṇa grāhaka tvam gandha rasa rūpa utkarṣāt tu yathākramam gandha rasa rūpa grāhaka tvam tasmāt ghrāṇa ādibhiḥ na sarveṣām guṇānām upalabdhiḥ iti yaḥ tu pratijānīte gandha guṇa tvāt ghrāṇam gandhasya grāhakam evam rasanā ādiṣu api iti tasya yathā guṇa yogam ghrāṇa ādibhiḥ guṇa grahaṇam prasajyate iti 
[0804,i_0804,iii]	kiṃkṛtam punar vyavasthānam kiñcid pārthivam indriyam na sarvāṇi kānicid āpya taijasa vāyavyāni indriyāṇi na sarvāṇi iti tad vyavasthānam tu bhūyas tvāt artha nirvṛtti samarthasya pravibhaktasya dravyasya saṃsargaḥ puruṣa saṃskāra kāritaḥ bhūyas tvam dṛṣṭaḥ hi prakarṣe bhūyas tva śabdaḥ yathā prakṛṣṭaḥ viṣayaḥ bhūyān iti ucyate yathā pṛthak artha kriyā samarthāni puruṣa saṃskāra vaśāt viṣa oṣadhi maṇi prabhṛtīni dravyāṇi nirvartyante na sarvam sarva artham evam pṛthak viṣaya grahaṇa samarthāni ghrāṇa ādīni nirvartyante na sarva viṣaya grahaṇa samarthāni iti 
[0805,i_0805,iii]	sva guṇān na upalabhante indriyāṇi kasmāt iti ced sa guṇānām indriya bhāvāt svān gandha ādīn na upalabhante ghrāṇa ādīni kena kāraṇena iti ced sva guṇaiḥ saha ghrāṇa ādīnām indriya bhāvāt ghrāṇam svena gandhena samāna artha kāriṇā saha bāhyam gandham gṛhṇāti tasya sva gandha grahaṇam saha kāri vaikalyāt na bhavati evam śeṣāṇām api 
[0805,iv_0806,i]	yadi punar gandhaḥ sahakārī ca syāt ghrāṇasya grāhyaḥ ca iti atas āha tena eva tasya agrahaṇāt ca na guṇa upalabdhiḥ indriyāṇām yaḥ brūte yathā bāhyam dravyam cakṣuṣā gṛhyate tathā tena eva cakṣuṣā tat eva cakṣuḥ gṛhyatām iti tādṛś idam tulyaḥ hi ubhayatra pratipatti hetu abhāvaḥ iti 
[0806,ii_0806,iii]	na śabda guṇa upalabdheḥ sva guṇān na upalabhantaḥ indriyāṇi iti etat na bhavati upalabhyate hi sva guṇaḥ śabdaḥ śrotreṇa iti 
[0807,i_0808,i]	tad upalabdhiḥ itaretara dravya guṇa vaidharmyāt na śabdena guṇena sa guṇam ākāśam indriyam bhavati na śabdaḥ śabdasya vyañjakaḥ na ca ghrāṇa ādīnām sva guṇa grahaṇam pratyakṣam na api anumīyate anumīyate tu śrotreṇa ākāśena śabdasya grahaṇam śabda guṇa tvam ca ākāśasya iti pariśeṣaḥ ca anumānam veditavyam ātmā tāvat śrotā na karaṇam manasaḥ śrotra tve badhira tva abhāvaḥ pṛthivī ādīnām ghrāṇa ādi bhāve sāmarthyam śrotra bhāve ca asāmarthyam asti ca idam śrotram ākāśam ca śiṣyate pariśeṣāt ākāśam śrotram iti 
[0809,i_0809,iii]	parīkṣitāni indriyāṇi arthāḥ ca buddheḥ idānīm parīkṣā kramaḥ sā kim anityā nityā vā iti kutas saṃśayaḥ karma ākāśa sādharmyāt saṃśayaḥ asparśavat tvam tābhyām samānaḥ dharmaḥ upalabhyate buddhau viśeṣaḥ ca upajana apāya dharmavat tvam viparyayaḥ ca yathāsvam anitya nityayoḥ tasyām buddau na upalabhyate tena saṃśayaḥ iti 
[0809,iv_0810,i]	anupapanna rūpaḥ khalu ayam saṃśayaḥ sarva śarīriṇām hi pratyātma vedanīyā anityā buddhiḥ sukha ādi vat bhavati ca saṃvittiḥ jñāsyāmi jānāmi ajñāsiṣam iti na ca upajana apāyau antareṇa traikālya vyāktiḥ tatas ca traikālya vyakteḥ anityā buddhiḥ iti etat śiddham pramāṇa siddham ca idam śāstare api uktam indriya artha sannikarṣa utpannam yugapad jñāna anutpattiḥ manasaḥ liṅgam iti evamādi tasmāt saṃśaya prakriyā anupapattiḥ iti 
[0810,ii_0811,ii]	dṛṣṭi pravāda upālambha arthan tu prakaraṇam evam hi paśyantaḥ pravadanti sāṅkhyāḥ puruṣasya antaḥkaraṇa bhūtāḥ nityā buddhiḥ iti sādhanam ca pracakṣate viṣaya pratyabhijñānāt kim punar idam pratyabhijñānam yam pūrvam ajñāsiṣam artham tam imam jānāmi iti jñānyoḥ samāne arthe pratisandhi jñānam pratyabhijñānam etat ca avasthitāyāḥ buddheḥ upapannam nānātve tu buddhi bhedeṣu utpanna apavargiṣu pratyabhijñāna anupapattiḥ na anya jñātam anyaḥ pratyabhijānāti iti 
[0811,iii_0812,i]	sādhya sama tvāt ahetuḥ yathā khalu nitya tvam buddheḥ sādhyam evam pratyabhijñānam api iti kim kāraṇam cetana dharmasya karaṇe anupapattiḥ puruṣa dharmaḥ khalu ayam jñānam darśanam upalabdhiḥ bodhaḥ pratyayaḥ adhyavasāyaḥ iti cetanaḥ hi pūrva jñātam artham pratyabhijānāti tasya etasmāt dhetoḥ nitya tvam yuktam iti karaṇa caitanya abhyupagame tu cetana svarūpam vacanīyam na anirdiṣṭa svarūpam ātma antaram śakyam asti iti pratipattum jñānam ced buddheḥ antaḥkaraṇasya abhyupagamyate cetanasya idānīm kim svarūpam kaḥ dharmaḥ kim tattvam jñānena ca buddhau vartamānena ayam cetanaḥ kim karoti iti 
[0812,ii_0813,i]	cetayate iti ced na jñānāt artha antara vacanam puruṣaḥ cetayate buddhiḥ jānāti iti na idam jñānāt artha antaram ucyate cetayate jānīte buddhyate paśyati upalabhate iti ekaḥ ayam arthaḥ iti buddhiḥ jñpayati iti ced addhā jānīte puruṣaḥ buddhiḥ jñāpayati iti satyam etat evam ca abhyupagame jñānam puruṣasya iti siddham bhavati na buddheḥ antaḥkaraṇasya iti prati puruṣam ca śabda antara vyavasthā pratijñāne pratiṣedha hetu vacanam yaḥ ca pratijānīte kaścid puruṣaḥ cetayate kaścid buddhyate kaścid upalabhate kaścid paśyati iti puruṣa antarāṇi khalu imāni cetanaḥ boddha upalabdhā draṣṭā iti na ekasya ete dharmāḥ iti atra kaḥ pratiṣedha hetuḥ iti 
[0813,ii_0815,i]	arthasya abhedaḥ iti ced samānam abhinna arthāḥ ete śabdāḥ iti tatra vyavasthā anupapattiḥ iti evam ced manyase samānam bhavati puruṣaḥ cetayate buddhiḥ jānīte iti atra api arthaḥ na bhidyate tatra ubhayoḥ cetana tvāt anyatara lopaḥ iti yadi punar budhyate anayā iti bodhanam buddhiḥ manaḥ eva ucyate tat ca nityam astu etat evam na tu manasaḥ viṣaya pratyabhijñānāt nitya tvam dṛṣṭam hi karaṇa bhede jñātuḥ eka tvāt pratyabhijñānam savya dṛṣṭasya itareṇa pratyabhijñānāt iti cakṣuḥ vat pradīpa vat ca pradīpa antara dṛṣṭasya pradīpa antareṇa pratyabhijñānam iti tasmāt jñātuḥ ayam nitya tve hetuḥ iti 
[0815,ii_0815,iv]	yat ca manyate buddheḥ avasthitāyāḥ yathā viṣayam vṛttayaḥ jñānāni niścaranti vṛttiḥ ca vṛttimataḥ na anyā iti tat ca na yugapad agrahaṇāt vṛtti vṛttimatoḥ ananya tve vṛttimataḥ avasthānāt vṛttīnām avasthānam iti yāni imāni viṣaya grahaṇāni tāni avatiṣṭantaḥ iti yugapad viṣayāṇām grahaṇam prasajyate iti 
[0816,i_0816,ii]	apratyabhijñāne ca vināśa prasaṅgaḥ atīte ca pratyabhijñāne vṛttimān api atītaḥ iti antaḥkaraṇasya vināśaḥ prasajyate viparyaye ca nānātvam iti 
[0816,iii_0816,v]	avibhu ca ekam manaḥ paryāyeṇa indriyaiḥ saṃyujyate iti krama vṛtti tvāt ayugapad grahaṇam indriya arthānām vṛtti vṛttimatoḥ nānātvam iti 
[0817,i_0817,ii]	apratyabhijñānam ca viṣaya antara vyāsaṅgāt apratyabhijñānam anupalabdhiḥ anupalabdhiḥ ca kasyācid arthasya viṣaya antara vyāsakte manasi upapadyate vṛtti vṛttimatoḥ nānātvāt eka tve hi anarthakaḥ vyāsaṅgaḥ iti 
[0817,iii_0818,i]	vibhu tve ca antaḥkaraṇasya paryāyeṇa indriyaiḥ saṃyogaḥ na gati abhāvāt prāptāni indriyāṇi antaḥkaraṇena iti prāpti arthasya gamanasya abhāvaḥ tatra krama vṛtti tva abhāvāt ayugapad grahaṇa anupapattiḥ iti gati abhāvāt ca pratiṣiddham vibhunaḥ antaḥkaraṇasya ayugapad grahaṇam na liṅga antareṇa anumīyate iti yathā cakṣuṣaḥ gatiḥ pratiṣiddhā sannikṛṣṭa viprakṛṣṭayoḥ tulya kāla grahaṇāt pāṇi candramasoḥ vyavadhānena pratīghāte saḥ anumīyate iti saḥ ayam na antar karaṇe vivādaḥ na tasya nitya tve 
[0819,i]	siddham hi manaḥ antaḥkaraṇam nityam ca iti kva tarhi vivādaḥ tasya vibhu tve tat ca pramāṇataḥ anupalabdheḥ pratiṣiddham iti ekam ca antaḥkaraṇam nānā ca etāḥ jñāna ātmakāḥ vṛttayaḥ cakṣuḥ vijñānam ghrāṇa vijñānam rūpa vijñānam gandha vijñānam etat ca vṛtti vṛtti matoḥ eka tve anupapannam iti puruṣaḥ jānīte na antaḥkaraṇam iti etena viṣaya antara vyāsaṅgaḥ pratyuktaḥ viṣaya antara grahaṇa lakṣaṇaḥ viṣaya antara vyāsaṅgaḥ puruṣasya na antaḥkaraṇasya iti kenacid indriyeṇa sannidhiḥ kenacid asannidhiḥ iti ayam tu vyāsaṅgaḥ anujñāyate manasaḥ iti 
[0820,i_0822,i]	ekam antaḥkaraṇam nānā vṛttayaḥ iti sati abhede vṛtteḥ idam ucyate sphaṭika anyatva abhimāna vat tad anyatva abhimānaḥ tasyām vṛttau nānātva abhimānaḥ yathā dravya antara upahite sphaṭike anyatva abhimānaḥ nīlaḥ lohitaḥ iti evam viṣaya antara upadhānāt iti na hetu abhāvāt sphaṭika anyatva abhimāna vat ayam jñāneṣu nānātva abhimānaḥ gauṇaḥ na punar gandha ādi anyatva abhimāna vat iti hetuḥ na asti hetu abhāvāt anupapannaḥ iti samānaḥ hetu abhāvaḥ iti ced na jñānānām krameṇa upajana apāya darśanāt krameṇa hi indriya artheṣu jñānāni upajāyante ca apayanti ca iti dṛśyate tasmāt gandha ādi anyatva abhimāna vat ayam jñāneṣu nānātva abhimānaḥ iti 
[0823,i_0824,i]	sphaṭika anyatva abhimāna vat iti etat amṛṣyamāṇaḥ kṣaṇika vādi āha sphaṭike api apara apara utpatteḥ kṣaṇika tvāt vyaktīnām ahetuḥ sphaṭikasya abhedena avasthitasya upadhāna bhedāt nānātva abhimānaḥ iti ayam avidyamāna hetukaḥ pakṣaḥ kasmāt sphaṭike api apara apara utpatteḥ sphaṭike api anyāḥ vyaktayaḥ utpadyante anyāḥ nirudhyante iti katham kṣaṇika tvāt vyaktīnām kṣaṇaḥ ca alpīyān kālaḥ kṣaṇa sthitikāḥ kṣaṇikāḥ katham punar gamyate kṣaṇikāḥ vyaktayaḥ iti upacaya apacaya prabandha darśanāt śarīra ādiṣu pakti nirvṛttasya āhāra rasasya śarīre rudhira ādi bhāvena upacayaḥ apacayaḥ ca prabandhena pravarttate upacayāt vyaktīnām utpādaḥ apacayāt vyakti nirodhaḥ evam ca sati avayava pariṇāma bhedena vṛddhiḥ śarīrasya kāla antare gṛhyate iti saḥ ayam vyakti viśeṣa dharmaḥ vyakti mātre veditavyaḥ iti 
[0825,i_0825,ii]	niyama hetu abhāvāt yathādarśanam abhyanujñā sarvāsu vyaktiṣu upacaya apacaya prabandhaḥ śarīra vat iti na ayam niyamaḥ kasmāt hetu abhāvāt na atra pratyakṣam anumānam vā pratipādakam asti iti tasmāt yathādarśanam abhyanujñā yatra yatra upacaya apacaya prabandhaḥ dṛśyate tatra tatra vyaktīnām apara apara utpattiḥ upacaya apacaya prabandha darśanena abhyanujñāyate yathā śarīra ādiṣu yatra yatra na dṛśyate tatra tatra pratyākhyāyate yathā grāva prabhṛtiṣu sphaṭike api upacaya apacaya prabandhaḥ na dṛśyate tasmāt ayuktam sphaṭike api apara aprotpattiḥ iti yathā ca arkasya kaṭu kimnā sarva dravyāṇām kaṭu kimānām āpādayet tādṛś etat iti 
[0825,iii_0827,i]	yaḥ ca aśeṣa nirodhena apūrva utpādam niranvayam dravya santāne kṣaṇika tām manyate tasya etat na utpatti vināśa kāraṇa upalabdheḥ utpatti kāraṇam tāvat upalabhyate avayava upacayaḥ valmīka ādīnām vināśa kāraṇam ca upalabhyate ghaṭa ādīnām avayava vibhāgaḥ yasya tu anapacita avayavam nirudhyate anupacita avayavam ca utpadyate tasya aśeṣa nirodhe niranvaye vā apūrva utpāde na kāraṇam ubhayatra api upalabhyate iti 
[0827,ii_0827,iii]	kṣīra vināśe kāraṇa anupalabdhi vat dadhi utpatti vat ca tad upapattiḥ yathā anupalabhyamānam kṣīra vināśa kāraṇam dadhi utpatti kāraṇam ca abhyanujñāyate tathā sphaṭike para aparāsu vyaktiṣu vināśa kāraṇam utpāda kāraṇam ca abhyanujñeyam iti 
[0830,i_0830,ii]	liṅgataḥ grahaṇāt na anupalabdhiḥ kṣīra vināśa liṅgam kṣīra vināśa kāraṇam dadhi utpatti liṅgam dadhi utpatti kāraṇam ca gṛhyate atas na anupalabdhiḥ viparyayaḥ tu sphaṭika ādiṣu dravyeṣu apara apara utpattau vyaktīnām na liṅgam asti iti anutpattiḥ eva iti 
[0846,i_0846,iv]	atra kaścid parihāram āha na payasaḥ pariṇāma guṇa antara prādurbhāvāt payasaḥ pariṇāmaḥ na vināśaḥ iti ekaḥ āha pariṇāmaḥ ca avasthitasya dravyasya pūrva dharma nivṛttau dharma antara utpattiḥ iti guṇa antara prādurbhāvaḥ iti aparaḥ āha satā dravyasya pūrva guṇa nivṛttau guṇa antaram utpadyate iti sa khalu eka pakṣībhāvaḥ iva 
[0847,i_0847,iii]	atra tu pratiṣedhaḥ vyūha antarāt dravya antara utpatti darśanam pūrva dravya nivṛtteḥ anumānam saṃmūrchana lakṣaṇāt avayava vyūhāt dravya antare dadhni utpanne gṛhyamāṇe pūrvam payaḥ dravyam avayava vibhāgebhyaḥ nivṛttam iti anumīyate yathā mṛd avayavānām vyūha antarāt dravya antare sthālyām utpannāyām pūrvam mṛd piṇḍa dravyam mṛdavayava vibhāgebhyaḥ nivarttate iti mṛdvat ca avayava anvayaḥ payaḥ dadhnoḥ na aśeṣa nirodhe niranvayaḥ dravya antara utpādaḥ ghaṭate iti 
[0848,i_0848,iii]	abhyanujñāya ca niṣkāraṇam kṣīra vināśam dadhi utpādam ca pratiṣedhaḥ ucyate kvacid vināśa kāraṇa anupalabdheḥ kvacid ca upalabdheḥ anekāntaḥ kṣīra dadhi vat niṣkāraṇau vināśa utpādau sphaṭika vyaktīnām iti na ayam ekāntaḥ iti kasmāt hetu abhāvāt na atra hetuḥ asti akāraṇau vināśa utpādau sphaṭika ādi vyaktīnām kṣīra dadhi vat na punar yathā vināśa kāraṇa bhāvāt kumbhasya vināśaḥ utpatti kāraṇa bhāvāt ca utpattiḥ evam sphaṭika ādi vyaktīnām vināśa utpatti kāraṇa bhāvāt vināśa utpatti bhāvaḥ iti 
[0849,i_0849,ii]	niradhiṣṭhānam ca dṛṣṭānta vacanam gṛhyamāṇayoḥ vināśa utpādayoḥ sphaṭika ādiṣu syāt ayam āśrayavān dṛṣṭāntaḥ kṣīra vināśa kāraṇa anupalabdhi vat dadhi utpatti vat ca iti tau tu na gṛhyete tasmāt niradhiṣṭhānaḥ ayam dṛṣṭāntaḥ iti abhyanujñāya ca sphaṭikasya utpāda vināśau yaḥ atra sādhakaḥ tasya abhyanujñānāt apratiṣedhaḥ kumbha vat na niṣkāraṇau vināśa utpādau sphaṭika ādīnām iti anujñeyaḥ ayam dṛṣṭāntaḥ pratiṣeddham aśakya tvāt kṣīra dadhi vat tu niṣkāraṇau vināśa utpādau iti śakyaḥ ayam pratiṣeddhum kāraṇataḥ vināśa utpatti darśanāt kṣīra dadhnoḥ vināśa utpattī paśyatā tad kāraṇam anumeyam kārya liṅgam hi kāraṇam iti 
[0850,i]	upapannam anityā buddhiḥ iti idam tu cintyate kasya iyam buddhiḥ ātma indriya manaḥ arthānām guṇaḥ iti prasiddhaḥ api khalu ayam arthaḥ parīkaṣa aśeṣam pravarttayāmi iti prakriyate saḥ ayam buddhau sannikarṣa utpatteḥ saṃśayaḥ viśeṣasya agrahaṇāt iti tatra ayam viśeṣaḥ na indriya arthayoḥ tad vināśe api jñāna avasthānāt 
[0850,ii_0851,i]	na indriyāṇām vā guṇaḥ jñānam teṣām vināśaḥ api jñānasya bhāvāt bhavati khalu idam indriye arthe ca vinaṣṭe jñānam adrākṣam iti na ca jñātari vinaṣṭe jñānam bhavitum arhati anyat khalu vai tat indriya artha sannikarṣa jam jñānam yat indriya artha vināśe na bhavati idam anyat ātma manaḥ sannikarṣa jam tasya yuktaḥ bhāvaḥ iti smṛtiḥ khalu iyam adrākṣam iti pūrva dṛṣṭa viṣayā na ca vijñātari naṣṭe pūrva upalabdheḥ smaraṇam yuktam na ca anya dṛṣṭam anyaḥ smarati na ca manasi jñātari abhyupagamyamāne śakyam indriya arthayoḥ jñātṛ tvam pratipādayitum 
[0851,ii_0852,i]	āstu tarhi manaḥ guṇāḥ jñānam yugapad jñeya anupalabdheḥ ca na manasaḥ yugapad jñeya anupalabdhiḥ antaḥkaraṇasya liṅgam tatra yugapad jñeyā anupalabdhyā yat anumīyate antaḥkaraṇam na tasya guṇaḥ jñānam kasya tarhi jñasya vaśitvāt vaśī jñātā vaśyam karaṇam jñāna guṇa tve ca karaṇa bhāva nivṛttiḥ ghrāṇa ādi sādhanasya ca jñātuḥ gandha ādi jñāna bhāvāt anumīyate antaḥkaraṇa sādhanasya sukha ādi jñānam smṛtiḥ ca iti tatra yat jñāna guṇam manaḥ saḥ ātmā yat tu sukha ādi upalabdhi sādhanam antaḥkaraṇam manaḥ tat iti saṃjñā bheda mātram na artha bhedaḥ iti 
[0853,i]	yugapad jñeya upalabdheḥ ca yoginaḥ iti vā ca arthaḥ yogī khalu ṛddhau prādurbhūtāyām vikaraṇa dharmāḥ nirmāya sa indriyāṇi śarīra antarāṇi teṣu yugapad jñeyāni upalabhate tat ca etat vibhau jñātarī upapadyate na aṇau manasi iti vibhu tve vā manasaḥ jñānasya na ātma guṇa tva pratiṣedhaḥ vibhu ca manaḥ tad antaḥkaraṇa bhūtam iti tasya sarva indriyaiḥ yugapad saṃyogāt yugapad jñānāni utpadyeran iti 
[0853,ii_0853,iii]	tad ātma guṇa tve api tulyam vibhuḥ ātmā sarva indriyaiḥ saṃyuktaḥ iti yugapad jñāna utpatti prasaṅgaḥ iti 
[0854,i_0854,ii]	indriyaiḥ manasaḥ sannikarṣa abhāvāt tad anutpattiḥ gandha ādi upalabdheḥ indriya artha sannikarṣa vat indriya manaḥ sannikarṣaḥ api kāraṇam tasya ca ayaugapadyam aṇu tvāt manasaḥ ayaugapadyāt anutpattiḥ yugapad jñānānām ātma guṇa tve api iti 
[0854,iii_0854,v]	yadi punar ātma indriya artha sannikarṣa mātrāt gandha ādi jñānam utpadyeta na utpatti kāraṇa anapadeśāt ātma indriya sannikarṣa mātrāt gandha ādi jñānam utpadyate iti na atra utpatti kāraṇam apadiśyate yena etat pratipadyemahi iti 
[0855,i_0855,ii]	vināśa kāraṇa anupalabdheḥ ca avasthāne tad nitya tva prasaṅgaḥ tad ātma guṇa tve api tulyam iti etat anena samuccīyate dvividhaḥ hi guṇa nāśa hetuḥ guṇānām āśraya abhāvaḥ virodhī ca guṇaḥ nitya tvāt ātmanaḥ anupapannaḥ pūrvaḥ virodhī ca buddheḥ guṇaḥ na gṛhyate tasmāt ātma guṇa tve sati buddheḥ nitya tva prasaṅgaḥ 
[0856,i_0856,ii]	anitya tva grahāt buddheḥ buddhi antarāt vināśaḥ śabdavat anityā buddhiḥ iti sarva śarīriṇām pratyātma vedanīyam etat gṛhyate ca buddhi santānaḥ tatra buddheḥ buddhi antaram virodhī guṇaḥ iti anumīyate yathā śabda santāne śabdaḥ śabda antara virodhi iti 
[0857,i_0857,iii]	asaṅkhyeyeṣu jñāna kāriteṣu saṃskāreṣu smṛti hetuṣu ātma samaveteṣu ātma manasoḥ ca sannikarṣe samāne smṛti hetau sati na kāraṇasya ayaugapadyam asti iti yugapad smṛtayaḥ prādurbhaveyuḥ yadi buddhiḥ ātma guṇaḥ syāt iti tatra kaścid sannikarṣasya ayaugapadyam upapādayiṣyan āha jñāna samaveta ātma pradeśa sannikarṣāt manasaḥ smṛti utpatteḥ na yugapad utpattiḥ jñāna sādhanaḥ saṃskāraḥ jñānam iti ucyate jñāna saṃskṛtaiḥ ātma pradeśaiḥ paryāyeṇa manaḥ sat nikṛṣyate ātma manaḥ sannikarṣāt smṛtayaḥ api paryāyeṇa bhavanti iti 
[0858,i_0858,ii]	na antar śarīra vṛtti tvāt manasaḥ sa dehasya ātmanaḥ manasā saṃyogaḥ vipacyamāna karma āśaya sahitaḥ jīvanam iṣyate tatra asya prāk prāyaṇāt antar śarīre vartamānasya manasaḥ śarīrāt bahis jñāna saṃskṛtaiḥ ātma pradeśaiḥ saṃyogaḥ na upapadyate iti 
[0859,i_0859,ii]	sādhya tvāt ahetuḥ vipacyamāna karma āśaya mātram jīvanam evam ca sati sādhyam antar śarīra vṛtti tvam manasaḥ iti 
[0859,iii_0859,iv]	smarataḥ śarīra dhāraṇa upapatteḥ apratiṣedhaḥ su smūrṣayā khalu ayam manaḥ praṇidadhānaḥ cirāt api kaṃcid artham smarati smarataḥ ca śarīra dhāraṇam dṛśyate ātma manaḥ sannikarṣa jaḥ ca prayatnaḥ dvividhaḥ dhārakaḥ prerakaḥ ca niḥsṛte ca śarīrāt bahis manāsi dhārakasya prayatnasya abhāvāt guru tvāt patanam syāt śarīrasya smarate iti 
[0860,i_0860,ii]	na tad ā āśu gati tvāt manasaḥ āśugati manaḥ tasya bahis śarīra ātma pradeśena jñāna saṃskṛtena sannikarṣaḥ pratyāgatasya ca prayatna utpādanam ubhayam yujyate iti utpādya vā dhārakam prayatnam śarīrāt niḥsaraṇam manasaḥ atas tatra upapannam dhāraṇam iti 
[0860,iii_0861,i]	na smaraṇa kāla aniyamāt kiñcid kṣipram smaryate kiñcid cireṇa yadā cireṇa tadā su smūrṣayā manasi dhāryamāṇe cintā prabandhe sati kasyacid arthasya liṅga bhūtasya cintanam ārādhitam smṛti hetuḥ bhavati tatra etat cira niścarite manasi na upapadyate iti śarīra saṃyoga anapekṣaḥ ca ātma manaḥ saṃyogaḥ na smṛti hetuḥ śarīrasya bhoga āyatana tvāt upabhoga āyatanam puruṣasya jñātuḥ śarīram na tatas niścaritasya manasaḥ ātma saṃyoga mātram jñāna sukha ādīnām utpattau kalpate kḷptau vā śarīra vaiyarthyam iti 
[0861,ii_0861,iii]	ātma preraṇa yadṛcchā jña tābhiḥ ca na saṃyoga viśeṣaḥ ātma preraṇena vā manasaḥ bahis śarīrāt saṃyoga viśeṣaḥ syāt yadṛcchayā vā ākasmika tayā jñatayā vā manasaḥ sarvathā ca anupapattiḥ katham smartavya tvāt icchātaḥ smaraṇāt jñānāsambhavāt ca yadi tāvat ātmā amuṣya arthasya smṛti hetuḥ saṃskāraḥ amuṣmin ātma deśe samavetaḥ tena manaḥ saṃyujyatām iti manaḥ prerayati tadā smṛtaḥ eva asau arthaḥ bhavati na smartavyaḥ na ca ātma pratyakṣaḥ ātma pradeśaḥ saṃskāraḥ vā tatra anupapanna ātma pratyakṣeṇa saṃvittiḥ iti su smūrṣayā ca ayam manaḥ praṇidadhānaḥ cirāt api kañcid artham smarati na akasmāt jña tvam ca manasaḥ na asti jñāna pratiṣedhāt iti 
[0862,i_0862,iii]	etat ca vyāsakta manasaḥ pāda vyathanena saṃyoga viśeṣeṇa samānam yadā khalu ayam vyāsakta manāḥ kvacid deśe śarkarayā kaṇṭakena vā pāda vyathanam āpnoti tadā ātma manaḥ saṃyoga viśeṣaḥ eṣitavyaḥ dṛṣṭam hi duḥkham duḥkha vedanam ca iti tatra ayam samānaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ yadṛcchayā tu na viśeṣaḥ nākasmikī kriyā na ākasmikaḥ saṃyogaḥ iti 
[0862,iv]	karma adṛṣṭam upabhoga artham kriyā hetuḥ iti ced samānam karma adṛṣṭam puruṣa stham puruṣa upabhoga artham manasi kriyā hetuḥ evam duḥkham duḥkha saṃvedanam ca sidhyati iti evam ced manyase samānam smṛti hetau api saṃyoga viśeṣaḥ bhavitum arhati tatra yat uktam ātma preraṇa yadṛcchā jña tābhiḥ ca na saṃyoga viśeṣaḥ iti ayam apratiṣedhaḥ iti pūrvaḥ tu pratiṣedhaḥ na antar śarīra vṛtti tvāt manasaḥ iti 
[0863,i_0863,iii]	kaḥ khalu idānīm kāraṇa yaugapadya sadbhāve yugapad asmaraṇasya hetuḥ iti praṇidhāna liṅga ādi jñānānām ayugapad bhāvāt yugapad asmaraṇam yathā khalu ātma manasoḥ sannikarṣaḥ saṃskāraḥ ca smṛti hetuḥ evam praṇidhānam liṅga ādi jñānāni tāni ca na yugapad bhavanti tad kṛtā smṛtīnām yugapad anutpattiḥ iti pratibhavat tu praṇidhāna ādi anapekṣe smārte yaugapadya prasaṅgaḥ yat khalu idam prātibham iva jñānam praṇidhāna ādi anapekṣam smārttam utpadyate kadācid tasya yugapad utpatti prasaṅgaḥ hetu abhāvāt sataḥ smṛti hetoḥ asaṃvedanāt prātibhena samāna abhimānaḥ bahu artha viṣaye vai cintā prabandhe kaścid eva arthaḥ kasyacid smṛti hetuḥ tasya anucintanāt tasya smṛtiḥ bhavati na ca ayam smartā sarvam smṛti hetum saṃvedayate evam me smṛtiḥ utpannā iti asaṃvedanāt prātibham iva jñānam idam smārtam iti abhimanyate na tu asti praṇidhāna ādi anapekṣam smārtam iti 
[0863,iv_0863,v]	prātibhe katham iti ced puruṣa karma viśeṣāt upabhoga vat niyamaḥ prātibham idānīm jñānam yugapad kasmāt na utpadyate yathā upabhoga artham karma yugapad upabhogam na karoti evam puruṣa karma viśeṣaḥ pratibhā hetuḥ na yugapad anekam prātibham jñānam utpādayati hetu abhāvāt ayuktam iti ced na karaṇasya pratyaya paryāye sāmarthyāt upabhoga vat niyamaḥ iti asti dṛṣṭāntaḥ hetuḥ na asti iti ced manyase na karaṇasya pratyaya paryāye sāmarthyāt na ekasmin jñeye yugapad anekam jñānam utpadyate na ca anekasmin tat idam dṛṣṭena pratyaya paryāyeṇa anumeyam karaṇa sāmarthyam ittham bhūtam iti na jñātuḥ vikaraṇa dharmaṇaḥ deha nānā tve pratyaya yaugapadyāt iti 
[0865,i_0866,i]	ayam ca dvitīyaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ avasthita śarīrasya ca aneka jñāna samavāyāt eka pradeśe yugapad aneka artha smaraṇam syāt kvacid deśe avasthita śarīrasya jñātuḥ indriya artha prabandhena jñānam anekam ekasmin ātma pradeśe samavaiti tena yadā manaḥ saṃyujyate tadā jñāta pūrvasya anekasya yugapad smaraṇam prasajyate pradeśa saṃyoga paryāya abhāvāt iti ātma pradeśānām adravya antara tvāt eka artha samavāyasya aviśeṣe sati smṛti yaugapadya pratiṣedha anupapattiḥ śabda santāne tu śrotra adhiṣṭhāna pratyāsattyā śabda śravaṇa vat saṃskāra pratyāsattyā manasaḥ smṛti utpatteḥ na yugapad utpatti prasaṅgaḥ pūrvaḥ eva tu pratiṣedhaḥ na aneka jñāna samavāyāt eka pradeśe yugapad smṛti prasaṅgaḥ iti 
[0866,ii_0867,ii]	puruṣa dharmaḥ jñānam antaḥkaraṇasya icchā dveṣa prayatna sukha duḥkhāni dharmāḥ iti kasyacid darśanam tat pratiṣidhyate jñasya icchā dveṣa nimitta tvāt ārambha nivṛttyoḥ ayam khalu jānāti tāvat idam me sukha sādhanam idam me duḥkha sādhanam iti jñātvā svasya sukha sādhanam āptum icchati duḥkha sādhanam hātum icchati prāpti icchā prayuktasya asya sukha sādhana avāptaye samīha aviśeṣaḥ ārambhaḥ jihāsā prayuktasya duḥkha sādhana parivarjanam nivṛttiḥ evam jñāna icchā prayatna dveṣa sukha duḥkhānām ekena abhisambandhaḥ eka kartṛka tvam jñāna icchā pravṛttīnām samāna āśraya tvam ca tasmāt jñasya icchā dveṣa prayatna sukha duḥkhāni dharmāḥ na acetanasya iti ārambha nivṛttyoḥ ca pratyagātmani dṛṣṭa tvāt paratra anumānam veditavyam iti 
[0868,i_0868,iii]	atra bhūta caitanikaḥ āha tad liṅga tvāt icchā dveṣayoḥ pārthiva ādyeṣu pratiṣedhaḥ ārambha nivṛtti liṅgau icchā dveṣau iti yasya ārambha nivṛttī tasya icchā dveṣau tasya jñānam iti prāptam pārthivā api ataijasa vāyavīyānām śarīrāṇām ārambha nivṛtti darśanāt icchā dveṣa jñānaiḥ yogaḥ iti caitanyam 
[0868,iv_0868,v]	paraśu ādiṣu ārambha nivṛtti darśanāt śarīre caitanya nivṛttiḥ ārambha nivṛtti darśanāt icchā dveṣa jñānaiḥ yogaḥ iti prāptam paraśu ādeḥ karaṇasya ārambha nivṛtti darśanāt caitanyam iti atha śarīrasya icchā ādibhiḥ yogaḥ paraśu ādeḥ tu karaṇasya ārambha nivṛttī vyabhicarataḥ na tarhi ayam hetuḥ pārthiva api ataijasa vāyavīyānām śarīrāṇām ārambha nivṛtti darśanāt icchā dveṣa jñānaiḥ yogaḥ iti 
[0869,i_0869,ii]	ayam tarhi anyaḥ arthaḥ tad liṅga tvāt icchā dveṣayoḥ pārthiva ādyeṣu apratiṣedhaḥ pṛthivī ādīnām bhūtānām ārambhaḥ tāvat trasa sthāvara śarīreṣu tad avayava vyūha liṅgaḥ pravṛtti viśeṣaḥ loṣṭa ādiṣu ca liṅga abhāvāt pravṛtti viśeṣa abhāvaḥ nivṛttiḥ ārambha nivṛtti liṅgau icchā dveṣau iti pārthiva ādyeṣu aṇuṣu tad darśanāt icchā dveṣa yogaḥ tad yogāt jñāna yogaḥ iti siddham bhūta caitanyam iti kumbha ādiṣu anupalabdheḥ ahetuḥ kumbha ādi mṛd avayavānām vyūha liṅgaḥ pravṛtti viśeṣaḥ ārambhaḥ sikata ādiṣu pravṛtti viśeṣa abhāvaḥ nivṛttiḥ na ca mṛtsikatānām ārambha nivṛtti darśanāt icchā dveṣa prayatna jñānaiḥ yogaḥ tasmāt tad liṅga tvāt icchā dveṣayoḥ iti ahetuḥ iti 
[0869,iii_0870,ii]	niyama aniyamau tu tad viśeṣakau tayoḥ icchā dveṣayoḥ niyama aniyamau viśeṣakau bhedakau jñasya icchā dveṣa nimitte pravṛtti nivṛttī na sva āśraye kim tarhi prayojya āśraye tatra prayujyamāneṣu bhūteṣu pravṛtti nivṛttī staḥ na sarveṣu iti aniyama upapattiḥ yasya tu jña tvāt bhūtānām icchā dveṣa nimitte ārambha nivṛttī sva āśraye tasya niyamaḥ syāt yathā bhūtānām guṇa antara nimittā pravṛttiḥ guṇa pratibandhāt ca nivṛttiḥ bhūtamātre bhavati niyamena evam bhūtamātre jñāna icchā dveṣa nimitte pravṛtti nivṛttī sva āśraye syātām na tu bhavataḥ tasmāt prayojaka āśritāḥ jñāna icchā dveṣa prayatnāḥ prayojya āśraye tu pravṛtti nivṛtti iti siddham 
[0871,i]	eka śarīre tu jñātṛ bahu tvam niranumānam bhūta caitanikasya eka śarīre bahūni bhūtāni jñāna icchā dveṣa prayatna guṇāni iti jñātṛ bahu tvam prāptam om iti bruvataḥ pramāṇam na asti yathā nānā śarīreṣu nānā jñātāraḥ buddhi ādi guṇa vyavasthānāt evam eka śarīre api buddhi ādi vyavasthā anumānam syāt jñātṛ bahutvasya iti 
[0872,i]	dṛṣṭaḥ ca anya guṇa nimittaḥ pravṛtti viśeṣaḥ bhūtānām saḥ anumānam anyatra api dṛṣṭaḥ karaṇa lakṣaṇeṣu bhūteṣu paraśu ādiṣu upādāna lakṣaṇeṣu ca mṛd prabhṛtiṣu anya guṇa nimittaḥ pravṛtti viśeṣaḥ saḥ anumānam anyatra api trasa sthāvara śarīreṣu tad avayava vyūha liṅgaḥ pravṛtti viśeṣaḥ bhūtānām anya guṇa nimittaḥ iti sa ca guṇaḥ prayatna samāna āśrayaḥ saṃskāraḥ dharma adharma samākhyātaḥ sarva arthaḥ puruṣa artha ārādhanāya prayojakaḥ bhūtānām prayatna vat iti 
[0872,ii]	ātma astitva hetubhiḥ ātma nitya tva hetubhiḥ ca bhūta caitanya pratiṣedhaḥ kṛtaḥ veditavyaḥ na indriya arthayoḥ tad vināśe api jjāna avasthānāt iti ca samānaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ iti kriyā mātram kriyā uparama mātram ca ārambha nivṛttī iti abhipretya uktam tad liṅga tvāt icchā dveṣayoḥ pārthiva ādyeṣu apratiṣedhaḥ anyathā tu ime ārambha nivṛttī ākhyāte na ca tathāvidhe pṛthivī ādiṣu dṛśyete tasmāt ayuktam tad liṅga tvāt icchā dveṣayoḥ pārthiva ādyeṣu apratiṣedhaḥ iti 
[0873,i_0874,i]	bhūta indriya manasām samānaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ manaḥ tu udāharaṇa mātram yathā ukta hetu tvāt pāratantryāt akṛta abhyāgamāt ca na manasaḥ icchā dveṣa prayatna sukha duḥkha jñānāni ātmanaḥ liṅgam iti atas prabhṛti yathoktam saṅgṛhyate tena bhūta indriya manasām caitanya pratiṣedhaḥ pāratantryāt paratantrāṇi bhūta indriya manāṃsi dhāraṇa preraṇa vyūhana kriyāsu prayatna vaśāt pravarttante caitanye punar svatantrāṇi syuḥ iti akṛta abhyāgamāt ca pravṛttiḥ vāc buddhi śarīra ārambhaḥ iti caitanye bhūta indriya manasām para kṛtam karma puruṣeṇa upabhujyate iti syāt acaitanye tu tad sādhanasya sva kṛta karma phala upabhogaḥ puruṣasya iti upapadyate iti 
[0875,i_0875,iv]	atha ayam siddha upasaṃgrahaḥ pariśeṣāt yathā ukta hetu upapatteḥ ca ātma guṇaḥ jñānam iti prakṛtam pariśeṣaḥ nāma prasakta pratiṣedhe anyatra aprasaṅgāt śiṣyamāṇe sampratyayaḥ bhūta indriya manasām pratiṣedhe dravya antaram na prasajyate śiṣyate ca ātmā tasya guṇaḥ jñānam iti jñāyate yathā ukta hetu upapatteḥ ca iti darśana sparśanābhyām eka artha grahaṇāt iti evamādīnām ātma pratipatti hetūnām apratiṣedhāt iti pariśeṣa jñāpana artham prakṛta sthāpana ādi jñāna artham ca yathā ukta hetu upapatti vacanam iti 
[0875,v]	atha vā upapatteḥ ca iti hetu antaram eva idam nityaḥ khalu ayam ātmā yasmāt ekasmin śarīre dharmam caritvā kāyasya bhedāt svarge deveṣu upapadyate adharmam caritvā deha bhedāt narakeṣu upapadyate iti upapattiḥ śarīra antara prāpti lakṣaṇā sā sati sattve nitye ca āśrayavatī buddhi prabandha mātre tu nirātmake nirāśrayā na upapadyate iti eka sattva adhiṣṭhānaḥ ca aneka śarīra yogaḥ saṃsāraḥ upapadyate śarīra prabandha ucchedaḥ ca apavargaḥ muktiḥ iti upapadyate buddhi santati mātre tu eka sattva anupapatteḥ na kaścid dīrgham adhvānam sandhāvati na kaścid śarīra prabandhāt vimucyate iti saṃsāra apavarga anupapattiḥ iti buddhi santati mātre ca sattva bhedāt sarvam idam prāṇi vyavahāra jātam apratisaṃhitam avyāvṛttam apariniṣṭham ca syāt tatas smaraṇa abhāvāt na anya dṛṣṭam anyaḥ smarati iti smaraṇam ca khalu pūrva jñātasya samānena jñātrā grahaṇam ajñāsiṣam amum artham jñeyam iti saḥ ayam ekaḥ jñātā pūrva jñātam artham gṛhṇāti tat ca asya grahaṇam smaraṇam iti tat buddhi prabandha mātre nirātmake na upapadyate 
[0875,vi_0875,vii]	smaraṇam tu ātmanaḥ jña svābhāvyāt upapadyate iti ātmanaḥ eva smaraṇam na buddhi santati mātrasya iti tuśabdaḥ avadhāraṇe katham jña svabhāva tvāt jñaḥ iti asya svabhāvaḥ svaḥ dharmaḥ ayam khalu jñāsyati jānāti ajñāsīt iti tri kāla viṣayeṇa anekena jñānena sambadhyate tat ca asya tri kāla viṣayam jñānam pratyātma vedanīyam jñāsyāmi jānāmi ajñāsiṣam iti varttate tat yasya ayam svaḥ dharmaḥ tasya smaraṇam na buddhi prabandha mātrasya nirātmakasya iti 
[0875,viii]	smṛti hetūnām ayaugapadyāt yugapad asmaraṇam iti uktam atha kebhyaḥ smṛtiḥ utpadyate iti smṛtiḥ khalu p r a ṇ i d h ā n a n i b a n d h ā b h y ā s a l i ṅ g a l a k ṣ a ṇ a s ā d ṛ ś y a p a r i g r a h ā ś r a y ā ś r ita sambandha ānantarya viyoga eka kārya virodha atiśaya prāpti vyavadhāna sukha duḥkha icchā dveṣa bhaya arthi tva kriyā rāga dharma adharma nimittebhyaḥ 
[0875,x_0878,ii]	susmūrṣayā manasaḥ dhāraṇam praṇidhānam su smūrṣita liṅga cintanam ca artha smṛti kāraṇam nibandhaḥ khalu eka grantha upayamaḥ arthānām eka grantha upayatāḥ khalu arthāḥ anyonya smṛti hetavaḥ ānupūrvyeṇa itarathāḥ vā bhavanti iti dhāraṇa śāstra kṛtaḥ vā prajñāteṣu vastuṣu smartavyānām upanikṣepaḥ nibandhaḥ iti abhyāsaḥ tu samāne viṣaye jñānānām abhyāvṛttiḥ abhyāsa janitaḥ saṃskāraḥ ātma guṇaḥ abhyāsa śabdena ucyate sa ca smṛti hetuḥ samānaḥ iti 
[0878,iii_0878,iv]	liṅgam punar saṃyogi samavāyi eka artha samavāyi virodhi ca iti yathā dhūmaḥ agneḥ goḥ viṣāṇam pāṇiḥ pādasya rūpam sparśasya abhūtam bhūtasya iti lakṣaṇam paśu avayava stham gotrasya smṛti hetuḥ vidānām idam gargāṇām idam iti sādṛśyam citra gatam pratirūpakam devadattasya iti evamādi parigrahāt svena vā svāmī svāminā vā svam smaryate āśrayāt grāmaṇyā tad adhīnam saṃsmarati āśritāt tad adhīnena grāmaṇyam iti sambandhāt antevāsinā yuktam gurum smarati ṛtvijā yājyam iti 
[0879,i]	ānantaryāt iti karaṇīyeṣu artheṣu viyogāt yena viyujyate tad viyoga pratisaṃvedī bhṛśam smarati eka kāryāt kartṛ antara darśanāt kartṛ antare smṛtiḥ virodhāt vijigīṣamāṇayoḥ anyatara darśanāt anyataraḥ smaryate atiśayāt yena atiśayaḥ utpāditaḥ prāpteḥ yatas anena kiṃcid prāptam āptavyam vā bhavati tam abhīkṣṇam smarati vyavadhānāt kośa ādibhiḥ asi prabhṛtīni smaryante 
[0880,i]	sukha duḥkhābhyām tad hetuḥ smaryate icchā dveṣābhyām yam icchati yam ca dveṣṭi tam smarati bhayāt yatas bibheti arthi tvāt yena arthī bhojanena ācchādanena vā kriyayā rathena rathakāram smarati rāgāt yasyām striyām raktaḥ bhavati tām abhīkṣṇam smarati dharmāt jāti antara smaraṇam iha ca adhīta śruta avadhāraṇam iti adharmāt prāk anubhūta duḥkha sādhanam smarati na ca eteṣu nimitteṣu yugapad saṃvedanāni bhavanti iti yugapad asmaraṇam iti nidarśanam ca idam smṛti hetūnām na parisaṅkhyānam iti 
[0881,i_0881,iii]	anityāyām ca buddhau utpanna apavargi tvāt kāla antarau āsthānāt ca anityānām saṃśayaḥ kim utpatpanna apavargiṇī buddhiḥ śabda vat āhosvit kāla antara avasthāyinī kumbha vat iti utpannā apavargiṇī iti pakṣaḥ parigṛhyate kasmāt karma anavasthāyi grahaṇāt karmaṇaḥ anavasthāyinaḥ grahaṇāt iti kṣiptasya iṣoḥ āpatanāt kriyā santānaḥ gṛhyate pratyartha niyamāt ca buddhīnām kriyā santāna vat buddhi santāna upapattiḥ iti avasthita grahaṇe ca vyavadhīyamānasya pratyakśa ni vṛtteḥ avasthite ca kumbhe gṛhyamāṇe santānena eva buddhiḥ vartate prāk vyavadhānāt tena vyavahite pratyakṣam jñānam nivartate kāla antara avasthāne tu buddheḥ dṛśya vyavadhāne api pratyakṣam avatiṣṭheta iti 
[0881,iv_0884,i]	smṛtiḥ ca aliṅgam buddhi avasthāne saṃskārasya buddhi jasya smṛti hetu tvāt yaḥ ca manyeta avatiṣṭhate buddhiḥ dṛṣṭā hi buddhi viṣaye smṛtiḥ sā ca buddhau anityāyām kāraṇa abhāvāt na syāt iti tat idam aliṅgam kasmāt buddhi jaḥ hi saṃskāraḥ guṇa antaram smṛti hetuḥ na buddhiḥ iti hetu abhāvāt ayuktam iti ced buddhi avasthānāt pratyakṣa tve smṛtyabhāvaḥ yāvat avatiṣṭhate buddhiḥ tāvat asau boddhavya arthiḥ pratyakṣaḥ pratyakṣe ca smṛtiḥ anupapannaḥ iti 
[0884,ii_0884,iii]	avyakta grahaṇam anavasthāyi tvāt vidyut sampāte rūpa avyakta grahaṇvat yadi utpannā apavargiṇī buddhiḥ prāptam avyaktam boddhavyasya grahaṇam yathā vidyut sampāte vaidyutasya prakāśasya anavasthānāt avyaktam rūpa grahaṇam iti vyaktam tu dravyāṇām grahaṇam tasmāt ayuktam etat iti 
[0884,iv_0885,i]	hetu upādanāt pratiṣeddhavyā abhyanujñā utapanna apavargiṇī buddhiḥ iti pratiṣeddhavyam tat eva abhyanujñāyate vidyut sampāte rūpa avyakta grahaṇa vat iti yatra avyakta grahaṇam tatra utpannāpavargiṇī buddhiḥ iti grahaṇa hetu vikalpāt grahaṇa vikalpaḥ na buddhi vikalpāt yat idam kvacid avyaktam kvacid vyaktam grahaṇam ayam vikalpaḥ grahaṇa hetu vikalpāt yatra anavasthitaḥ grahaṇa hetuḥ tatra avyaktam grahaṇam yatra avasthitaḥ tatra vyaktam na tu buddheḥ avasthāna anavasthānābhyām iti kasmāt artha grhaṇam hi buddhiḥ yat tad artha grahaṇam avyaktam vyaktam vā buddhiḥ sā iti viśeṣa agrahaṇe ca sāmānya grahaṇa mātram avyakta grahaṇam tatra viṣaya antare buddhi anatara anutpattiḥ nimitta abhāvāt yatra samāna dharma yuktaḥ ca dharmī gṛhyate viśeṣa dharma yuktaḥ ca tat vyaktam grahaṇam yatra tu viśeṣe agṛhyamāṇe sāmānya grahaṇa mātram tat avyaktam grahaṇam samāna dharma yogāt ca viśiṣṭa dharma yogaḥ viṣaya antaram tatra yat grahaṇam na bhavati tat grahaṇa nimitta abhāvāt na buddheḥ anavasthānāt iti 
[0886,i_0886,ii]	yathā viṣayam ca grahaṇam vyaktam eva pratyartha niyata tvāt ca buddhīnām sāmānya viṣayam ca grahaṇam sva viṣayam prati vyaktam viśeṣa viṣayam ca grahaṇam sva viṣayam prati vyaktam pratyartha niyatāḥ hi buddhayaḥ tat idam avyakta grahaṇam deśitam kva viṣaye buddhi anavasthāna kāritam syyat iti dharmiṇaḥ tu dharma bhede buddhi nānātvasya bhāva abhāvābhyām tad upapattiḥ dharmiṇaḥ khalu arthasya samānāḥ ca dharmāḥ viśiṣṭāḥ ca teṣu pratyartha niyatāḥ nānā buddayaḥ tāḥ ubhayaḥ yadi dharmiṇi vartante tadā vyakatam grahaṇam dharmiṇam abhipretya yadā tu sāmānya grahaṇa mātram tadā avyaktam grahaṇam iti evam dharmiṇam abhipretya vyakta avyakatayoḥ grahaṇayoḥ upapattiḥ iti 
[0887,i_0887,iii]	na ca idam avyaktam grahaṇam buddeḥ boddhavyasya vā anavasthāyi tvāt upapadyate iti idam hi na pradīpa arciḥ santattsa bhivyakta grahaṇa vat tad grahaṇam anavasthāyi tve api buddheḥ teṣām grahaṇam vyaktam pratipattavyam katham pradīpa arciḥ santati abhivyakta grahaṇa vat pradīpa arciṣām santatyā vartamānānām grahaṇa anavasthānam grāhya anavasthānam ca pratyartha niyata tvāt buddhīnām yāvanti pradīpa arcīṃṣi tāvatyaḥ buddayaḥ iti dṛśyate ca atra vyaktam pradīpa arciṣām grahaṇam iti 
[0888,i_0888,ii]	cetanā śarīra guṇaḥ sati śarīre bhāvāt asati ca abhāvāt iti dravye sva guṇa para guṇa upalabdheḥ saṃśayaḥ sāṃśayikaḥ sati bhāvaḥ sva guṇaḥ apsu drava tvam upalabhyate para guṇaḥ ca uṣṇa tā tena ayam saṃśayaḥ kim śarīra guṇaḥ cetanā śarīre gṛhyate atha dravya antara guṇaḥ iti 
[0888,iii_0889,i]	na śarīra guṇaḥ cetanā kasmāt yāvat dravya bhāvi tvāt rūpa ādīnām na rūpa ādi hīnam śarīram gṛhyate cetanā hīnan tu gṛhyate yathā uṣṇatā hīnāḥ āpaḥ tasmāt na śarīra guṇaḥ cetanā iti saṃskāra vat iti ced na kāraṇa anucchedāt yathāvidhe dravye saṃskāraḥ tathāvidhaḥ eva uparamaḥ na tatra kāraṇa ucchedāt atyantam saṃskāra anupapattiḥ bhavati yathāvidhe śarīre cetanā gṛhyate tathāvidhe eva atyanta uparamaḥ cetanāyāḥ gṛhyate tasmāt saṃskāra vat iti asamaḥ samādhiḥ 
[0889,ii]	atha api śarīra stham cetanā utpatti kāraṇam syāt dravya antara stham vā ubhaya stham vā tat na niyama hetu abhāvāt śarīra sthena kadācid cetanā utpadyate kadācid na iti niyame hetuḥ na asti iti dravya antara sthena ca śarīraḥ eva cetanā utpadyate na loṣṭa ādiṣu iti atra na niyame hetuḥ asti iti ubhaya sthasya nimitta tve śarīra samāna jātīya dravye cetanā na utpadyate śarīraḥ eva ca utpadyate iti niyame hetuḥ na asti iti 
[0890,i_0890,iii]	yat ca manyeta sati śyāma ādi guṇe dravye śyāma ādi uparamaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ evam cetanā uparamaḥ syāt iti na pāka ja guṇa antara utpatteḥ na atyantam rūpa uparamaḥ dravyasya śyāme rūpe nivṛtte pāka jam guṇa antaram raktam rūpam utpadyate śarīre tu cetanā mātra uparamaḥ atyantam iti 
[0891,i_0891,iii]	atha api pratidvandvi siddheḥ pāka jānām apratiṣedhaḥ yāvatsu dravyeṣu pūrva guṇa pratidvandvi siddhiḥ tāvatsu pākaja utpattiḥ dṛśyate pūrva guṇaiḥ saha pāka jānām avasthānasya agrahaṇāt na ca śarīre cetanā pratidvandvi siddhau saha anavasthāyi guṇa antaram gṛhyate yena anumīyeta tena cetanāyāḥ virodhaḥ tasmāt apratiṣiddhā cetanā yāvat śarīram varteta na tu vartate tasmāt na śarīra guṇaḥ cetanā iti 
[0892,i_0892,iii]	itas ca na śarīra guṇaḥ cetanā śarīra vyāpi tvāt śarīram śarīra avayavāḥ ca sarve cetanā utpattyā vyāptāḥ iti na kvacid anutpattiḥ cetanāyāḥ śarīra vat śarīra avayavāḥ cetanā iti prāptam cetana bahu tvam tatra yathā pratiśarīram cetana bahutve sukha duḥkha jñānānām vyavasthā liṅgam evam eka śarīre api syāt na tu bhavati tasmāt na śarīra guṇaḥ cetanā iti 
[0892,iv_0892,vi]	yat uktam na kvacid śarīra avayave cetanāyāḥ anutpattiḥ iti sā na keśa nakha ādiṣu anupalabdheḥ keśeṣu nakha ādiṣu ca anutpattiḥ cetanāyāḥ iti anupapannam śarīra vyāpi tvam iti 
[0893,i_0893,ii]	tvac paryanta tvāt śarīrasya keśa nakha ādiṣu aprasaṅgaḥ indriya āśraya tvam śarīra lakṣaṇam tvac paryantam jīva manaḥ sukha duḥkha saṃvitti āyatana bhūtam śarīram tasmāt na keśa ādiṣu cetanā utpadyate artha kāritaḥ tu śarīra upanibandhaḥ keśa ādīnām iti 
[0893,iii_0894,i]	itas ca na śarīra guṇaḥ cetanā śarīra guna vaidharmyāt dvividhaḥ śarīra guṇaḥ apratyakṣaḥ ca guru tvam indriya grāhyaḥ ca rūpa ādiḥ vidha antaram tu cetanā na apratyakṣā saṃvedya tvāt na indriya grāhyāḥ manaḥ viṣaya tvāt tasmāt dravya antara guṇaḥ iti 
[0894,ii_0894,iii]	na rūpa ādīnām itaretara vaidharmyāt yathā itaretara vidharmāṇaḥ rūpa ādayaḥ na śarīra guṇa tvam jahati evam rūpa ādi vaidharmyāt cetanā śarīra guṇa tvam na hāsyati iti 
[0895,i_0895,iii]	aindriyaka tvāt rūpa ādīnām apratiṣedhaḥ apratyaksa tvāt ca iti yathā itaretara vidharmāṇaḥ rūpa ādayaḥ na dvaividhyam ativartante tathā rūpa ādi vaidharmyāt cetanā na dvaividhyam ativarteta yadi śarīra guṇaḥ syāt iti ativarttate tu tasmāt na śarīra guṇaḥ iti bhūta indriya manasām jñāna pratiṣedhāt siddhe sati ārambhaḥ viśeṣa jñāpana arthaḥ bahudhā parīkṣyamāṇam tattvam su niścitataram bhavati iti 
[0896,i_0896,iii]	parīkṣitā buddhiḥ manasaḥ idānīm parīkṣā kramaḥ tat kim pratiśarīram ekam anekam iti vicāre jñāna ayaugapadyāt ekam manaḥ asti khalu vai jñāna ayaugapadyam ekaikasya indriyasya yathā viṣayam karaṇasya eka pratyaya nirvṛttau sāmarthyāt na tad eka tve manasaḥ liṅgam yat tu khalu idam indriya antarāṇām viṣaya antareṣu jñāna ayaugapadyam iti tat liṅgam kasmāt sambhavati khalu vai bahuṣu manaḥsu indriya manaḥ saṃyoga yaugapadyam iti jñāna yaugapadyam syāt na tu bhavati tasmāt viṣaye pratyaya paryāyāt ekam manaḥ 
[0897,i_0897,ii]	na yugapad aneka kriyā upalabdheḥ ayam khalu adhyāpakaḥ adhīte vrajati kamaṇḍalum dhārayati panthānam paśyati śṛṇoti āraṇya jān śabdān bibhyat vyāla liṅgāni bubhutsate smarati ca gantavyam sthānīyam iti kramasya agrahaṇāt yugapad etāḥ kriyāḥ iti prāptam manasaḥ bahu tvam iti 
[0897,iii_0898,i]	alāta cakra darśana vat tad upalabdhiḥ āśu sañcārāt āśu sañcārāt alātasya bhramataḥ vidyamānaḥ kramaḥ na gṛhyate kramasya agrahaṇāt aviccheda buddhyā cakra vat buddhiḥ bhavati iti tathā buddhīnām kriyāṇām ca āśu vṛtti tvāt vidyamānaḥ kramaḥ na gṛhyate kramasya agrahaṇāt yugapad kriyāḥ bhavan ti iti abhimānaḥ bhavati 
[0898,ii]	kim punar kramasya agrahaṇāt yugapad kriyā abhimānaḥ atha yugapad bhāvāt eva yugapad aneka kriyā upalabdhiḥ iti na atra viśeṣa pratipatteḥ kāraṇam ucyate iti uktam indriya antarāṇām viṣaya antareṣu paryāyeṇa buddhayaḥ bhavanti iti tat ca apratyākhyeyam ātma pratyakṣa tvāt atha api dṛṣṭa śrutān arthān cintayataḥ krameṇa buddhayaḥ vartante na yugapad anena anumātavyam iti varṇa pada vākya buddhīnām tad artha buddhīnām ca āśu vṛtti tvāt kramasya agrahaṇam katham vākya stheṣu khalu varṇeṣu uccaratsu prativarṇam tāvat śravaṇam bhavati śrutam varṇam ekam anekam vā pada bhāvena sa pratisandhatte pratisandhāya padam vyavasyati pada vyavasāyena smṛtyā padārtham pratipadyate pada samūha pratisandhānāt ca vākyam vyavasyati sambaddhān ca padārthān gṛhītvā vākya artham pratipadyate na ca āsām krameṇa vartamānānām buddhīnām āśu vṛtti tvāt kramaḥ gṛhyate tat etat anumānam anyatra buddhi kriyā yaugapadya abhimānasya iti na ca asti mukta saṃśayāḥ yugapad utpattiḥ buddhīnām yayā manasām bahu tvam eka śarīre anumīyeta iti 
[0899,i_0899,ii]	yathā ukta hetu tvāt ca aṇu aṇu manaḥ ekam ca iti dharma samuccayaḥ jñāna ayaugapadyāt mahat tve manasaḥ sarva indriya saṃyogāt yugapad viṣaya grahaṇam syāt iti 
[0899,iii_0899,vi]	manasaḥ khalu bhoḥ sa indriyasya śarīre vṛtti lābhaḥ na anyatra śarīrāt jñātuḥ ca puruṣasya śarīra āyatanāḥ buddhi ādayaḥ viṣaya upabhogaḥ jihāsita hānam īpsita avāptiḥ ca sarve ca śarīra āśrayāḥ vyavahārāḥ tatra khalu vipratipatteḥ saṃśayaḥ kim ayam puruṣa karma nimittaḥ śarīra sargaḥ āhosvit bhūtamātrāt akarma nimittaḥ iti śrūyate khalu atra vipratipattiḥ iti tatra idam tattvam pūrva kṛta phala anubandhāt tad utpattiḥ pūrva śarīre yā pravṛttiḥ vāc buddhi śarīra ārambha lakṣaṇā tat pūrva kṛtam karma uktam tasya phalam tad janitau dharma adharmau 
[0900,i_0901,i]	tad phalasya anubandhaḥ ātma samavetasya avasthānam tena prayuktebhyaḥ bhūtebyaḥ tasya utpattiḥ śarīrasya na svatantrebhyaḥ iti yat adhiṣṭhānaḥ ayam ātmā ayam aham iti manyamānaḥ yatra abhiyuktaḥ yatra upabhoga tṛṣṇayā viṣayān upalabhamānaḥ dharma adharmau saṃskaroti tat asya śarīram tena saṃskāreṇa dharma adharma lakṣaṇena bhūta sahite patite asmin śarīraḥ uttaram niṣpadyate niṣpannasya ca asya pūrva śarīra vat puruṣa artha kriyā puruṣasya ca pūrva śarīra vat pravṛttiḥ iti karma apekṣebhyaḥ bhūtebhyaḥ śarīra sarge sati etat upapadyate iti dṛṣṭā ca puruṣa guṇena prayatnena prayuktebhyaḥ bhūtebhyaḥ puruṣa artha kriyā samarthānām dravyāṇām ratha prabhṛtīnām utpattiḥ tathā anumātavyam śarīram api puruṣa artha kriyā samartham utpadyamānam puruṣasya guṇa antara apekṣebhyaḥ bhūtebhyaḥ utpadyate iti 
[0902,i_0902,iii]	atra nāstikaḥ āha bhūtebhyaḥ mūrti upādāna vat tad upādānam yathā karma nirapekṣebhyaḥ bhūtebhyaḥ nirvṛttāḥ mūrtayaḥ sikatā śarkarā pāṣāṇa gairika añjana prabhṛtayaḥ puruṣa artha kāri tvāt upādīyante tathā karma nirapekṣebhyaḥ bhūtebhyaḥ śarīram utpannam puruṣa artha kāri tvāt upādīyate iti 
[0902,iv_0902,v]	na sādhya sama tvāt yathā śarīra utpattiḥ akarma nimittā sādhyā tathā sikatā śarkarā pāṣāṇa gairika añjana prabhṛtīnām api akarma nimittaḥ sargaḥ sādhyaḥ sādhya sama tvāt asādhanam iti bhūtebhyaḥ mūrti upādāna vat iti ca anena sādhyam 
[0903,i_0903,ii]	na utpatti nimitta tvāt mātā pitroḥ viṣamaḥ ca ayam upanyāsaḥ kasmāt nirbījāḥ imāḥ mūrtayaḥ utpadyante bīja pūrvikā tu śarīra utpattiḥ mātā pitṛ śabdena lohita retasī bīja bhūte gṛhyete tatra sattvasya garbha vāsa anubhavanīyam karma pitroḥ ca putra phala anubhavanīye karmaṇī mātuḥ garbha āśraye śarīra utpattim bhūtebhyaḥ prayojayanti iti upapannam bīja anuvidhānam iti 
[0904,i_0904,ii]	tathā āhārasya utpatti nimitta tvāt iti prakṛtam bhuktam pītam āhāraḥ tasya pakti nirvṛttam rasa dravyam mātṛ śarīre ca upacīyate bīje garbhāśaya sthe bīja samāna pākam mātrayā ca upacayaḥ bīje yāvat vyūha samarthaḥ sañcaye iti sañcitam ca kalala arbuda māṃsa peśī kaṇḍarāśiraḥ pāṇi ādinā ca vyūhena indriya adhiṣṭhāna bhedena vyuhyate vyūhe ca garbha nāḍyā avatāritam rasa dravyam upacīyate yāvat prasava samartham iti na ca ayam anna pānasya sthālī ādi gatasya kalpate iti etasmāt kāraṇāt karma nimitta tvam śarīrasya vijñāyate iti 
[0905,i_0905,ii]	prāptau ca aniyamāt na sarvaḥ dampatyoḥ saṃyogaḥ garbhādhāna hetuḥ dṛśyate tatra asati karmaṇi na bhavati sati ca bhavati iti anupapannaḥ niyama abhāvaḥ iti karma nirapekṣeṣu bhūteṣu śarīra utpatti hetuṣu niyamaḥ syāt na hi atra kāraṇa abhāvaḥ iti 
[0906,i_0906,iii]	atha api śarīra utpatti nimitta vat saṃyoga utpatti nimittam karma yathā khalu idam śarīram dhātu prāṇa saṃvāhinīnām nāḍīnām śukra antānām dhātūnām ca snāyu tvac asthi śirā peśī kalala kaṇḍarāṇām ca śiraḥ bāhu udarāṇām sakthnām ca koṣṭha gānām vāta pitta kaphānām ca mukha hṛdaya āmāśaya pakvāśaya adhas srotasām ca parama duḥkha sampādanīyena sanniveśena vyūhanam aśakyam pṛthivī ādibhiḥ karma nirapekṣaiḥ utpādayitum iti karma nimittā śarīra utpattiḥ iti vijñāyate evam ca pratyātma niyatasya nimittasya abhāvāt niratiśayaiḥ ātmabhiḥ sambandhāt sarva ātmanām ca samānaiḥ pṛthivī ādibhiḥ utpāditam śarīram pṛthivī ādi gatasya ca niyama hetoḥ abhāvāt sarva ātmanām sukha duḥkha saṃvitti āyatanam samānam prāptam yat tu pratyātmam vyavatiṣṭhate tatra śarīra utpatti nimittam karma vyavasthā hetuḥ iti vijñāyate paripacyamānaḥ hi pratyātma niyataḥ karma āśayaḥ yasmin ātmani vartate tasya eva upabhoga āyatanam śarīram utpādya vyavasthāpayati tat evam śarīra utpatti nimitta vat saṃyoga nimittam karma iti vijñāyate pratyātma vyavasthānam tu śarīrasya ātmanā saṃyogam pracakṣmahe iti 
[0907,i_0908,i]	etena aniyamaḥ pratyuktaḥ yaḥ ayam akarma nimitte śarīra sarge sati aniyamaḥ iti ucyate ayam śarīra utpatti nimitta vat saṃyoga utpatti nimittam karma iti anena pratyuktaḥ kaḥ tāvat ayam niyamaḥ yathā ekasya ātmanaḥ śarīram tathā sarveṣām iti niyamaḥ anyasya anyathā anyasya anyathā iti aniyamaḥ bhedaḥ vyāvṛttiḥ viśeṣaḥ iti 
[0909,i]	dṛṣṭā ca janma vyāvṛttiḥ ucca abhijanaḥ nikṛṣṭa abhijanaḥ iti praśastam nindatam iti vyādhi bahulam arogam iti samagram vikalam iti pīḍā bahulam sukha bahulam iti puruṣa atiśaya lakṣaṇa upapannam viparītam iti praśasta lakṣaṇam nindita lakṣaṇam iti paṭu indriyam mṛṣ u indriyam iti sūkṣmaḥ ca bhedaḥ aparimeyaḥ saḥ ayam janma bhedaḥ pratyātma niyatāt karma bhedāt upapadyate asati karma bhede pratyātma niyate niratiśaya tvāt ātmanām samāna tvāt ca pṛthivī ādīnām pṛthivī ādi gatasya niyama hetoḥ abhāvāt sarvam sarva ātmanām prasajyeta na tu idam ittham bhūtam janma tasmāt na akarma nittā śarīra utpattiḥ iti 
[0909,ii]	upapannaḥ ca tad viyogaḥ karma kṣaya upapatteḥ karma nimitte śarīra sarge tena śarīreṇa ātmanaḥ viyogaḥ upapannaḥ kasmāt karma kṣaya upapatteḥ upapadyate khalu karma kṣayaḥ samyak darśanāt prakṣīṇe mohe vīta rāgaḥ punarbhava hetu karma kāya vāc manobhiḥ na karoti iti uttarasya anupacayaḥ pūrva upacitasya vipāka pratisaṃvedanāt prakṣayaḥ evam prasava hetoḥ abhāvāt patire asmin śarīre punar śarīra antara anupapatteḥ apratisandhiḥ akarma nimitte tu śarīra sarge bhūta kṣaya anupapatteḥ tad viyoga anupapattiḥ iti
