[0910,i_0910,ii]	tat adṛṣṭa kāritam iti ced punar tad prasaṅgaḥ apavarge adarśanam khalu adṛṣṭam iti ucyate adṛṣṭa kāri tā bhūtebhyaḥ śarīra utpattiḥ na jātu anutpanne śarīre draṣṭā nirāyatanaḥ dṛśyam paśyati tat ca asya dṛśyam dvividham viṣayaḥ ca nānātvam ca avyakta ātmanaḥ tad arthaḥ śarīra sargaḥ tasmin avasite caritārthāni bhūtāni na śarīram utpādayanti iti upapannaḥ śarīra viyogaḥ iti evam ced manyase punar tat prasaṅgaḥ apavarge punar śarīra utpattiḥ prasajyate iti yā ca anutpanne śarīre darśana anutpattiḥ adarśana abhimatā yā ca apavarge śarīra nivṛttau darśana anutpattiḥ adarśana bhūtāḥ na etayoḥ adarśanayoḥ kvacid viśeṣaḥ iti adarśanasya anivṛtteḥ apavarge punar śarīra utpatti prasaṅgaḥ iti 
[0910,iii]	caritārtha tā viśeṣaḥ iti ced na karaṇa akaraṇayoḥ ārambha darśanāt caritārthāni bhūtāni darśana avasānāt na śarīra antaram ārabhante iti ayam viśeṣaḥ evam ced ucyate na karaṇa akaraṇayoḥ ārambha darśanāt caritārthānām bhūtānām viṣaya upalabdhi karaṇāt punar punar śarīra ārambhaḥ dṛśyate prakṛti puruṣayoḥ nānātva darśanasya akaraṇāt nirarthakaḥ śarīra ārambhaḥ punar punar dṛśyate tasmāt akarma nimittāyām bhūta sṛṣṭau na darśana arthā śarīra utpattiḥ yuktā yuktā tu karma nimitte sarge darśana arthā śarīra utpattiḥ karma vipāka saṃvedanam darśanam iti 
[0911,i_0911,ii]	tat adṛṣṭa kāritam iti ced kasyacid darśanam adṛṣṭam nāma paramāṇūnām guṇa viśeṣaḥ kriyā hetuḥ tena preritāḥ paramāṇavaḥ sammūrcchitāḥ śarīram utpādayanti iti tat manaḥ samāviśati sva guṇena adṛṣṭena preritam sa manaske śarīre draṣṭuḥ upalabdhiḥ bhavati iti etasmin vai darśane guṇa an ucchedāt punar tad prasaṅgaḥ apavarge apavarge śarīra utpattiḥ paramāṇu guṇasya adṛṣṭasya anucchedya tvāt iti 
[0914,i_0914,ii]	manaḥ karma nimitta tvāt ca saṃyoga avyucchedaḥ manaḥ guṇena adṛṣṭena samāveśite manasi saṃyoga vyucchedaḥ na syāt tat ca kiṃkṛtam śarīrāt apasarpaṇam manasaḥ iti karma āśaya kṣaye tu karma āśaya antarāt vipacyamānāt apasarpaṇa upapattiḥ iti adṛṣṭāt eva apasarpaṇam iti ced yaḥ adṛṣṭaḥ śarīra upasarpaṇa hetuḥ saḥ eva apasarpaṇa hetuḥ api iti na ekasya jīvana prāyaṇa hetutva anupapatteḥ evam ca sati ekam adṛṣṭam jīvana prāyaṇayoḥ hetuḥ iti prāptam na etat upapadyate 
[0915,i_0915,ii]	nitya tva prasaṅgaḥ ca prāyaṇa anupapatteḥ vipāka saṃvedanāt karma āśaya kṣaye śarīra pātaḥ prāyaṇam karma āśaya antarāt ca punarjanma bhūtamātrāt tu karma nirapekṣāt śarīra utpattau kasya kṣayāt śarīra pātaḥ prāyaṇam iti prāyaṇa anupapatteḥ khalu vai nitya tva prasaṅgam vidmaḥ yādṛcchike tu prāyaṇe prāyaṇa bheda anupapattiḥ iti 
[0916,i_0916,iii]	punar tad prasaṅgaḥ apavargaḥ iti etat samādhitsuḥ āha aṇu śyāma tā anitya tva vat etat syāt yathā aṇoḥ śyāma tā nityāḥ agni saṃyogena pratiṣiddhā na punar utpadyate evam adṛṣṭa kāritam śarīram apavarge punar na utpadyate iti 
[0916,iv_0916,vi]	na akṛta abhyāgama prasaṅgāt na ayam asti dṛṣṭāntaḥ kasmāt akṛta abhyāgama prasaṅgāt akṛtam pramāṇataḥ anupapannam tasya abhyāgamaḥ abhyupapattiḥ vyavasāyaḥ etat śraddadhānena pramāṇataḥ ṇu papannam mantavyam tasmāt na ayam dṛṣṭāntaḥ na pratyakṣam na ca anumānam kiṃcid ucyate iti tat idam dṛṣṭāntasya sādhya sama tvam abhidhīyate iti atha vā na akṛta abhyāgama prasaṅgāt aṇu śyāma tā dṛṣṭāntena akarma nimittām śarīra utpattim samādadhānasya akṛta abhyāgama prasaṅgaḥ akṛte sukha duḥkha hetau karmaṇi puruṣasya sukham duḥkham abhyāgacchati iti prasajyeta om iti bruvataḥ pratyakṣa anumāna āgama virodhaḥ 
[0917,i]	pratyakṣa virodhaḥ tāvat bhinnam idam sukha duḥkham pratyātma vedanīya tvāt pratyakṣam sarva śarīriṇām kaḥ bhedaḥ tīvram mandam ciram āśu nānā prakāram eka prakāram iti evam ādiḥ viśeṣaḥ na ca asti pratyātma niyataḥ sukha duḥkha hetu viśeṣaḥ na ca asati hetu viśeṣe phala viśeṣaḥ dṛśyate karma nimitte tu sukha duḥkha yoge karmaṇām tīvra manda tā upapatteḥ karma sañcayānām ca utkarṣa apakarṣa bhāvāt nānāvidha ekavidha bhāvāt ca karmaṇām sukha duḥkha bheda upapattiḥ saḥ ayam hetu bheda abhāvāt dṛṣṭaḥ sukha duḥkha bhedaḥ na syāt iti pratyakṣa virodhaḥ 
[0917,ii]	tathā anumāna virodhaḥ dṛṣṭam hi puruṣa guṇa vyavasthānāt sukha duḥkha vyavasthānam yaḥ khalu cetanāvān sādhana nirvartanīyam sukham buddhvā tat īpsan sādhana avāptaye prayatate sa sukhena yujyate na viparītaḥ yaḥ ca sādhana nirvartanīyam duḥkham buddhvā tat jihāsuḥ sādhana parivarjanāya yatate sa ca duḥkhena tyajyate na viparītaḥ asti ca idam yatnam antareṇa cetanānām sukha duḥkha vyavasthānam tena api cetana guṇa antara vyavasthā kṛtena bhavitavyam iti anumānam 
[0918,i_0918,ii]	tat etat akarma nimitte sukha duḥkha yoge virudhyate iti tat ca guṇa antaram asaṃvedya tvāt adṛṣṭam vipāka kāla aniyamāt ca avyavasthitam buddhi ādayaḥ tu saṃvedyāḥ ca apavargiṇaḥ ca iti atha āgama virodhaḥ bahu khalu idam ārṣam ṛṣīṇām upadeśa jātam anuṣṭhāna parivarjana āśrayam upadeśa phalam ca śarīriṇām varṇa āśrama vibhāgeṇa anuṣṭhāna lakṣaṇā pravṛttiḥ parivarjana lakṣaṇā nivṛttiḥ tat ca ubhayam etasyām dṛṣṭau na asti karma su caritam duścaritam vā karma nimittaḥ puruṣāṇām sukha duḥkha yogaḥ iti virudhyate sā iyam pāpiṣṭhānām mithyādṛṣṭiḥ akarma nimittā śarīra sṛṣṭiḥ akarma nimittaḥ sukha duḥkha yogaḥ iti 
[0921,i_0921,iii]	manasaḥ anantaram pravṛttiḥ parīkṣitavyā tatra khalu yāvat dharma adharma āśraya śarīra ādi parīkṣitam sarvā sā pravṛtteḥ parīkṣā iti āha pravṛttiḥ yathā uktā tathā parīkṣitā iti 
[0923,i_0923,iii]	pravṛtti anantarāḥ tarhi doṣāḥ parīkṣyantām iti atas āha tathā doṣāḥ parīkṣitāḥ iti buddhi samāna āśraya tvāt ātma guṇāḥ pravṛtti hetu tvāt punarbhava pratisandhāna sāmarthyāt ca saṃsāra hetavaḥ saṃsārasya anādi tvāt anādinā prabandhena pravartante mithyājñāna nivṛttiḥ tattva jñānāt tad nivṛttau rāga dveṣa prabandha ucchyede apavargaḥ iti prādurbhāva tirodhāna dharmakāḥ iti evamādi uktam doṣāṇām iti 
[0924,i_0924,iii]	pravartanā lakṣaṇāḥ doṣāḥ iti uktam tathā ca ime māna īrṣyā asūyā vicikitsā matsara ādayaḥ te kasmāt na upasaṅkhyāyante iti atas āha tat trairāśyam rāga dveṣa moha artha antara bhāvāt teṣām doṣāṇām trayaḥ rāśayaḥ trayaḥ pakṣāḥ rāga pakṣaḥ kāmaḥ matsaraḥ spṛhā tṛṣṇā lobhaḥ iti dveṣapakṣaḥ krodhaḥ īrṣyā asūyā drohaḥ amarṣaḥ iti mohapakṣaḥ mithyājñānam vicikitsā mānaḥ pramādaḥ iti trairāśyān na upasaṅkhyāyante iti lakṣaṇasya tarhi abhedāt tritvam anupapannam na anupapannam rāga dveṣa moha artha antara bhāvāt āsakti lakṣaṇaḥ rāgaḥ amarṣa lakṣaṇaḥ dveṣaḥ mithyāpratipatti lakṣaṇaḥ mohaḥ iti etat pratyātma vedanīyam sarva śarīriṇām vijānāti ayam śarīrī rāgam utpannam asti me adhyātmam rāga dharmaḥ iti virāgam ca vijānāti na asti me adhyātmam rāga dharmaḥ iti evam itarayoḥ api iti māna īrṣyā asūyā prabhṛtayaḥ tu trairāśyam anupatitāḥ iti na upasaṅkhyāyante 
[0927,i_0927,ii]	na eka pratyanīka bhāvāt na artha antaram rāga ādayaḥ kasmāt eka pratyanīka bhāvāt tattva jñānam samyak matiḥ ārya prajñā sambodhaḥ iti ekam idam pratyanīkam trayāṇām iti 
[0928,i_0928,ii]	vyabhicārāt ahetuḥ eka pratyanīkāḥ pṛthivyām śyāma ādayaḥ agni saṃyogena ekena eka yonayaḥ ca pāka jāḥ iti 
[0928,iii_0928,v]	sati ca artha antara bhāve teṣām mohaḥ pāpīyān na amūḍhasya itara utpatteḥ mohaḥ pāpaḥ pāpataraḥ vā dvau abhipretya uktam kasmāt na amūḍhasya itara utpatteḥ amūḍhasya rāga dveṣāḥ na utpadyante mūḍhasya tu yathā saṅkalpam utpattiḥ viṣayeṣu rañjanīyāḥ saṅkalpāḥ rāga hetavaḥ kopanīyāḥ saṅkalpāḥ dveṣa hetavaḥ ubhaye ca saṅkalpāḥ na mithyā pratipatti lakṣaṇa tvāt mohāt anye tau imau moha yonī rāga dveṣau iti tattva jñānāt ca moha nivṛttau rāga dveṣa anutpattiḥ iti eka pratyanīka bhāva upapattiḥ evam ca kṛtvā tattva jñānāt duḥkha janma pravṛtti doṣa mithyā jñānānām uttarottara apāye tad anantara abhāvāt apavargaḥ iti vyākhyātam iti 
[0930,i_0930,iii]	prāptaḥ tarhi nimitta naimittika bhāvāt artha antara bhāvaḥ doṣebhyaḥ anyat dhi nimittam anyat ca naimittikam iti doṣa nimitta tvāt adoṣaḥ mohaḥ iti 
[0930,iv_0930,v]	na doṣa lakṣaṇa avarodhāt mohasya pravarttanā lakṣaṇāḥ doṣāḥ iti anena doṣa lakṣaṇena avarudhyate doṣeṣu mohaḥ iti 
[0931,i_0931,ii]	nimitta naimittika upapatteḥ ca tulya jātīyānām apratiṣedhaḥ dravyāṇām guṇānām vā anekavidha vikalpaḥ nimitta naimittika bhāve tulya jātīyānām dṛṣṭaḥ iti 
[0931,iii_0931,v]	doṣān antaram pretyabhāvaḥ tasya asiddhiḥ ātmanaḥ nitya tvāt na khalu nityam kiṃcid jāyate mriyate vā iti janma maraṇayoḥ nitya tvāt ātmanaḥ anupapattiḥ ubhayam ca pretyabhāvaḥ iti tatra ayam siddha anuvādaḥ ātma nitya tve pretyabhāva siddhiḥ nityaḥ ayam ātmā praiti pūrva śarīram jahāti mriyate iti pretya ca pūrva śarīram hitvā bhavati jāyate śarīra antaram upādattaḥ iti tat ca etat ubhayam punar utpattiḥ pretyabhāvaḥ iti atra uktam pūrva śarīram hitvā śarīra antara upādānam pretyabhāvaḥ iti tat ca etat nitya tve sambhavati iti yasya tu sattva utpādaḥ sattva nirodhaḥ pretyabhāvaḥ tasya kṛta hānam akṛta abhyāgamaḥ ca doṣaḥ uccheda hetuvāde ṛṣi upadeśāḥ ca anarthakāḥ iti 
[0933,i_0934,i]	katham utpattiḥ iti ced vyaktāt vyaktānām pratyakṣa prāmāṇyāt kena prakāreṇa kiṃdharmakāt kāraṇāt vyaktam śarīra ādi utpadyate iti vyaktāt bhūta samākhyātāt pṛthivī āditaḥ parama sūkṣmāt nityāt vyaktam śarīra indriya viṣaya upakaraṇa ādhāram prajñātam dravyam utpadyate vyaktam ca khalu indriya grāhyam tad sāmānyāt kāraṇam api vyaktam kim sāmānyam rūpa ādi guṇa yogaḥ rūpa ādi guṇa yuktebhyaḥ pṛthivī ādibhyaḥ nityebhyaḥ rūpa ādi guṇa yuktam śarīra ādi utpadyate pratyakṣa prāmāṇyāt dṛṣṭaḥ hi rūpa ādi guṇa yuktebhyaḥ mṛd prabhṛtibhyaḥ tathābhūtasya dravyasya utpādaḥ tena ca adṛṣṭasya anumānam iti rūpa ādīnām anvaya darśanāt prakṛti vikārayoḥ pṛthivī ādīnām nityānām atīndriyāṇām kāraṇa bhāvaḥ anumīyate iti 
[0934,ii_0934,iii]	na ghaṭāt ghaṭa aniṣpatteḥ idam api pratyakṣam na khalu vyaktāt ghaṭāt vyaktaḥ ghaṭaḥ utpadyamānaḥ dṛśyate iti vyaktāt vyaktasya anutpatti darśanāt na vyaktam kāraṇam iti 
[0935,i_0935,ii]	vyaktāt ghaṭa niṣpatteḥ apratiṣedhaḥ na brūmaḥ sarvam sarvasya kāraṇam iti kin tu yat utpadyate vyaktam dravyam tat tathābhūtāt eva utpadyate iti vyaktam ca tat mṛd dravyam kapāla saṃjñakam yatas ghaṭaḥ utpadyate na ca etat nihnuvānaḥ kvacid abhyanujñām labdhum arhati iti tat etat tattvam 
[0935,iii_0936,i]	atas param prāvādukānām dṛṣṭayaḥ pradarśyante abhāvāt bhāva utpattiḥ na anupamṛdya prādurbhāvāt asataḥ sat utpadyate iti ayam pakṣaḥ kasmāt upamṛdya prādurbhāvāt upamṛdya bījam aṅkuraḥ utpadyate na anupamṛdya na ced vīja upamardaḥ aṅkura kāraṇam anupamarde api bījasya aṅkura utpattiḥ syāt iti 
[0936,ii_0936,iv]	atra abhidhīyate vyāghātāt aprayogaḥ upamṛdya prādurbhāvāt iti ayuktaḥ prayogaḥ vyāghātāt yat upamṛdnāti na tat upamṛdya prādurbhavitum arhati vidyamāna tvāt yat ca prādurbhavati na tena aprādurbhūtena avidyamānena upamardaḥ iti 
[0937,i_0937,ii]	na atīta anāgatayoḥ kāraka śabda prayogāt atīte ca anāgate ca avidyamāne kāraka śabdāḥ prayujyante putraḥ janiṣyate janiṣyamāṇam putram abhinandati putrasya janiṣyamāṇasya nāma karoti abhūt kumbhaḥ bhinnam kumbham anuśocati bhinnasya kumbhasya kapālāni ajātāḥ putrāḥ pitaram tāpayanti iti bahulam bhāktāḥ prayogāḥ dṛśyante kā punar iyam bhaktiḥ ānantaryam bhaktiḥ ānantarya sāmarthyāt upamṛdya prādurbhāva arthaḥ prādurbhaviṣyan aṅkuraḥ upamṛdnāti iti bhāktam kartṛ tvam iti 
[0938,i_0938,ii]	na vinaṣṭebhyaḥ aniṣpatteḥ na vinaṣṭāt bījāt aṅkuraḥ utpadyate iti tasmāt na abhāvāt bhāva utpattiḥ iti 
[0939,i_0939,ii]	krama nirdeśāt apratiṣedhaḥ upamarda prādurbhāvayoḥ paurvāparya niyamaḥ kramaḥ sa khalu abhāvāt bhāva utpatteḥ hetuḥ nirdiśyate sa ca na pratiṣidhyate iti vyāhata vyūhānām avayavānām pūrva vyūha nivṛttau vyūha antarāt dravya niṣpattiḥ na abhāvāt bīja avayavāḥ kutaścid nimittāt prādurbhūta kriyāḥ pūrva vyūham jahati vyūha antaram ca āpadyante vyūha antarāt aṅkuraḥ utpadyate dṛśyante khalu avayavāḥ tad saṃyogāḥ ca aṅkura utpatti hetavaḥ na ca anivṛtte pūrva vyūhe bīja avayavānām śakyam vyūha antareṇa bhavitum iti upamarda prādurbhāvayoḥ paurvāparya niyamaḥ kramaḥ tasmāt na abhāvāt bhāva utpattiḥ iti na ca anyat bīja avayavebhyaḥ aṅkura utpatti kāraṇam iti upapadyate bīja upādāna niyamaḥ iti 
[0939,iii_0939,v]	atha aparaḥ āha īśvaraḥ kāraṇam puruṣa karma aphalya darśanāt puruṣaḥ ayam samīhamānaḥ na avaśyam samīha aphalam prāpnoti tena anumīyate para adhīnam puruṣasya karma phala ārādhanam iti yat adhīnam saḥ īśvaraḥ tasmāt īśvaraḥ kāraṇam iti 
[0942,i_0942,ii]	na puruṣa karma abhāve phala aniṣpatteḥ īśvara adhīnā ced phala niṣpattiḥ syāt api tarhi puruṣasya samīhām antareṇa phalam niṣpadyeta iti 
[0943,i_0945,i]	tad kārita tvāt ahetuḥ puruṣakāram īśvaraḥ anugṛhṇāti phalāya puruṣasya yatamānasya īśvaraḥ phalam sampādayati iti yadā na sampādayati tadā puruṣa karma aphalam bhavati iti tasmāt īśvara kārita tvāt ahetuḥ puruṣa karma abhāve phala aniṣpatteḥ iti guṇa viśiṣṭam ātma antaram īśvaraḥ tasya ātma kalpāt kalpa antara anupapattiḥ adharma mithyā jñāna pramāda hānyā dharma jñāna samādhi sampadā ca viśiṣṭam ātma antaram īśvaraḥ tasya ca dharma samādhi phalam aṇima ādi aṣṭavidham aiśvaryam saṅkalpa anuvidhāyī ca asya dharmaḥ pratyātma vṛttīn dharma adharma sañcayān pṛthivī ādīni ca bhūtāni pravartayati evam ca sva kṛta abhyāgamasya ālopena nirmāṇa prākāmyam īśvarasya sva kṛta karma phalam veditavyam āpta kalpaḥ ca ayam yathā pitā apatyānām tathā pitṛ bhūtaḥ īśvaraḥ bhūtānām na ca ātma kalpāt anyaḥ kalpaḥ sambhavati na tāvat asya buddhim vinā kaścid dharmaḥ liṅga bhūtaḥ śakyaḥ upapādayitum āgamāt ca draṣṭā boddhā sarva jñātā īśvaraḥ iti buddhi ādibhiḥ ca ātma liṅgaiḥ nirupākhyam īśvaram pratyakṣa anumāna āgama viṣaya atītam kaḥ śaktaḥ upapādayitum sva kṛta abhyāgama lopena ca pravartamānasya asya yat uktam pratiṣedha jātam akarma nimitte śarīra sarge tat sarvam prasajyate iti 
[0958,i_0958,iii]	aparaḥ idānīm āha animittataḥ bhāva utpattiḥ kaṇṭaka taikṣṇya ādi darśanāt animittā śarīra ādi utpattiḥ kasmāt kaṇṭaka taikṣṇya ādi darśanāt kaṇṭakasya taikṣṇyam parvata dhātūnām citra tā grāvṇām ślakṣṇa tā nirnimittam ca upādāna vat ca dṛṣṭam tathā śarīra ādi sargaḥ api iti 
[0958,iv_0958,v]	animitta nimitta tvāt na animittataḥ animittataḥ bhāva utpattiḥ iti ucyate yatas ca utpadyate tad nimittam animittasya nimitta tvāt na animittāḥ bhāva utpattiḥ iti 
[0960,i_0960,ii]	nimitta animittayoḥ artha antara bhāvāt apratiṣedhaḥ anyat dhi nimittam anyat ca nimitta pratyākhyānam na ca pratyākhyānam eva pratyākhyeyam yathānudakaḥ kamaṇḍaluḥ iti na udaka pratiṣedhaḥ udakam bhavati iti sa khalu ayam vādaḥ akarma nimittaḥ śarīra ādi sargaḥ iti etasmāt na bhidyate abhedāt tad pratiṣedhena eva pratiṣiddhaḥ veditavyaḥ iti 
[0962,i_0962,iii]	anye tu manyante sarvam anityam utpatti vināśa dharmaka tvāt kim anityam nāma yasya kadācid bhāvaḥ tat anityam utpatti dharmakam anutpannam na asti vināśa dharmakam ca vinaṣṭam na asti kim punar sarvam bhautikam ca śarīra ādi abhautikam ca buddhi ādi tat ubhayam utpatti vināśa dharmakam vijñāyate tasmāt tat sarvam anityam iti 
[0962,iv_0962,v]	na anitya tā nitya tvāt yadi tāvat sarvasya anitya tā nityā tad nitya tvāt na sarvam anityam atha anityā tasyām avidyamānāyām sarvam nityam iti 
[0964,i_0964,ii]	tat anitya tvam agneḥ dāhyam vināśya anuvināśa vat tasyāḥ anitya tāyāḥ api anitya tvam katham yathā agniḥ dāhyam vināśya anuvinaśyati evam sarvasya anitya tā sarvam vināśya anuvinaśyati iti 
[0964,iii_0964,iv]	nityasya apratyākhyānam yathā upalabdhi vyavasthānāt ayam khalu vādaḥ nityam pratyācaṣṭe nityasya ca pratyākhyānam anupapannam kasmāt yathā upalabdhi vyavasthānāt yasya utpatti vināśa dharmaka tvam upalabhyate pramāṇataḥ tat anityam yasya na upalabhyate tad viparītam na ca parama sūkṣmāṇām bhūtānām ākāśa kāla diś ātma manasām tad guṇānām ca keṣāñcid sāmānya viśeṣa samavāyānām ca utpatti vināśa dharmaka tvam pramāṇataḥ upalabhyate tasmāt nityāni etāni iti 
[0966,i_0966,iii]	ayam anyaḥ ekāntaḥ sarvam nityam pañcabhūta nitya tvāt bhūtamātram idam sarvam tāni ca nityāni bhūta uccheda anupapatteḥ iti 
[0966,iv_0966,v]	na utpatti vināśa kāraṇa upalabdheḥ utpatti kāraṇam ca upalabhyate vināśa kāraṇam ca tat sarva nitya tve vyāhanyate iti 
[0967,i_0967,ii]	tad lakṣaṇa avarodhāt apratiṣedhaḥ yasya utpatti vināśa kāraṇam upalabhyate iti manyase na tat bhūta lakṣaṇa hīnam artha antaram gṛhyate bhūta lakṣaṇa avarodhāt bhūtamātram idam iti uktaḥ ayam pratiṣedhaḥ iti 
[0968,i_0968,ii]	na utpatti tad kāraṇa upalabdheḥ kāraṇa samāna guṇasya utpattiḥ kāraṇam ca upalabhyate na ca etat ubhayam nitya viṣayam na ca utpatti tad kāraṇa upalabdhiḥ śakyā pratyākhyātum na ca āviṣayā kācid upalabdhiḥ upalabdhi sāmarthyāt kāraṇena samāna guṇam kāryam utpadyate iti anumīyate sa kha lu upalabdheḥ viṣayaḥ iti evam ca tad lakṣaṇa avarodha upapattiḥ iti 
[0968,iii_0969,i]	utpatti vināśa kāraṇa prayuktasya jñātuḥ prayatnaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti prasiddhaḥ ca avayavī tad dharmā utpatti vināśa dharmā ca avayavī siddhaḥ iti śabda karma buddhi ādīnām ca avyāptiḥ pañcabhūta nitya tvāt tad lakṣaṇa avarodhāt ca iti anena śabda karma buddhi sukha duḥkha icchā dveṣa prayatnāḥ ca na vyāptāḥ tasmāt anekāntaḥ 
[0969,ii_0970,i]	svapna viṣaya abhimāna vat mithyā upalabdhiḥ iti ced bhūta upalabdhau tulyam yathā svapne viṣaya abhimānaḥ evam utpatti kāraṇa abhimānaḥ iti evam ca etat bhūta upalabdhau tulyam pṛthivī ādi upalabdhiḥ api svapna viṣaya abhimāna vat prasajyate pṛthivī ādi abhāve sarva vyavahāra vilopaḥ iti ced tat itaratra samānam utpatti vināśa kāraṇa upalabdhi viṣayasya api abhāve sarva vyavahāra vilopaḥ iti saḥ ayam nityānām atīndriya tvāt aviṣaya tvāt ca utpatti vināśayoḥ svapna viṣaya abhimāna vat iti ahetuḥ iti 
[0970,ii_0971,iii]	avasthitasya upādānasya dharma mātram nivartate dharma mātram upajāyate sa khalu utpatti vināśayoḥ viṣayaḥ yat ca upajāyate tat prāk api upajananāt asti yat ca nivartate tat nivṛttam api asti iti evam ca sarvasya nitya tvam iti na vyavasthā anupapatteḥ ayam upajanaḥ iyam nivṛttiḥ iti vyavasthā na upapadyate upajāta nivṛttayoḥ vidyamāna tvāt ayam dharmaḥ upajātaḥ ayam nivṛttaḥ iti sadbhāva aviśeṣāt avyavasthā idānīm upajana nivṛttī na idānīm iti kāla vyavasthā na upapadyate sarvadā vidyamāna tvāt asya dharmasya upajana nivṛttī na asya iti vyavasthā anupapattiḥ ubhyoḥ aviśeṣāt anāgataḥ atītaḥ iti ca kāla vyavasthā anupapattiḥ vartamānasya sadbhāva lakṣaṇa tvāt avidyamānasya ātma lābhaḥ upajanaḥ vidyamānasya ātma hānam nivṛttiḥ iti etasmin sati na ete doṣāḥ tasmāt yat uktam prāk api upajanāt asti nivṛttam ca asti tat ayuktam iti 
[0971,iv_0973,i]	ayam anyaḥ ekāntaḥ sarvam pṛthak bhāva lakṣaṇa pṛthaktvāt sarvam nānā na kaścid ekaḥ bhāvaḥ vidyate kasmāt bhāva lakṣaṇa pṛthaktvāt bhāvasya lakṣaṇam abhidhānam yena lakṣyate bhāvaḥ sa samākhyā śabdaḥ tasya pṛthak viṣaya tvāt sarvaḥ bhāva samākhyā śabdaḥ samūha vācī kumbhaḥ iti saṃjñā śabdaḥ gandha rasa rūpa sparśa samūhe budhna pārśva grīvā ādi samūhe ca varttate nidarśana mātram ca idam iti 
[0973,ii_0973,iii]	na aneka lakṣaṇaiḥ eka bhāva niṣpatteḥ anekavidha lakṣaṇaiḥ iti madhyama pada lopī samāsaḥ gandha ādibhiḥ ca guṇaiḥ budhna ādibhiḥ ca avayavaiḥ sambaddhaḥ ekaḥ bhāvaḥ niṣpadyate guṇa vyatiriktam ca dravyam avayava atiriktaḥ ca avayavi iti vibhakta nyāyam ca etat ubhayam iti 
[0974,i_0974,iii]	atha api lakṣaṇa vyavasthānāt eva apratiṣedhaḥ na kaścid ekaḥ bhāvaḥ iti ayuktaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ kasmāt lakṣaṇa vyavasthānāt eva yat iha lakṣaṇam bhāvasya saṃjñā śabda bhūtam tat ekasmin vyavasthitam yam kumbham adrākṣam tam spṛśāmi yam eva asprākṣam tam paśyāmi iti na aṇu samūhaḥ gṛhyate iti aṇu samūhe ca agṛhyamāṇe yat gṛhyate tat ekam eva iti 
[0974,iv]	atha api etat anūktam na asti ekaḥ bhāvaḥ yasmāt samudāyaḥ eka anupapatteḥ na asti eva samūhaḥ na asti ekaḥ bhāvaḥ yasmāt samūhe bhāva śabda prayogaḥ ekasya ca anupapatteḥ samūhaḥ na upapadyate eka samuccayaḥ hi samūhaḥ iti vyāhata tvāt anupapannam na asti ekaḥ bhāvaḥ iti yasya pratiṣedhaḥ pratijñāyate samūhe bhāva śabda prayogāt iti hetum bruvatā saḥ eva abhyanujñāyate eka samuccayaḥ hi samūhaḥ iti samūhe bhāva śabda prayogāt iti ca samūham āśritya pratyekam samūhi pratiṣedhaḥ na asti ekaḥ bhāvaḥ iti saḥ ayam ubhayatas vyāghātāt yat kiñcana vādaḥ iti 
[0977,i_0977,iii]	ayam aparaḥ ekāntaḥ sarvam abhāvaḥ bhāveṣu itaretarābhāva siddheḥ yāvat bhāva jātam tat sarvam abhāvaḥ kasmāt bhāveṣu itaretarābhāva siddheḥ asan gauḥ aśva ātmanā anaśvaḥ gauḥ asan aśvaḥ gavā ātmanā agauḥ aśvaḥ iti asat pratyayasya pratiṣedhasya ca bhāva śabdena sāmānādhikaraṇyāt sarvam abhāvaḥ iti 
[0978,i]	pratijñā vākye padayoḥ pratijñā hetvoḥ ca vyāghātāt ayuktam anekasya aśeṣa tā sarva śabdasya arthaḥ bhāva pratiṣedhaḥ ca abhāva śabdasya arthaḥ pūrvam sa upākhyam uttaram nirupākhyam tatra samupākhyāyamānam katham nirupākhyam abhāvaḥ syāt iti na jātu abhāvaḥ nirupākhyaḥ aneka tayā aśeṣa tayā śakyaḥ pratijñātum iti sarvam etat abhāvaḥ iti ced yat idam sarvam iti manyase tad abhāvaḥ iti evam ced anivṛttaḥ vyāghātaḥ anekam aśeṣam ca iti na abhāve pratyayena śakyam bhavitum asti ca ayam pratyayaḥ sarvam iti tasmāt na abhāvaḥ iti 
[0978,ii]	pratijñā hetvoḥ ca vyāghātaḥ sarvam abhāvaḥ iti bhāva pratiṣedhaḥ pratijñā bhāveṣu itaretara abhāva siddheḥ iti hetuḥ bhāveṣu itaretarābhāvam anujñāya āśritya ca itaretara abhāva siddhyā sarvam abhāvaḥ iti ucyate yadi sarvam abhāvaḥ bhāveṣu itaretara abhāva siddheḥ iti na upapadyate atha bhāveṣu itaretarābhāva siddhiḥ sarvam abhāvaḥ iti na upapadyate 
[0980,i_0980,iii]	sūtreṇa ca abhisambandhaḥ na svabhāva siddheḥ bhāvānām na sarvam abhāvaḥ kasmāt svena bhāvena sadbhāvāt bhāvānām svena dharmeṇa bhāvāḥ bhavanti iti pratijñāyate kaḥ ca svaḥ dharmaḥ bhāvānām dravya guṇa karmaṇām sat ādi sāmānyam dravyāṇām kriyāvat iti evamādi viśeṣaḥ sparśa paryantāḥ pṛthivyāḥ iti ca pratyekam ca anantaḥ bhedaḥ sāmānya viśeṣa samavāyānām ca viśiṣṭāḥ dharmāḥ gṛhyante 
[0981,i_0981,iii]	saḥ ayam abhāvasya nirupākhya tvāt sampratyāyakaḥ artha bhedaḥ na syāt asti tu ayam tasmāt na sarvam abhāvaḥ iti atha vā na svabhāva siddheḥ bhāvānām iti svarūpa siddheḥ iti gauḥ iti prayujyamāne śabde jāti viśiṣṭam dravyam gṛhyate na abhāva mātram yadi ca sarvam abhāvaḥ gauḥ iti abhāvaḥ pratīyeta go śabdena ca abhāvaḥ ucyeta yasmāt tu go śabda prayoge dravya viśeṣaḥ pratīyate na abhāvaḥ tasmāt ayuktam iti atha vā na svabhāva siddheḥ iti asan gauḥ aśva ātmanā iti gavā ātmanā kasmāt na ucyate avacanāt gavā ātmanā gauḥ asti iti svabhāva siddhiḥ anaśvaḥ aśvaḥ iti vā gauḥ agauḥ iti vā kasmāt na ucyate avacanāt svena rūpeṇa vidyamāna tā dravyasya iti vijñāyate 
[0982,i]	avyatireka pratiṣedhe ca bhāvena asat pratyaya sāmānādhikaraṇyam bhāve saṃyoga ādi sambandhaḥ vyatirekaḥ atra avyatirekaḥ abheda ākhya sambandhaḥ tad pratiṣedhe sadā ca asat pratyaya sāmānādhikaraṇyam yathā na santi kuṇḍe badarāṇi iti asan gauḥ aśva ātmanā anaśvaḥ gauḥ iti ca gavāśvayoḥ avyatirekaḥ pratiṣidhyate gavāśvayoḥ eka tvam na asti iti tasmin pratiṣidhyamāne bhāvena gavā sāmānādhikaraṇyam asat pratyayasya asan gauḥ aśva ātmanā iti yathā na santi kuṇḍe badarāṇi iti kuṇḍe badara saṃyoge pratiṣidhyamāne sadbhiḥ asat pratyayasya sāmānādhikaraṇyam iti 
[0983,i_0983,ii]	na svabhāva siddhiḥ āpekṣika tvāt apekṣā akṛtam āpekṣikam hrasva apekṣā akṛtam dīrgham dīrgha apekṣā akṛtam hrasvam na svena ātmanā avasthitam kiñcid kasmāt apekṣā sāmarthyāt tasmāt na svabhāva siddhiḥ bhāvānām iti 
[0983,iii_0985,i]	vyāhata tvāt ayuktam yadi hrasva apekṣā akṛtam dīrgham hrasvam anāpekṣikam kim idānīm apekṣya hrasvam iti gṛhyate atha dīrgha apekṣā akṛtam hrasvam dīrgham anāpekṣikam evam itaretara āśrayayoḥ eka abhāve anyatara abhāvāt ubhaya abhāvaḥ iti apekṣā vyavasthā anupapannā svabhāva siddhau asatyām samayoḥ parimaṇḍalayoḥ vā dravyayoḥ āpekṣike dīrgha tva hrasva tve kasmāt na bhavataḥ apekṣāyām anapekṣāyām ca dravyayoḥ abhedaḥ yāvatī dravye apekṣamāṇe tāvatī eva anapekṣamāṇe na anyataratra bhedaḥ āpekṣika tve tu sati anyataratra viśeṣa upajanaḥ syāt iti kim apekṣā sāmarthyam iti ced dvayoḥ grahaṇe atiśaya grahaṇa upapattiḥ dve dravye paśyan ekatra vidyamānam atiśayam gṛhṇāti tat dīrgham iti vyavasyati yat ca hīnam gṛhṇāti tat dhrasvam iti vyavasyati iti etat ca apekṣā sāmarthyam iti 
[0986,i_0988,ii]	atha ime saṅkhyā ekānta vādāḥ sarvam ekam sat aviśeṣāt sarvam dvedhā nitya anityabhedāt sarvam tredhā jñātā jñānam jñeyam iti sarvam caturddhā pramātā pramāṇam prameyam pramitiḥ iti evam yathāsambhavam anye api iti tatra parīkṣā saṅkhyā ekānta asiddhiḥ kāraṇa anupapatti upapattibhyām yadi sādhya sādhanayoḥ nānātvam ekāntaḥ na siddhi ati vyatirekāt atha sādhya sādhanayoḥ abhedaḥ evam api ekāntaḥ na sidhyati sādhana abhāvāt na hi hetum antareṇa kasyacid siddhiḥ iti 
[0988,iii_0988,iv]	na kāraṇa avayava bhāvāt na saṅkhyā ekāntānām asiddhiḥ kasmāt kāraṇasya avayava bhāvāt avayavaḥ kaścid sādhana bhūtaḥ iti avyatirekaḥ evam dvaita ādīnām api iti 
[0990,i_0991,i]	niravayava tvāt ahetuḥ kāraṇasya avayava bhāvāt iti ahetuḥ kasmāt sarvam ekam iti anapavargeṇa pratijñāya kasyacid eka tvam ucyate tatra vyapavṛktaḥ avayavaḥ sādhana bhūtaḥ na upapadyate evam dvaita ādiṣu api iti te khalu ime saṅkhyā ekāntāḥ yadi viśeṣa kāritasya artha bheda vistārasya pratyākhyānena varttante pratyakṣa anumāna āgama virodhān mithyā vādāḥ bhavanti atha abhyanujñānena varttante samāna dharma kāritaḥ artha saṃgrahaḥ viśeṣa kāritaḥ ca artha bhedaḥ iti evam ekānta tvam jahati iti te khalu ete tattva jñāna praviveka artham ekāntāḥ parīkṣitāḥ iti 
[0992,i_0992,iii]	pretya bhāva anantaram phalam tasmin sadyas kāla antare ca phala niṣpatteḥ saṃśayaḥ pacati dogdhi iti sadyas phalam odana payasī karṣati vapati iti kāla antare phalam śasya adhigamaḥ iti asti ca iyam kriyā agnihotram juhuyāt svarga kāmaḥ iti etasyāḥ phale saṃśayaḥ na sadyas kāla antara upabhogya tvāt svargaḥ phalam śrūyate tat ca bhinne asmin deha bhedāt utpadyate iti na sadyas grāma ādi kāmānām ārambha phalam iti 
[0995,i_0995,ii]	kāla antareṇa aniṣpattiḥ hetu vināśāt dhvastāyām pravṛttau pravṛtteḥ phalam na kāraṇam antareṇa utpattum arhati na khalu vai vinaṣṭāt kāraṇāt kiñcid utpadyate iti 
[0995,iii_0995,iv]	prāk niṣpatteḥ vṛkṣa phala vat tat syāt yathā phala arthinā vṛkṣa mūle seka ādi parikarma kriyate tasmin ca pradhvaste pṛthivī dhātuḥ abdhātunā saṃgṛhīta āntareṇa tejasā pacyamānaḥ rasa dravyam nirvartayati sa dravya bhūtaḥ rasaḥ vṛkṣa anugataḥ pāka viśiṣṭaḥ vyūha viśeṣeṇa sanniviśamānaḥ parṇa ādi phalam nirvartayati evam pariṣeka ādi karma ca arthavat na ca vinaṣṭāt phala niṣpattiḥ tathā pravṛttyā saṃskāraḥ dharma adharma lakṣaṇaḥ janyate sa jātaḥ nimitta antara anugṛhītaḥ kāla antare phalam niṣpādayati iti uktan ca etat pūrva kṛta phala anubandhāt tad utpattiḥ iti 
[0996,i_0996,iii]	tat idam prāk niṣpatteḥ niṣpadyamānam na āsat na san na sat asat sat asatoḥ vaidharmyāt prāk niṣpatteḥ niṣpatti dharmakam na asat upādāna niyamāt kasyacid utpattaye kiñcid upādeyam na sarvam sarvasya iti asadbhāve niyamaḥ na upapadyate iti na sat prāṅ utpatteḥ vidyamānasya utpattiḥ anupapanna iti na sat asat sat asatoḥ vaidharmyāt sat iti artha abhyanujñā asat iti artha pratiṣedhaḥ etayoḥ vyāghātaḥ vaidharmyam vyāghātāt avyatireka anupapattiḥ iti 
[0996,iv_0999,i]	prāk utpatteḥ utpatti dharmakam asat iti addhā kasmāt utpāda vyaya darśanāt yat punaruktam prāk utpatteḥ kāryam na asat upādāna niyamāt iti 
[0999,ii_0999,iii]	buddhi siddham tu tat asat idam asya utpattaye samartham na sarvam iti prāk utpatteḥ niyata kāraṇam kāryam buddhyā siddham utpatti niyama darśanāt tasmāt upādāna niyamasya upapattiḥ sati tu kārye prāk utpatteḥ utpattiḥ eva na asti iti 
[1003,i_1003,ii]	āśraya vyatirekāt vṛkṣa phala utpatti vat iti ahetuḥ mūla seka ādi parikarma phalam ca ubhayam vṛkṣa āśrayam karma ca iha śarīre phalam ca amutraḥ iti āśraya vyatirekāt ahetuḥ iti 
[1004,i_1004,ii]	prīteḥ ātma āśraya tvāt apratiṣedhaḥ prītiḥ ātma pratyakṣa tvāt ātma āśrayā tad āśrayam eva karma dharma saṃjñitam dharmasya ātma guṇa tvāt tasmāt āśraya vyatireka anupapattiḥ iti 
[1004,iii_1004,iv]	na putra paśu strī paricchada hiraṇya anna ādi phala nirdeśāt putra ādi phalam nirdiśyate na prītiḥ grāma kāmaḥ yajeta putra kāmaḥ yajete ti tatra yat uktam prītiḥ phalam iti etat ayuktam iti 
[1005,i_1005,ii]	tad sambandhāt phala niṣpatteḥ teṣu phalavat upacāraḥ putra ādi sambandhāt phalam prīti lakṣaṇam utpadyate iti putra ādiṣu phalavat upacāraḥ yathā anne prāṇa śabdaḥ annam vai prāṇāḥ iti 
[1006,i_1006,ii]	phala anantaram duḥkham uddiṣṭam uktam ca bādhanā lakṣaṇam duḥkham iti tat kim idam pratyātma vedanīyasya sarva jantu pratyakṣasya sukhasya pratyākhyānam āhosvit anyaḥ kalpaḥ iti anyaḥ iti āha katham na vai sarva loka sākṣikam sukham śakyam pratyākhyātum ayam tu janma maraṇa prabandha anubhava nimittāt duḥkhāt nirviṇṇasya duḥkham jihāsataḥ duḥkha saṃjñā bhāvanā upadeśaḥ duḥkha hāna arthaḥ iti 
[1007,i_1008,i]	kayā yuktyā sarve khalu sattva nikāyāḥ sarvāṇi utpatti sthānāni sarvaḥ punarbhavaḥ bādhana anuṣaktaḥ duḥkha sāhacaryād bādhanā lakṣaṇam duḥkham iti uktam ṛṣibhiḥ duḥkha saṃjñā bhāvanam upadiśyate atra ca hetuḥ upādīyate vividha bādhana ayogāt duḥkham eva janma utpattiḥ janma jāyate iti śarīra indriya buddhayaḥ śarīra ādīnām ca saṃsthāna viśiṣṭānām prādurbhāvaḥ utpattiḥ vividhā ca bādhanā hīnā madhyamā utkṛṣṭā ca iti utkṛṣṭā nārakiṇām tiraścām tu madhyamā manuṣyāṇām tu hīnā devānām hīnatarā vīta rāgāṇām ca evam sarvam utpatti sthānam vividha bādhana anuṣaktam paśyataḥ sukhe tad sādhaneṣu ca śarīra indriya buddhiṣu duḥkha saṃjñā vyavatiṣṭhate duḥkha saṃjñā vyavasthānāt sarva lokeṣu anabhirati saṃjñā bhavati anabhirati saṃjñām upāsīnasya sarva loka viṣayā tṛṣṇā vicchidyate tṛṣṇā prahāṇāt sarva duḥkhāt vimucyate iti yathā viṣa yogāt payaḥ viṣam iti budhyamānaḥ na upādatte anupādadānaḥ maraṇa duḥkham na āpnoti 
[1008,ii_1008,iv]	duḥkha uddeśaḥ tu na sukhasya pratyākhyānam kasmāt na sukhasya antarāla niṣpatteḥ na khalu ayam duḥkha uddeśaḥ sukhasya pratyākhyānam kasmāt sukhasya antarāla niṣpatteḥ niṣpadyate khalu bādhana antarāleṣu sukham pratyātma vedanīyam śarīriṇām tat aśakyam pratyākhyātum iti 
[1009,i_1010,iii]	artha api bādhanā nivṛtteḥ vedayataḥ paryeṣaṇa doṣāt apratiṣedhaḥ sukhasya duḥkha uddeśena iti prakaraṇāt paryeṣaṇam prārthanā viṣaya arjana tṛṣṇā paryeṣaṇasya doṣaḥ yat ayam vedayamānaḥ prārthayate tat ca asya prārthitam na sampadyate sampadya vā vipadyate nyūnam vā sampadyate bahu pratyanīkam vā sampadyate iti etasmāt paryeṣaṇa doṣāt nānāvidhaḥ mānasaḥ santāpaḥ bhavati evam vedayataḥ paryeṣaṇa doṣāt bādhanāyāḥ anivṛttiḥ bādhanā nivṛtteḥ duḥkha saṃjñā bhāvanam upadiśyate anena kāraṇena duḥkham janma na tu sukhasya abhāvāt iti atha api etat anūktam kāmam kāmayamānasya yadā kāmaḥ samṛdhyati atha enam aparaḥ kāmaḥ kṣipram eva prabādhate api ced udanemi samantāt bhūmim imām labhate sa gavāśvām na sa tena dhanena dhanaiṣī tṛpyati kid nu sukham dhana kāme iti 
[1011,i_1011,ii]	duḥkha vikalpe sukha abhimānāt ca duḥkha saṃjñā bhāvanā upadeśaḥ kriyate ayam khalu sukha saṃvedane vyavasthitaḥ sukham parama puruṣa artham manyate na sukhāt anyat niḥśreyasam asti sukhe prāpte caritārthaḥ kṛta karaṇīyaḥ bhavati mithyā saṅkalpāt sukhe tad sādhaneṣu ca viṣayeṣu saṃrajyate saṃraktaḥ sukhāya ghaṭate ghaṭamānasya asya janma jarā vyādhi prāyaṇa aniṣṭa saṃyoga iṣṭa viyoga prārthita anupapatti nimittam anekavidham yāvat duḥkham utpadyate tam duḥkha vikalpam sukham iti abhimanyate sukha aṅga bhūtam dukham na duḥkham anāsādya śakyam sukham avāptum tādarthyāt sukham eva idam iti sukha saṃjñā upahata prajñaḥ jāyasva ca iti saṃdhāvatī iti saṃsāram na ativarttate tat asyāḥ sukha saṃjñāyāḥ pratipakṣaḥ duḥkha saṃjñā bhāvanam upadiśyate duḥkha anuṣaṅgāt duḥkham janma iti na sukhasya abhāvāt 
[1011,iii]	yadi evam kasmāt duḥkham janma iti na ucyate saḥ ayam evam vācye yat evam āha duḥkham eva janma iti tena sukha abhāvam jñāpayati iti janma vinigraha arthīyaḥ vai khalu ayam eva śabdaḥ katham na duḥkham janma svarūpataḥ kim tu duḥkha upacārāt evam sukham api iti etat anena eva nirvarttyate na tu duḥkham eva janma iti 
[1013,i_1013,iii]	duḥkha uddeśa anantaram apavargaḥ sa pratyākhyāyate ṛṇa kleśa pravṛtti anubandhāt apavarga abhāvaḥ ṛṇa anubandhāt na asti apavargaḥ jāyamānaḥ ha vai brāhmaṇaḥ tribhiḥ ṛṇaiḥ ṛṇavān jāyate brahmacaryeṇa ṛṣibhyaḥ yajñena devebhyaḥ prajayā pitṛbhyaḥ iti ṛṇāni teṣām anubandhaḥ sva karmabhiḥ sambandhaḥ karma sambandha vacanāt jarā maryam vai etat satram yat agnihotram darśa pūrṇam āsau ca iti jarayā ha vai eṣa tasmāt satrāt vimucyate mṛtyunā ha vā iti ṛṇa anubandhāt apavarga anuṣṭhāna kālaḥ na asti iti apavarga abhāvaḥ 
[1014,i_1014,ii]	kleśa anubandhāt na asti apavargaḥ kleśa anubaddhaḥ eva ayam mriyate kleśa anubaddhaḥ ca jāyate na asya kleśa anubandha vicchedaḥ gṛhyate pravṛtti anubandhāt na asti apavargaḥ janma prabhṛti ayam yāvat prāyaṇam vāc buddhi śarīra ārambheṇa avimuktaḥ gṛhyate tatra yat uktam duḥkha janma pravṛtti doṣa mithyā jñānānām uttarottara apāye tad anantara abhāvāt apavargaḥ iti tat anupapannam iti 
[1014,iii_1015,i]	atra abhidhīyate yat tāvat ṛṇa anubandhāt iti ṛṇaiḥ iva ṛṇaiḥ iti pradhāna śabda anupapatteḥ guṇa śabdena anuvādaḥ nindā praśaṃsā upapatteḥ ṛṇaiḥ iti na ayam pradhāna śabdaḥ yatra khalu ekaḥ pratyādeyam dadāti dvitīyaḥ ca pratideyam gṛhṇāti tatra asya dṛṣṭa tvāt pradhānam ṛṇa śabdaḥ na ca etat iha upapadyate pradhāna śabda anupapatteḥ guṇa śabdena ayam anuvādaḥ ṛṇaiḥ iva ṛṇaiḥ iti prayukta upamam ca etat yathā agniḥ māṇavakaḥ iti anyatra dṛṣṭaḥ ca ayam ṛṇa śabdaḥ iha prayujyate yathā agni śabdaḥ māṇavake katham guṇa śabdena anuvādaḥ nindā praśaṃsā upapatteḥ karma lope ṛṇī iva ṛṇa ādānāt nindyate karma anuṣṭhāne ca ṛṇī iva ṛṇa dānāt praśasyate saḥ eva upama arthaḥ iti 
[1016,i]	jāyamānaḥ iti guṇa śabdaḥ viparyaye anadhikārāt jāyamānaḥ ha vai brāhmaṇaḥ iti ca guṇa śabdaḥ gṛhasthaḥ sampadyamānaḥ jāyamānaḥ iti yadā ayam gṛhasthaḥ jāyate tadā karmabhiḥ adhikriyate mātṛtaḥ jāyamānasya anadhikārāt yadā tu mātṛtaḥ jāyate kumāraḥ na tadā karmabhiḥ adhikriyate arthinaḥ śaktasya ca adhikārāt arthinaḥ karmabhiḥ adhikāraḥ karma vidhau kāma saṃyogaḥ mṛteḥ agnihotram juhuyāt svarga kāmaḥ iti evamādi śaktasya ca pravṛtti sambhavāt śaktasya karmabhiḥ adhikāraḥ pravṛtti sambhavāt śaktaḥ khalu vihite karmaṇi pravarttate na itaraḥ iti ubhaya abhāvaḥ tu pradhāna śabda arthe mātṛtaḥ jāyamāne kumāre ubhayam arthitā śaktiḥ ca na bhavati iti 
[1017,i]	na bhidyate ca laukikāt vākyāt vaidikam vākyam prekṣā pūrva kāri puruṣa praṇīta tvena tatra laukikaḥ tāvat aparīkṣakaḥ api na jāta mātram kumārakam evam brūyāt adhīṣva yajasva brahmacaryam cara iti kutas evam ṛṣiḥ upapannāna vadya vādī upadeśa arthena prayuktaḥ upadiśati na khalu vai narttakaḥ andheṣu pravarttate na gāyakaḥ badhireṣu iti 
[1017,ii_1017,iii]	upadiṣṭa artha vijñānam ca upadeśa viṣayaḥ yaḥ ca upadiṣṭam artham vijānāti tam prati upadeśaḥ kriyate na ca etat asti jāyamāna kumārakaḥ iti gārhasthya liṅgam ca mantra brāhmaṇam karma abhivadati yat ca mantra brāhmaṇam karma abhivadati tat patnī sambandha ādinā gārhasthya liṅgena upapannam tasmāt gṛhasthaḥ ayam jāyamānaḥ abhidhīyate iti arthi tvasya ca avipariṇāme jarā maryavāda upapattiḥ 
[1018,i]	yāvat ca asya phalena arthi tvam na vipariṇamate na nivartate tāvat anena karma anuṣṭheyam iti upapadyate jarā maryavādaḥ tam prati iti jarayā ha vā iti āyuṣaḥ turīyasya caturthasya pravrajyā yuktasya vacanam jarayā ha vai eṣaḥ etasmāt vimucyate iti āyuṣaḥ turīyam caturtham pravrajyā yuktam jarā iti ucyate tatra hi pravrajyā vidhīyate atyanta jarā saṃyoge jarayā ha vā iti anarthakam aśaktaḥ vimucyate iti etat api na upapadyate svayam aśaktasya bāhyām śaktim āha antevāsī vā juhuyāt brahmaṇā sa parikrītaḥ kṣīra hotā vā jahuyāt dhanena sa parikrītaḥ iti 
[1019,i]	atha api vihitam vānūdyeta kāmāt vā arthaḥ parikalpyeta vihita anuvacanam nyāyyam iti ṛṇavān iva asvatantraḥ gṛhasthaḥ karmasu pravarttate iti upapannam vākyasya sāmarthyam phalasya hi sādhanāni prayatna viṣayaḥ na phalam tāni sampannāni phalāya kalpante vihitam ca jāyamānam vidhīyate ca jāyamānam tena yaḥ sambaddhyate saḥ ayam jāyamānaḥ iti 
[1019,ii_1019,iii]	pratyakṣa vidhāna abhāvāt iti ced na pratiṣedhasya api pratyakṣa vidhāna abhāvāt iti pratyakṣataḥ vidhīyate gārhasthyam brāhmaṇena yadi ca āśrama antaram abhaviṣyat tat api vyadhāsyata pratyakṣataḥ pratyakṣa vidhāna abhāvāt na asti āśrama antaram iti na pratiṣedhasya api pratyakṣataḥ vidhāna abhāvāt na pratiṣedhaḥ api vai brāhmaṇena pratyakṣataḥ vidhīyate na santi āśrama antarāṇi ekaḥ eva gṛhastha āśramaḥ iti pratiṣedhasya pratyakṣataḥ aśravaṇāt ayuktam etat iti adhikārāt ca vidhānam vidyā antara vat yathā śāstra antarāṇi sve sve adhikāre pratyakṣataḥ vidhāyakāni na artha antara abhāvāt evam idam brāhmaṇam gṛhastha śāstram sve adhikāre pratyakṣataḥ vidhāyakam na āśrama antarāṇām abhāvāt iti 
[1022,i]	ṛc brāhmaṇam ca apavarga abhidhāyi abhidhīyate ṛcaḥ ca brāhmaṇāni ca apavarga abhivādīni bhavanti ṛcaḥ ca tāvat karmabhiḥ mṛtyum ṛṣayaḥ niṣeduḥ prajāvantaḥ draviṇam icchamānāḥ atha apare ṛṣayaḥ manīṣiṇaḥ param karmabhyaḥ amṛta tvam ānaśuḥ na karmaṇā na prajayā dhanena tyāgena eke amṛta tvam ānaśuḥ pareṇa nākam nihitam guhāyām vibhrājate yat yatayaḥ viśanti veda aham etam puruṣam mahāntam āditya varṇam tamasaḥ parastāt tam eva viditvā atimṛtyum eti na anyaḥ panthāḥ vidyate ayanāya 
[1022,iii_1023,i]	atha brāhmaṇāni trayaḥ dharma skandhāḥ yajñaḥ adhyayanam dānam iti prathamaḥ tapaḥ eva dvitīyaḥ brahmacārī ācārya kula vāsī iti tṛtīyaḥ atyantam ātmānam ācārya kule avasādayan sarve eva ete puṇya lokāḥ bhavanti brahma saṃsthaḥ amṛta tvam eti etam eva pravrājinaḥ lokam icchantaḥ pravrajanti iti atho khalu āhuḥ kāma mayaḥ eva ayam puruṣaḥ iti sa yathākāmaḥ bhavati tad kratuḥ bhavati yat kratuḥ bhavati tat karma kurute yat karma kurute tat abhisaṃpadyate 
[1023,ii_1023,iii]	iti karmabhiḥ saṃsaraṇam uktvā prakṛtam anyat upadiśanti iti nu kāmayamānaḥ atha akāmayamānaḥ yaḥ akāmaḥ niṣkāmaḥ ātma kāmaḥ āpta kāmaḥ bhavati na tasya prāṇāḥ utkrāmanti iha eva samavalīyante brahmā eva san brahmā api eti iti tatra yat uktam ṛṇa anubandhāt apavarga abhāvaḥ iti etat ayuktam iti ye catvāraḥ pathayaḥ deva yānāḥ iti ca cāturāśramya śruteḥ aikāśramyān upapattiḥ 
[1023,iv_1024,ii]	phala arthinaḥ ca idam brāhmaṇam jarā maryam vai etat satram yat agnihotram darśa pūrṇam āsau ca iti katham samāropaṇāt ātmani apratiṣedhaḥ prājāpatyām iṣṭam nirūpya tasyām sarva vedasam hutvā ātmani agnīn samāropya brāhmaṇaḥ pravrajet iti śrūyate tena vijānīmaḥ prajā vitta loka eṣaṇābhyaḥ vyutthitasya nivṛtte phala arthi tve samāropaṇam vidhīyate iti evam ca brāhmaṇāni saḥ anyat vratam upākariṣyamāṇaḥ yājñavalkyaḥ maitreyīm iti ha uvāca pravrajiṣyan vai are aham asmāt sthānāt asmi hanta te anayā kātyāyanyā sahāntam karavāṇi iti atha api ukta anuśāsanā asi maitreyi etāvat are khalu amṛta tvam iti ha uktvā yājñavalkyaḥ pravavrāja iti 
[1025,i_1025,ii]	pātra caya anta anupapatteḥ ca phala abhāvaḥ jarā āmarye ca karmaṇi aviśeṣeṇa kalpyamāne sarvasya pātra caya antāni karmāṇi iti prasajyate tatra eṣaṇā vyutthānam na śrūyeta etat dha sma vai tat pūrve brāhmaṇāḥ anūcānāḥ vidvāṃsaḥ prajām na kāmayante kim prajayā kariṣyāmaḥ yeṣām naḥ ayam ātmā ayam lokaḥ iti te ha sma putra eṣaṇāyāḥ ca vitta eṣaṇāyāḥ ca loka eṣaṇāyāḥ ca vyutthāya atha bhikṣā caryam caranti iti eṣaṇābhyaḥ ca vyutthitasya pātra caya antāni karmāṇi na upapadyante iti na aviśeṣeṇa karttuḥ prayojakam phalam bhavati iti 
[1026,i]	cāturāśramya vidhānāt ca itihāsa purāṇa dharma śāstreṣu aikāśramya anupapattiḥ tat apramāṇam iti ced na pramāṇena prāmāṇya abhyanujñānāt pramāṇena khalu brāhmaṇena itihāsa purāṇasya prāmāṇyam abhyanujñāyate te vā khalu ete atharva aṅgirasaḥ etat itihāsa purāṇam abhyavadan itihāsa purāṇam pañcamam vedānām vedaḥ iti tasmāt ayuktam etat aprāmāṇyam iti aprāmāṇye ca dharma śāstrasya prāṇabhṛtām vyavahāra lopāt loka uccheda prasaṅgaḥ 
[1027,i_1027,ii]	draṣṭṛ pravaktṛ sāmāṇyāt ca aprāmānya anupapattiḥ ye eva mantra brāhmaṇasya draṣṭāraḥ pravaktāraḥ ca te khalu itihāsa purāṇasya dharma śāstrasya ca iti viṣaya vyavasthānāt ca yathā viṣayam prāmāṇyam anyaḥ mantra brāhmaṇasya viṣayaḥ anyat ca itihāsa purāṇa dharma śāstrāṇām iti yajñaḥ mantra brāhmaṇasya loka vṛttam itihāsa purāṇasya loka vyavahāra vyavasthānam dharma śāstrasya viṣayaḥ tatra ekena na sarvam vyavasthāpyate iti yathā viṣayam etāni pramāṇāni indriya ādi vat iti 
[1028,i_1028,iii]	yat punar etat kleśa anubandhasya avicchedāt iti suṣuptasya svapna adarśane kleśa abhāvāt apavargaḥ yathā suṣuptasya khalu svapna adarśane rāga anubandhaḥ sukha duḥkha anubandhaḥ ca vicchidyate tathā apavarge api iti etat ca brahma vidaḥ muktasya ātmanaḥ rūpam udāharanti iti 
[1029,i_1029,iv]	yat api pravṛtti anubandhāt iti na pravṛttiḥ pratisandhānāya hīna kleśasya prakṣīṇeṣu rāga dveṣa moheṣu pravṛttiḥ na pratisandhānāya pratisandhiḥ tu pūrva janma nivṛttau punarjanma tat ca adṛṣṭa kāritam tasyām prahīṇāyām pūrva janma abhāve janma antara abhāvaḥ apratisandhānam apavargaḥ karma vaiphalya prasaṅgaḥ iti ced na karma vipāka pratisaṃvedanasya apratyākhyānāt pūrva janma nivṛttau punarjanma na bhavati iti ucyate na tu karma vipāka pratisaṃvedanam pratyākhyāyate sarvāṇi pūrva karmāṇi hi ante janmani pipacyante iti 
[1030,i_1030,ii]	na kleśa santateḥ svābhāvika tvāt na upapadyate kleśa anubandha vicchedaḥ kasmāt kleśa santateḥ svābhāvika tvāt anādiḥ iyam kleśa santatiḥ na ca anādiḥ śakyaḥ ucchetum iti 
[1030,iii_1030,v]	atra kaścid parīhāram āha prāk utpatteḥ abhāva anitya tva vat svābhāvike api anitya tvam yathā anādiḥ prāk utpatteḥ abhāvaḥ utpannena bhāvena nivartyate evam svābhāvikī kleśa santatiḥ anityā iti 
[1031,i_1031,iii]	aparaḥ āha aṇu śyāma tā antya tva vat vā yathā anādiḥ aṇu śyāma tā atha ca agni saṃyogāt anityā tathā kleśa santatiḥ api iti sataḥ khalu dharmaḥ nitya tvam anitya tvam ca tattvam bhāve abhāve bhāktam iti anādiḥ aṇuśyāma tā iti hetu abhāvāt ayuktam anutpatti dharmakam anityam iti na atra hetuḥ asti iti 
[1032,i_1032,iii]	ayam tu samādhiḥ na saṅkalpa nimitta tvāt ca rāga ādīnām karma nimitta tvāt itaretara nimitta tvāt ca iti samuccayaḥ mithyā saṅkalpebhyaḥ rañjanīya kopanīya mohanīyebhyaḥ rāga dveṣa mohāḥ utpadyante karma ca sattva nikāya nirvartakam naiyamikān rāga dveṣa mohān nirvarttayati niyama darśanāt dṛśyate hi kaścid sattva nikāyaḥ rāga bahulaḥ kaścid dveṣa bahulaḥ kaścid moha bahulaḥ iti itaretara nimittā ca rāga ādīnām utpattiḥ mūḍhaḥ rajyati mūḍhaḥ kupyati raktaḥ muhyati kupitaḥ muhyati 
[1033,i]	sarva mithyā saṅkalpānām tattva jñānāt anutpattiḥ kāraṇa anutpātau ca kārya anutpatteḥ iti rāga ādīnām atyantam anutpattiḥ iti anādiḥ ca kleśa santatiḥ iti ayuktam sarve ime khalu ādhyātmikāḥ bhāvāḥ anādinā prabandhena pravarttante śarīra ādayaḥ na jātu atra kaścid anutpanna pūrvaḥ prathamatas utpadyate anyatra tattva jñānāt na ca evam sati anutpatti dharmakam kiñcid avyaya dharmakam pratijñāyate iti karma ca sattva nikāya nirvartakam tattva jñāna kṛtāt mithyā saṅkalpa vighātāt na rāga ādi utpatti nimittam bhavati sukha duḥkha saṃvittiḥ phalam tu bhavati iti 
[1035,i]	kim nu khalu bhoḥ yāvantaḥ viṣayāḥ tāvatsu pratyekam tattva jñānam utpadyate atha kvacid utpadyate iti kaḥ ca atra viśeṣaḥ na tāvat eka ekatra yāvat viṣayam utpadyate jñeyānām ānantyāt na api kvacid utpadyate yatra na utpadyate tatra anivṛttaḥ mohaḥ iti moha śeṣa prasaṅgaḥ na ca anya viṣayeṇa tattva jñānena anya viṣayaḥ mohaḥ śakyaḥ pratiṣeddhum iti 
[1036,i_1036,ii]	mithyājñānam vai khalu mohaḥ na tattva jñānasya anutpatti mātram tat ca mithyājñānam yatra viṣaye pravartamānam saṃsāra bījam bhavati sa viṣayaḥ tattvataḥ jñeyaḥ iti kim punar tat mithyājñānam anātmani ātma grahaḥ aham asmi iti mohaḥ ahaṅkāraḥ iti anātmānam khalu aham asmi iti paśyataḥ dṛṣṭiḥ ahaṅkāraḥ iti kim punar tad artha jātam yat viṣayaḥ ahaṅkāraḥ śarīra indriya manaḥ vedanā buddhayaḥ katham tat viṣayaḥ ahaṅkāraḥ saṃsāra bījam bhavati 
[1037,i]	ayam khalu śarīra ādi artha jātam aham asmi iti vyavasitaḥ tad ucchedena ātma ucchedam manyamānaḥ anuccheda tṛṣṇā pariplutaḥ punar punar tat upādatte tat upādadānaḥ janma maraṇāya yatate tena aviyogāt na atyantam duḥkhāt vimucyate iti yaḥ tu duḥkham duḥkha āyatanam duḥkha anuṣaktam sukham ca sarvam idam duḥkham iti paśyati sa duḥkham parijānati parijñātam ca duḥkham prahīṇam bhavati anupādānāt sa viṣān na vat evam doṣān karma ca duḥkha hetuḥ iti paśyati na ca aprahīṇeṣu doṣeṣu duḥkha prabandha ucchedena śakyam bhavitum iti doṣān jahāti prahīṇeṣu ca doṣeṣu na pravṛttiḥ pratisandhānāya iti uktam 
[1037,ii_1037,iii]	pretyabhāva phala duḥkhāni ca jñeyāni vyavasthāpayati karma ca doṣān ca praheyān apavargaḥ adhigantavyaḥ tasya adhigama upāyaḥ tattva jñānam evam catasṛbhiḥ vidhābhiḥ prameyam vibhaktam āsevamānasya abhyasyataḥ bhāvayataḥ samyak darśanam yathābhūta avabodhaḥ tattva jñānam utpadyate evam ca doṣa nimittānām tattva jñānāt ahaṅkāra nivṛttiḥ 
[1038,i]	śarīra ādi duḥkha antam prameyam doṣa nimittam tad viṣaya tvāt mithyājñānasya tat idam tattva jñānam tat viṣayam utpannam ahaṅkāram nivartayati samāna viṣaye tayoḥ virodhāt evam tattva jñānāt duḥkha janma pravṛtti doṣa mithyā jñānānām uttarottara apāye tad anantara abhāvāt apavargaḥ iti sa ca ayam śāstra artha saṃgrahaḥ anūdyate na apūrvaḥ vidhīyate iti 
[1039,i_1040,i]	prasaṅkhyān ānupūrvī tu khalu doṣa nimittam rūpa ādayaḥ viṣayāḥ saṅkalpa kṛtāḥ kāma viṣayāḥ indriya arthāḥ iti rūpa ādayaḥ ucyante te mithyā saṅkalpyamānāḥ rāga dveṣa mohān pravartayanti tān pūrvam prasañcakṣīta tān ca prasañca kṣāṇasya rūpa ādi viṣayaḥ mithyā saṅkalpaḥ nivartate tad nivṛttau adhyātmam śarīra ādi prasañcakṣīta tad prasaṅkhyānāt adhyātma viṣayaḥ ahaṅkāraḥ nivartate saḥ ayam adhyātmam bahis ca vivikta cittaḥ viharan muktaḥ iti ucyate 
[1040,ii_1040,iv]	atas param kācid saṃjñā heyā kācid bhāvayitavyā iti upadiśyate nātha nirākaraṇam artha upādānam vā katham iti tad nimittam tu avayavi abhimānaḥ teṣām doṣāṇām nimittam tu avayavi abhimānaḥ sā ca khalu strī saṃjñā sa pariṣkārā puruṣasya puruṣa saṃjñā ca striyāḥ sa pariṣkārā nimitta saṃjñā anuvyañjana saṃjñā ca 
[1041,i_1041,ii]	nimitta saṃjñā rasanā śrotram danta uṣṭham cakṣuḥ nāsikam anuvyañjana saṃjñā ittham daṇḍāḥ ittham oṣṭhau iti sā iyam saṃjñā kāmam vardhayati tad anuṣaktān ca doṣān vivarjanīyān varjanam tu asyāḥ bhedena avayava saṃjñā keśa loma māṃsa śoṇita asthi snāyu śirā kapha pitta uccāra ādi saṃjñā tām aśubha saṃjñā iti ācakṣate tām asya bhāvayataḥ kāma rāgaḥ prahīyate sati eva ca dvividhe viṣaye kācid saṃjñā bhāvanīyā kācid parivarjanīya iti upadiśyate yathā viṣa sampṛkte anne anna saṃjñā upādānāya viṣa saṃjñā prahāṇāya iti 
[1043,i_1043,iii]	atha idānīm artham nirākariṣyata avayavi nirākaraṇam upapādyate vidyā avidyā dvaividhyāt saṃśayaḥ sat asatoḥ upalambhāt vidyā dvividhā sat asatoḥ anupalambhāt avidyā api dvividhā upalambhyamāne avayavini vidyāt vaividhyāt saṃśayaḥ anupalabhyamāne ca avidyāt vaividhyāt saṃśayaḥ saḥ ayam avayavī yat upalabhyate atha api na upalabhyate na kathañcana saṃśayāt mucyate iti 
[1044,i_1044,ii]	tad asaṃśayaḥ pūrva hetu prasiddha tvāt tasmin anupapannaḥ saṃśayaḥ kasmāt pūrva ukta hetūnām apratiṣedhāt asti dravya antara ārambhaḥ iti 
[1045,i_1045,ii]	vṛtti anupapatteḥ api na saṃśayaḥ vṛtti anupapatteḥ api tarhi saṃśaya anupapattiḥ na asti avayavi iti 
[1045,iii_1045,v]	tat vibhajate kṛtsna eka deśa avṛtti tvāt avayavānām avayavi abhāvaḥ ekaikaḥ avayavaḥ na tāvat kṛtsne avayavini vartate tayoḥ parimāṇa bhedāt avayava antara sambandha abhāva prasaṅgāt ca na api avayavi eka deśena na hi asya anye avayavāḥ eka deśa bhūtāḥ santi iti 
[1046,i_1046,iii]	atha avayaveṣu eva avayavī vartate teṣu ca āvṛtteḥ avayavi abhāvaḥ na tāvat pratyavayavam vartate tayoḥ parimāṇa bhedāt dravyasya ca eka dravya tva prasaṅgāt na api eka deśaiḥ sarveṣu anya avayava abhāvāt tat evam na yuktaḥ saṃśayaḥ na asti avayavi iti 
[1047,i_1047,ii]	pṛthak ca avayavebhyaḥ avṛtteḥ avayavi abhāvaḥ iti vartate na ca ayam pṛthak avayavebhyaḥ vartate agrahaṇāt nitya tva prasaṅgāt ca tasmāt na asti avayavi iti 
[1048,i_1048,ii]	na ca avayavi avayavāḥ na ca avayavānām dharmaḥ avayavī kasmāt dharma mātrasya dharmibhiḥ avayavaiḥ pūrvavat sambandha anupapatteḥ pṛthak ca avayavebhyaḥ dharmibhyaḥ dharmasya agrahaṇāt iti samānam 
[1049,i_1049,ii]	ekasmin bheda abhāvāt bheda śabda prayoga anupapatteḥ apraśnaḥ kim pratyavayavam kṛtsnaḥ avayavī vartate atha eka deśena iti na upapadyate praśnaḥ kasmāt ekasmin bheda abhāvāt bheda śabda prayoga anupapatteḥ kṛtsnam iti anekasya aśeṣa abhidhānam eka deśaḥ iti nānātve kasyacid abhidhānam tau imau kṛtsna eka deśa śabdau bheda viṣayau na ekasmin avayavini upapadyete bheda abhāvāt iti 
[1049,iii_1050,i]	anya avayava abhāvāt na eka deśena vartate iti ahetuḥ avayava antara bhāve api avṛtteḥ ahetuḥ avayava antara abhāvāt iti yadi api eka deśaḥ avayava antara bhūtaḥ syāt tathā api avayave avayava antaram vartate na avayavī iti anyaḥ avayavi iti anya avayava bhāve api avṛtteḥ avayavinaḥ na eka deśena vṛttiḥ anya avayava abhāvāt iti ahetuḥ 
[1050,ii_1053,i]	vṛttiḥ katham iti ced ekasya anekatra āśraya āśrita sambandha lakṣaṇā prāptiḥ āśraya āśrita bhāvaḥ katham iti ced yasya yatas anyatra ātma lābha anupapattiḥ saḥ āśrayaḥ na kāraṇa dravyebhyaḥ anyatra kārya dravyam ātmānam labhate viparyayaḥ tu kāraṇa dravyeṣu iti nityeṣu katham iti ced anityeṣu darśanāt siddham nityeṣu dravyeṣu katham āśraya āśrayi bhāvaḥ iti ced anityeṣu dravya guṇeṣu darśanāt āśraya āśrita bhāvasya nityeṣu siddhiḥ iti tasmāt avayavi abhimānaḥ pratiṣidhyate niḥśreyasa kāmasya na avayavī yathā rūpa ādiṣu mithyā saṅkalpaḥ na rūpa ādayaḥ iti 
[1054,i_1054,iii]	sarva agrahaṇam avayavi asiddheḥ iti pratyavasthitaḥ api etat āha keśa samūhe taimirika upalabdhi vat tad upalabdhiḥ yathā ekaikaḥ keśaḥ taimirikeṇa na upalabhyate keśa samūhaḥ tu upalabhyate tathā ekaikaḥ aṇuḥ na upalabhyate aṇu sañcayaḥ tu upalabhyate tat idam aṇu samūha viṣayam grahaṇam iti 
[1054,iv_1054,v]	sva viṣayān atikrameṇa indiḥ yasya paṭu manda bhāvāt viṣaya grahaṇasya tathā abhāvaḥ na aviṣaye pravṛttiḥ yathā viṣayam indriyāṇām paṭu manda bhāvāt viṣaya grahaṇānām paṭu manda bhāvaḥ bhavati cakṣuḥ khalu prakṛṣyamāṇam na aviṣayam gandham gṛhṇāti nikṛṣyamāṇam ca na sva viṣayāt pracyavate saḥ ayam taimirikaḥ kaścid cakṣuḥ viṣayaṃkeśam na gṛhṇāti kaścid gṛhṇāti keśa samūham 
[1055,i]	ubhayam hi ataimimirikeṇa cakṣuṣā gṛhyate paramāṇavaḥ tu atīndriyāḥ indriya aviṣaya bhūtāḥ na kenacid indriyeṇa gṛhyante samuditāḥ tu gṛhyante iti aviṣaye pravṛttiḥ indriyasya prasajyeta na jātu artha antaram aṇubhyaḥ gṛhyate iti te khalu ime paramāṇavaḥ sannihitā gṛhyamāṇā atīndriya tvam jahati viyuktāḥ ca āgṛhyamāṇāḥ indriya viṣaya tvam na labhantaḥ iti saḥ ayam dravya antara anutpattau ati mahān vyāghātaḥ iti upapadyate dravya antaram yat grahaṇasya viṣayaḥ iti 
[1055,ii_1056,i]	sañcaya mātram viṣayaḥ iti ced na sañcayasya saṃyoga bhāvāt tasya ca atīndriyasya agrahaṇāt ayuktam sañcayaḥ khalu anekasya saṃyogaḥ sa ca gṛhyamāṇa āśrayaḥ gṛhyate na ati indriya āśrayaḥ bhavati hi idam anena saṃyuktam iti tasmāt yuktam etat iti gṛhyamāṇasya ca indriyeṇa viṣayasya āvaraṇa ādi anupalabdhi kāraṇam upalabhyate tasmāt na indriya daurbalyāt anupalabdhiḥ aṇūnām yathā na indriya daurbalyāt cakṣuṣā anupalabdhiḥ gandha ādīnām iti 
[1056,ii_1056,iii]	avayava avayavi prasaṅgaḥ ca evam ā pralayāt yaḥ khalu avayavinaḥ avayaveṣu vṛtti pratiṣedhāt abhāvaḥ saḥ ayam avayavasya avayaveṣu prasajyamānaḥ sarva pralayāya vā kalpeta niravayavāt vā paramāṇutaḥ nivarteta ubhayathā ca upalabdhi viṣayasya abhāvaḥ tad abhāvāt upalabhya bhāvaḥ upalabhya āśrayaḥ ca ayam vṛtti pratiṣedhaḥ saḥ āśrayam vyāghnan ātma ghātāya kalpate iti 
[1057,i_1057,iii]	atha api na pralayaḥ anusadbhāvāt avayava vibhāgam āśritya vṛtti pratiṣedhāt abhāvaḥ prasajyamānaḥ niravayavāt paramāṇoḥ nivartate na sarva pralayāya kalpate niravayava tvam tu paramāṇoḥ vibhāgaiḥ alpatara prasaṅgasya yatas na alpīyaḥ tatra avasthānāt loṣṭasya khalu pravibhajyamāna avayavasya alpataram alpatamam uttaram uttaram bhavati sa ca ayam alpatara prasaṅgaḥ yasmāt na alpataram asti yaḥ paramaḥ alpaḥ tatra nivartate yatas ca na alpīyaḥ asti tam parama anum pracakṣmahe iti 
[1058,i_1058,ii]	param vā truṭeḥ avayava vibhāgasya anavasthānāt dravyāṇām asaṅkhyeya tvāt truṭi tva nivṛttiḥ iti 
[1059,i_1059,iii]	atha idānīm ānupalambhikaḥ sarvam na asti iti manyamānaḥ āha ākāśa vyatibhedāt tad anupapattiḥ tasya aṇoḥ niravayavasya nityasya anupapattiḥ kasmāt ākāśa vyatibhedāt antar bahis ca aṇuḥ ākāśena samāviṣṭaḥ vyatibhinnaḥ vyatibhedāt sāvayavaḥ sāvayava tvāt anityaḥ iti 
[1060,i_1060,ii]	ākāśa asarva gata tvam vā atha etat na iṣyate paramāṇoḥ antar na asti ākāśam iti asarva gata tvam prasajyate iti 
[1060,iii_1061,i]	antar bahis ca kārya dravyasya kāraṇa antara vacanāt akārye tad abhāvaḥ antar iti pihitam kāraṇa antaraiḥ kāraṇam ucyate bahis iti ca vyavadhāyakam avyavahitam kāraṇam eva ucyate tat etat kārya dravyasya sambhavati na aṇoḥ akārya tvāt akārye hi paramāṇau antar bahis iti asya abhāvaḥ yatra ca asya bhāvaḥ anukāryam tat na paramāṇuḥ yatas hi na alpataram asti sa paramāṇuḥ iti 
[1062,i_1062,ii]	śabda saṃyoga vibhavāt ca sarva gatam yatra kvacid utpannāḥ śabdāḥ vibhavanti ākāśe tad āśrayāḥ bhavanti manobhiḥ paramāṇubhiḥ tad kāryaiḥ ca saṃyogāḥ vibhavanti ākāśe na asaṃyuktam ākāśena kiñcid mūrta dravyam upalabhyate tasmāt na asarva gatam iti 
[1062,iii_1063,i]	avyūha aviṣṭambha vibhu tvāni ca ākāśa dharmāḥ saṃsarpatā pratighātinā dravyeṇa na vyuhyate yathā kāṣṭhena udakam kasmāt niravayava tvāt sarpat ca pratighāti na viṣṭambhāti na asya kriyā hetum guṇam pratibadhnāti kasmāt asparśa tvāt viparyaye hi viṣṭambhaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti sa bhavān sa avayave sparśavati dravye dṛṣṭam dharmam viparīte nāśa aṅkitum arhati 
[1063,ii_1063,iii]	aṇu avayavasya aṇutara tva prasaṅgāt anukārya pratiṣedhaḥ sāvayava tve ca aṇoḥ aṇu avayavaḥ anutaraḥ iti prasajyate kasmāt kārya kāraṇa dravyayoḥ parimāṇa bheda darśanāt tasmāt aṇu avayavasya aṇutara tvam yaḥ tu sāvayavaḥ anukāryam tat iti tasmāt anukāryam idam pratiṣidhyate iti kāraṇa vibhāgāt ca kāryasya anitya tvam na ākāśa vyatibhedāt loṣṭasya avayava vibhāgāt anitya tvam na ākāśa samāveṣāt iti 
[1064,i_1064,ii]	mūrtimatām ca saṃsthāna upapatteḥ avayava sadbhāvaḥ paricchinnānām hi sparśavatām saṃsthānam tri koṇam catur asram samam parimaṇḍalam iti upapadyate yat tat saṃsthānam saḥ avayava sanniveṣaḥ parimaṇḍalāḥ ca aṇavaḥ tasmāt sa avayavāḥ iti 
[1064,iii_1064,v]	saṃyoga upapatteḥ ca madhye san aṇuḥ pūrva aparābhyām aṇubhyām saṃyuktaḥ tayoḥ vyavadhānam kurute vyavadhānena anumīyate pūrva bhāgena pūrveṇa aṇunā saṃyujyate para bhāgena pareṇa aṇunā saṃyujyate yau tau pūrva aparau bhāgau tau asya avayavau evam sarvatas saṃyujyamānasya sarvatas bhāgāḥ avayavāḥ iti yat tāvat mūrtimatām saṃsthāna upapatteḥ avayava sadbhāvaḥ iti atra uktam kim uktam vibhāge alpatara prasaṅgasya yatas na alpīyaḥ tatra nivṛtteḥ aṇava yavasya ca aṇutara tva prasaṅgāt aṇu kārya pratiṣedhaḥ iti 
[1065,i]	yat punar etat saṃyoga upapatteḥ ca iti sparśavat tvāt vyavadhānam āśrayasya ca avyāptyā bhāga bhaktiḥ uktam ca atra sparśavān aṇuḥ sparśavatoḥ aṇvoḥ pratighātāt vyavadhāyakaḥ na sāvayava tvāt sparśavat tvāt ca vyavadhāne sati aṇu saṃyogaḥ na āśrayam vyāpnoti iti bhāga bhaktiḥ bhavati bhāgavān iva ayam iti uktam ca atra vibhāge alpatara prasaṅgasya yatas na alpīyaḥ tatra avasthānāt tad avayavasya ca aṇutara tva prasaṅgāt aṇu kārya pratiṣedhaḥ iti 
[1065,ii_1071,i]	mūrtimatām ca saṃsthāna upapatteḥ saṃyoga upapatteḥ ca paramāṇūnām sāvayava tvam iti hetvoḥ anavasthā kāri tvāt anavasthā anupapatteḥ ca apratiṣedhaḥ yāvat mūrtimat yāvat ca saṃyujyate tat sarvam sa avayavam iti anavasthā kāriṇau imau hetū sā ca anavasthā na upapadyate satyām anavasthāyām satyau hetū syātām tasmāt apratiṣedhaḥ ayam niravayavatvasya iti vibhāgasya ca vibhajyamāna hāniḥ na upapadyate tasmāt pralaya anta tā na upapadyate iti anavasthāyām ca pratyadhikaraṇam dravya avayavānām ānantyāt parimāṇa bhedānām guru tvasya ca agrahaṇam samāna parimāṇa tvam ca avayava avayavinoḥ paramaṇva vayavi bhāgāt ūrdhvam iti 
[1072,i_1073,i]	yat idam bhavān buddhīḥ āśritya buddhi viṣayāḥ santi iti manyate mithyā buddhayaḥ etāḥ yadi hi tattva buddhayaḥ syuḥ buddhyā vivecane yāthātmyam buddhi viṣayāṇām upalabhyeta buddhyā vivecanāt tu bhāvānām yāthātmya anupalabdhiḥ tantu apakarṣaṇe paṭa sadbhāva anupalabdhi vat tad anupalabdhiḥ yathā ayam tantuḥ ayam tantuḥ iti pratyekam tantuṣu vivicyamāneṣu na artha antaram kiñcid upalabhyate yat paṭa buddheḥ viṣayaḥ syāt yāthātmya anupalabdheḥ asati viṣaye paṭa buddhiḥ bhavantī mithyā buddhiḥ bhavati evam sarvatra iti 
[1073,ii_1074,i]	vyāhata tvāt ahetuḥ yadi buddhyā vivecanam bhāvānām na sarva bhāvānām yāthātmya anupalabdhiḥ atha sarva bhāvānām yāthātmya anupalabdhiḥ na buddhyā vivecanam bhāvānām buddhyā vivecanam yāthātmya anupalabdhiḥ ca iti vyāhanyate tat uktam avayava avayavi prasaṅgaḥ ca evam ā pralayāt iti 
[1074,ii_1074,iii]	tad āśraya tvāt apṛthak grahaṇam kārya dravyam kāraṇa dravya āśritam tat kāraṇebhyaḥ pṛthak na upalabhyate viparyaye pṛthak grahaṇāt yatra āśraya āśrita bhāvaḥ na asti tatra pṛthak grahaṇam iti buddhyā vivecanāt tu bhāvānām pṛthak grahaṇam atīndriyeṣu aṇuṣu yat indriyeṇa gṛhyate tat etayā buddhyā vivicyamānam anyat iti 
[1074,iv_1074,v]	pramāṇataḥ ca artha pratipatteḥ buddhyā vivecanāt bhāvānām yāthātmya upalabdhiḥ yat asti yathā ca yat na asti yathā ca tat sarvam pramāṇataḥ upalabdhyā sidhyati yā ca pramāṇataḥ upalabdhiḥ tat buddhyā vivecanam bhāvānām tena sarva śāstrāṇi sarva karmāṇi sarve ca śarīriṇām vyavahārāḥ vyāptāḥ parīkṣamāṇaḥ hi buddhyā adhyavasyati idam asti idam na asti iti tatra na sarva bhāva anupapattiḥ 
[1076,i_1076,ii]	pramāṇa anupapatti upapattibhyām evam ca sati sarvam na asti iti na upapadyate kasmāt pramāṇa anupapatti upapattibhyām yadi sarvam na asti iti pramāṇam upapadyate sarvam na asti iti etat vyāhanyate atha pramāṇam na upapadyate sarvam na asti iti asya katham siddhiḥ atha pramāṇam antareṇa siddhiḥ sarvam asti iti asya katham na siddhiḥ 
[1076,iii_1076,iv]	svapna viṣaya abhimāna vat ayam pramāṇa prameya abhimānaḥ yathā svapne na viṣayāḥ santi atha ca abhimānaḥ bhavati evam na pramāṇāni prameyāṇi ca santi atha ca pramāṇa prameya abhimānaḥ bhavati 
[1076,v]	māyā gandharvanagara mṛgatṛṣṇikā vat vā 
[1077,i_1080,i]	hetu abhāvāt asiddhiḥ svapna ante viṣaya abhimāna vat pramāṇa prameya abhimānaḥ na punar jāgarita ante viṣaya upalabdhi vat iti atra hetuḥ na asti hetu abhāvāt asiddhiḥ svapna ante ca asantaḥ viṣayāḥ upalabhyante iti atra api hetu abhāvaḥ pratibodhe anupalambhāt iti ced pratibodha viṣaya upalambhāt apratiṣedhaḥ yadi pratibodhe ṇu palambhāt svapne viṣayāḥ na santi iti tarhi ye ime pratibuddhena viṣayāḥ upalabhyante upalambhāt santi iti viparyaye hi hetu sāmarthyam upalambhāt sadbhāve sati anupalambhāt abhāvaḥ siddhyati ubhayathā tu abhāve na anupalambhasya sāmarthyam asti yathā pradīpasya abhāvāt rūpasya adarśanam iti tatra bhāvena abhāvaḥ samarthyate iti svapna anta vikalpe ca hetu vacanam svapna viṣaya abhimāna vat iti bruvatā svapna anta vikalpe hetuḥ vācyaḥ kaścid svapnaḥ bhaya upasaṃhitaḥ kaścid pramoda upasaṃhitaḥ kaścid ubhaya viparītaḥ kadācid svapnam eva na paśyati iti nimittavataḥ tu svapna viṣaya abhimānasya nimitta vikalpāt vikalpa upapattiḥ 
[1083,i_1084,i]	smṛti saṅkalpa vat ca svapna viṣaya abhimānaḥ pūrva upalabdha viṣayaḥ yathā smṛtiḥ ca saṅkalpaḥ ca pūrva upalabdha viṣayau na tasya pratyākhyānāya kalpete tathā svapne viṣaya grahaṇam pūrva upalabdha viṣayam na tasya pratyākhyānāya kalpate iti evam dṛṣṭa viṣayaḥ ca svapna antaḥ jāgarita antena yaḥ suptaḥ svapnam paśyati saḥ eva jāgrat svapna darśanāni pratisandhattaḥ idam adrākṣam iti tatra jāgrat buddhi vṛtti vaśāt svapna viṣaya abhimānaḥ mithyā iti vyavasāyaḥ sati ca pratisandhāne yā jāgrataḥ buddhi vṛttiḥ tad vaśāt ayam vyavasāyaḥ svapna viṣaya abhimānaḥ mithyā iti 
[1085,i_1085,ii]	ubhaya aviśeṣe tu sādhana ānarthakyam yasya svapna anta jāgarita antayoḥ aviśeṣaḥ tasya svapna viṣaya abhimāna vat iti sādhanam anarthakam tad āśraya pratyākhyānāt atasmin tat iti ca vyavasāyaḥ pradhāna āśrayaḥ apuruṣe sthāṇau puruṣaḥ iti vyavasāyaḥ sa pradhāna āśrayaḥ na khalu puruṣe anupalabdhe puruṣaḥ iti apuruṣe vyavasāyaḥ bhavati evam svapna viṣayasya vyavasāyaḥ hastinam adrākṣam parvatam adrākṣam iti pradhāna āśrayaḥ bhavitum arhati 
[1087,i_1087,iii]	evam ca sati mithyā upalabdhi vināśaḥ tattva jñānāt svapna viṣaya abhimāna praṇāśa vat pratibodhe sthāṇau pruṣaḥ ayam iti vyavasāyaḥ mithyā upalabdhiḥ atasmin tat iti jñānam sthāṇau sthāṇuḥ iti vyavasāyaḥ tattva jñānam tad tvad jānena ca mithyā upalabdhiḥ nivartyate na arthaḥ sthāṇu puruṣa sāmānya lakṣaṇaḥ yathā pratibodhe yā jñāna vṛttiḥ tayā svapna viṣaya abhimānaḥ nivartyate na arthaḥ viṣaya sāmānya lakṣaṇaḥ tathā māyā gandharvanagara mṛga tṛṣṇikāṇām api yā buddhayaḥ atasmin tat iti vyavasāyāḥ tatra api anena eva kalpena mithyā upalabdhi vināśaḥ tattva jñānāt na artha pratiṣedhaḥ iti 
[1087,iv_1088,i]	upādāna vat ca māyā ādiṣu mithyājñānam prajñāpanīya sarūpam ca dravyam upādāya sādhanavān aparasya mithyā adhyavasāyam karoti sā māyā nīhāra prabhṛtīnām naga rasa rūpa sanniveśe dūrāt nagara buddhiḥ utpadyate viparyaye tad abhāvāt sūrya marīciṣu bhaumena ūṣmaṇā saṃsṛṣṭeṣu spandamāneṣu udaka buddhiḥ bhavati sāmānya grahaṇāt antika sthasya viparyaye tad abhāvāt kvacid kadācid kasyacid ca bhāvān na animittam mithyājñānam dṛṣṭam ca buddhi dvaitam māyā prayoktuḥ parasya ca dūrānika sthayoḥ gandharvanagara mṛgatṛṣṇikāsu su puta pratibuddhayoḥ ca svapna viṣaye tat etat sarvasya abhāve nirupākhya tāyām nirātmaka tve na upapadyate iti 
[1088,ii_1088,iii]	buddheḥ ca evam nimitta sadbhāva upalambhāt mithyā buddheḥ ca arthavat apratiṣedhaḥ kasmāt nimitta upalambhāt sadbhāva upalambhāt ca upalabhyate hi mithyā buddhi nimittam mithyā buddhiḥ ca pratyātmam utpannā gṛhyate saṃvedya tvāt tasmāt mithyā buddhiḥ api asti iti 
[1089,i_1090,i]	tattva pradhāna bhedāt ca mithyā buddheḥ dvaividhya upapattiḥ tattvam sthāṇuḥ iti pradhānam puruṣaḥ iti tattva pradhānayoḥ alopāt bhedāt sthāṇau puruṣaḥ iti mithyā buddhiḥ utpadyate sāmānya grahaṇāt evam patākāyām balākā iti loṣṭe kapotaḥ iti na tu samāne viṣaye mithyā buddhīnām samāveśaḥ sāmānya grahaṇa vyavasthānāt yasya tu nirātmakam nirupākhyam sarvam tasya samāveśaḥ prasajyate gandha ādau ca prameye gandha ādi buddayaḥ mithyā abhimatāḥ tattva pradhānayoḥ sāmānya grahaṇasya ca abhāvāt tattva buddhayaḥ eva bhavanti tasmāt ayuktam etat pramāṇa prameya buddhayaḥ mithyā iti 
[1090,ii_1091,i]	doṣa nimittānām tattva jñānāt ahaṅkāra nivṛttiḥ iti uktam atha katham tattva jñānam utpadyate iti samādhi viśeṣa abhyāsāt sa tu pratyāhṛtasya indriyebhyaḥ manasaḥ dhārakeṇa prayatnena dhāryamāṇasya ātmanā saṃyogaḥ tattva bubhutsā viśiṣṭaḥ sati hi tasmin indriya artheṣu buddhayaḥ na utpadyante tad abhyāsa vaśāt tattva buddhiḥ utpadyate 
[1091,ii_1091,iv]	yat uktam sati hi tasmin indriya artheṣu buddhayaḥ na utpadyante iti etat na artha viśeṣa prābalyāt anicchataḥ api buddhi utpatteḥ na etat yuktam kasmāt artha viśeṣa prābalyāt abubhutsamānasya api buddhi utpattiḥ dṛṣṭā yathā stanayitnu śabda prabhṛtiṣu tatra samādhi viśeṣaḥ na upapadyate 
[1091,v_1092,i]	kṣudh ādibhiḥ pravartanāt ca kṣudh pipāsābhyām śīta uṣṇābhyām vyādhibhiḥ ca anicchataḥ api buddhayaḥ pravartante tasmāt aikāgrya anupapattiḥ iti 
[1092,ii_1093,i]	astu etat samādhim vihāya vyutthānam vyutthāna nimittam samādhi pratyanīkam ca sati tu etasmin pūrva kṛta phala anubandhāt tad utpattiḥ pūrva kṛtaḥ janma antara upacitaḥ tattva jñāna hetuḥ dharma pravivekaḥ phala anubandhaḥ yoga abhyāsa sāmarthyam niṣphale hi abhyāse na abhyāsam ādriyeran dṛṣṭam hi laukikeṣu karmasu abhyāsa sāmarthyam 
[1093,ii_1093,iv]	pratyanīka parihāra artham ca araṇya guhā pulina ādiṣu yoga abhyāsa upadeśaḥ yoga abhyāsa janitaḥ dharmaḥ janma antare api anuvartate pracaya kāṣṭha āgate tattva jñāna hetau dharme prakṛṣṭāyām samādhi bhāvanāyām tattva jñānam utpadyate iti dṛṣṭaḥ ca samādhinā artha viśeṣa prābalya abhibhavaḥ na aham etat aśrauṣam na aham etat ajñāsiṣam anyatra me manaḥ abhūt iti āha laukikaḥ iti 
[1094,i_1094,iii]	yadi artha viśeṣa prābalyāt anicchataḥ api buddhi utpattiḥ anujñāyate apavarge api evam prasaṅgaḥ muktasya api bāhya artha sāmarthyāt buddhayaḥ utpadyeran iti 
[1094,iv_1094,v]	na niṣpanna avaśyambhāvi tvāt karma vaśāt niṣpanne śarīre ceṣṭa indriya artha āśraye nimitta bhāvāt avaśyambhāvī buddhīnām utpādaḥ na ca prabalaḥ api san bāhyaḥ ṛthe ātmanaḥ buddhi utpāde samarthaḥ bhavati tasya indriyeṇa saṃyogāt buddhi utpāde sāmarthyam dṛṣṭam iti 
[1095,i_1095,ii]	tad abhāvaḥ ca apavarge tasya buddhi nimitta āśrayasya śarīra indriyasya dharma adharma abhāvāt abhāvaḥ apavarge tatra yat uktam apavarge api evam prasaṅgaḥ iti tat ayuktam tasmāt sarva duḥkha vimokṣaḥ apavargaḥ yasmāt sarva duḥkha bījam sarva duḥkha āyatanam ca apavarge vicchidyate tasmāt sarveṇa duḥkhena vimuktiḥ apavargaḥ na nirbījam nirāyatanam ca duḥkham utpadyate iti 
[1095,iii_1095,iv]	tad artham yama niyamābhyām ātma saṃskāraḥ yogāt ca adhyātma vidhi upāyaiḥ tasya apavargasya adhigamāya yama niyamābhyām ātma saṃskāraḥ yamaḥ samānam āśramiṇām dharma sādhanam niyamaḥ tu viśiṣṭam ātma saṃskāraḥ punar adharma hānam dharma upacayaḥ ca yoga śāstrāt ca adhyātma vidhiḥ pratipattavyaḥ sa punar tapaḥ prāṇāyāmaḥ pratyāhāraḥ dhyānam dhāraṇa iti indriya viṣayeṣu prasaṃkhyāna abhyāsaḥ rāga dveṣa prahāṇa arthaḥ upāyaḥ tu yoga ācāra vidhānam iti 
[1097,i_1097,ii]	jñāna grahaṇa abhyāsaḥ tad vidyaiḥ ca saha saṃvādaḥ tad artham iti prakṛtam jñāyate anena iti jñānam ātma vidyā śāstram tasya grahaṇam adhyayana dhāraṇe abhyāsaḥ satata kriyā adhyayana śravaṇa cintanāni tad vidyaiḥ ca saha saṃvādaḥ iti prajñā paripāka artham paripākaḥ tu saṃśaya chedanam avijñāta artha bodhaḥ adhyavasita abhyanujñānam iti samayāvādaḥ saṃvādaḥ 
[1097,iii_1097,v]	tad vidyaiḥ ca saha saṃvādaḥ iti avibhakta artham vacanam vibhajyate tam śiṣya guru sabrahmacāri viśiṣṭa śreyaḥ arthibhiḥ anasūyibhiḥ abhyupeyāt etat nigadena eva nīta artham iti 
[1098,i_1098,iii]	yadi ca manyeta pakṣa pratipakṣa parigrahaḥ pratikūlaḥ parasya iti pratipakṣa hīnam api vā prayojana artham arthi tve tam abhyupeyāt iti vartate paratas prajñām upāditsamānaḥ tattva bubhutsā prakāśanena sva pakṣam anavasthāpayan sva darśanam pariśodhayet iti anyonya pratyanīkāni ca prāvādukānām darśanāni 
[1099,i_1099,iii]	sva pakṣa rāgeṇa ca eke nyāyam ativartante tatra tattva adhyavasāya saṃrakṣaṇa artham jalpa vitaṇḍe bīja praroha saṃrakṣaṇa artham kaṇṭaka śākhā āvaraṇa vat anutpanna tattva jñānānām aprahīṇa doṣāṇām tad artham ghaṭamānānām etat iti 
[1099,iv_1100,i]	vidyā nirveda ādibhiḥ ca pareṇa avajñāyamānasya tābhyām vigṛhya kathanam vigṛhya iti vijigīṣayā na tattva bubhutsayā iti tat etat vidyā pāla artham na lābha pūjā khyātyartham iti 
[1101,i_1102,i]	sādharmya vaidharmyābhyām pratyavasthānasya vikalpāt jāti bahutvam iti saṅkṣepeṇa uktam tat vistareṇa vibhajyate tāḥ khalu imāḥ jātayaḥ sthāpana ahetau prayukte caturviṃśatiḥ pratiṣedha hetavaḥ s ā d h a r m y a v a i d h a r m y o t k a r ṣ ā p a k a r ṣ a v a r ṇ y ā v a r ṇ y a v i k a l p a s ā d h y aprāpti aprāpti prasaṅga pratidṛṣṭānta an utpatti saṃśaya prakaraṇā hetu artha apatti aviśeṣa upapatti upalabdhi anupalabdhi anitya nitya kārya samāḥ sādharmyeṇa pratyavasthānam aviśiṣyamāṇam sthāpanā hetutaḥ sādharmya samaḥ aviśeṣam tatra tatra udāhariṣyāmaḥ evam vaidharmya sama prabhṛtayaḥ api nirvaktavyāḥ 
[1105,i_1105,iii]	lakṣaṇam tu sādharmya vaidharmyābhyām upasaṃhāre tad dharma viparyaya upapatteḥ sādharmya vaidharmya samau sādharmyeṇa upasaṃhāre sādhya dharma viparyaya upapatteḥ sādharmyeṇa eva pratyavasthānam aviśiṣyamāṇam sthāpanā hetutaḥ sādharmya samaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ nidarśanam kriyāvān ātmā dravyasya kriyā hetu guṇa yogāt dravyam loṣṭaḥ kriyā hetu guṇa yuktaḥ kriyāvān tathā ca ātmā tasmāt kriyāvān iti evam upasaṃhṛte paraḥ sādharmyeṇa eva pratyavatiṣṭhate niṣkriyaḥ ātmā vibhunaḥ dravyasya niṣkriya tvāt vibhu ca ākāśam niṣkriyam ca tathā ca ātmā tasmāt niṣkriyaḥ iti 
[1106,i_1106,ii]	na ca asti viśeṣa hetuḥ kriyāvat sādharmyāt kriyāvatā bhavitavyam na punar akriya sādharmyāt niṣkriyeṇa iti viśeṣa hetu abhāvāt sādharmya samaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ bhavati atha vaidharmya samaḥ kriyā hetu guṇa yuktaḥ loṣṭaḥ paricchinnaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ na ca tathā ātmā tasmāt na loṣṭa vat kriyāvān iti na ca asti viśeṣa hetuḥ kriyāvat sādharmyāt kriyāvatā bhavitavyam na punar kriyāvat vaidharmyāt akriyeṇa iti viśeṣa hetu abhāvāt vaidharmya samaḥ 
[1106,iii_1107,i]	vaidharmyeṇa ca upasaṃhāraḥ niṣkriyaḥ ātmā vibhu tvāt kriyāvat dravyam avibhu dṛṣṭam yathā loṣṭaḥ na ca tathā ātmā tasmāt niṣkriyaḥ iti vaidharmyeṇa pratyavasthānam niṣkriyam dravyam ākāśam kriyā hetu guṇa rahitam dṛṣṭam na ca tathā ātmā tasmāt na niṣkriyaḥ iti na ca asti viśeṣa hetuḥ kriyāvat vaidharmyāt niṣkriyeṇa bhavitavyam na punar akriya vaidharmyāt kriyāvatā iti viśeṣa hetu abhāvāt vaidharmya samaḥ atha sādharmya samaḥ kriyāvān loṣṭaḥ kriyā hetu guṇa yuktaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tathā ca ātmā tasmāt kriyāvān iti na ca asti viśeṣa hetuḥ kriyāvat vaidharmyāt niṣkriyaḥ na punar kriyāvat sādharmyāt kriyāvān iti viśeṣa hetu abhāvāt sādharmya samaḥ 
[1107,ii_1107,iv]	anayoḥ uttaram go tvāt go siddhi vat tad siddhiḥ sādharmya mātreṇa vaidharmya mātreṇa ca sādhya sādhane pratijñāyamāne syāt avyavasthā sā tu dharma viśeṣe na upapadyate go sādharmyāt go tvāt jāti viśeṣāt gauḥ sidhyati na tu sāsnādi sambandhāt aśva ādi vaidharmyāt go tvāt eva gauḥ sidhyati na guṇa ādi bhedāt tat ca etat kṛta vyākhyānam avayava prakaraṇe pramāṇānām abhisambandhāt ca eka artha kāri tvam samānam vākyaḥ iti hetvābhāsa āśrayā khalu iyam avyavasthā iti 
[1109,i]	sādhya dṛṣṭāntayoḥ dharma vikalpāt ubhaya sādhya tvāt ca utkarṣa apakarṣa varṇyāvarṇya vikalpa sādhya samāḥ dṛṣṭānta dharmam sādhye samāsañjayate utkarṣa samaḥ yadi kriyā hetu guṇa yogāt loṣṭa vat kriyāvān ātmā loṣṭa vat eva sparśavān api prāpnoti atha na sparśavān loṣṭa vat kriyāvān api na prāpnoti viparyaye vā viśeṣaḥ vaktavyaḥ iti 
[1109,ii_1109,v]	sādhye dharma abhāvam dṛṣṭāntāt prasañjayataḥ apakarṣa samaḥ loṣṭaḥ khalu kriyāvān avibhuḥ dṛṣṭaḥ kāmam ātmā api kriyāvān avibhuḥ astu viparyaye vā viśeṣaḥ vaktavyaḥ iti khyāpanīyaḥ varṇyaḥ viparyayāt avarṇyaḥ tau etau sādhya dṛṣṭānta dharmau viparyasyataḥ varṇyāvarṇya samau bhavataḥ sādhana dharma yukte dṛṣṭānte dharma antara vikalpāt sādhya dharma vikalpam prasañjayataḥ vikalpa samaḥ kriyā hetu guṇa yuktam kiñcid guru yathā loṣṭaḥ kiṃcid laghu yathā vāyuḥ evam kriyā hetu guṇa yuktam kiñcid kriyāvat syāt yathā loṣṭaḥ kiñcid akriyam yathā ātmā viśeṣaḥ vā vācyaḥ iti hetu ādi avayava sāmarthya yogī dharmaḥ sādhyaḥ tam dṛṣṭānte prasañjayataḥ sādhya samaḥ yadi yathā loṣṭaḥ tathā ātmā prāptaḥ tarhi yathā ātmā tathā loṣṭaḥ iti sādhyaḥ ca ayam ātmā kriyāvān iti kāmam loṣṭaḥ api sādhyaḥ atha na evam na tarhi yathā loṣṭaḥ tathā ātmā 
[1113,i_1114,i]	eteṣām uttaram kiñcid sādharmyāt upasaṃhāra siddheḥ vaidharmyāt apratiṣedhaḥ alabhyaḥ siddhasya nihnavaḥ siddham ca kiñcid sādharmyāt upamānam yathā gauḥ tathā gavayaḥ iti tatra na labhyaḥ go gavayayoḥ dharma vikalpaḥ codayitum evam sādhake dharme dṛṣṭānta ādi sāmarthya yukte na labhyaḥ sādhya dṛṣṭāntayoḥ dharma vikalpāt vaidharmyāt pratiṣedhaḥ vaktum iti 
[1114,ii_1114,iii]	sādhya atideśāt ca dṛṣṭānta upapatteḥ yatra laukika parīkṣakāṇām buddhi sāmyam tena aviparītaḥ arthaḥ atidiśyate prajñāpana artham evam sādhya atideśāt dṛṣṭānte upapadyamāne sādhya tvam anupapannam iti 
[1116,i_1116,iii]	prāpya sādhyam aprāpya vā hetoḥ prāptyā viśiṣṭa tvāt aprāpti ā asādhaka tvāt ca prāpti aprāpti samau hetuḥ prāpya vā sādhyam sādhayet aprāpya vā na tāvat prāpya prāptyām aviśiṣṭa tvāt asādhakaḥ dvayoḥ vidyamānayoḥ prāptau satyām kim kasya sādhakam sādhyam vā aprāpya sādhakam na bhavati na aprāptaḥ pradīpaḥ prakāśayati iti prāptyā pratyavasthānam prāpti samaḥ aprāptyā pratyavasthānam aprāpti samaḥ 
[1117,i_1117,iii]	anayoḥ uttaram ghaṭa ādi niṣpatti darśanāt pīḍane ca abhicārāt apratiṣedhaḥ ubhayathā khalu ayuktaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ kartṛ karaṇa adhikaraṇāni prāpya mṛdam ghaṭa ādi kāryam niṣpādayanti abhicārāt ca pīḍane sati dṛṣṭam aprāpya sādhaka tvam iti 
[1118,i_1119,i]	dṛṣṭāntasya kāraṇa anapadeśāt pratyavasthānāt ca pratidṛṣṭāntena prasaṅga pratidṛṣṭānta samau sādhanasya api sādhanam vaktavyam iti prasaṅgena pratyavasthānam prasaṅga samaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ kriyā hetu guṇa yogī kriyāvān loṣṭaḥ iti hetuḥ na apadiśyate na ca hetum antereṇa siddhiḥ asti iti pratidṛṣṭāntena pratyavasthānam pratidṛṣṭānta samaḥ kriyāvān ātmā kriyā hetu guṇa yogāt loṣṭa vat iti ukte pratidṛṣṭāntaḥ upādīyate kriyā hetu guṇa yuktam ākāśam niṣkriyam dṛṣṭam iti kaḥ punar ākāśasya kriyā hetu guṇaḥ vāyunā saṃyogaḥ saṃskāra apekṣaḥ vāyu vanaspati saṃyoga vat iti 
[1120,i_1120,iii]	anayoḥ uttaram pradīpa upādāna prasaṅga vinivṛtti vat tad vinivṛttiḥ idam tāvat ayam pṛṣṭaḥ vaktum arhati atha ke pradīpam upādadate kimartham vā iti didṛkṣamāṇā dṛśya darśana artham iti atha pradīpam didṛkṣamāṇāḥ pradīpa antaram kasmāt na upādadate antareṇa api pradīpa antaram dṛśyate pradīpaḥ tatra pradīpa darśana artham pradīpa upādānam nirarthakam atha dṛṣṭāntaḥ kimartham ucyate iti aprajñātasya jñāpana artham iti atha dṛṣṭānte kāraṇa apadeśaḥ kim artham deśyate yadi prajñāpana artham prajñātaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ sa khalu laukika parīkṣakāṇām yasmin arthe buddhi sāmyam sa dṛṣṭāntaḥ iti tad prajñāpana arthaḥ kāraṇa apadeśaḥ nirarthakaḥ iti prasaṅga samasya uttaram 
[1121,i_1121,iii]	atha pratidṛṣṭānta samasya uttaram pratidṛṣṭānta hetu tve ca na ahetuḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ pratidṛṣṭāntam bruvatā na viśeṣa hetuḥ apadiśyate anena prakāreṇa pratidṛṣṭa ānataḥ sādhakaḥ na dṛṣṭāntaḥ iti evam pratidṛṣṭānta hetu tve na ahetuḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ iti upapadyate sa ca katham ahetuḥ na syāt yadi apratiṣiddhaḥ sādhakaḥ syāt iti 
[1122,i_1122,ii]	prāk utpatteḥ kāraṇa abhāvāt anutpatti samaḥ anityaḥ śabdaḥ prayatna anantarīyaka tvāt ghaṭa vat iti ukte aparaḥ āha prāk utpatteḥ anutpanne śabde prayatna ānantarīyaka tvam anitya tva kāraṇam na asti tad abhāvāt nitya tvam prāptam nityasya ca utpattiḥ na asti anutpattyā pratyavasthānam anutpatti samaḥ 
[1123,i_1123,iii]	asya uttaram tathā abhāvāt utpannasya kāraṇa upapatteḥ na kāraṇa pratiṣedhaḥ tathā abhāvāt utpannasya iti utpannaḥ khalu ayam śabdaḥ iti bhavati prāguta patteḥ śabdaḥ eva na asti utpannasya śabda bhāvāt śabdasya sataḥ prayatna anantarīyaka tvam anitya tva kāraṇam upapadyate kāraṇa upapatteḥ ayuktaḥ ayam doṣaḥ prāk utpatteḥ kāraṇa abhāvāt iti 
[1125,i_1125,ii]	sāmānya dṛṣṭāntayoḥ aindriyaka tve samāne nitya anitya sādharmyāt saṃśaya samaḥ anityaḥ śabdaḥ prayatna anantarīyaka tvāt ghaṭa vat iti ukte hetau saṃśayena pratyavatiṣṭate sati prayatna anantarīyaka tve asti eva asya nityena sāmānyena sādharmyam aindriyaka tvam asti ca ghaṭena anityena atas nitya anitya sādharmyāt anivṛttiḥ saṃśayaḥ iti 
[1126,i_1126,iii]	asya uttaram sādharmyāt saṃśaye na saṃśayaḥ vaidharmyāt ubhayathā vā saṃśaye atyanta saṃśaya prasaṅgaḥ nitya tva anabhyupagamāt ca sāmānyasya apratiṣedhaḥ viśeṣāt vaidharmyāt avadhāryamāṇe arthe puruṣaḥ iti na sthāṇu puruṣa sādharmyāt saṃśayaḥ avakāśam labhate evam vaidharmyāt viśeṣāt prayatna anantarīyaka tvāt avadhāryamāṇe śabdasya anitya tve nitya anitya sādharmyāt saṃśayaḥ avakāśam na labhate yadi vai labhate tatas sthāṇu puruṣa sādharmya anucchedāt atyantam saṃśayaḥ syāt gṛhyamāṇe ca viśeṣe nityam sādharmyam saṃśaya hetuḥ iti na abhyupagamyate na hi gṛhyamāṇe puruṣasya viśeṣe sthāṇu puruṣa sādharmyam saṃśaya hetuḥ bhavati 
[1127,i_1127,ii]	ubhaya sādharmyāt prakriyā siddheḥ prakaraṇa samaḥ ubhayena nityena ca anityena ca sādharmyāt pakṣa pratipakṣayoḥ pravṛttiḥ prakriyā anityaḥ śabdaḥ prayatna anantarīyaka tvāt ghaṭa vat iti ekaḥ pakṣam pravarttayati dvitīyaḥ ca nitya sādharmyāt pratipakṣam pravarttayati nityaḥ śabdaḥ śrāvaṇa tvāt śabda tva vat iti evam ca sati prayatna anantarīyaka tvāt iti hetuḥ anitya sādharmyeṇa ucyamānaḥ na prakaraṇam ativarttate prakaraṇa anativṛtteḥ nirṇaya anativartanam samānam ca etat nitya sādharmyeṇa ucyamāṇe hetau tat idam prakaraṇa anativṛttyā pratyavasthānam prakaraṇa samaḥ samānam ca etat vaidharmye api ubhaya vaidharmyāt prakriyā siddheḥ prakaraṇa samaḥ iti 
[1128,i_1128,iii]	asya uttaram pratipakṣāt prakaraṇa siddheḥ pratiṣedha anupapattiḥ pratipakṣa upapatteḥ ubhaya sādharmyāt prakriyā siddhim bruvatā pratipakṣāt prakriyā siddhiḥ uktā bhavati yadi ubhaya sādharmyam tatra ekataraḥ pratipakṣaḥ iti evam sati upapannaḥ pratipakṣaḥ bhavati pratipakṣa upapatteḥ anupapannaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ yadi pratipakṣa upapattiḥ pratiṣedhaḥ na upapadyate atha pratiṣedha upapattiḥ pratipakṣaḥ na upapadyate pratipakṣa upapattiḥ pratiṣedha upapattiḥ ca iti vipratiṣiddham iti tattva anavadhāraṇāt ca prakriyā siddhiḥ viparyaye prakaraṇa avasānāt tattva avadhāraṇe hi avasitam prakaraṇam bhavati iti 
[1129,i_1129,ii]	traikālya asiddheḥ hetoḥ ahetu samaḥ hetuḥ sādhanam tat sādhyāt pūrvam paścāt saha vā bhavet yadi pūrvam sādhanam asati sādhye kasya sādhanam atha paścāt asati sādhane kasya idam sādhyam atha yugapad sādhya sādane dvayoḥ vidyamānayoḥ kim kasya sādhanam kim kasya sādhyam iti hetuḥ ahetunā na viśiṣyate ahetunā sādharmyāt pratyavasthānam ahetu samaḥ 
[1130,i_1130,iii]	asya uttaram na hetutaḥ sādhya siddheḥ traikālya asiddhiḥ na traikālya asiddhiḥ kasmāt hetutaḥ sādhya siddheḥ nirvartanīyasya nirvṛttiḥ vijñeyasya vijñānam ubhayam kāraṇataḥ dṛśyate saḥ ayam mahān pratyakṣa viṣayaḥ udāharaṇam iti yat tu khalu uktam asati sādhye kasya sādhanam iti yat tu nirvatyate yat ca vijñāpyate tasya iti 
[1130,iv_1130,v]	pratiṣeda anupapatteḥ ca pratiṣeddhavya apratiṣedhaḥ pūrvam paścāt yugapad vā pratiṣedhaḥ iti na upapadyate pratiṣedha anupapatteḥ sthāpanā hetuḥ siddhaḥ iti 
[1131,i_1131,ii]	arthāpattitaḥ pratipakṣa siddheḥ arthāpatti samaḥ anityaḥ śabdaḥ prayatna anantarīyaka tvāt ghaṭa vat iti sthāpite pakṣe arthāpattyā pratipakṣam sādhayataḥ arthāpatti samaḥ yadi prayatna anantarīyaka tvāt anitya sādharmyāt anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti arthāt āpadyate nitya sādharmyāt nityaḥ iti asti ca asya nityena sādharmyam asparśa tvam iti 
[1132,i_1133,i]	asya uttaram anuktasya arthāpatteḥ pakṣa hāneḥ upapattiḥ anukta tvāt anaika ānatika tvāt ca arthāpatteḥ anupapādya sāmarthyam anuktam arthāt āpadyate iti bruvataḥ pakṣa hāneḥ upapattiḥ anukta tvāt anitya pakṣa siddhau arthāt āpannam nitya pakṣasya hāniḥ iti anaika ānatika tvāt ca arthāpatteḥ ubhaya pakṣa samā ca iyam arthāpattiḥ yadi nitya sādharmyāt asparśa tvāt ākāśa vat ca nityaḥ śabdaḥ arthāt āpannam anitya sādharmyāt prayatna anantarīyaka tvāt anityaḥ iti na ca iyam viparyaya mātrāt ekāntena arthāpattiḥ na khalu vai ghaṇasya grāvṇaḥ patanam iti arthāt āpadyate dravāṇām apām patana abhāvaḥ iti 
[1133,ii_1133,iii]	eka dharma upapatteḥ aviśeṣe sarva aviśeṣa prasaṅgāt sadbhāva aupapatteḥ aviśeṣa samaḥ ekaḥ dharmaḥ prayatna ānantarīyaka tvam śabda ghaṭayoḥ upapadyate iti aviśeṣe ubhayoḥ anitya tve sarvasya aviśeṣaḥ prasajyate katham sadbhāva upapatteḥ ekaḥ dharmaḥ sadbhāvaḥ sarvasya upapadyate sadbhāva upapatteḥ sarva aviśeṣa prasaṅgāt pratyavasthānam aviśeṣa samaḥ 
[1133,iv_1133,vii]	asya uttaram kvacid tad dharma upapatteḥ kvacid ca anupapatteḥ pratiṣedha abhāvaḥ yathā sādhya dṛṣṭāntayoḥ eka dharmasya prayatna anantarīyaka tvasya upapatteḥ anitya tvam dharma antaram aviśeṣaḥ na evam sarva bhāvānām sadbhāva upapatti nimittam dharma antaram asti yena aviśeṣaḥ syāt atha matam anitya tvam eva dharma ānataram sadbhāva upapatti nimittam bhāvānām sarvatra syāt iti evam khalu vai kalpyamāne anityāḥ sarve bhāvāḥ sadbhāva upapatteḥ iti pakṣaḥ prāpnoti tatra pratijñā artha vyatiriktam anyat udāharaṇam na asti anudāharaṇaḥ ca hetuḥ na asti iti pratijña eka deśasya ca udāharaṇa tvam anupapannam na hi sādhyam udāharaṇam bhavati sataḥ ca nitya anityabhāvāt anitya tva anupapattiḥ tasmāt sadbhāva upapatteḥ sarva aviśeṣa prasaṅgaḥ iti nirabhidheyam etat vākyam iti sarva bhāvānām sadbhāva upapatteḥ anitya tvam iti bruvatā anujñātam śabdasya anitya tvam tatra anupapannaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ iti 
[1136,i_1136,ii]	ubhaya kāraṇa upapatteḥ upapatti samaḥ yadi anitya tva kāraṇam upapadyate śabdasya iti anityaḥ śabdaḥ nitya tva kāraṇam api upapadyate asya asparśa tvam iti nitya tvam api upapadyate ubhayasya anitya tvasya nitya tvasya ca kāraṇa upapattyā pratyavasthānam upapatti samaḥ 
[1136,iii_1137,i]	asya uttaram upapatti kāraṇa abhyanujñānāt apratiṣedhaḥ ubhaya kāraṇa upapatteḥ iti bruvatā na anitya tva kāraṇa upapatteḥ anitya tvam pratiṣidhyate yadi pratiṣidhyate na ubhaya kāraṇa upapattiḥ syāt ubhaya kāraṇa upapatti vacanāt anitya tva kāraṇa upapattiḥ abhyanujñāyate abhyanujñānāt anupapannaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ vyāghātāt pratiṣedhaḥ iti ced samānaḥ vyāghātaḥ ekasya nitya tva anitya tva prasaṅgam vyāhatam bruvata uktam pratiṣedhaḥ iti ced sva pakṣa para pakṣayoḥ samānaḥ vyāghātaḥ sa ca na ekatarasya sādhakaḥ iti 
[1137,ii_1138,i]	nirdiṣṭa kāraṇa abhāve api upalambhāt upalabdhi samaḥ nirdiṣṭasya prayatna ānantarīyaka tvasya anitya tva kāraṇasya abhāve api vāyunodanāt vṛkṣa śākhā bhaṅga jasya śabdasya anitya tvam upalabhyate nirdiṣṭasya sādhanasya abhāve api sādhya dharma upalabdhyā pratyavasthānam upalabdhi samaḥ
