[1139,i_1139,iii]	asya uttaram kāraṇa antarāt api tad dharma upapatteḥ apratiṣedhaḥ prayatna anantarīyaka tvāt iti bruvatā kāraṇatas utpattiḥ abhidhīyate na kāryasya kāraṇa niyamaḥ yadi ca kāraṇa antarāt api utpadyamānasya śabdasya tat anitya tvam upapadyate kim atra pratiṣidhyate iti 
[1140,i_1140,ii]	na prāk uccāraṇāt vidyamānasya śabdasya anupalabdhiḥ kasmāt āvaraṇa ādi anupalabdheḥ yathā vidyamānasya udaka ādeḥ arthasya āvaraṇa ādeḥ anupalabdhiḥ na evam śabdasya agrahaṇa kāraṇena āvaraṇa ādinā anupalabdhiḥ gṛhyeta ca etat asya agrahaṇa kāraṇam udaka ādi vat na gṛhyate tasmāt udaka ādi viparītaḥ śabdaḥ anupalabhyamānaḥ iti tad anupalabdheḥ anupalambhāt abhāva siddhau tad viparīta upapatteḥ anupalabdhi samaḥ 
[1140,iii]	teṣām āvaraṇa ādīnām anupalabdhiḥ na upalabhyate anupalambhāt na asti iti abhāvaḥ asyāḥ sidhyati abhāva siddhau hetu abhāvāt tad viparītam astitvam āvaraṇa ādīnām avadhāryate tad viparīta upapatteḥ yat pratijñātam na prāk uccāraṇāt vidyamānasya śabdasya anupalabdhiḥ iti etat na sidhyati saḥ ayam hetuḥ āvaraṇa ādi anupalabdheḥ iti āvaraṇa ādiṣu ca āvaraṇa ādi anupalabdhau ca samaya anupalabdhyā pratyavasthitaḥ anupalabdhi samaḥ bhavati 
[1141,i_1141,iii]	asya uttaram anupalambha ātmaka tvāt anupalabdheḥ ahetuḥ āvaraṇa ādi anupalabdhiḥ na asti anupalambhāt iti ahetuḥ kasmāt anupalambha ātmaka tvāt anupalabdheḥ upalambha abhāva mātra tvāt anupalabdheḥ yat asti tat upalabdheḥ viṣayaḥ upalabdhyā tat asti iti pratijñāyate yat na asti tat anupalabdheḥ viṣayaḥ anupalabhyamānam na asti iti pratijñāyate saḥ ayam āvaraṇa ādi anupalabheḥ anupalambhaḥ upalabdhi abhāve anupalabdhau sva viṣaye pravarttamānaḥ na sva viṣayam pratiṣedhati 
[1142,i]	apratiṣiddhā ca āvaraṇa ādi anupalabdhiḥ hetu tvāya kalpate āvaraṇa ādīni tu vidyamāna tvāt upalabdheḥ viṣayāḥ teṣām upalabdhyā bhavitavyam yat tāni na upalabhyante tat upalabdheḥ sva viṣaya pratipādikāyāḥ abhāvāt anupalambhāt anupalabdheḥ viṣayaḥ gamyate na santi āvaraṇa ādīni śabdasya agrahaṇa kāraṇāni iti anupalambhāt tu anupalabhiḥ sidhyati viṣayaḥ sa tasya iti 
[1143,i_1143,ii]	jñāna vikalpānām ca bhāva abhāva saṃvedanāt adhyātmam ahetuḥ iti varttate śarīre śarīre jñāna vikalpānām bhāva abhāvau saṃvedanīyau asti me saṃśaya jñānam na asti me saṃśaya jñānam iti evam pratyakṣa anumāna āgama smṛti jñāneṣu sā iyam āvaraṇa ādi anupalabdhiḥ upalabdhi abhāvaḥ sva saṃvedyaḥ na asti me śabdasya āvaraṇa ādi upalabdhiḥ iti na upalabhyante śabdasya agrahaṇa kāraṇāni āvaraṇa ādīni iti tatra yat uktam tat anupalabdheḥ anupalambhāt abhāva siddhiḥ iti etat na upapadyate 
[1144,i_1144,ii]	sādharmyāt tulya dharma upapatteḥ sarva anitya tva prasaṅgāt anitya samaḥ anityena ghaṭena sādharmyāt anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti bruvataḥ asti ghaṭena anityena sarva bhāvānām sādharmyam iti sarvasya anitya tvam aniṣṭam sampadyate saḥ ayam anitya tvena pratyavasthānāt anitya samaḥ iti 
[1145,i_1145,iii]	asya uttaram sādharmyāt asiddheḥ pratiṣedha asiddhiḥ pratiṣedhya sādharmyāt pratijña ādi avayava yuktam vākyam pakṣa nivartakam pratipakṣa lakṣaṇam pratiṣedhaḥ tasya pakṣeṇa pratiṣedhyena sādharmyam pratijña ādi yogaḥ tat yadi anitya sādharmyāt anitya tvasya asiddhiḥ sādharmyāt asiddheḥ pratiṣedhasya api asiddhiḥ pratiṣedhyena sādharmyāt iti 
[1145,iv_1145,v]	dṛṣṭānte ca sādhya sādhana bhāvena prajñātasya dharmasya hetu tvāt tasya ca ubhayatha abhāvāt na aviśeṣaḥ dṛṣṭānte yaḥ khalu dharmaḥ sādhya sādhana bhāvena prajñāyate sa hetu tvena abhidhīyate sa ca ubhayathā bhavati kenacid samānaḥ kutaścid viśiṣṭaḥ sāmānyāt sādharmyam viśeṣāt ca vaidharmyam evam sādharmya viśeṣaḥ hetuḥ na aviśeṣeṇa sādharmya mātram vaidharmya mātram vā sādharmya mātram vaidharmya mātram ca āśritya bhavān āha sādharmyāt tulya dharma upapatteḥ sarva anitya tva prasaṅgāt anityasam iti etat ayuktam iti aviśeṣa sama pratiṣedhe ca yat uktam tat api veditavyam 
[1147,i_1147,ii]	nityam anitya bhāvāt anitye nitya tva upapatteḥ nitya samaḥ anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti pratijñāyate tat anitya tvam kim śabde nityam atha anityam yadi tāvat sarvadā bhavati dharmasya sadā bhāvāt dharmiṇaḥ api sadā bhāvaḥ iti nityaḥ śabdaḥ iti atha na sarvadā bhavati anitya tvasya abhāvāt nityaḥ śabdaḥ evam nitya tvena pratyavasthānāt nitya samaḥ 
[1148,i_1148,iii]	asya uttaram pratiṣedhye nityam anitya bhāvāt anitye anitya tva upapatteḥ pratiṣedha abhāvaḥ pratiṣedhye śabde nityam anitya tvasya bhāvāt iti ucyamāne anujñātam śabdasya anitya tvam anitya tva upapatteḥ ca na anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti pratiṣedhaḥ na upapadyate atha na abhyupagamyate nityam anitya tvasya bhāvāt iti hetuḥ na bhavati iti hetu abhāvāt pratiṣedha anupapattiḥ iti 
[1149,i_1150,i]	utapannasya nirodhāt abhāvaḥ śabdasya anitya tvam tatra paripraśna anupapattiḥ yaḥ ayam paripraśnaḥ tat anitya tvam kim śabde sarvadā bhavati atha na iti ayam anupapannaḥ kasmāt utpannasya yaḥ nirodhāt abhāvaḥ śabdasya tat anitya tvam evam ca sati adhikaraṇa ādheya vibhāgaḥ vyāghātāt na asti iti nitya anitya tva virodhāt ca nitya tvam anitya tvam ca ekasya dharmiṇaḥ dharmau iti virudhyete na sambhavataḥ tatra yat uktam nityam anitya tvasya bhāvān nityaḥ eva tat avartamāna artham uktam iti 
[1150,ii_1151,i]	prayatna kārya aneka tvāt kārya samaḥ prayatna anantarīyaka tvāt anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti yasya prayatna anantaram ātma lābhaḥ tat khalu abhūtvā bhavati yathā ghaṭa ādi kāryam anityam iti ca bhūtvā na bhavati iti etat vijñāyate evam avasthite prayatna kārya anekatvāt iti pratiṣedhaḥ ucyate prayatna anantaram ātma lābhaḥ ca dṛṣṭaḥ ghaṭa ādīnām vyavadhāna apohāt ca abhivyaktiḥ vyavahitānām tat kim prayatna anantaram ātma lābhaḥ śabdasya aho abhivyaktiḥ iti viśeṣaḥ na asti kāryā viśeṣeṇa pratyavasthānam kārya samaḥ 
[1152,i_1152,iii]	asya uttaram kārya anya tve prayatna ahetu tvam anupalabdhi kāraṇa upapatteḥ sati kārya anya tve anupalabdhi kāraṇa upapatteḥ prayatnasya ahetu tvam śabdasya abhivyaktau yatra prayatna anantaram abhivyaktiḥ tatra anupalabdhi kāraṇam vyavadhānam upapadyate vyavadhāna apohāt ca prayatna anantara bhāvinaḥ arthasya upalabdhi lakṣaṇā abhivyaktiḥ bhavati iti na tu śabdasya anupalabdhi kāraṇam kiñcid upapadyate yasya prayatna anantaram apohāt śabdasya upalabhilakṣaṇā abhivyaktiḥ bhavati iti tasmāt utpadyate śabdaḥ na abhivyajyate iti 
[1154,i_1154,iii]	hetoḥ ced anaikāntika tvam upapadyate anaikātika tvāt asādhakaḥ syāt iti yadi ca anaikāntika tvāt asādhaka tvam pratiṣedhe api samānaḥ doṣaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ api anaikāntikaḥ kiñcid pratiṣedhati kiñcid na iti anaikāntika tvāt asādhakaḥ iti atha vā śabdasya anitya tva pakṣe prayatna anantaram utpādaḥ na abhi vyaktiḥ iti viśeṣa hetu abhāvaḥ nitya tva pakṣe api prayatna anantaram abhivyaktiḥ na utpādaḥ iti viśeṣa hetu abhāvaḥ saḥ ayam ubhaya pakṣa samaḥ viśeṣa hetu abhāvaḥ iti ubhayam api anaikātikam iti 
[1155,i_1155,ii]	sarvatra evam sarveṣu sādharmya prabhṛtiṣu pratiṣedha hetuṣu yatra yatra aviśeṣaḥ dṛśyate tatra ubhayoḥ pakṣayoḥ samaḥ prasajyate iti 
[1155,iii_1156,i]	pratiṣedha vipratiṣedhe pratiṣedha doṣa vat doṣaḥ yaḥ ayam pratiṣedhe api samānaḥ doṣaḥ anaikāntika tvam āpadyate saḥ ayam pratiṣedhasya vipratiṣedhe api samānaḥ tatra anityaḥ śabdaḥ prayatna anantarīyaka tvāt iti sādhana vādinaḥ sthāpanā prathamaḥ pakṣaḥ prayatna kārya aneka tvāt kārya samaḥ iti dūṣaṇa vādinaḥ pratiṣedha hetunā dvitīyaḥ pakṣaḥ sa ca pratiṣedhaḥ iti ucyate tasya asya pratiṣedhe api samānaḥ doṣaḥ iti tṛtīyaḥ pakṣaḥ vipratiṣedhaḥ ucyate tasmin pratiṣedha vipratiṣedhe api samānaḥ doṣaḥ anaikāntika tvam caturthaḥ pakṣaḥ 
[1156,ii_1156,iii]	pratiṣedham sa doṣam abhyupetya pratiṣedha vipratiṣedhe samānaḥ doṣa prasaṅgaḥ mata anujñā pratiṣedham dvitīyam pakṣam sa doṣam abhyupetya tad uddhāram akṛtvā anujñāya pratiṣedha vipratiṣedhe tṛtīya pakṣe samānam anaikāntika tvam iti samānam dūṣaṇam prasañjayataḥ dūṣaṇa vādinaḥ mata anujñā prasajyate iti pañcamaḥ pakṣaḥ 
[1157,i_1158,i]	sva pakṣa lakṣaṇa apekṣā upapatti upasaṃhāre hetu nirdeśe para pakṣa doṣa abhyupagamāt samānaḥ doṣaḥ sthāpanā pakṣe prayatna kārya anekatvāt iti doṣaḥ sthāpanā hetu vādinaḥ sva pakṣa lakṣaṇaḥ bhavati kasmāt sva pakṣa samuttha tvāt saḥ ayam sva pakṣa lakṣaṇam doṣam apekṣamāṇaḥ anuddhṛtya anujñāya pratiṣedhe api samānaḥ doṣaḥ iti upapadyamānam doṣam para pakṣe upasaṃharati ittham ca anaikāntikaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ iti hetum nirdiśati tatra sva pakṣa lakṣaṇa apekṣayā upapadyamāna doṣa upasaṃhāre hetu nirdeśe ca sati anena para pakṣa doṣaḥ abhyupagataḥ bhavati katham kṛtvā yaḥ pareṇa prayatna kārya anekatvāt ityādinā anaikāntika doṣaḥ uktaḥ tam anuddhṛtya pratiṣedhe api samānaḥ doṣaḥ iti āha evam sthāpanām sa doṣām abhyupetya pratiṣedhe api samānam doṣam prasañjayataḥ para pakṣa abhyupagamāt samānaḥ doṣaḥ bhavati yathā parasya pratiṣedham sa doṣam abhyupetya pratiṣedha vipratiṣedhe api samānaḥ doṣa prasaṅgaḥ mata anujñā prasajyate iti tathā asya api sthāpanām sa doṣām abhyupetya pratiṣedhe api samānam doṣam prasañjayataḥ mata anujñā prasajyate iti sa khalu ayam ṣaṣṭhaḥ pakṣaḥ 
[1158,ii]	tatra khalu sthāpanā hetu vādinaḥ prathama tṛtīya pañcama pakṣāḥ pratiṣedha hetu vādinaḥ dvitīya caturtha ṣaṣṭha pakṣāḥ teṣām sādhu asādhu tāyām mīmāṃsyamānāyām caturtha ṣaṣṭhayoḥ artha aviśeṣāt punar ukta doṣa prasaṅgaḥ caturtha pakṣe samāna doṣa tvam parasya ucyate pratiṣedha vipratiṣedhe pratiṣedha doṣa vat doṣaḥ iti ṣaṣṭhe api para pakṣa doṣa abhyupagamāt samānaḥ doṣaḥ iti samāna doṣa tvam eva ucyate na artha viśeṣaḥ kaścid asti samānaḥ tṛtīya pañcamayoḥ punar ukta doṣa prasaṅgaḥ tṛtīya pakṣe api pratiṣedhe api samānaḥ doṣaḥ iti samāna tvam abhyupagamyate pañcama pakṣe api pratiṣedha vipratiṣedhe samānaḥ doṣa prasaṅgaḥ abhyupagamyate na artha viśeṣaḥ kaścid ucyate iti tatra pañcama ṣaṣṭha pakṣayoḥ artha aviśeṣāt punar ukta doṣa prasaṅgaḥ tṛtīya caturthayoḥ mata anujñā prathama dvitīyayoḥ viśeṣa hetu abhāvaḥ iti ṣaṣ pakṣyām ubhayoḥ asiddhiḥ 
[1158,iii]	kadā ṣaṣ pakṣī yadā pratiṣedhe api samānaḥ doṣaḥ iti evam pravarttate tad ā ubhayoḥ pakṣayoḥ asiddhiḥ yadā tu kārya anya tve prayatna ahetu tvam anupalabdhi kāraṇa upapatteḥ iti anena tṛtīya pakṣaḥ yujyate tadā viśeṣa hetu vacanāt prayatna anantaram ātma lābhaḥ śabdasya na abhi vyaktiḥ iti siddhaḥ prathama pakṣaḥ na ṣaṭpakṣī pravartate iti 
[1160,i_1163,i]	vipratipatti apratipattyoḥ vikalpāt nigraha sthāna bahu tvam iti saṅkṣepeṇa uktam tat idānīm vibhajanīyam nigraha sthānāni khalu parājaya vastūni aparādha adhikaraṇāni prāyeṇa pratijña ādi avayava āśrayāṇi tattva vādinam atattva vādinam ca abhisaṃplavante teṣām vibhāgaḥ pratijñāhāniḥ pratijñāntaram pratijñā virodhaḥ pratijñāsannyāsaḥ hetu antaram artha antaram nirarthakam avijñāta artham apārthakam aprāpta kālam nyūnam adhikam punaruktam ananubhāṣaṇam ajñānam apratibhā vikṣepaḥ mata anujñā paryanuyojya upekṣaṇam niranuyojya anuyogaḥ apasiddhāntaḥ hetvābhāsāḥ ca nigraha sthānāni tāni imāni dvāviṃśatidhā vibhajya lakṣyante 
[1163,ii_1165,i]	pratidṛṣṭānta dharma abhyanujñā sva dṛṣṭānte pratijñāhāniḥ sādhya dharma pratyanīkena dharmeṇa pratyavasthite pratidraṣṭānta dharmam sva dṛṣṭānte abhyanujānan pratijñām jahāti iti pratijñā hāniḥ nidarśanam aindriyaka tvāt anityaḥ śabdaḥ ghaṭa vat iti kṛte aparaḥ āha dṛṣṭam aindriyaka tvam sāmānye nitye kasmāt na tathā śabdaḥ iti pratyavasthite idam āha yadi aindriyakam sāmānyam nityam kāmam ghaṭaḥ nityaḥ astu iti sa khalu ayam sādhakasya dṛṣṭāntasya nitya tvam prasañjayan nigamana antam eva pakṣam jahāti pakṣam jahat pratijñām jahāti iti ucyate pratijña āśraya tvāt pakṣasya iti 
[1167,i_1168,i]	pratijñāta artha pratiṣedhe dharma vikalpāt tad artha nirdeśaḥ pratijñāntaram pratijñāta arthaḥ anityaḥ śabdaḥ aindriyaka tvāt ghaṭa vat iti ukte yaḥ asya pratiṣedhaḥ pratidṛṣṭāntena hetu vyabhicāraḥ sāmānyam aindriyakam nityam iti tasmin ca pratijñāta artha pratiṣedhe dharma vikalpāt iti dṛṣṭānta pratidṛṣṭa antayoḥ sādharmya yoge dharma bhedāt sāmānyam aindriyakam sarva gatam aindriyakaḥ tu asarva gataḥ ghaṭaḥ iti dharma vikalpāt tad artha nirdeśaḥ iti sādhya siddhi artham katham yathā ghaṭaḥ asarva gataḥ evam śabdaḥ api asarva gataḥ ghaṭa vat eva anityaḥ iti tatra anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti pūrvā pratijñā asarva gataḥ iti dvitīyā pratijñā pratijñāntaram tat katham nigraha sthām iti na pratijñāyāḥ sādhanam pratijñāntaram kim tu hetu dṛṣṭāntau sādhanam pratijñāyāḥ tat etat asādhana upādānam anarthakam iti ānarthakyāt nigraha sthānam iti 
[1169,i_1171,i]	pratijñā hetvoḥ virodhaḥ pratijñā virodhaḥ guṇa vyatiriktam dravyam iti pratijñā rūpa āditaḥ artha antarasya anupalabdheḥ iti hetuḥ saḥ ayam pratijñā hetvoḥ virodhaḥ katham yadi guṇa vyatiriktam dravyam rūpa ādibhyaḥ artha antarasya anupalabdhiḥ na upapadyate atha rūpa ādibhyaḥ artha antarasya anupalabdhiḥ guṇa vyatiriktam dravyam iti na upapadyate guṇa vyatiriktam ca dravyam rūpa ādibhyaḥ ca artha antarasya anupalabdhiḥ iti virudhyate vyāhanyate na sambhavati iti 
[1172,i_1172,ii]	pakṣa pratiṣedhe pratijñāta artha apanayanam pratijñāsannyāsaḥ anityaḥ śabdaḥ aindriyaka tvāt iti ukte paraḥ brūyāt sāmānyam aindriyakam na ca anityam evam śabdaḥ api aindriyakaḥ na ca anitya iti evam pratiṣiddhe pakṣe yadi brūyāt kaḥ punar āha anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti saḥ ayam pratijñāta artha nihnavaḥ pratijñāsannyāsaḥ iti 
[1172,iii_1172,iv]	aviśeṣa ukte hetau pratiṣiddhe viśeṣam icchataḥ hetu antaram nidarśanam eka prakṛti idam vyaktam iti pratijñā kasmāt dhetoḥ eka prakṛtīnām vikārāṇām parimāṇāt mṛd pūrvakāṇām śarāva ādīnām dṛṣṭam parimāṇam yāvān prakṛteḥ vyūhaḥ bhavati tāvān vikāraḥ iti dṛṣṭam ca prativikāram parimāṇam asti ca idam parimāṇam prativyaktam tad eka prakṛtīnām vikārāṇām parimāṇāt paśyāmaḥ vyaktam idam eka prakṛti iti 
[1174,i]	asya vyabhicāreṇa pratyavasthānam nānā prakṛtīnām eka prakṛtīnām ca vikārāṇām dṛṣṭam parimāṇam iti evam pratyavasthite āha eka prakṛti samanvaye sati śarāva ādi vikārāṇām parimāṇa darśanāt sukha duḥkha moha samanvitam hi idam vyaktam parimitam gṛhyate tatra prakṛti antara rūpa samanvaya abhāve sati eka prakṛti tvam iti tat idam aviśeṣa ukte hetau pratiṣiddhe viśeṣam bruvataḥ hetu antaram bhavati sati ca hetu antara bhāve pūrvasya hetoḥ asādhaka tvāt nigraha sthānam hetu antara vacane sati yadi hetu artha nidarśanaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ upādīyate na idam vyaktam eka prakṛti bhavati prakṛti antara upādānāt atha na upādīyate dṛṣṭānte hetu arthasya anidarśitasya sādhaka bhāva anupapatteḥ ānarthakyāt dhetoḥ anivṛttam nigraha sthānam iti 
[1176,i_1177,i]	prakṛtāt arthāt apratisambaddha artham artha antaram yathā ukta lakṣaṇe pakṣa pratipakṣa parigrahe hetutaḥ sādhya siddhau prakṛtāyām brūyāt nityaḥ śabdaḥ asparśa tvāt iti hetuḥ hetuḥ nāma hinoteḥ dhātoḥ tuni pratyaye kṛdantam padam padam ca nāma ākhyāta upasarga nipātāḥ abhidheyasya kriyā antara yogāt viśiṣyamāṇa rūpaḥ śabdaḥ nāma kriyā kāraka samudāyaḥ kāraka saṅkhyā viśiṣṭa kriyā kāla yoga abhidhāya ākhyātam dhātu artha mātram ca kāla abhidhāna viśiṣṭam prayogeṣu arthāt abhidyamānā rūpāḥ nipātāḥ upasṛjyamānāḥ kriyā avat yotakāḥ upasargāḥ iti evamādi tad artha antaram veditavyam iti 
[1177,ii_1177,iii]	varṇa krama nirdeśa vat nirarthakam yathā anityaḥ śabdaḥ kacaṭa tapāḥ java gaḍa daśa tvāt jhabhan ghaḍha dhaṣa vat iti evamprakāram nirarthakam abhidhāna abhidheya bhāva anupapattau artha gateḥ abhāvāt varṇāḥ eva krameṇa nirdiśyante iti 
[1177,iv_1177,v]	pariṣad prativādibhyām tris abhihitam api avijñātam avijñāta artham yat vākyam pariṣadā prativādinā ca tris abhihitam api na vijñāyate śliṣṭa śabdam apratīta prayogam atidruta uccaritam iti evamādinā kāraṇena tat avijñātam avijñāta artham asāmarthya saṃvaraṇāya prayuktam iti nigraha sthānam iti 
[1177,vi_1177,vii]	paurvāparya ayogāt apratisambaddha artham apārthakam yatra anekasya padasya vākyasya vā paurvāparyeṇa anvaya yogaḥ na asti iti asambaddha artha tva gṛhyate tat samudāya arthasya apāyāt apārthakam yathā daśa dāḍimāni ṣaṭ apūpāḥ kuṇḍam aja ajinam palala piṇḍaḥ atha raurukam etat kumāryāḥ pāyam tasyāḥ pitā apratiśīnaḥ iti 
[1181,i_1181,ii]	avayava viparyāsa vacanam aprāpta kālam pratijña ādīnām avayavānām yathālakṣaṇam artha vaśāt kramaḥ tatra avayava viparyāsena vacanam aprāpta kālam asambaddha artham nigraha sthānam iti 
[1185,i_1185,ii]	hīnam anyatamena api avayavena nyūnam pratijña ādīnām avayavānām anyatamena api avayavena hīnam nyūnam nigraha sthānam sādhana abhāve sādhya asiddhiḥ iti 
[1186,i_1186,ii]	hetu udāharaṇa adhikam adhikam ekena kṛta tvāt anyatarasya ānarthakyam iti tat etat niyama abhupagame veditavyam iti 
[1187,i_1187,iii]	śabda arthayoḥ punar vacanam punar uktam anyatra anuvādāt anyatra anuvādāt śabda punaruktam artha punaruktam vā nityaḥ śabdaḥ nityaḥ śabdaḥ iti śabda punaruktam artha punaruktam anityaḥ śabdaḥ nirodha dharmakaḥ dhvaniḥ iti anuvāde tu apunaruktam śabda abhyāsāt artha viśeṣa upapatteḥ yathā hetu apadeśāt pratijñāyāḥ punar vacanam nigamanam iti 
[1187,iv_1187,v]	arthāt āpannasya sva śabdena punarvacanam punaruktam iti prakṛtam nidarśanam utpatti dharmaka tvāt anityam iti uktvā arthād āpannasya yaḥ abhidhāyakaḥ śabdaḥ tena sva śabdena brūyāt anutpatti dharmakam nityam iti tat ca punarukatam veditavyam artha sampratyaya arthe śabda prayoge pratītaḥ saḥ arthaḥ artha āpttyeti 
[1189,i_1189,ii]	vijñātasya pariṣadā tris abhihitasya api apratyuccāraṇam ananubhāṣaṇam vijñātasya vākya arthasya pariṣadā prativādinā tris abhihitasya yat apratyauccāraṇam tat ananubhāṣaṇam nāma nigraha sthānam iti apratyuccārayan kim āśrayam para pakṣa pratiṣedham brūyāt 
[1191,i_1191,ii]	avijñātam ca ajñānam vijñāta arthasya pariṣadā prativādinā tris abhihitasya yat avijñātam tat ajñānam nāma nigraha sthānam iti ayam khalu avijñāya kasya pratiṣedham brūyāt iti 
[1191,iii_1191,iv]	uttarasya apratipattiḥ apratibhā para pakṣa pratiṣedhaḥ uttaram tat yadā na pratipadyate tadā nigṛhītaḥ bhavati 
[1192,i_1192,ii]	kārya vyāsaṅgāt kathā vicchedaḥ vikṣepaḥ yatra kartavyam vyāsajya kathām vyavacchinatti idam me karaṇīyam vidyate tasmin avasite paścāt kathayāmi iti vikṣepaḥ nāma nigraha sthānam eka nigraha avasānāyām kathāyām svayam eva kathā antaram pratipadyate iti 
[1193,i_1193,ii]	sva pakṣe doṣa abhyupagamāt para pakṣe doṣa prasaṅgaḥ mata anujñā yaḥ pareṇa coditam doṣam sva pakṣe abhyupagamyān uddhṛtya vadati bhavat pakṣe api samānaḥ doṣaḥ iti sa sva pakṣe doṣa abhyupagamāt para pakṣe doṣam prasañjayan para matam anujānāti iti matānujñām nāma nigraha sthānam āpadyate iti 
[1195,i_1195,ii]	nigraha sthāna prāptasya anigrahaḥ paryanuyojya upekṣaṇam paryanuyojyaḥ nāma nigraha upapattyā codanīyaḥ tasya upekṣaṇam nigraha sthānam prāptaḥ asi iti ananuyogaḥ etat ca kasya parājaya iti anuyuktayā pariṣadā vacanīyam na khalu nigraham prāptaḥ sva kaupīnam vivṛṇuyāt iti 
[1196,i_1196,ii]	anigraha sthāne nigraha sthāna abhiyogaḥ niranuyojya anuyogaḥ nigraha sthā lakṣaṇasya mithyā adhyavasāyāt anigraha sthāne nigṛhītaḥ asi iti param bruvan niranuyojya anuyogāt nigṛhītaḥ veditavyaḥ iti 
[1197,i_1197,ii^1]	siddhāntam abhyupetya aniyamāt kathā prasaṅgaḥ apasiddhāntaḥ kasyacid arthasya tathā abhāvam pratijñāya pratijñāta artha viparyayāt aniyamāt kathām prasañjayataḥ apasiddhāntaḥ veditavyaḥ yathā na sat ātmānam jahāti na sataḥ vināśaḥ na asat ātmānam labhate na asat utpadyate iti siddhāntam abhyupetya sva pakṣam vyavasthāpayati eka prakṛti idam vyaktam vikārāṇām anvaya darśanāt mṛd anvitānām śarāva ādīnām dṛṣṭam eka prakṛti tvam tathā ca ayam vyakta bhedaḥ sukha duḥkha moha anvitaḥ dṛśyate tasmāt samanvaya darśanāt sukha ādibhiḥ eka prakṛti idam viśvam iti evam uktavān anuyujyate atha pratṛtiḥ vikāraḥ iti katham lakṣitavyam iti yasya avasthitasya dharma antara nivṛttau dharma antaram pravartate sā prakṛtiḥ 
[1197,ii^2]	yat dharma antaram pravartate nivartate vā sa vikāraḥ iti saḥ ayam pratijñāta artha viparyāsāt aniyamāt kathām prasañjayati pratijñātam khalu anena na asat āvirbhavati na sat tirobhavati iti sat asatoḥ ca tirobhāva āvirbhāvam antareṇa na kasyacid pravṛttiḥ pravṛtti uparamaḥ ca bhavati mṛdi khalu avasthitāyām bhaviṣyati śarāva ādi lakṣaṇam dharma antaram iti pravṛttiḥ bhavati abhūt iti ca pravṛtti uparamaḥ tat etat mṛd dharmāṇām api na syāt evam pratyavasthitaḥ yadi sataḥ ca ātmahānam asataḥ ca ātma lābham abhyupaiti tat asya apasiddhānataḥ nigraha sthānam bhavati atha na abhyupaiti pakṣaḥ asya na sidhyati 
[1199,i_1200,ii]	hetvābhāsāḥ ca yathā uktāḥ hetvābhāsāḥ ca nigraha sthānāni kim punar lakṣaṇa antara yogāt hetvābhāsāḥ nigraha sthāna tvam āpannāḥ yathā pramāṇāni prameya tvam iti atas āha yathā uktāḥ iti hetvābhāsa lakṣaṇena eva nigraha sthāna bhāvaḥ iti te ime pramāṇa ādayaḥ padārthāḥ uddiṣṭāḥ lakṣitāḥ parīkṣitāḥ ca iti yaḥ akṣapādam ṛṣim nyāyaḥ pratyabhāt vadatām varam tasya vātsyāyanaḥ idam bhāṣya jātam avartayat
